Peng5-Bin5 e5 Ki-Tok-Toan7

Tan5 Chheng-chun3  Phah-ji7

Lim5 Chun3-iok8  Cheng2-li2

Te7  I  Koan3
Ti7 Khi2-thau5

Te7-1 chiuN	Be7 u7 Se3-Kai3, I Chiu7 I2-Keng Ti7-teh

	“Ti7 khi2-thau5 u7 To7, To7 kap Siong7-te3 saN-kap ti7-teh, To7 chiu7-si7 Siong7-te3.”  Lan2 ai3 tui3 chia lai5 kong2-khi2 Ki-tok e5 seng-gai5.  Ti7 se3-kan bo5 lun7 sim2-mih8 ui2-tai7 e5 lang5, i e5 toan7-ki3, lan2 long2 si7 tui3 i chhut-si3, i chhou chhut-hian7 e5 jit8 lai5 kong2-khi2.  Chong2-si7 lun7 lan2 e5 Chu2 e5 toan7-ki3, lan2 e5 su-siuN2 tioh8 ai3 to3-tng2 siuN7 kau3 ti7 I sou2 siok8 hit e5 eng2-oan2 e5 se3-kai3, chai7 ti7 hit e5 se3-kai3 teh khoaN3, lan2 chit e5, si7 kan-ta ngou2-jian5 e5 su7.  PoaN5-ke3 lan2 sou2 bat chit e5 se3-kai3, poaN5-ke3 cheng3 chhiN-sin5, i2-kip8 but8-chit, khong-kan, si5-kan e5 kai3-han7 goa7, u7 chit8 e5 sit8-chai7 e5 se3-kai3, Eng2-oan2-chia2 e5 se3-kai3, chiu7-si7 Siong7-te3 i2-kip8 cheng3 seng3-sai3 sou2 tiam3 e5, chiu7-si7 lan2 chit e5 se3-kai3 i2-kip8 ki5-thaN--e5 e5 goan5-thau5 e5 se3-kai3 ti7-teh.  Che si7 lan2 e5 sin3-giong2 e5 it-chhe3 sou2 kun-ku3 e5 su7-sit8. Lan2 be7 thang khoaN3-kiN3 hit e5 se3-kai3, lan2 be7 thang chhek-liong7 hit e5 liok8-toe7, hit e5 hai2-hoaN7. Hit e5 ng5-kim siaN5-chhi7 e5 kong-chhai2, be7 bat khap8-tioh8 lan2 e5 bak8-chiu.  Chong2-si7 lan2 sin3 hit e5 se3-kai3 si7 tui3 eng2-oan2 u7 pau-ui5 ti7 lan2 e5 sin-piN, iah8 Hit e5 tui3 hia lai5 e5, u7 ka7 lan2 kong2-khi2 hit sou2-chai7 e5 siau-sit.
	I m7 han7-tiaN7 po3 lan2 chai hit e5 se3-kai3 si7 chit8 e5 bo5 han7-liong7 e5 seng3 e5 se3-kai3, iau2-ku2, kiam2-chhai2 oe7 khah khak-chhiat lai5 kam2-tong7 lan2 choe7-choe7 lang5 e5, chiu7-si7 kong2, hit e5 se3-kai3 si7 chit8 e5 bo5 han7-liong7 e5 chhin-chhiat, iu2-ai3 e5 se3-kai3, ia7 in ti7 hit-peng5 e5 lang5 jiat8-jiat8 teh koan-sim ti7 lan2 chit- peng5 e5 lang5.  Chiau3 Seng3-chheh e5 kian3-kai2, ti7 hit e5 Bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 e5 se3-kai3, u7 kui toa7 tin7 e5 lang5 chhim-chhim teh koan-sim lan2 se3-kan lang5 e5 seng-oah8.  “Lan2 i2-keng u7 choe3 kan-cheng3 e5 lang5 kau3 hiah choe7, chhin-chhiuN7 hun5 ui5 lan2.”  Hit e5 eng2-oan2 e5 se3-kai3, si7 Ia5-sou e5 chou2-ke, sou2-i2 I u7 si5-siong5 kam2-kak chit e5 tai7-chi3.  I u7 po3 lan2 chai thiN-nih8 e5 Pe7, si5-siong5 eng7 thiaN3-thang3 kap ai-siong e5 sim teh khoaN3-kou3 lan2.  I u7 po3 lan2 chai, ti7 toe7-nih8 chit8 e5 choe7-jin5 hoan2-hoe2, chiu7 ti7 thiN-nih8 ui7-tioh8 an2-ne lai5 hoaN-hi2. I u7 po3 lan2 chai, hiah e5 teh chiau3-kou3 toe7-chiuN7 e5 soe3-han3 gin2-na2 e5 thiN-sai3 u7 “siong5-siong5 kiN3 goa2 ti7 thiN-nih8 e5 Pe7 e5 bin7.”  I u7 po3 lan2 chai, A-pek-liap8-han2 ti7 hit e5 Bo5-khoaN3-kiN3 e5 se3-kai3, teh hoaN-hi2 lai5 khoaN3 I e5 jit8 ti7-chia, chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni, hit e5 se3-kai3 u7 put-chi2 teh koan-sim ti7 lan2.  Ti7 Ia5-sou pian3 iong5-mau7 e5 kou3-su7-tiong, u7 nng7 ui7 Ku7-iok si5-tai7 e5 seng3-tou5, chiu7-si7 Mou5-se, I2-li7-a tui3 hit e5 Bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 e5 se3-kai3 u7 lai5 chih-chiap in e5 Chu2, lai5 kap I kong2-oe7,--- Si7 kong2 sim2-mih8?  Kiam2 si7 kong2-khi2 Hoat-lo2 ong5 kap Ang5-hai2 e5 su7, A-khap ong5 kap Na2-pok8 e5 phu5-to5-hng5 e5 su7, chiu7-si7 in ti7 toe7-chiuN7 sou2 te7-it koan-sim e5 su7 mah?  He2, m7-si7.  In iu5-goan5 u7 tui-jip ti7 hit e5 ui2-tai7 e5 cheng-sin5, chiu7-si7 tui3 hit e5 eng2-oan2 e5 se3-kai3 sou2 teh chu3-i3 lan2--e5 e5 chhin-chhiat e5 liam7-thau5.  “In tam5-lun7 I e5 ke3-si3, chiu7-si7 I ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 sou2 beh lek8-ke3 e5.”  Che kiam2 m7-si7 am3-si7 lan2 chai in chhim-chhim sou2 koan-sim e5, chiu7-si7 ti7 hit e5 TiuN3-li5 lai7, in i2-kip8 in e5 toa7 e5 tang5-phoaN7 ti7 toe7-bin7-chiuN7 chin2-kiu3 e5 su7-giap8 tiong sou2 koan-sim e5 mah?
	Chit e5 pi2-kau3-tek, long2 si7 khah kun7-tai7 e5 su7,---chi2-u7 si7 2000 ni5 cheng5 e5 su7.  chong2-si7 Po2-lo5 u7 tui3 I2-hut-sou2 lang5 kong2-khi2, tui3 goan5 khi2-thau5 hit e5 se3-kai3, chiu7 i2-keng u7 chhim-chhim teh koan-sim ti7 lan2, iah8 Ia5-sou lim5-kau3 se3-kan chit e5 ke3-ek8, m7-si7 Siong7-te3 choe3 pat8 hang7 su7 liau2, chiah siuN7-tioh8 e5.  Che chiu7-si7 be7 chhong3-cho7 thiN-toe7 e5 i2-cheng5, tui3 Siong7-te3 e5 thiaN3-thang3, chiu7 i2-keng u7 chit e5 eng2-oan2 e5 ke3-ek8, chiu7-si7 beh hou7 eng2-oan2 e5 Ki-tok lai5 chin2-kiu3 jin5-lui7, lai5 chu7-chip8 toe7-bin7-chiuN7 cheng3 kho2-lin5 e5 kiaN2-ji5, kui ti7 thiN-nih8 e5 Pe7 e5 Seng3-chhiu2.  Siong7-te3 u7 si5-siong5 teh khoaN3-kou3 lan2.
	Ng3-bang7 lan2 chiong che khek-tiau5 ti7 sim--nih8, thang khah oe7 liau2-kai2 Seng3-chheh sou2 ka3-si7 e5 to7-li2, chiu7-si7 kong2, “Jin5-lui7 e5 keng-giam7 tiong, Siong7-te3 tak8 teng2-ho7 e5 khe2-si7, ti7 be7 piau2-hian7 ti7-chia chit e5 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 e5 se3-kai3 e5 i2-cheng5, i2-keng u7 pi7-pan7 ti7-hia hit e5 Bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 e5 se3-kai3.  Be7 hian2-hian7 ti7 chit-peng5 e5 tai7-seng, chiu7 i2-keng ku2-ku2 ti7 hit-peng5 long2 chai hit e5 su7-sit8.”  Tiam3 ti7 hit e5 chhin-chhiat e5 se3-kai3, “Ti7 khi2-thau5 u7 To7, To7 kap Siong7-te3 saN-kap ti7-teh, To7 chiu7-si7 Siong7-te3.”  Ti7 hit e5 hng7-hng7 eng2-oan2 e5 se3-kai3, Siong7-te3 e5 thiaN3-thang3 e5 ke3-ek8 tiong, chiu7 i2-keng u7 pi7-pan7 Siong7-te3 e5 Seng3 KiaN2 hoa3-sin ai3 “beh ui7-tioh8 lan2 cheng3-lang5 i2-kip8 lan2 e5 chin2-kiu3.”
	Sou2-i2 lan2 beh tui-chhe7 lan2 e5 Chu2 e5 seng-oah8, tioh8 ai3 to3-tng2 siuN7 kau3 chin hng7 e5 sou2-chai7, si7 tioh8 ai3 poaN5-ke3 lan2 e5 siong2-siong7 e5 khui3-lat8, sou2 tat8 oe7 kau3 e5 kek8-tiam2, si7 tioh8 ai3 kau3 ti7 Chhong3-se3-ki3 teh kong2-khi2 goan5 khi2-thau5 Siong7-te3 u7 chhong3-cho7 thiN-toe7, hit-si5 koh khi2-khi3 be7 sng3 tit e5 si5, si7 tioh8 ai3 kau3 ti7 Seng3 KiaN2 hoa3-sin, “Hi-lut8 ong5 e5 si5, Ia5-sou u7 chhut-si3 ti7 Iu5-thai3 e5 Pek-li7-heng5,” Hit-si5 koh khi2-khi3 bo5 han7-liong7 e5 si5, chiah oe7 thang tui-chhe7-tioh8 lan2 e5 Chu2 e5 toan7-ki3 e5 khi2-goan5.
	Teng2-bin7 sou2 kong2 chiah-e5, si7 Iok-han7 teh sia2 Ki-tok-toan7 e5 thai3-tou7.
	Goa2 ai3 siau3-liam7-tioh8 tiam3 ti7 I2-hut-sou2 hit e5 sou2 thiaN3 e5 ni5-lau7 e5 kam3-tok, chiu7-si7 “Ia5-sou sou2 thiaN3 e5 hak8-seng Iok-han7, “ tng i be7 si2 e5 tai7-seng, u7 che7-teh giah8-pit lai5 sia2 hit pun2 “Lan2 e5 Chu2 e5 Seng-gai5,” hit-pun2 “It lau7-lang5 e5 ki3-ek e5 Hok-im-toan7.”
	Ia5-sou chai7-se3 saN-ni5 ku2, ti7 Pa-lek-su-theng3 kek8 chhin-bit8 lai5 kap i kau-poe5, ti7 i Iok-han7 e5 ki3-ek tiong, u7 eng2-oan2 e5 Ki-tok, chit e5 khah chhim, giam5-siok e5 su-siong2 ti7-teh, chit e5 eng2-oan2 e5 Ki-tok, chiu7-si7 “tui3 kou2-cha2 i2-lai5 pun2 u7 e5, chiap8-chiap8 tu3-hian7” ti7 se3-kan.  Sou2-i2 Iok-han7 u7 kan-cheng3 kong2, “Ti7 khi2-thau5 u7 To7, To7 kap Siong7-te3 saN-kap ti7-teh. To7 chiu7-si7 Siong7-te3.”  Hit-si5 Iok-han7 u7 siuN7-tioh8 eng2-oan2 e5 Ki-tok ti7 be7 hoa3-sin e5 tai7-seng ku2-ku2 chaiN2-iuN7 u7 teh khoaN3-kou3 chit e5 kho2-lin5 e5 se3-kai3.  Tng chit e5 se3-kai3 be7 bat siuN7-tioh8 I, iau2 kap I li7 hng7-hng7 ti7 hit e5 am3-am3 ke3-khi3 e5 si5, “I i2-keng ti7 se3-kan, se3-kan tui3 I lai5 chhong3-cho7, ia7 se3-kan m7-bat I.”  “Oah8-mia7 ti7 I e5 lai7-bin7; chit e5 oah8-mia7 si7 lang5 e5 kng.”  “U7 chin e5 kng lai5 jip8 se3-kan, teh chio3 ban7-lang5.”
	I2-siong7 sou2 kong2 chiah-e5, long2 si7 o3-biau7 e5 oe7, se3-kan lang5 e5 su-siong2, sit8-chai7 si7 oh-tit liau2-kai2.  Chin ki5-koai3! an2-choaN2 kong2, “Chit e5 Ki-tok put-si5 ti7-chia.  I tiam3 ti7 U2-tiu7 lai7, choe3 U2-tiu7 e5 oah8-mia7.  I tiam3 ti7 lang5 e5 lai7-bin7, choe3 liong5-sim e5 kng.  Sui-jian5 lan2 be7 bat I, iau2-ku2 be7 u7 se3-kan e5 tai7-seng, I chiu7 i2-keng khia7-khi2 ti7 lan2 tiong-kan.”  Che tu2-tu2 si7 chiau3 Au-gu5-tin7 (Augustine) e5 i3-su3, sou2 kong2, Ki-tok-kau3 si7 tui3 khai-pit8 thiN-toe7 e5 si5, chiu7 kap lan2 saN-kap ti7-teh.  Che tu2-tu2 si7 chiau3 Tek-tou-liong5 (Tertullian) e5 sim-su tiong ho2-taN2 lai5 siuN7 kong2, tui3 ban7-se3 i2-lai5 Ki-tok chiu7 pi7-pan7 beh hoa3-sin chiaN5 choe3 lang5.
	Iok-han7 chai ti7 be7 hoa3-sin e5 i2-cheng5, chhin-chhiuN7 ti7 toe7-bin7-chiuN7 e5 khoan2-sit, I u7 tui3 ti7 Chu7-jian5, Li2-seng3, Liong5-sim, lai5 khe2-si7 hit e5 bu5-han7-liong7 e5 Siong7-te3.  Sou2-i2 i u7 chhai2-iong7 tong-si5 Hi-li7-ni5 lang5, Iu5-thai3 lang5, ti7 su-siong2 kai3 sou2 koan3-iong7 hit ku3 “Siong7-te3 e5 To7” e5 oe7, lai5 kan-cheng3 kong2, “Ti7 khi2-thau5 u7 To7.”  Eng7 chit-ji7 “To7” lai5 piau2-beng5 Ki-tok, chhou-chhou thiaN-liau2, si7 ki5-koai3 e5 khoan2.  Chong2-si7 ki5-sit8 u7 piau2-beng5 chit e5 su3-tou5 e5 tiong-sim su-siong2, koh-chai3 ia7 u7 li7-pian7 e5 sou2-chai7, in-ui7 tong-si5 Hi-li7-ni5 lang5 e5 tiat-hak8 i2-kip8 Iu5-thai3 lang5 e5 su-siong2, long2 kiong7-thong koaiN3-si3 teh eng7 hit ku3 oe7.  Chiau3 Hi-li7-ni5 e5 tiat-hak8 su-siong2, kan2-liok8 lai5 kong2, lang5 si7 be7 thang khoaN3-kiN3, ia7 be7 thang bong-tioh8 ban7-mih8 e5 bu5-han7-liong7 e5 goan5-thau5.  Lan2 chi2-u7 thang tui3 ti7 lan2 e5 sin-piN ti7 se3-kai3 tiong, I sou2 hian2-hian7 e5 lai5 bat I.  Sou2-i2 in u7 eng7 hit ku3 sui2-sui2, chhin-chhiuN7 si e5 phi3-ju7, lai5 chheng-hou Siong7-te3 sou2 hian2-hian7 e5, kio3-choe3 si7 “I e5 To7.”
	ChhiaN2 lai5 siuN7 hit e5 li2-khi3.  Na7 lun7 lan2 lang5 bo5-lun7 chi7-chui7, si7 an2-choaN2 teh piau2-hian7 i e5 sim-su i2-kip8 i e5 lai7-bin7 seng-oah8? chi2-u7 si7 tui3 i sou2 kong2-chhut e5 oe7.  Tui3 i sou2 kong2 e5 oe7, u7 piau2-hian7 i pun2-sin, tui3 i pun2-sin kap lan2 kau-poe5, lai5 chhian2-beng5 i e5 sim-su, i2-kip8 i e5 kam2-cheng5, lai5 sit8-heng5 i e5 i3-hiong3.  Tui3 i e5 sim-su, i3-hiong3 sou2 hoat-chhut e5 oe7, u7 piau2-chhut i e5 lai7-bin7 cheng-sin5 kap i e5 phin2-seng3.  Sou2-i2 kong2 tui3 i e5 oe7 lan2 thang bat i.
	TaN lan2 beh chaiN2-iuN7 thang lai5 bat hit e5 bu5-han7-liong7, be7 thang khoaN3-kiN3, be7 thang bat e5 Siong7-te3 mah?  chi2-u7 thang tui3 lang5 e5 liong5-sim, ki5-iN7 e5 oah8-mia7, toa7-hong i2-kip8 chheng-thian pek8-jit8, mi5-kan e5 kiong-chhong, ki5-iN7 e5 le5-beng5, sui2 e5 toe7-bin7, eng5-kng e5 hai2-tiong, i2-kip8 hit e5 teh iuN2-chhi7 se3-kan lang5 e5 ng3-kim-sek e5 beh8-hng5, tui3 chiah e5 hian7-siong7, thang lai5 bat I.  Chiah-e5 si7 Siong7-te3 e5 hian2-hian7, si7 I tui3 lang5 sou2 kong2 e5 oe7, chiu7-si7 I e5 To7, put-lun7 siaN2-khoan2 khui3-lat8 lai5 chhong3-cho7 chiah-e5, lian5 iN7-pang lang5 e5 tiat-hak8-chia2 to seng5-jin7 kong2, che si7 “Chi3-koaiN5--e5 e5 To7.”
	Sit8-chai7 iN7-pang lang5 e5 su-siong2, si7 kan-ta oe7 thang siuN7 kau3 chia na7-tiaN7.  Chong2-si7 chit e5 su3-tou5 e5 su-siong2, si7 chin3-jip8 koh-khah chhim.  I chai-iaN2 u7 chit8 e5 khah oan5-choan5 e5 hian2-hian7 ti7-teh.  In-ui7 saN-ni5 ku2 e5 tiong-kan, i u7 kap I saN-kap kiaN5 ti7 Pa-lek8-su-theng3 e5 chhan5-hng5, taN chit-tiap8 i chai, I si7 hit e5 khah oan5-choan5 e5 hian2-hian7, si7 Siong7-te3 tui3 se3-kan sou2 kong2-chhut e5 To7.  Sou2-i2 i u7 soa3-chiap kong2, “To7 u7 chiaN5-choe3 jiok8-the2.”  Chit e5 To7, chiu7-si7 ti7 goan5 khi2-thau5, ti7 bi5-biau7 e5 chu7-jian5, sin5-pi3 e5 oah8-mia7, u7 piau2-hian7 Siong7-te3 e5, kiat-kiok8 kau3 hit e5 si5-ki5 moa2, chiu7 chiaN5-choe3 chit8 e5 khah oan5-choan5 e5 hian2-hian7.  “To7 chiaN5 jiok8-the2, khia7-khi2 ti7 lan2 tiong-kan, u7 un-tian2 kap chin-li2 moa2-moa2.”  Che chiu7-si7 Siong7-te3 e5 khe2-si7 e5 kek8-tiam2, put-tan3 si7 Siong7-te3 khe2-si7 I e5 khui3-lat8 i2-kip8 I e5 ui2-tai7, iah8 si7 khe2-si7 I e5 sim, I e5 bu5-han7-liong7 e5 iu2-ai3, kap thiaN3-thang3.  Tui3 an2-ni, lan2 chai Iok-han7 teh eng7 chit ku3 lai5 chheng-hou I si7 Siong7-te3 e5 To7, hit e5 choan5 cheng-sin5 si7 chhin-chhiuN7 chit-khoan2.
	Chong2-si7 chit e5 kho2-lin5 e5 se3-kai3, tioh8 ku2-ku2 lai5 theng3-hau7 hit e5 hian2-hian7.  Lan2 m7-chai, siaN2-su7 Siong7-te3 ian5-chhian5 I e5 hoa3-sin kau3 hiah-nih8 ku2, chong2-si7 lan2 chai, I u7 teh khoaN3-kou3 Ki-tok be7 chhut-si3 i2-cheng5 hit e5 kou-tok8 e5 se3-kai3.  Lan2 chai I u7 tui3 eng2-oan2 lai5 pou2-chhiong in sou2 sit-loh8 e5 ki-hoe7.  Siong7-te3 ti7 eng2-oan2 e5 chit-peng5 kap hit-peng5 e5 tiong-kan, put-si5 to teh choe3 kang.
	Lan2 tai7-ke khiok si7 oe7 thang tong5-cheng5 Ki-tok i2-cheng5 hiah e5 khia7-khi2 ti7 hit e5 kou-tok8 e5 se3-kai3 e5 lang5.  In chhin-chhiuN7 lan2 chit8-poaN, iu5-goan5 u7 teh him-bou7 ho2 e5 sim ti7-teh.  In u7 in e5 khoa3-lu7, in e5 sim iu5-goan5 u7 tong7-iau5,  in chhin-chhiuN7 lan2 chit8-poaN, oe7-hiau2 toa7 pi-siong ka-ki7 e5 kiaN2 si2 ti7 chian3-tiuN5.  Ti7 in e5 sim-sin5, jiok8-the2 i2-kip8 in e5 keng2-hong2, chhin-chhiuN7 lan2 chit8-poaN, iu5-goan5 u7 kan-khou2 ti7-teh.  Kho2-sioh bo5 u7 chu5-pi e5 Siong7-te3 thang chhin-kun7.  In pi-chham2 lai5 teh chhe7 I.  In e5 tiat-hak8-ka tui3 chu7-jian5-kai3 e5 hian2-hian7 lai5 kan-cheng3 u7 chit8 e5 cho7-but8 Chu2; chong2-si7 chu7-jian5-kai3 chi2-u7 oe7 chi2-si7 lan2 bat I si7 chit8 e5 ui2-tai7 koh u7 khui3-lat8 e5 na7-tiaN7.  Khah u7 bun5-beng5 e5 bin5-chok8, chiu7 chiong in e5 chhui-siong2, lai5 piau2-hian7 ti7 Jiu5-pi2-tah (Jupitor) i2-kip8 Jiu5-no2 (Juno) e5 sin5-beng5.  Chong2-si7 chin kho2-sioh!  Chit khoan2 sin5 m7-si7 oe7 thiaN iu-bun7 e5 lang5 e5 ki5-to2.  Chai7 hiah e5 khah ia2-ban5 e5 bin5-chok8, hit e5 be7 thang ti2-khong3 e5 chu7-jian5-kai3 e5 toa7 khui3-lat8, u7 hou7 in put-chi2 kiaN-hiaN5.  In thiaN-kiN3 toa7 hong hiu3-hiu3 kio3, chhiu7-ki sihN-soaihN8(**siNh-soaiNh8)-kio3, i2-kip8 lui5-kong sih-na3, loh8 phauh e5 cheng5-keng2, hit-si5 in chiu7 chhiN-kiaN, lai5 bih ti7 toe7-ham7-lai7, lai5 choe3 ngou2-siong7, tah hu5, hok8-sai7 kiu5-kio3 in, ng3-bang7 thang tin3-cheng7 hit e5 kek8-toa7 khui3-lat8 e5 chun5-chai7-chia2 e5 siu7-khi3.  Hiah e5 ngou2-siong7 chiu7-si7 in chi2-i3 beh lai5 piau2-hian7 Siong7-te3.
	Lan2 kian3 thak8 kou2-cha2 e5 lek8-su2, khah siong5 chiu7 thang chai hit e5 kho2-lin5 kou-tok8 e5 cha2 e5 se3-kai3, “u7 teh chhe7 Siong7-te3.”  In e5 tiat-hak8, sin5-oa7, ngou2-siong7, i2-kip8 in sou2 pai3 e5 mih8, si7 in sou2 chhe7 oe7 kau3 it-chhe3 e5 kiat-ko2.  Che si7 chin7-chai7 kho2-lin5 e5 su7.  Bo5 chit8 lang5 thang po3 in chai-iaN2 in sou2 teh him-bou7 ai3 chai e5.  In kiam2-chhai2 ai3 mng7 kong2, “I kiam2 si7 jin5-keh-tek e5 Siong7-te3, ti7 I kiam2 u7 sim-cheng5 ti7-teh mah?  Ti7 I kiam2 u7 cheng3-gi7, thiaN3-thang3 e5 sim-cheng5 mah?  I kiam2 oe7 thiaN khou2-lan7 e5 lau7-bu2 teh thi5-khau3 i sou2 sit-loh8 e5 kiaN2-ji5 mah?  I kiam2 si7 bat teh siau3-liam7 lan2 se3-kan lang5 mah?  Khak-sit8 chit-khoan2 e5 giau5-gi5, si7 thang kho2-lin5 e5 su7.  Siat-su2 lan2 na7 bo5 sin3 Siong7-te3 u7 chiau3-kou3 in, u7 chit8-jit8, ti7 sim2-mih8 se3-kai3, I beh pou2-chhiong in sou2 sit-loh8 e5 ki-hoe7, lan2 thang siuN7 I si7 kau3-giah8 chan5-jim2 kam-sim pang3-sak se3-kan lang5.
	Siong7-te3 e5 khe2-si7 u7 kong2, tioh8 chiong in kau-thok Siong7-te3.  Ki-tok u7 teh khoaN3-kou3 in, Ia5-sou Ki-tok saN jit8 ku2 e5 tiong-kan, u7 tui3 Sip8-ji7-ke3 tit8-tit8 khi3 chhe7 hiah e5 tiam3 ti7 “KaN-lai7 e5 Sin5-hun5,” lai5 tui3 in thoan5 ho2 e5 siau-sit.
	Sou2-i2 lan2 thang chiong Ku7-iok si5-tai7 e5 lang5 kau-tai7 Ia5-sou Ki-tok.  Kiam2 si7 iau2 u7 sim2-mih8 khah tu2-ho2 e5 sou2-chai7 thang kau-tai7 mah?
	Hit e5 tng5-tng5 ou-am3 e5 si5-tai7, saN-soa3 ku2-ku2.  Chiau3-khoaN3 Siong7-te3 ia7 bo5 hian2-chhut sim2-mih8 tiau7-thau5.  Chong2-si7 ti7 hit e5 Ku7-iok si5-tai7, na7 khoaN3 khah chhim, Siong7-te3 e5 ke3-ek8 si7 i2-keng bo5 chheN-kong5, koh ia7 bo5 theng5-khun3, ti7-teh chin3-heng5.  Eng7 choe7-choe7 e5 hong-hoat, “Ki-tok u7 teh pi7-pan7 I e5 hoa3-sin.”  Ti7 lek8-su2 tiong, lan2 bo5 kau3-giah8 ti3-sek thang phian2-chhut I sou2 eng7 e5 hoat-tou7.  Kan-ta oe7 thang tui3 chhui-li2 lai5 tit-tioh8 khoaN3-kiN3 tam7-poh8 e5 iaN2-jiah ji5-i2.  Lan2 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 kou2-cha2 cheng3 pang-kok e5 heng-bong5, u7 A-sut8, u7 Pa-pi2-lun5, u7 Pho-su, u7 Hi-li7-ni5, u7 Lo5-ma2.  Lan2 iah8 u7 thiaN-kiN3 ##kou2-cha2, cheng3 sian-ti u7 soan-gian5 kong2, chiah e5 kok-kok e5 heng-bong5, si7 siok8 ti7 hit e5 ui2-tai7 e5 ke3-ek8 e5 chit8-pou7-hun7, thang lai5 oan5-seng5 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 toa7 e5 bok8-tek.
	Kau3 u7 chit8 jit8, lan2 u7 kam2-chhiok-tioh8 koh chit8-sut8-a2 khah beng5 e5 kng.  Ti7 Chu2-cheng5 2000 ni5 e5 u7 chit8-jit8, u7 khoaN3-kiN3 chit8 e5 siau3-lian5 bok8-chia2, khia7 ti7 Su7-li7-a e5 soaN-teng2, i e5 sim-lai7 jiat8-jiat8, khng3 ko-siong7 e5 chi3-khi3, siu7 keng2-tiau3 lai5 li7-khui pai3 ngou2-siong7 e5 kou3-hiong i2-kip8 chhin-chhek, chhut-goa7 khi3 kau3 ti7 i sou2 m7-chai e5 sou2-chai7.  Chit-e5 chiu7-si7 A-pek-liap8-han2.  A-pek-liap8-han2 ti7 i e5 sim-lai7 thiaN-kiN3 Eng2-oan2-chia2 teh kio3 e5 siaN, chiu7 chhut-hoat hiong3-cheng5 lai5 chin7 i e5 su2-beng7.  Ti7 put-ti put-kak e5 tiong-kan, i chin3-cheng5 lai5 tam-tng KiaN5 soe2-le2 e5 Iok-han7 e5 kang, ti7 Ku7-iok e5 si5-tai7, “lai5 pi7-pan7 Chu2 e5 lou7.”  Tui3 an2-ni lai5 khai-si2 Iu5-thai3 bin5-chok8 e5 hun3-lian7.  Tui3-chia khi2, Iu5-thai3 lang5 tek8-piat8 u7 keng2-soan2 lai5 kap se3-kan it-poaN saN keh-li7, khui in e5 sim lai5 seng5-siu7 Siong7-te3 sin e5 khe2-si7.  In li7-piat8 chou2-kong e5 ngou2-siong7 kap to-sin5 e5 to7-li2, lai5 chong5-hong7 tok8-it e5 Siong7-te3 e5 ka3-si7; chit e5 to7-li2, si7 i2-cheng5 be7-bat u7 chit8 e5 bin5-chok8 sou2 bat siu7 e5.  Ji5-hou7 ti7 in e5 lek8-su2 tiong, u7 thiaN-kiN3 sian-ti e5 siaN, lai5 soan-thoan5 Siong7-te3 gi7 e5 sim-chi3.  Ti7 lek8-tai7 e5 sian-ti e5 tiong-kan, u7 kong2-chhut chin o3-biau7 e5 tek8-piat8 e5 iok-sok, chiu7-si7 kong2, ti7 au7-jit8 Iu5-thai3 lang5 i2-kip8 in e5 kiaN2-sun ti7 cheng3 pang-kok e5 tiong-kan, beh tit-tioh8 toa7-toa7 e5 chiok-hok.  Ti7 chiah e5 sian-ti sou2 khoaN3 e5 iN7-siong7 tiong, u7 chit8 e5 bo5 loa7 hun-beng5 e5 jin5-but8, chiap8-chiap8 hian2-hian7.  Hit e5 bo5 loa7 hun-beng5 e5 jin5-but8, u7-e5 khoaN3-choe3 si7 lang5, u7-e5 khoaN3-choe3 si7 sin5, ia7 u7-e5 khoaN3-choe3 si7 Tai7-pit8 e5 kiaN2, Jin5-chu2, Siong7-te3 e5 KiaN2, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 lou5-pok8, sin5-biau7 e5 bou5-su7, a2-si7 eng2-oan2 thong2-ti7 se3-kan e5 peng5-an e5 jin5-kun; koh-chai3 u7-e5 khoaN3-choe3 si7 iuN5-ko, si7 beh hou7 lang5 khan khi3 thai5, lai5 choe3 lan2 e5 Chu2, tam-tng lan2 long2-chong2 e5 choe7.
	Chong2 kong2 chit8 ku3, chiu7-si7 lang5 long2 teh chu3-sin5 theng3-hau7 Siong7-te3 e5 chi2-i3 hian2-beng5.  M7-ku2 Siong7-te3 iau2 si7 tiam7-tiam7, long2 bo5 tong7-cheng7.  chong2-si7 Iu5-thai3 e5?? cheng3 kun-ong5, i2-kip8 cheng3 sian-ti si7 it-tit8 ke3-ong2--khi3.  Siong7-chhiaN2 Iu5-thai3 lang5 soa3 tu2-tioh8 kok phoa3, siu7-liah8 lai5 keng-giam7 hit e5 chhiN-chham2 e5 jit8-chi2.  Tui3 an2-ni, Iu5-thai3 lang5 si3-soaN3 khia7-khi2 ti7 phou2 thiN-e7.  Se3-cheng5 e5 pian3-chhian bu5-siong5, u7 hoaN-hi2, u7 pi-siong, u7 saN-chiN, u7 hoan7-choe7.  M7-ku2, Siong7-te3 iu5-goan5 si7 cheng7-cheng7, long2 bo5 hian2-chhut sim2-mih8 tiau7-thau5.



Te7-2 chiuN	Se3-Ka3 u7 Teh Pi7-Pan7

	Keng3-jian5 si5 tit8-tit8 pek-kun7.  ChhiaN2 lai5 chu3-i3 khoaN3 i2-ha7 sou2 beh kong2 chit e5 ki5-iN7 e5 su7-sit8!  Chit e5 se3-kai3 si7 i2-keng u7 teh pi7-pan7!  Chhin-chhiuN7 toa7-hai2 ti7 bo5 i3-sek e5 tiong-kan, i e5 hai2-eng2 te3 geh8 teh tin2-tang7 e5 khoan2-sit, lan2 chit e5 se3-kai3, ia7 ti7 bo5 i3-sek e5 tiong-kan, iu5-goan5 u7 te3 hit e5 eng2-oan2 e5 se3-kai3 ti7-teh tin2-tang7.  Tng hit e5 se3-kai3 teh pi7-pan7 beh chhe-khian2 Ia5-sou hou7 lan2 e5 si5, lan2 chit e5 se3-kai3, ia7 si7 u7 pi7-pan7 beh geng5-chiap I.  Lan2 chit-tiap8 na7 hoe5-kou3 ke3-khi3 e5 se3-kai3 si7 chaiN2-iuN7 teh chun2-pi7, chiu7 thang chai, chhin-chhiuN7 u7 chit8 e5 Sin5 teh cho7-chiu7 jin5-lui7 e5 lek8-su2, lai5 pi7-pan7 Ia5-sou e5 lou7.
	Ti7 chia u7 kui2-na7 hang7 su7-sit8 ti7-teh.  Tng Ki-tok lai5 e5 si5, ti7 se3-kai3 u7 saN-e5 bin5-chok8 chiam3 te7-it toa7 e5 se3-lek8.  Hit saN-e5 bin5-chok8, chiu7-si7 Hi-li7-ni5, Lo5-ma2, i2-kip8 Iu5-thai3, chiu7-si7 hit e5 u7 bun5-nga2 e5 Hi-li7-ni5 lang5, u7 koan5-peng3 e5 Lo5-ma2 lang5, i2-kip8 siu7 lang5 oan3-hun7, siu7 lang5 iam3-chian7 e5 Iu5-thai3 lang5.  In si7 ti7 hit e5 u7 bun5-beng5 e5 se3-kai3 tiong te7-it tu3-hian7 e5 bin5-chok8.  He2, m7-si7!  Iau2-ku2 si7 tioh8 kong2, in chiah si7 u7 bun5-beng5 e5 se3-kai3.  I2-goa7 si7 bo5 lah.  Pi2-liap8-to u7 seng5-jin7 chit e5 su7-sit8, chiu7 eng7 Hi-pek-lai5, Hi-li7-ni5, i2-kip8 Liap8-teng e5 bun5-ji7, lai5 sia2 Sip8-ji7-ke3 teng2 e5 cham2-tiau5.  TaN chit saN-e5 bin5-chok8, ti7 bo5 phah-sng3 e5 tiong-kan, chiau3 khoaN3 chha-put-to chhin-chhiuN7 tai7-ke choe3-he2 lai5 teh pi7-pan7 theng3-hau7 I e5 lim5-kau3; chit e5 su7-sit8, chi3-chio2 hou7 lang5 thang siuN7 si7 Siong7-te3 sou2 an-pai5 e5, kong2 an2-ni, kiam2 u7 ke3-thau5 mah?  Hoan7-na7 lang5 bo5 chun-chong5 Ki-tok e5, kiam2-chhai2 beh khoaN3 chit e5 su7-sit8 si7 lek8-su2 tiong ngou2-gu5-jian5 e5 tai7-chi3.  Chong2-si7 goa2 teh siuN7, hoan7-na7 u7 seng5-jin7 ti7  au7-lai5 beh u7 chiaN5 chit e5 hui-siong5 toa7 e5 tai7-chi3 e5 Ki-tok-tou5, thak8-tioh8 tong-si5 e5 lek8-su2, tek-khak chai, put-tan3 si7 KiaN5 soe2-le2 e5 Iok-han7, lian5 chiu-ui5 e5 se3-kai3, iu5-goan5 si7 hong7-chhe lai5 “teh pi7-pan7 Chu2 e5 lou7.”  Put-koan2 siaN2 khoan2, i2-ha7 ai3 lai5 khoaN3 tong-si5 sou2 tu2-tioh8 e5 chong7-hong2.
	Thau5-chit8 hang7, Lo5-ma2 lang5 u7 siu-cheng2 in e5 to7-lou7, lai5 choe3 toa7 e5 Jin5-kun lim5-kau3 e5 lou7-eng7.  Chu2-cheng5 e5 chit8 se3-ki3, hit-tiap8 e5 se3-kai3 si7 kek8 gau5 hun kai3-han7, hun-lih8 chiaN5-choe3 choe7-choe7 saN keh-li7 e5 soe3-soe3 e5 pang-kok, kok-kok u7 in e5 chong-kau3, hong-siok8, lut8-hoat, koh-chai3 tai7-ke gau5 saN oan3-tou3, ngi7-sim, gau5 sio-thai5.  In sou2 khia7 hit e5 koaiN5-koaiN5 e5 kok-kai3, chou2-chi2 tai7-ke e5 ong2-lai5.  PiN5-iuN5 ui7-tioh8 chian3-loan7 e5 peng-be2 sou2 kiau2-jiau2, hai2-bin7 in-ui7 hai2-chhat8 chin-choe7, ti3-kau3 be7 thang thong-heng5.  Sit8-chai7 lai5 kong2, Chu2-cheng5 e5 chit8 se3-ki2, Pa-lek8-su-theng3 e5 lang5 be7-bat khui mng5 kap goa7-bin7 e5 lang5 saN ong2-lai5.  Sou2-i2 chiau3 lang5 e5 i3-su3 lai5 khoaN3, chit e5 phou2-pian3-tek e5 Hok-im beh tit-tioh8 seng3-li7, thang chu7-iu5 thong-heng5 ti7 choan5 se3-kai3, si7 put-kho2-leng5 e5 su7.
	Tu2-tu2 ti7 chit ho7 gui5-ki, u7 khoaN3-kiN3 put-chi2 tu3-hian7 e5 pian3-chhian.  Lo5-ma2 lang5 u7 oan5-seng5 chit8 e5 toa7 su7-giap8.  Tng Ia5-sou lim5-kau3 e5 si5, hiah e5 khia7 kok-kai3 lai5 saN keh-li7 e5 kok, bo5 koh saN hun-khui, saN giau5-gi5, Ia5-sou u7 khoaN3-kiN3 chit8 e5 bo5 saN-thai5 peng5-ho5 e5 se3-kai3.  Lo5-ma2 lang5 u7 chu7-chip8 hiah e5 bo5 saN lian5-lok8 e5 pang-kok, lai5 chiaN5-choe3 chit8-the2, phah-phoa3 kok lang5 e5 ai3-kok sim, kap kok lang5 ka-ki7 e5 chong-kau3, lai5 thong2-it se3-kai3 choe3-chiaN5 it-tai7 e5 ong5-kok.  Lo5-ma2 e5 toa7-lou7 u7 koan3-chhoan3 ti7 i e5 bun5-beng5 e5 kok-lai7.  Kai-sat e5 toa7 koan5-lek8, gau5 i5-chhi5 te3-kok e5 thai3-peng5.  Lo5-ma2 e5 toa7-lou7 khui-khoah, teh theng3-hau7 toa7 e5 Jin5-kun lim5-kau3.  Lan2 na7 khoaN3 Po2-lo5 u7 hiah-nih8 chu7-iu5 bo5 chou2-gai7, thang lu2-heng5 kau3 ti7 te3-kok e5 tak8 sou2-chai7, tui3 chit hang7 chiu7 thang khoaN3-chhut Lo5-ma2 e5 toa7-lou7, Lo5-ma2 e5 cheng3-ti7, Lo5-ma2 e5 thai3-peng5, lai5 khui-khoah sin e5 chong-kau3 e5 i3-gi7 kau3 siaN2 khoan2.
	Lun7 Lo5-ma2 lang5 kap in e5 toa7-lou7 e5 kong-chek, kong2 kau3-chia chiu7 ho2.  TaN lai5 lun7-khi2 Hi-li7-ni5 lang5 si7 an2-choaN2?  Sui-jian5 u7 khui-khoah e5 to7-lou7 choe3 soan-thoan5 teh lai5 e5 Hok-im e5 lou7-eng7, na7 bo5 u7 thong-iong7 e5 khiuN-khau2 thang chhian2-beng5 hit e5 Hok-im hou7 i khui-khoah kau3 ti7 tak8 sou2-chai7, ia7 si7 bo5 sim2-mih8 u7 lou7-eng7.  Goan5-lai5 Iu5-thai3 lang5 si7 eng7 A-lan5 e5 khiuN-khau2, Lo5-ma2 lang5 bat Liap8-teng e5 bun5-ji7; i2-goa7 choe7-choe7 khoan2 lang5 kong2 choe7-choe7 khoan2 e5 khiuN-khau2, hit e5 hun7-chap8 e5 khoan2-sit, si7 chhin-chhiuN7 ti7 Pa-piat, Siong7-te3 phah-loan7 se3-kan lang5 e5 khiuN-khau2 chit8-iuN7, chong2-si7 kun7-oa2 ti7 Bi2-sai3-a beh lim5-kau3 e5 si5, Hi-li7-ni5 oe7, ti7 bo5 i3-sek e5 tiong-kan u7 hoat-hui i e5 su2-beng7 lai5 pi7-pan7 Chu2 e5 lou7.  Hit e5 sui2 koh li7-pian7 e5 Hi-li7-ni5 oe7, u7 chiaN5-choe3 Lo5-ma2 te3-kok chu2-iau3 e5 khiuN-khau2.  Te7-tiong-hai2 chiu-ui5 e5 lang5, sui-jian5 u7 teh eng7 in pun2-sin e5 khiuN-khau2, iu5-goan5 u7 hak8-sip8 Hi-li7-ni5 oe7.  Tui3 an2-ni, Hi-li7-ni5 oe7 si7 chiaN5-choe3 choan5 bun5-beng5 e5 se3-kai3 e5 khiuN-khau2.  Hi-li7-ni5 oe7 chiu7 chiaN5-choe3 kong-ke e5 khi3-khu7 lai5 soan-thoan5 hit e5 sin e5 ka3-si7.
	Lan2 koh-chai3 thang tui3 Po2-lo5 e5 thoan5-to7 lu2-heng5 tiong e5 kou3-su7 tiong, lai5 tit-tioh8 koh-khah tiong7-iau3 e5 chi2-si7.  Bo5-lun7 ng3 Lo5-ma2 lang5 a2-si7 Ko-lim5-to lang5, ng3 hiah e5 bun5-nga2 e5 Nga2-tian2 lang5, a2-si7 hiah e5 khia7-khi2 ti7 Ka-liap8-thai3 koaiN5 soaN-teng2 e5 bo5 bun5-beng5 e5 iN7-kau3 e5 bin5-chok8, lan2 u7 thiaN-kiN3 Po2-lo5 eng7 “cheng3-lang5 sou2 bat” e5 khiuN-khau2 lai5 thoan5 Siong7-te3 bi5-biau7 e5 Hok-im.
	Bo5-lun7 Hi-li7-ni5 lang5, Lo5-ma2 lang5, a2-si7 Iu5-thai3 lang5, long2 si7 pi7-pan7 Chu2 e5 lou7 e5 sian-hong.  Lo5-ma2 lang5 u7 khui-khoah to7-lou7, Hi-li7-ni5 lang5 u7 kiong-kip khiuN-khau2.  Na7-si7 Iu5-thai3 lang5 si7 an2-choaN2?  In oe7 cho7-chiu7 sim2-mih8?  In siu7 iu-seng3 e5 bin5-chok8 sou2 oan3-hun7, sou2 iam3-chian7, siu7 lang5 pi3-so2 ti7 Lo5-ma2 te3-kok tiong hit e5 soe3-soe3 li7 hng7-hng7 phian-phiah e5 sou2-chai7, sou2-i2 chai7 hit e5 Hok-im tioh8 thoan5 kau3 phou2 thiN-e7 e5 un7-tong7, tui3 in kiam2 u7 sim2-mih8 thang ki5-thai7 mah?
	Chai7 hiah e5 u7 teh ng3-bang7 Siong7-te3 e5 Seng3-chhiu2 tioh8 thoe3 Ki-tok pi7-pan7 lou7 e5 lang5 teh khoaN3, Iu5-thai3 lang5 chiu7-si7 choe3 te7-it u7 siu7 Siong7-te3 keng2-tiau3 e5 khoan2.  Ti7 kui2-na7 se3-ki2 e5 tiong-kan, in siu7 khi3-choat8 tiam3 ti7 phian-phiah e5 Pa-lek8-su-theng3 e5 soaN-kan, iau2-ku2 u7 ui7-tioh8 se3-kai3 lai5 po2-chun5 Siong7-te3 e5 oe7 (Oracles), cheng-sin5-tek e5 chong-kau3 e5 to7-li2, i2-kip8 hit e5 sou2 beh lai5--e5 e5 ng5-kim si5-tai7 e5 chham3-gu2.  Au7-lai5 in u7 tu2-tioh8 chiau3 in sou2 khoaN3 si7 chhiN-chham2 hit e5 siu7-liah8 e5 keng-giam7.  Chong2-si7 tui3 lan2 lai5 hoe5-kou3 ke3-khi3 hit e5 su7-sit8, in e5 siu7-liah8, beng5-beng5 si7 chhut tui3 hit e5 Chi3-koaiN5--e5 e5 ke3-ek8 e5 sou2 choe3.
	In-ui7 Iu5-thai3 lang5 tu2-tioh8 kek-tiok8 siu7-liah8 si3-soaN3 ti7 thong se3-kai3, che oan2-jian5 chhin-chhiuN7 oan5-teng tui3 i e5 ke2-chi2 hng5 lai5 poaN-soa2 soe3-chang5 ke2-chi2 chhiu7 khi3 chai ti7 goa7-bin7 e5 sou2-chai7, Siong7-te3 u7 poaN-soa2 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 hou7 in si3-soaN3 khia7-khi2 ti7 cheng3 pang-kok, siu7-liah8 au7 chi2-u7 sio2 pou7-hun7 u7 to3-tng2 lai5 tiam3 Pa-lek8-su-theng3, toa7 pou7-hun7 long2 chu7 an2-ni khia7-khi2 ti7 in sin e5 sou2-chai7, lai5 khui-khoah in e5 seng-li2 ti7 chiu-ui5 e5 pang-kok.  Tong-si5 u7 choe7-choe7 lek8-su2-ka chi2-si7 lan2 kong2, bo5 chit8-kok bo5 Iu5-thai3 lang5 khia7-khi2 ti7-hia, ia7 chiam7-chiam7 tit-tioh8 koan5-peng3, ti7 seng-li2 hong-bin7 put-chi2 u7 toa7 e5 se3-lek8.  In u7 heng-ong7 ti7 Lo5-ma2 te3-kok e5 tak8 sou2-chai7, chai7 Lo5-ma2 kok goa7 ti7 Pa-pi2-lun5, A-lek8-san-tai7, u7 kian3-siat in e5 toa7 e5 sit8-bin5 toe7, choe3 hit e5 bin5-chok8 e5 thong2-leng2.  “Toa7 e5 I2-sek-liat8” u7 khui-khoah si3-soaN3 ti7 u7 bun5-beng5 e5 se3-kai3 e5, si7 pi2 khia7-khi2 ti7 Pa-lek8-su-theng3 e5 chong-chok8 cham2-jian5 khah choe7, chong2-si7 chhin-chhiuN7 liu5-tou5 teh him-bou7 kou3-hiong e5 khoan2-sit, in siong5-siong5 bin7 oat8-lin-tng2 lai5 siau3-liam7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2.  Ai-kip8 e5 choan5 jin5-khau2, poeh-hun7-chit8 si7 Iu5-thai3 lang5.  Lan2 soe3-ji7 lai5 khoaN3, ti7 in tiong-kan e5 chit8 kun5, chiu7-si7 ti7 Chu2-au7 50 ni5 tng2-lai5 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 hu3 PoaN5-ke3-choeh e5, chiu7 thang tam7-poh8 chhui-chhek chhut-goa7 e5 Iu5-thai3 lang5 e5 lang5-sou3 kap in si3-soaN3 e5 hoan7-ui5 kau3 siaN2-khoan2.  “Chiah e5 PhaN3-the5-a lang5, Bi2-thai3 lang5, I2-lan5 lang5, kap tiam3 ti7 Bi2-sou2-pho-tai7-bi2, Iu5-thai3 kap Ka-phaN3-tou-ka, Pun2-tou kap A-se-a, Hut-lu5-ka kap Pong5-hui-li7-a, Ai-kip8 kun7-oa2 Kou2-li7-nai7 e5 Lu7-pi2-a, chiah e5 toe7-hng e5 lang5, i2-kip8 tui3 Lo5-ma2 lai5 e5 chhut-goa7 lang5, u7-e5 si7 Iu5-thai3 lang5, u7-e5 si7 jip8 Iu5-thai3 kau3 e5 lang5, Kek-li2-ti2 lang5, A-lat-pek lang5.”
	In kau3 tak8 sou2-chai7, chiu7 soa3 toa3 in e5 chong-kau3 kap in e5 Seng3-chheh, chhin-chhiuN7 lan2 u7 thak8-tioh8 kong2, “In-ui7 tui3 cha2 i2-lai5 ti7 tak8 sou2-chai7 e5 siaN5 u7 thoan5 Mou5-se e5 chheh, chiu7-si7 ti7 tak8 e5 An-hioh-jit8 ti7 hoe7-tng5 sou2 thak8 e5.”  Kau3 ti7 tak8 sou2-chai7, in tek8-piat8 chip-siu2 in e5 bin5-chok8 e5 hi-bang7, teh theng3-hau7 sou2 beh lai5 e5 Bi2-sai3-a.  Bi2-sai3-a lim5-kau3 si7 in e5 ng3-bang7 e5 choe3 ko-tiam2.  Iu5-thai3-kau3 e5 chun5-lip8 si7 chai7 ti7 chit-tiam2.  In e5 Keng-tian2 (Talmud) u7 kong2, “Cheng3 sian-ti chi2-u7 si7 chham3-gu2 Bi2-sai3-a,”  “In-ui7 chit e5 se3-kai3 siu7 chhong3-cho7 si7 ui7-tioh8 Bi2-sai3-a.  U7-iaN2, in m7-chai Bi2-sai3-a ti7-sibeh5 lim5-kau3, u7-iaN2, in eng7 eh8-teh8, hui cheng-sin5-tek e5 i3-su3 lai5 siuN7, lai5 khoaN3 I si7 ui7-tioh8 beh lai5 chin2-kiu3 Iu5-thai3 lang5 thoat-chhut goa7-pang lang5 e5 chhiu2-thau5, beh lai5 ko-seng in e5 te7-ui7.  In bo5 teh ng3-bang7 beh u7 chin kng thang lai5 chio3 iN7-pang lang5, chi2-u7 si7 teh ng3-bang7 in e5 peh-siN3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 tit-tioh8 toa7-toa7 e5 eng5-kng.  Sui-jian5 si7 an2-ni, chhiaN2 lai5 siuN7 chiah e5 peh-siN3 sim-lai7 chun5 hit ho7 sin3-giong2 lai5 si3-soaN3 ti7 iN7-kau3 e5 tiong-kan, che su7-sit8 tui3 u7-pi7 Ia5-sou Ki-tok e5 lou7, hit e5 kang e5 i3-gi7 sit8-chai7 m7-si7 sio2-khoa2!
	Sui-jian5 ko3-jin5 si7 hou7 lang5 iam3-ouN3, chong2-si7 in tai7-ke e5 se3-lek8 si7 put-chi2 kong2-khoah, in e5 chhu3-piN thau5-be2, hiah e5 khah chhim-tim5 e5 iN7-pang lang5, sim-lai7 bo5 boan2-chiok in pun2-sin hit e5 chhiN-chham2 e5 to-sin5 kap ngou2-siong7 e5 chong-kau3, iau2-ku2 ti7 in tiong-kan sou2 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 chit e5 Iu5-thai3-kau3 si7 kau3-giah8 u7 lat8, oe7 giu2 in e5 sim, in-ui7 chit e5 Iu5-thai3-kau3 si7 eng7 khak-sit8 e5 siaN, lai5 soan-thoan5 tok8-it e5 Siong7-te3, si7 ko-siong7, koh seng3 e5 Siong7-te3, koh u7 khoaN3-tang7 lang5 e5 chong-kau3 heng5-ui5, khoaN3-kou3 lan2 cheng3-lang5, u7 aN3 hi7-khang lai5 thiaN lang5 e5 ki5-to2, u7 ui7-tioh8 jin5-lui7 ti7 chiong-lai5 tou5-bou5 toa7 e5 su7.  Ti7 tak8 e5 siaN5-chhi7 u7 choe7-choe7 iN7-kau3-tou5, kai2-chong lai5 chham-ka ti7 hoe7-tng5 e5 keng3-pai3, iu7-koh tu5-khi2 chiah e5 i2-goa7, iau2 u7 toa7 to-sou3 e5 “keng3-khian5 e5 lang5,” chhin-chhiuN7 Sin-iok tiong sou2 ki3-chai3 hit e5 pe2(**peh)-chong2 Ko-ni5-liu5; in u7 siu7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 Seng3-chheh tiong sou2 ki3 e5 kau3-li2 lai5 tin2-tang7 in e5 sim, lai5 cheng-thok8 in e5 Seng3-chheh, put-ko3 iau2 lau5 chit8-sut-a2 iN7-pang lang5 e5 khoan2 chham-chhap ti7 in e5 hoe7-tng5 e5 seng-oah8.
	Koan-lian5 ti7 chit-e5, iau2 u7 chit8 hang7 chin tiong7-iau3 e5 su7 ti7-teh,--- chiu7-si7 ti7 Chu2-cheng5 oa2 nng7-pah ni5, hit pun2 Hi-pek-lai5 oe7 e5 Ku7-iok, u7 hoan-ek8 choe3 Hi-li7-ni5 oe7, chiu7-si7 hit-si5 e5 thong-iong7 gu2.  Sou2 hoan-ek8 chit-pun2, lan2 khah-siong5 si7 kio3-choe3 “Chhit-chap8 lang5 ek8” (Septuagint) e5 Seng3-chheh.  Chit pun2 thang choe3 Iu5-thai3 lang5 i2-kip8 iN7-pang lang5 e5 lou7-eng7, hou7 in thang thak8, piN5-piN5 lai5 tui3 in soan-thoan5 chit8 e5 gi7 e5 Siong7-te3, i2-kip8 u7 Chit8 e5 ui2-tai7 e5 beh lim5-kau3 e5 su7.
	Sui-jian5 toa7-pou7-hun7 e5 Iu5-thai3 lang5, in e5 bak8-chiu ou-am3, in e5 sim tun7, sui-jian5 Bi2-sai3-a chin-chiaN3 lim5-kau3 e5 si5, Pa-lek8-su-theng3 e5 lang5 u7 teng3 I ti7 Sip8-ji7-ke3, iau2-ku2 lan2 tioh8 koh-chai3 lai5 khoaN3 Po2-lo5 e5 toan7-ki3, ti7-hia u7 chhian2-beng5 Iu5-thai3 lang5 e5 hoe7-tng5, ti7 tak8 sou2-chai7 si7 choe3 Ki-tok e5 Seng3-hoe7 e5 ng-chioh(**chhioh8)-toe7, tui3 an2-ni iah8 thang soa3 hou7 lan2 liau2-kai2 si3-soaN3 ti7 tak8 sou2-chai7 e5 I2-sek-liat8 lang5, u7 toa7 e5 khui3-lat8, “ti7-teh pi7-pan7 Chu2 e5 lou7.”
	Tu2-tu2 Siong7-te3 e5 Seng3-KiaN2 beh lim5-kau3 se3-kan e5 si5, chou-chit tong si5 e5 bun5-beng5 e5 se3-kai3 chit saN-e5 toa7 e5 bin5-chok8, ti7 bo5 i3-sek e5 tiong-kan, tai7-ke saN hiap8-lek8 choe3-he2 lai5 pi7-pan7 Chu2 e5 lou7, che khak-sit8 si7 u7 chin toa7 e5 i3-su3 ti7-teh.  Che beng5-beng5 u7 am3-si7 lan2 chai, Siong7-te3 u7 chhun-chhut I e5 Seng3-chhiu2, tui3 choe7-choe7 hong-bin7 lai5 teh cho7-chiu7 chit8 e5 ui2-tai7 e5 kiat-ko2.

Te7-3 chiuN	Se3-Kai3 U7 Teh Theng3-Hau7

	Ti7 te7-li2-siong7 i2-kip8 cheng3-ti7-siong7 chiah e5 goa7-heng5 e5 pian3-chhian i2-goa7, lan2 thang tui3 ti7 tong-si5 lang5 e5 su-siong2 i2-kip8 liam7-thau5 e5 hong-bin7 lai5 khoaN3-chhut hit e5 sio-siang7 u7 i3-gi7 e5 lai7-bin7-tek e5 pi7-pan7.  Tong-si5 si7 chit8 e5 ia3-sian7 sit-i3, bo5 boan2-chiok e5 se3-kai3, ti7-teh theng3-hau7 Ki-tok e5 lim5-kau3.  Put-chi2 khiam3-eng7 lang5 thang pang-chan7 lai5 kou2-bu2 in e5 sim.  Bian2 kong2, Ki-tok i2-cheng5 ti7 tak8 si5-tai7 to-siau2 u7-iaN2 long2 si7 an2-ni.  Chong2-si7 jin5-lui7 u7 teh chin3-pou7.  Lang5 e5 liong5-sim put-si5 u7 teh oah8-tang7 lai5 po2-chhi5 in choe3 ko e5 koan5-ui.  Jin5-lui7 chiam7-chiam7 khah u7 teh siuN7 khah u7 kam2-kak bo5 boan2-chiok e5 liam7-thau5 ti7-teh.
	ChhiaN2 koh khoaN3 chit saN-e5 bin5-chok8, chiu7-si7 Hi-li7-ni5 lang5, Lo5-ma2 lang5 i2-kip8 Iu5-thai3 lang5.
	Seng lai5 khoaN3 Hi-li7-ni5 lang5.  In si7 kiau-ngou7, jiat8-seng5, phu5-phio3 bi2-mau7 e5 bin5-chok8, u7 ko-siong7 e5 ge7-sut8, bun5-hak8, tiat-hak8 ti7-teh; in si7 gau5 hiong2-lok8 ge7-sut8, koh u7 gau5 choe3 si e5 thian-hun7, tui3 an2-ni u7 an-ti3 choe7-choe7 sin5-beng5 ti7 Ou-lin2-phuh (Olympus) e5 soaN-teng2.  Chai7 kin-na2-jit8 ti7 se3-kai3, siok8 ti7 bun5-beng5 e5 kok, long2 eng7 kiaN-hiaN5 kap kam2-sia7 e5 liam7-thau5 teh chu3-i3 khoaN3 kou2-cha2 hiah e5 Hi-li7-ni5 lang5.  Lan2 kin-na2-jit8 sou2 u7 choe3-ho2 e5 bun5-hoa3, toa7-pou7-hun7 si7 chhut-tui3 in e5 kong-lo5.  In ui7-tioh8 bun5-hoa3 lai5 lou2-lek8 khoaN3-choe3 si7 te7-it tui3-tiong7 e5 kang.  Koat-toan3 bo5 u7 sim2-mih8 kok thang tui3 in lai5 khoa-khau2 in e5 bun5-hoa3, ia7 koat-toan3 bo5 u7 sim2-mih8 kok thang pi2 in khah siu7 lang5 e5 chheng-chan3.
	Chong2-si7, haiN3-ah!  Ti7 choe3-kun7 e5 tai7-chian3, lan2 u7 siu7 ka3-si7, chai-iaN2 bun5-hoa3 bo5 chong-kau3 ti7-teh, si7 boe7 thang choe3 sim2-mih8, ia7 chai tong-si5 hit e5 kho2-lin5 e5 Hi-li7-ni5 lang5 u7 seng5-jin7, kiam2-chhai2 kin-na2-jit8 e5 Tek-kok lang5 ia7 tioh8 ai3 seng5-jin7, chai-iaN2 se3-kai3 kan-ta bun5-hoa3 si7 boe7 thang chin3-pou7.  Chiau3 goa2 teh siuN7 hiah e5 Hi-li7-ni5 lang5 oan2-jian5 chhin-chhiuN7 kun7-tai7 e5 Pa-li2-siaN5 e5 lang5, si7 phu5-phio3, ai3 ngou7-lok8, oah8 tang7, si7 ai3 iu5-iu5 chu7-sek e5 bin5-chok8.  Sui-jian5 si7 an2-ni, ti7 in hit e5 seng-oah8 e5 e7-bin7 si7 iau2-ku2 u7 ham5 chit8-cheng2 e5 ai-tiau7 ti7-teh.  In sou2 u7 hit e5 choe3 eng5-iau7 e5 si5-ki5 i2-keng ke3-liau2.  Hi-li7-ni5 e5 ng5-kim si5-tai7 si7 i2-keng khi3 lah.  In cheng3-ti7-siong7 e5 chhan3-lan7 i2-keng sit-loh8.  Kiat-kiok8 si7 hui3-liau2 in e5 it-seng ti7 hit e5 phu5-phio3, im5-lok8 e5 seng-oah8.  Hong3-tong7 kap sia5-ok e5 liam7-thau5 si7 chhin-chhiuN7 hoan-hoe siN ti7 in e5 seng-oah8 lai7.  In e5 sui2-sui2 e5 chong-kau3 i2-keng bo5 lat8 thang chou2-chi2 in e5 sia5-ok e5 seng3-phiah.  Thai2-tho2 oe7 le3?  Lian5 tong-si5 ti7 hit e5 choe3 eng5-iau7 e5 jit8, in sou2 hok8-sai7 ti7 hit e5 Ou-lin2-phuh (Olympus) soaN-teng2 e5 cheng3 sin5-beng5, ia7 to long2 si7 im5-loan7 e5 sou2 choe3.  Sou2-i2 lan2 kiam2 oe7 thang siuN7 kong2, u7 sim2-mih8 lang5 beh tui3 hiah e5 sin5-beng5 lai5 ko3-sou3 in e5 cheng-sin5-siong7 e5 ki5-kiu5 mah?
	Tng in siau3-lian5 e5 si5, sim-cheng5 si7 kek8 tan-sun5, in put-chi2 u7 sin3-sim, khoaN3 hiah e5 sin5-beng5 si7 chin-tu2-chin, sit8-tu2-sit8.  In u7 sin3-hong7 in e5 sin5-beng5.  In-ui7 in sou2 sin3 e5 to m7-si7 choan-choan si7 phaiN2-lui7 e5 sin5-beng5, chhin-chhiuN7 Jiu5-bu2 (Jove) sin5 si7 ho2 seng3-cheng5 e5 pe7, si7 cho7-but8 chu2.  In sou2 sin3 e5 sin5-beng5 ia7 u7 kap in choe3-he2 saN-kap kau-chian3 ti7 The5-mou5-pou-li2 (Thermopylae) e5 soaN-kok, ti7-hia u7 saN-pah e5 u7 mia5-siaN e5 lang5, kheng2 ui7-tioh8 Hi-li7-ni5, ui7-tioh8 cheng3-gi7 lai5 song3-sit in e5 siN3-mia7.
	Chong2-si7 in taN i2-keng tui7-loh8 chiaN5-choe3 si7 bo5 ng3-bang7, loan2-jiok8 e5 bin5-chok8.  Sui-jian5 in u7 po2-chun5 hiah e5 sin5-beng5 e5 heng5-the2, ki5-sit8 si7 choan5-jian5 sit-loh8 i2-cheng5 sou2 u7 chin-sit8 e5 sin3-sim.  In e5 sin5-oa7 pian3-chiaN5 chit8 khoan2 hong-tong5 e5 kou3-su7.  Sou2-i2 chai7 chiah e5 kho2-lin5 e5 Hi-li7-ni5 lang5 teh khoaN3, chit e5 se3-kai3 put-ko3 si7 chit8 e5 bu5-liau5 e5 sou2-chai7.  Tng in chheng-lian5 e5 si5 sou2 tiau-khek lai5 chong5-hong7 e5 sin5, na7-si7 in iau2 u7 sin3-sim, chiu7 iau2 oe7 thang tam7-poh8 lai5 an-ui3 in e5 sim, m7-ku2 in taN to bo5 sin3 lah!
	ChhiaN2 lai5 khoaN3 Lo5-ma2 lang5.  In bo5 kah chhin-chhiuN7 Hi-li7-ni5 lang5 e5 hu2-pai7.  In si7 u7 iong2-kam2, hian2-hek e5 bin5-chok8, u7 thang khoa-khau2 i e5 koan5-peng3, se3-lek8, i2-kip8 i e5 seng5-kong.  Chong2-si7 choe7-choe7 e5 lek8-su2-ka, iu5-goan5 u7 chi2-si7 lan2 chai, ti7 hit e5 eng5-hoa5 chhan3-lan7 e5 seng-oah8 e5 e7-bin7 u7 hu2-pai7 e5 sou2 choe3 ti7-teh.  In e5 ka-teng5 seng-oah8 si7 be7 thang heng5-iong5-tit e5 chhiN-chham2.  Po7-giok8 kap chan5-jim2 si7 moa2 si3-koe3.  Cheng3 peh-siN3 e5 to7-tek seng-oah8 sit-tui7, chiaN5-choe3 chhin-chhiuN7 khim5-siu3 e5 khoan2-sit, seng3-cheng5 chan5-jim2.  In te7-it hoaN-hi2 e5 ngou7-lok8, chiu7-si7 ti7 hi3-hng5 tiong khoaN3 lang5 sit8-chai7 sio-thai5 choe3 sim-sek, che si7 chin-chiaN3 kho2-ouN3 e5 su7!  In e5 lou5-le7 e5 che3-tou7 si7 kok-ka siu7 chiu3-chou2 e5 goan5-in.  Ti7 Lo5-ma2 e5 koe-lou7 siong7, saN lang5 tiong, nng7 lang5 si7 lou5-chai5; hu7-jin5-lang5 saN lang5 tiong, nng7 lang5 si7 lu2-pi7; si7 choe3 chu2-lang5 e5 phu5-phio3 e5 jiok8-iok8 e5 tui3-chhiu2.  Choe3 lang5 e5 lou5-chai5 si7 tiam3 ti7 chhiN-chham2 e5 keng2-gu7.  Ki-tok-kau3 kau3 Lo5-ma2 e5 si5, ti7 lou5-chai5 e5 tiong-kan, hiah e5 chin phaiN2 e5, u7 pai7-hoai7 Lo5-ma2.  In u7 eng7 sin e5 khoan2, m7 cheng3-keng e5 choe7-ok lai5 pai7-hoai7 in e5 chu2-lang5 kap in e5 hou7-e3.  Lo5-ma2 e5 choan5-seng5 e5 chheng-lian5 sou2 u7 it-chhe3 e5 jiat8 cheng5, long2 si7 su2-iong7 ti7 sia5-ok e5 seng-oah8.  Ti3-kau3 Lo5-ma2 e5 siau3-lian5 ti7 be7 tiong2-seng5 e5 i2-cheng5, in e5 sin-the2 chiu7 chiam7-chiam7 soe-lam2, sim-sin5 ia3-sian7, seng3-cheng5 pai7-hoai7.  Ti7 Chu2-au7 oa2 poaN3 se3-ki2, Po2-lo5 u7 chi2-si7 hit e5 cheng5-heng5 ti7 Lo5-ma2 jin5-su, hit e5 hou7 lang5 oe7 thang chhiN-kiaN e5 thau5-chit8 chiuN e5 lai7-bin7.  Siong7-te3 u7 chiau3 in sim-lai7 e5 su-iok8, lai5 kau-hu3 in ti7 bo5 chheng-khi3.  In sui-jian5 u7 choe7-choe7 ui2-tai7 thang khoa-khau2 e5 su7, iau2-ku2 Lo5-ma2 e5 sia7-hoe7, tui3 ti7 ko3-ko3 e5 lam5-lu2 lai5 khoaN3, sng3 choe3 si7 bo5 thang ng3-bang7 e5 sia7-hoe7, bo5 Siong7-te3 e5 sia7-hoe7.  Bo5 lun7 sim2-mih8 si5-chun7, in ti7 khou2-lan7, ti7 iam3-hun7 jin5-seng, ti7-teh him-bou7 gi7 e5 si5, tu5-khi2 hit e5 lu2-sin5 Lo5-ma2 i2-kip8 hiah e5 hou7 lang5 hok8-sai7 choe3 sin5-beng5 e5 hong5-te3 i2-goa7, to bo5 u7 Siong7-te3 thang ki5-kiu5.  Lan2 pun2-sin na7 lai5 tiam3 ti7 hit e5 cheng5-keng2, chhi3-siuN7 lan2 e5 kam2-siong2 siaN2 khoan2.
	Chong2-si7 che m7-si7 lan2 sou2 tioh8 chu3-i3 e5 choe3 iau3-kin2 e5 tiam2.  In-ui7 che si7 iN7-kau3 tiong e5 siong5-su7.  Lan2 sou2 tioh8 chu3-i3 e5 choe3 iau3-kin2 e5 tiam2, chiu7-si7 ti7 Lo5-ma2 lang5 e5 tiong-kan u7 choe7-choe7 chin ho2-sim e5 lang5, long2 iam3-ouN3 hit e5 cheng5-heng5.  Sou2-i2 chai7 tong-si5, hoan7-na7 u7 the5-ko sia7-hoe7 to7-tek, bo5 lun7 siaN2 khoan2 e5 un7-tong7, to long2 siu7 toa7 e5 hoan-geng5.  Koh ti7 chiah e5 iN7-kau3-tou5 e5 tiong-kan, iu5-goan5 si7 u7 choe7-choe7 sui2 e5 jin5-keh-chia2 ti7-teh.  Lan2 oe7 ki3-tit khah au7-lai5 ti7 Sin-iok tiong u7 ki3-chai3 kui2-na7 mia5 e5 Lo5-ma2 e5 pe2(**peh)-chong2, in chiap-chhiok--tioh8 Ki-tok-kau3 e5 si5, sim-lai7 chaiN2-iuN7 e5 loan5-bou7 i.  KhoaN3-tioh8 hiah e5 su-siuN2 e5 chi2-to7-chia2, u7 chaiN2-iuN7 teh thong3-hun7 hit-si5 e5 sia7-hoe7 chong7-thai3, che su7-sit8, lan2 thiaN-liau2 bo5 m7 kap in saN-kap siong-sim.  Chit e5 si5-tai7 choe7-choe7 tiat-hak8-chia2, long2 teh tui-chhe7 chin-li2, tui-kiu5 khoaN3 u7 sim2-mih8 thang choe3 heng5-ui5 e5 chi2-to7 goan5-li2.  Cheng3-lang5 chiam7-chiam7 chin3-pou7, thoat-chhut hit e5 gu5-gong7 bo5 teh siuN7 e5 si5-ki5.  Cheng3-lang5 i2-keng long2 khou2-sim teh su-siong2.  In-ui7 cheng3-lang5 khoaN3-kiN3 in e5 sia7-hoe7, si7 bo5 koh-iuN7 Hi-li7-ni5 lang5 e5 sia7-hoe7, long2 bo5 u7 sin5-beng5 ti7-teh.  tui3 an2-ni, in u7 kek8-lek8 koat-i3 teh chhe7 khoaN3 u7 sim2-mih8 sin5-beng5 thang lai5 tui-kiu5 in e5 chong-kau3 seng-oah8.  In u7 kang2-kiu3 Liong5-sim e5 o3-biau7 e5 to7-li2, u7 seng5-jin7 i e5 koan5-ui.  Sou2-i2 au7-lai5 ti7 in tiong-kan u7 chit8 lang5 kiat-lun7 kong2, “Liong5-sim si7 chit8 cheng2 Loe7-chai7 e5 sin5(內在的神)”  Chit ho7 su-siong2 chai7 iN7-kau3-tou5 sng3 choe3 si7 chit8 e5 oan2-tai7 e5 chin3-pou7.
	Su-to-a hak8-phai3 e5 tiat-hak8-chia2 u7 khui-khe2 lang5 e5 sim, lai5 ka3-si7 ho2 e5 to7-li2 kong2, “Tioh8 kiu5 ho2 e5 tek-heng7, tioh8 thiaN Liong5-sim e5 siaN, in-ui7 Liong5-sim si7 chit8-cheng2 Lai7-chai7 e5 sin5.  Toa7-bin7 ti7 Liong5-sim e5 poe3-au7, u7 bou2 ui2-tai7 e5 sin5 ti7-teh.  Chong2-si7 sui-si7 bo5 lai5 kong2, iah8 si7 tioh8 thiaN-than3 Liong5-sim e5 SiaN.”  Chai7 iN7-kau3-tou5, che kiam2 bo5 sng3 choe3 si7 ko-siong7 sui2-sui2 e5 thai3-tou7 mah?
	Khak-sit8, Siong7-te3 u7 put-si5 teh pang-chan7 lang5 e5 sim lai5 bat ho2 e5 ka3-si7.  Hit e5 sou2 beh lai5 choe3 se3-kan e5 kng e5, iu5-goan5 u7 teh chio3 kng ti7 in e5 sim-lai7.
	Kou2-cha2 hiah e5 su-siuN2-ka i2-keng u7 chin7 in choe3-sian7 e5 lou2-lek8.  Chong2-si7 in sou2 lou2-lek8 e5, long2 si7 li2-lun7, hak8-soat na7-tiaN7.  In bo5 thang chhin-chhiuN7 Iu5-thai3 lang5 e5 khoan2-sit, u7 kian-kou3 e5 kun-ki, thang lai5 khi2-cho7 in e5 chong-kau3.  Tui3 an2-ni, in e5 choe3-ko e5 lou2-lek8 si7 long2 kui ti7 khang-khang, in e5 li2-lun7, hak8-soat si7 bo5 lat8 thang pang-chan7 lang5 lai5 jim2-siu7 chit e5 bo5 piN5-thaN2 e5 jin5-seng, in hiah e5 sui2-sui2 e5 hak8-soat, koat-toan3 boe7 thang giu2 it-poaN e5 lang5 e5 sim.  In kek8-lek8 hoat-hui lan2 lang5 ka-ki7 e5 li2-seng3, lai5 beh su-siong2 chong-kau3 e5 to7-li2.  Iau2-ku2 in e5 kiat-kiok8 si7 sit-pai7.
	In si7 sit-pai7. Tu2-tu2 iN7-pang lang5 chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni teh tui-chhe7 chin kng e5 si5 --- tu2-tu2 tng lan2 lang5 kho3 ka-ki7 e5 lou2-lek8 sit-pai7 e5 si5 --- tu2-tu2 ti7 chit e5 se3-kai3 su2 siong7 e5 gui5-ki e5 si5, Ki-tok lai5 lim5-kau3 se3-kan, che kiam2 m7-si7 oe7 kham-tit hou7 lan2 chu3-i3 e5 su7 mah?
	TaN lai5 kong2-khi2 chou-chit bun5-beng5 e5 se3-kai3 hit e5 te7-saN e5 bin5-chok8, Iu5-thai3 lang5 si7 an2-choaN2?  Toa7-bin7 u7 lang5 beh pian7-pok kong2, sui-jian5 Hi-li7-ni5 lang5 a2-si7 Lo5-ma2 lang5, kiam2-chhai2 thang kong2 si7 u7 teh ki5-thai7 e5 sim ti7-teh, iau2-ku2 kiaN-liau2 Iu5-thai3 lang5, put-lun7 siaN2 khoan2, si7 goan2-kou3, heng5-gek8, bo5 u7 hoaN-hi2 ai3 geng5-chiap Ki-tok e5 lim5-kau3 e5 sim, ia7 ku2 kaN2.
	Lan2 thang siuN7, che kong2 liau2 oe7 u7 khah ke3-thau5.  Lan2 kan-ta khoaN3-kiN3 Ia5-sou ti7 Sin-iok tiong sou2 kong-kek e5 tu3-hian7 e5 su7-sit8, chiu7 an2-ni lai5 phoaN3-toan3 in si7 goan2-kou3, gau5 khng3 phian-kian3 e5 Iu5-thai3 lang5.  ChhiaN2 lan2 tioh8 oe7 ki3-tit ti7 Iu5-thai3 lang5 e5 tiong-kan, u7 choe7-choe7 chin ho2 e5 lang5, u7 liau2-kai2 Ia5-sou chiu7-si7 oan5-seng5 Ku7-iok e5 sian-ti sou2 teh chham3-gu2 e5, soa3 lai5 chiaN5-choe3 goan5-si2 si5-tai7 e5 kau3-hoe7, choe3-chhou e5 choe3 te7-it keng3-khian5 e5 sin3-tou5.
	Lan2 na7 cha-kho2 tong-si5 e5 tu3-chok, chiu7 oe7 chai u7 choe7-choe7 chhim-tim5 e5 Iu5-thai3 lang5, bo5 koh-iuN7 Hi-li7-ni5 lang5 a2-si7 Lo5-ma2 lang5, iu5-goan5 si7 bo5 boan2-chiok in e5 chong-kau3.  Hiah e5 li7-khui Pa-lek8-su-theng3 si3-ke3 iu5-lek8 ti7 goa7-kok e5 Iu5-thai3 lang5 u7 chiap-chhiok--tioh8 pat8-kok e5 bin5-chok8, soa3 put-chi2 tong5-cheng5 in e5 hak8-bun7, tui3 an2-ni u7 khui-khoah in e5 gan2-kai3.  In i2-keng thoat-chhut Pa-lek8-su-theng3 e5 pai5-goa7 e5 sim-su.  In chhin-bit8 lai5 kap iN7-pang e5 peng5-iu2 choe3-he2 khia7-khi2, tui3 an2-ni u7 kam2-kak in e5 Iu5-thai3-kau3, na7-si7 boe7 thang iong5-un2 iN7-pang lang5, chiu7 koat-toan3 boe7 thang chiaN5-choe3 choan5 jin5-lui7 e5 chong-kau3.  Siat-su2 na7 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa chi2-u7 si7 I2-sek-liat8 it bin5-chok8 e5 Siong7-te3, i2-goa7 e5 se3-kai3 e5 lang5, chi2-u7 tioh8 keng-iu5 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 chhiu2, than3 in e5 kat-le2, than3 sou2 bo5 ai3 e5 choe7-choe7 oh-tit tam-tng e5 kui-ku2, chiah thang chhin-kun7 I, chhin-chhiuN7 chit khoan2 i3-su3, si7 chin khun3-lan5 e5 su7.  Tui3 an2-ni, lan2 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 choe7-choe7 Iu5-thai3 lang5 e5 tu3-chok, koat-i3 u7 khng3 khah khoah-toa7 e5 ng3-bang7 beh lai5 tiau5-ho5 in e5 chong-kau3, chiaN5-choe3 chit8 e5 se3-kai3-tek e5 chong-kau3, lai5 li7-ek choan5 jin5-lui7.
	Siat-su2 Iu5-thai3-kau3, to u7 hiah ko-siong7 e5 sin5-hak8, na7 oe7-tit thang khui-hoe lai5 chiaN5-choe3 chit8 e5 ui2-tai7 e5 se3-kai3-tek e5 chong-kau3, hou7 choan5 jin5-lui7, bo5 hun-piat Iu5-thai3 a2-si7 iN7-pang, Hi-li7-ni5 a2-si7 hoa3-goa7 e5, lou5-pok8 a2-si7 chu7-iu5 e5, long2 thang tit-tioh8 Siong7-te3 e5 un-tian2, si7 chin ban7-heng7!  Ki5-sit8 choe7-choe7 chhim-tim5 e5 Iu5-thai3 lang5 chai, che tu2-tu2 si7 Ku7-iok cheng3 sian-ti sou2 khoaN3 e5 iN7-siong7, chiu7-si7 u7 chit8 jit8 Bi2-sai3-a beh lim5-kau3, tui3 Iu5-thai3 e5 kun-chang5 beh hoat-hian7 chit8 lui2 se3-kai3-tek e5 chong-kau3 e5 toa7 lui2 e5 hoe, thang lai5 chiok-hok choan5 jin5-lui7.
	Lan2 ti7-chia iau2 u7 chit8 hang7 tioh8 siuN7.  Lun7 lut8-hoat, chhin-chhiuN7 Po2-lo5 hit khoan2 jiat8-seng5 e5 cheng-sin5-tek e5 lang5 teh khoaN3, si7 i2-keng ku7--khi3 e5 mih8.  Chiau3 Po2-lo5 e5 i3-su3, lut8-hoat si7 oe7 bo5--khi3, lut8-hoat put-ko3 si7 chiam7-si5, si7 choe3 gin2-na2 e5 kau3-su, in2-chhoa7 lang5 chiu7-kun7 Ki-tok.  Ti7 i teh ko3-pek8 hoan2-hoe2 cheng5 e5 cheng-sin5-chiuN7 e5 chhiN-chham2 e5 tou3-cheng, hit ku3 oe7 e5 tiong-kan, u7 piau2-si7 hou7 lan2 chai, u7 choe7-choe7 jiat8-seng5 e5 Iu5-thai3 lang5 chaiN2-iuN7 u7 chhin-chhiuN7 i e5 khoan2-sit, teh tui-chhe7 khoaN3 u7 sim2-mih8 khah u7 ng3-bang7 e5 lou7 thang chhin-kun7 Siong7-te3.  Chai7 hit teng2-ho7 lang5, in chhe7-tioh8 Ki-tok si7 chit8 e5 thang hoaN-hi2 e5 hoat-kian3.
	Tng Ki-tok teh-beh lim5-kau3 hit-si5, choan5 Iu5-thai3 e5 se3-kai3 u7 hian2-chhut chin kin2-sin7 teh ki5-thai7 e5 cheng-sin5 ti7-teh, che su7-sit8, chai7 hiah e5 m7-bat Iu5-thai3-kau3 e5 lang5 teh khoaN3, sit8-chai7 si7 te7-it tu3-hian7, koh si7 chin thang chhiN-kiaN e5 tai7-chi3.  Lan2 thang ho2-taN2 lai5 sin3, bo5 u7 chit8 kok bat piau2-si7 chhin-chhiuN7 Ia5-sou beh lim5-kau3 hit si5 e5 choan5 Iu5-thai3 e5 se3-kai3 e5 cheng-sin5 chong7-thai7, hiah oe7 giu2 lang5 e5 sim, hou7 lang5 chin chhiN-kiaN e5 hian7-siong7.
	In-ui7 siang7 lou2-be2 teh kan-cheng3, “Hit e5 sou2 beh lai5 e5” e5 sian-ti e5 chham2-gu2 si7 i2-keng ke3-liau2 gou7-pah ni5 ku2, ia7 ti7 hit tiong-kan long2 bo5 tong7 bo5 cheng7.  Sou2-i2 kiam2-chhai2 lang5 kau3-giah8 thang liau7-siong2, i2-keng keng-ke3 gou7-pah ni5 ku2, cheng3-lang5 un2-tang3 boe7 ki3-tit, a2-si7 pang3-sak in teh ng3-bang7 e5 cheng-sin5 chiah tioh8.  Ki5-sit8 tng ti7 hit e5 si5-ki5 na2 pek-kun7 choan5 bin5-chok8, si7 na2 pek-chhiat teh theng3-hau7.  Sin Ku7-iok e5 tiong-kan sou2 u7 chhut-mia5 e5 bun5-hak8, long2 u7 hian2-chhut hit ho7 ki5-thai7 e5 cheng-sin5 ti7-teh.  Lan2 ti7-chia bo5 ui7 thang lai5 kong2-khi2 chit khoan2 bun5-hak8 e5 su7.  Put-ko3 lan2 ai3 kan-ta ti7-chia lai5 khoaN3 chit pun2 soe3-soe3 e5 chheh, thang kong2 si7 chit khoan2 bun5-hak8 e5 tai7-piau2, si7 kio3-choe3 “I2-lok8 e5 chheh” (Book of Enoch).  Chit pun2 chheh si7 thong-heng5 ti7 Chu2-cheng5 oa2 200 ni5 e5 tiong-kan, Iu5-thai3 u7 bat thak8-tioh8 chit pun2 chheh.  Lan2 m7-bian2 giau5-gi5, Ia5-sou un2-tang3 iu5-goan5 u7 thak8-tioh8 chiah tioh8.  Sou2-i2 goa2 siong5-siong5 teh siuN7, Ia5-sou u7 tui3 chit pun2 lai5 tit-tioh8 I sou2 hoaN-hi2 eng7 lai5 chi2-si7 I pun2-sin hit ku3 “Jin5-chu2” e5 oe7.
	Hit pun2 chheh e5 tiong-kan, u7 chit8-cham7 chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni:
	“Goa2 ti7 iN7-siong7 tiong, u7 khoaN3-kiN3 hit e5 kap Eng2-oan2-chia2 saN-kap ti7-teh e5.  I e5 iong5-mau7 si7 chhin-chhiuN7 lang5, koh u7 un-hui7 moa2-moa2, goa2 u7 chheng2-mng7 thiN-sai3, iah8 i u7 ka7 goa2 kong2, Chit e5 si7 Jin5-chu2, u7 gi7 tiam3 ti7 I, I si7 beh khe2-si7 it-chhe3 sou2 un2-bat8 e5 su7……Chit e5 Jin5-chu2 beh chiaN5-choe3 gi7 e5 lang5 e5 kun3, e5 koaiN2, iN7-pang lang5 e5 kng, i2-kip8 kiN3-na7 tioh8-boa5 e5 lang5 e5 ng3-bang7.  KiN3-na7 khia7-khi2 ti7 toe7-bin7-chiuN7 e5 cheng3-lang5, long2 beh pai3-kui7 ti7 I e5 bin7-cheng5.  In-ui7 chit e5 in-toaN, I si7 tui3 khai-pit8 thiN-toe7 i2-lai5 kau3 eng2-oan2, chiu7 i2-keng siu7 keng2-soan2.”
	Chiah e5 chheh si7 teh chi2-si7 tong-si5 iau2 ti7-teh chin3-pou7 tiong e5 ng3-bang7 e5 cheng-sin5.  Chong2-si7 ti7 Hok-im-su e5 thau5-cham7, lan2 u7 khoaN3-tioh8 hit e5 ng3-bang7 e5 cheng-sin5, u7 tio5-thiau3 ti7 tak8 tiuN e5 choa2-bin7.  Ku7-iok sian-ti sou2 thoan5 e5 siau-sit u7 kiat-chiaN5 chit8 e5 khak-sit8, tiaN7-tioh8 e5 ng3-bang7.  Sou2-i2 put-lun7 sim2-mih8 si5-chun7, na7 u7 bou2 chi2-to7-chia2 chhut-thau5 e5 si5, hit e5 ng3-bang7 e5 sim u7 hoat-chhut jiat8-jiat8 e5 chit-bun7.  Chhin-chhiuN7 tng Iu5-tai7 chhut-thau5 lai5 ti2-khong3 Lo5-ma2 cheng3-hu2 e5 thiu-hiong3 e5 si5, chiu7 u7 chin-choe7 e5 lang5 lai5 te3 i, phah-sng3 i si7 Bi2-sai3-a.  Tng KiaN5 soe2-le2 e5 Iok-han7 chhut-thau5 e5 si5, cheng3-lang5 choe3-chhou tui3 i si7 phau7 siaN2-khoan2 e5 su-siong2?  Chiu7-si7 “cheng3-lang5 sim-lai7 teh gi7-lun7 Iok-han7 kiam2-chhai2 si7 Ki-tok.”  Tng Iok-han7 chhut-thau5 lai5 soan-thoan5 e5 si5, lang5 choe3-chhou si7 mng7 i an3-choaN2?  Chiu7-si7 mng7 kong2, “ChhiaN2 ka7 goan2 kong2, li2 si7 Bi2-sai3-a mah?  Sou2 beh lai5 e5, si7 li2 mah?” Chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni, lan2 chi2-u7 kam2-kak lan2 si7 tiam3 ti7 hit e5 chin kin2-sin7 teh ki5-thai7 e5 khong-khi3 tiong.
	Lan2 chit-tiap8 ai3 lai5 hoe5-kou3 i2-siong7 sou2 kong2 hiah e5 su7-sit8, chiu7 khah oe7 thang liau2-kai2 hit e5 cheng5-heng5.  Chiau3 i2-siong7 sou2 kong2, chiu7-si7 hou7 lan2 chai ti7 lek8-su2 tiong u7 chit8 e5 si5-tai7, toe7-bin7-chiuN7 toa7 e5 pang-kok, ti7 bo5 phah-sng3 e5 tiong-kan, long2 u7 teh thoe3 Ki-tok pi7-pan7 lou7, ia7 choan5 Iu5-thai3 e5 bin5-chok8 chhiat-chhiat teh theng3-hau7 I e5 lim5-kau3, iu7-koh hit e5 kho2-lin5 e5 se3-kai3, khia7-khi2 ti7 hit e5 choe3 chhiN-chham2 e5 chong7-thai3 u7 bong5-bok8 ti7-teh tui-chhe7, ng3-bang7 u7 sim2-mih8 thang the5-ko in e5 seng-oah8.
	Tu2-tu2 chhin-chhiuN7 ti7 chit ho7 e5 si5,  Ki-Tok U7 Lim5-Kau3 ti7 chit se3-kan! 



Te7  II  Koan3
Ki-tok Lai5 e5 Si5

Te7-1 chiuN	Chhut-Si3

	Tu2-tu2 ti7 chhin-chhiuN7 chit ho7 e5 si5-tai7, Ki-tok u7 lim5-kau3 se3-kan, chiu7-si7 chiau3 Seng3-chheh sou2 kong2, “Na7-si7 kau3 hit e5 si5 i2-keng moa2, Siong7-te3 u7 chhe I e5 KiaN2 lai5 chhut-si3.”  Ia5-sou Ki-tok u7 tui3 hit e5 Eng2-oan2 e5 se3-kai3 lai5 chhut-si3 ti7 chit e5 se3-kai3.  ChhiaN2 lan2 siong5-siong5 oe7 ki3-tit chit nng7 e5 se3-kai3 e5 su7.
	Lan2 chit-tiap8 ai3 lai5 siuN7, ti7 jin5-lui7 su2 tiong, ti7 ke3-khi3 e5 lek8-su2 sou2 teh pi7-pan7, teh theng3-hau7 e5 chit8 e5 tiong7-tai7 e5 su7-kiaN7, ia7 lan2 sou2 beh kong2 chit e5 tiong7-tai7 e5 su7-kiaN7, si7 choe3 chit8 cheng2 e5 kio5-niu5, lai5 khoa3 ti7 Siong7-te3 kap lang5 e5 tiong-kan sou2 u7 e5 chhim-khiN e5 teng2-bin7.  Chit e5 tiong7-tai7 e5 su7-kiaN7, chiu7-si7 Hit e5 “tui3 kou2-cha2 i2-lai5 pun2 u7 e5, chiap8-chiap8 tu3-hian7” e5 Ki-tok, u7 chiaN5-choe3 lang5 e5 iuN7-siuN3 lai5 lim5-kau3 se3-kan.
	Lan2 thau5 chit8-e7 khoaN3-liau2 si7 put-chi2 chhiN-kiaN, chin ki5-koai3, in-ui7 chit e5 tiong7-tai7 e5 su7-kiaN7, si7 eng7 hit ho7 kek8 tan-sun5, peng5-siong5 e5 hoat-tou7, lai5 hian2-hian7, ti3-kau3 lan2 be7 bian2-tit siuN7 kong2, che si7 bo5-iaN2,soa3 chha-put-to long2 m7-kaN2 sin3.  Siat-su2 I na7-si7 oe7 thang hian2-chhut toa7 e5 pian3-tong7, a2-si7 ti7 thiN-nih8 u7 phoa3-khiah e5 hian7-siong7, chiah lai5 lim5-kau3 se3-kan, si7 cham2-jian5 khah chiau3 lan2 sou2 ki5-thai7 e5 khoan2.  Chong2-si7 I long2 bo5 an2-ni.  I si7 eng7 tan-sun5 peng5-siong5 e5 hoat-to7 lai5 chhut-si3!  Ki5-sit8 lan2 koh chai3 chim-chiok lai5 siuN7, che kiam2 m7-si7 Siong7-te3 teh chhong3-cho7 it-chhe3 ki5-iN7 e5 su7 e5 hoat-tou7 mah?  Che chiu7-si7 tu2-tu2 chiau3 lan2 sou2 bat teh kong2 e5, “I e5 khoan2 tu2-tu2 si7 an2-ni.”  Ti7 hit e5 Eng2-oan2 e5 se3-kai3, su7-su7 bo5 m7-si7 long2 chiau3 an2-ni lai5 choe3.  Chhin-chhiuN7 I teh hou7 chit8 chang5 chhiu7 tiong2-toa7, teh chhong3-cho7 chit8 liap8 e5 chhiN-siu3, teh hou7 cha2-khi2 si5 e5 jit8 chhut, teh hou7 gou7-kak tit-tioh8 hong-siu chit ho7 e5 sin5-jiah, it-chhe3 bo5 m7-si7 Siong7-te3 si5-siong5 eng7 thiam5-cheng7 tan-sun5 e5 hoat-tou7 ti7 lang5 sou2 bo5 chu3-i3--tioh8 e5 tiong-kan, lai5 teh hou7 i an2-ni.
	Chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni, Ia5-sou si7 eng7 hit ho7 kek8 tan-sun5, bo5 lang5 liau7-tioh8 e5 hoat-tou7, m7-si7 u7 hian2-chhut sim2-mih8 chhiaN-iaN7, a2-si7 chhan3-lan7 e5 hian7-siong7, a2-si7 thiN-nih8 u7 phoa3-khiah e5 kong-keng2, put-ko3 si7 eng7 hit ho7 un5-un5 koh thiam5-cheng7 e5 hoat-tou7, chhin-chhiuN7 cha2-khis2i e5 lou7-chui2, a2-si7 jit8-thau5 e5 hoat-hian7 chit8 poaN, lai5 chhut-si3 ti7 se3-kan, lan2 ti7-chia sou2 beh siuN7 chit chan5, ki5-sit8 si7 chit8 e5 hui-siong5 toa7 e5 su7-kiaN7, si7 chhiau-oat8 lan2 sou2 siuN7 oe7 kau3 e5, iau2-ku2 si7 khoai3-khoai3 kap jin5-seng choe3 te7-it tan-sun5 e5 su7 saN chhap-lam7, sou2-i2 lan2 chhin-chhiuN7 u7 kam2-kak beh eng7 ki5-iN7 kap kiaN-hiaN5 e5 liam7-thau5, lai5 su-siuN2 chit chan5 si7 u7 tam7-poh8 khun3-lan5 e5 khoan2.  Lan2 chhin-chhiuN7 u7 kam2-kak teh thak8 phou2-thong e5 ni5-tai7-ki3 chit8-poaN-iuN7.
	Chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni, Ki-tok u7 eng7 hiah-nih8 iong5-iN7, tan-sun5, chu7-jian5 e5 hoat-tou7, lai5 chhut-si3 chiaN5-choe3 lang5, khia7-khi2 ti7 lan2 tiong-kan.
	Lan2 chit8-e7 hian-khui chit e5 kou3-su7, chiu7 liam5-piN khoaN3-kiN3 chit8 e5 siam2-phiah ti7 Ka-li7-li7 e5 soaN-lai7 e5 hiong-chhoan.  Ti7 chit e5 hiong-chhoan koe-a2, u7 chit8 kham2 choe3 bak8 e5 tiam3, ia7 ti7 hit lai7-bin7 u7 chit8 e5 hiong-chhoan e5 bak8-chhiuN7 kio3 choe3 Iok-sek, tak8-jit8 che7 ti7 tng5-i2, chhiu2 giah8 ku3-a2, pou2-thau5, i2-kip8 chhak8-a2, ti7-teh choe3 i2 kap choe3 toh, i2-kip8 gu5-le5-taN, lai5 kiong-kip chiu-ui5 e5 hiong-chhoan e5 lou7-eng7.  I u7 put-chi2 chhut-lat8, koh khoai3-lok8 teh choe3, ia7 na2 teh choe3 e5 si5, i u7 na2 teh su-siong2 i sou2 pheng3-tiaN7 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5, i2-kip8 ui7-tioh8 hit e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 sou2 tioh8 pi7-pan7 e5 ka-teng5 e5 su7.
	Iok-sek sou2 pheng3-tiaN7 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5, si7 tiam3-ti7 chit e5 hiong-chhoan e5 khah be2-bin7 hia, kio3-choe3 Ma2-li7-a, i si7 A-na2 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2, sui-jian5 i si7 siok8 ti7 Tai7-pit8 e5 hou7-e3, iau2-ku2 si7 chhin-chhiuN7 pat8 e5 hiong-chhoan e5 cha2-bou2 gin2-na2 chit8 poaN, tiam3 chhu3-lai7 gau5 tau3 choe3 kang, phang2-chit, choe3 piaN2, ia7 cha2-am3 kap ki5-u5 e5 hiong-chhoan e5 cha2-bou2 gin2-na2 choe3-he2 saN-kap ti7 chiN2-nih8 chhiuN7 chui2.  Lan2 chai, i si7 chit8 e5 cheng-siok e5 tong5-lu2.  Lan2 thang siong2-siong7 i un2-tang3 u7 sui2-sui2 e5 iong5-mau7, lai5 ho5-hap8 ti7 i sui2-sui2 e5 cheng-sin5 chiah tioh8.
	Chit e5 bak8-chhiuN7 Iok-sek si7 u7 put-chi2 ai3-sioh Ma2-li7-a.  Chiau3 khoaN3 it-chhe3 e5 ki3-su7, u7 am3-si7 lan2 chai, Iok-sek si7 pi2 Ma2-li7-a khah choe7 he3.  Kiam2-chhai2 in-ui7 an2-ni, Iok-sek si7 u7 it-hoat kin2-sin7, un-jiu5 lai5 su-bou7 i.  Iok-sek eng2-eng2 ai3 thau-khoaN3 Ma2-li7-a teh ke3-lou7, ma7-si7 ai3 bong7-siong2 in chiong-lai5 e5 seng-oah8.  Ki5-sit8 tak8-pai2 Iok-sek choe3 kang liau2, Ma2-li7-a ia7-si7 put-chi2 hoaN-hi2 khi3 chhe7 i, lai5 thiaN i kong2-khi2 i e5 iong2-kam2 e5 ke3-ek8 kap ng3-bang7; in-ui7 chiau3 Ka-li7-li7 lang5 e5 hong-siok8, lam5-lu2 si7 chu7-iu5 thang kau-poe5, khah bo5 chhin-chhiuN7 ti7 lam5-peng5 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 hong-bin7 hiah-nih8 giam5.
	Chong2-si7 ti7 in nng7 lang5 e5 sim-su tiong, iau2 u7 pat8-khoan2 koh khah ko-siong7 e5 su7 ti7-teh.  Chit nng7 lang5 m7-si7 chhin-chhiuN7 peng5-siong5 e5 siau3-lian5 lang5, chu-chu teh siuN7 in pun2-sin i2-kip8 in e5 chiong-lai5 e5 su7 na7-tiaN7.  In-ui7 lan2 u7 thiaN-kiN3 kong2, Iok-sek si7 “Gi7 e5 lang5,” Ma2-li7-a si7 u7 chheng-khi3-siuN3 ko-siong7 e5 cheng-sin5, si7 hap8-gi5 thang siu7 keng2-soan2 choe3 Siong7-te3 e5 eng2-oan2 e5 ke3-ek8 e5 chhe-eng7.  Ti7 in e5 seng-oah8 chit e5 giam5-siok, sui2-sui2 e5 choan2-ki, in e5 sim si7 chin jiat8-seng5 u7 chong-kau3 sin3-liam7 ti7-teh, che si7 kin-a2-jit8 e5 siau3-lian5 e5 lam5-lu2 sou2 eng-kai tioh8 oh8 e5 khoan2-sit.  In m7-si7 kan-ta teh siuN7 in e5 chiong-lai5 e5 heng7-hok na7-tiaN7, ma7-si7 siong5-siong5 chhim-chhim teh siuN7 Siong7-te3 e5 ho2 e5 chi2-i3.  Khak-sit8 in un2-tang3 si7 u7 siong5-siong5 saN-kap tam5-lun7, ti7 tong-si5 cheng3 jiat8-sim e5 Iu5-thai3 lang5 sou2 chhiat-chhiat teh ng3-bang7 hit e5 hui-siong5 toa7 e5 su7, chiu7-si7 teh-beh lai5 e5 Bi2-sai3-a e5 su7.  Lan2 thang siuN7, Ma2-li7-a tak8 pai2 kap Iok-sek saN-kap siong-hoe7 liau2, tng2-khi3 in tau e5 si5, u7 kui7-loh8 ti7 in tau e5 thang-a2 khau2, lai5 ui7-tioh8 Iok-sek i2-kip8 i e5 it-seng ki5-to2.
	Chi7-chui7 oe7 thang bong7-siong2 tui3 ti7 chit e5 tan-sun5 e5 ka-teng5, oe7 thang cho7-chiu7 chit8 e5 eng2-oan2 e5 sin5-jiah!  Hit e5 Bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 e5 se3-kai3 ti7 ku2-ku2 u7 khng3 hok8-bu7 e5 liam7-thau5, teh chun2-pi7 I e5 chhut-si3, taN chit-tiap8 i2-keng teh-beh chhian-soa2 chit e5 chin2-kiu3 e5 su7-giap8 loh8-lai5 se3-kan, chit si5 in u7 tai7-seng chhut-thau5 lai5 chi2-si7 I e5 lim5-kau3.
	U7 chit8 jit8 e5 u7 chit8 am3, kiam2-chhai2 tu2-tu2 si7 Ma2-li7-a kui-teh beh ki5-to2 e5 si5, i u7 thiaN-tioh8 chit8 e5 chhiau chu7-jian5, put-chi2 thang chhiN-kiaN e5 siau-sit; u7 io5-choah i e5 choan5 sim-sin5, i u7 khoaN3-kiN3 thiN-sai3 e5 iN7-siong7, soa3 u7 thiaN-kiN3, tui3 hit e5 Bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 e5 se3-kai3 chhut-siaN teh kong2:

Tit-tioh8 toa7 un e5 lang5 ah,
Peng5-an, Chu2 kap li2 ti7-teh.

	Hit-si5 Ma2-li7-a chu7 an2-ni phak ti7 hia, sim-lai7 kiaN kau3 ngiauh8-ngiauh8-chhoah, koh u7 thiaN-kiN3 chin thang chhiN-kiaN e5 oe7, soan-po3 kong2, I2-sek-liat8 lang5 ti7 ku2-ku2 sou2 khng3 e5 toa7 e5 ng3-bang7, taN si7 i2-keng sit8-hian7 lah.
	“Ma2-li7-a boh8-tit kiaN, in-ui7 li2 tit-tioh8 Siong7-te3 e5 un-tian2.  TaN li2 beh hoai5-in7 siN KiaN2, tioh8 ka7 I ho7 mia5 kio3 Ia5-sou.  I beh choe3 toa7, chheng-choe3 Chi3-koai5--e5 e5 KiaN2, Chu2 Siong7-te3 beh eng7 I e5 chou2 Tai7-pit8 e5 ui7 hou7 I.  I beh choe3 ong5 ti7 Nga2-kok e5 ke kau3 tai7-tai7, I e5 kok ia7 bo5 kiong5-chin7…..Seng3 Sin5 beh lim5-kau3 li2.  Chi3-koai5--e5 e5 koan5-leng5 beh ti3-im3 li2.  Sou2-i2 tui3 li2 sou2 siN e5, beh chheng-choe3 Seng3, choe3 Siong7-te3 e5 KiaN2.”
	Hit si5, Ma2-li7-a kong2, “Goa2 si7 Chu2 e5 lu2-pi7, goan7 chiau3 li2 e5 oe7 eng3-giam7 ti7 goa2.”
	Tui3 an2-ni, thiN-sai3 chiu7 li7-khui i.  Lan2 ti7-chia chi2-u7 tioh8 tiam7-tiam7 bo5 thang kong2-khi2 siaN2-khoan2, in-ui7 che si7 sin5-pi3 e5 tai7-chi3.  Sou2-i2 lan2 tek-khak si7 be7 thang chu7-iu5 lai5 ki3-chai3, a2-si7 kai2-sek chit e5 kou3-su7, chi2-u7 tioh8 eng7 khian5-seng5 e5 sim, tiam7-tiam7 chiah ho2.  Chit e5 kou3-su7 na7 m7-si7 Ma2-li7-a pun2-sin u7 kong2-chhut, chiu7 bo5 lang5 oe7 chai-iaN2 siaN2-khoan2.
	Ma2-li7-a sim-lai7 ui7-tioh8 chit e5 tai7-chi3, kiaN-kau3 beh si2, in-ui7 i u7 keng-giam7 tioh8 chiong5-lai5 be7 bat u7 hu7-jin5-lang5 sou2 bat keng-giam7--tioh8 e5 sin5-pi3 e5 su7, tui3 an2-ni chiu7 “khi2-sin koaN2-kin2 khi3 soaN-toe7, kau3 Iu5-thai3 chit8 e5 siaN5,” lai5 ka7 chit8 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 kong2-khi2 i sou2 tu2-tioh8 e5 su7.  Ti7 chit si5, lian5 i sou2 hun-iok e5 tiong7-hu, to m7-kaN2 tui3 i kong2-khi2.  Ti7 chit ho7 si5-chun7, hu7-jin5-lang5 chi2-u7 si7 khiam3-eng7 hu7-jin5-lang5.  Sou2-i2 Ma2-li7-a chiu7 khi3 chhe7 i e5 piau2 chi2-be7, kio3-choe3 I2-li7-sa-pek.  I si7 chit8 e5 hiong-chhoan e5 che3-si e5 hu7-jin5-lang5.  ThiN-sai3 iu5-goan5 u7 tui3 i kong2-khi2 i ma7-si7 u7 siu7 keng2-soan2 beh lai5 choe3 Chi3-koaiN5--e5 e5 ke3-ek8 e5 chhe-eng7.  Chiu7-si7 beh u7 pat8 e5 gin2-na2 tui3 i lai5 chhut-si3, ng3 I2-sek-liat8 lai5 choe3 hit e5 sou2 beh lai5 e5 Bi2-sai3-a e5 sian-hong.
	Chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni, Ma2-li7-a u7 khi3 Hi-pek-lun5 e5 soaN-toe7, jip8 hit e5 che3-si e5 chhu3, ti7-hia Ma2-li7-a kap I2-li7-sa-pek saN-kap bian7-hoe7, tai7-ke lai5 kong2-khi2 in e5 kou3-su7, sim-lai7 kiaN-hiaN5, chai3-saN lai5 tam5-lun7 hit e5 siong5-se3 e5 cheng5-heng5.  In mi5-jit8 tiam3 ti7 soaN-piN hit e5 siok-cheng7 soe3-soe3 e5 chhu3-lai7, saN-kap tam5-lun7, bek8-siong2 teng2-teng2 e5 su7, lai5 saN-kap kau-poe5 Siong7-te3.  Ti7 hit saN geh8 jit8 ku2, in sou2 tit-tioh8 e5 khian5-seng5 e5 keng-giam7, un2-tang3 bo5 boe7 ki3-tit chiah tioh8.  Sit8-chai7 goa7-bin7 e5 se3-kai3, kan-ta si7 teh bo5 eng5 teh chau2-chong5 hiah e5 sio2-sio2 khoa2-khoa2 e5 su7, ia7 long2 m7-chai-iaN2 sou2 beh tu2-tioh8 e5 hui-siong5 toa7 e5 tai7-chi3.
	Chit e5 siu7-un e5 chai7-sek-lu2 Ma2-li7-a, au7-lai5 u7 to3-tng2-khi3 i e5 kou3-hiong Na2-sat-lek8.  TaN i si7 bo5 koh chhin-chhiuN7 cheng5 be7 li7-khui Na2-sat-lek8 e5 khoan2, iau2 koh choe3 chit8 e5 bo5 hoan5 bo5 lo2 e5 cha-bou2 gin2-na2.  Ti7 hit saN geh8 jit8 e5 tiong-kan, Ma2-li7-a si7 i2-keng piN3-chiaN5 chit8 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5; i e5 cheng-sin5 seng-oah8 u7 toa7 chin3-pou7, u7 chin3-jip8 ti7 sin-sin ki5-iN7 e5 se3-kai3, lai5 bit8-chiap kap Siong7-te3 kau-poe5, ka-ki7 chit8 lang5 na2 siuN7 na2 chheN-kiaN, khiok ia7 si7 na2 hoaN-hi2, soa3 khng3-bat8 hit e5 chhiau-oat8-tek e5 sin5-pi3 e5 su7.  Khi2-thau5 Iok-sek khiok si7 m7-chai hit e5 su7-sit8, chong2-si7 ke3-liau2 kui2-na7 geh8 jit8, Ma2-li7-a e5 ki5-iN7 hoaN-hi2 e5 gan2-kong, u7 chiam7-chiam7 hian2-chhut thong3-khou2 e5 khoan2.  In-ui7 Ma2-li7-a u7 un5-un5-a2 chai, i sou2 hun-iok e5 tiong7-hu Iok-sek u7 teh kiaN-hiaN5, teh giau5-gi5 i.  Che si7 Iok-sek e5 sin3-sim sou2 tu2-tioh8 e5 chin thang kiaN e5 chhi3.  “I sou2 hun-iok e5 tiong7-hu Iok-sek si7 gi7 e5 lang5, m7 ai3 hian2-jian5 pan7 i, an3-sng3 beh am3-chiN7 hoe3-chhin.”  ChhiaN2 lan2 lai5 siuN7 hit si5 in nng7 lang5 e5 sim-sin5 kan-khou2 kau3 siaN2-khoan2.  Ki5-sit8 Ma2-li7-a i2-keng u7 lai7 e5 kiam3 chhak8 ke3 i e5 sim, in-ui7 tai7-chi3 si7 beh lou7-hian7, choe7-choe7 lang5 e5 sim-koaN un2-tang3 beh giau5-gi5 i.
	Iok-sek kap Ma2-li7-a ti7 ku2-ku2 e5 tiong-kan sou2 teh kan-khou2, chhiN-chham2 e5 jit8 i2-keng ke3-khi3 liau2.  U7 chit8 am3 ti7 iN7-siong7 tiong, hit e5 sin5-leng5 e5 se3-kai3, u7 lai5 chiap-chhiok--tioh8 lang5 e5 sim-sin5, ti7 hit si5 u7 Siong7-te3 e5 siau-sit thoan5 kau3 ti7 hit e5 sim put-chi2 teh kan-khou2 e5 Iok-sek, tui3 an2-ni i khun3-chhiN2 liau2, chiu7 tit-tioh8 khak-sin3, ia7 ka-ki7 tam7-poh8 kian3-siau3, soa3 hoaN-hi2 lai5 chhoa7 i e5 bou2 Ma2-li7-a ke3-mng5.  I chiu7 eng7 thiaN3-thang3 e5 sim, lai5 chun-keng3, soa3 lai5 chiau3-kou3 chit e5 iau2-be7 chhut-ke3 e5 lau7-bu2 Ma2-li7-a i2-kip8 hit e5 iau2-be7 chhut-si3 e5 KiaN2 Ki-tok.  Ki5-sit8 Ma2-li7-a si7 be7 thang khoai3-khoai3 lai5 boe7 ki3-tit hiah e5 kan-khou2 e5 jit8.  Hit khoan2 e5 keng-giam7 si7 u7 put-si5 khek-tiau5 ti7 i e5 sim-lai7.
	SaN geh8 jit8 au7 e5 u7 chit8 jit8, to i2-keng hong5-hun am3, jit8-thau5 ia7 chhia5 ke3 Pek-li7-heng5 e5 soaN, u7 tam3-loh8 khi3 kau3 ti7 Iu5-thai3 toe7 hiah e5 liu3-hiah8 e5 ko-goan5 e5 khong3-ia2, i2-kip8 saN-li7 hng7-hng7 kap kiong-chhong saN-tui3-chio3 hiah e5 chi2-sek e5 Mou5-ap e5 soaN-nia2.  Hit si5 ti7 hit tiau5 thang3 Pek-li7-heng5 e5 soaN-kan e5 lou7-nih8, si7 u7 kui toa7 tin7 e5 chhut-goa7 lang5. chiap-soa3 pai5 chin tng5 teh kiaN5, ia7 ti7 hit e5 heng5-liat8 e5 tiong-kan, u7 chit8 e5 hiong-chhoan e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 chin ia3-sian7 khia5 ti7 lu5-nih8, koh u7 i e5 bi7-hun e5 tiong7-hu, ti7 sin-piN ka7 i khan lu5 teh kiaN5.  In-ui7 “tng hit-si5 Kat-sat A-lou2-su7-tok u7 chhut-chiau3, beng7-leng7 thong thiN-e7 long2 cho7 ke-kah.  Iok-sek e5 se3-he7 siok8 ti7 Tai7-pit8 e5 ke, sou2-i2 tui3 Ka-li7-li7 e5 Na2-sat-lek8 siaN5, chiuN7 khi3 Iu5-thai3 kau3 Tai7-pit8 e5 siaN5, mia5 kio3 Pek-li7-heng5, beh kap i sou2 pheng3-tiaN7 e5 Ma2-li7-a saN-kap cho7 ke-kah.  Hit-si5 Ma2-li7-a i2-keng u7 sin-in7.”
	Chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni, in u7 keng-ke3 choe7-choe7 iau2 beng5-beng5 oe7 ki3-tit e5, u7 lek8-su2 e5 sou2-chai7.  Phi3-ju7 lai5 kong2, in kiaN5 kau3 ti7 Pek-li7-heng5, ti7 hit e5 chiu-ui5 u7 chit8 e5 toa7 e5 chhau2-tiuN5; chiu7-si7 cha2 Lou7-tek bat ti7 Pho-su7 e5 beh8-hng5 khioh beh-sui7 e5 sou2-chai7.  Ti7 siaN5-goa7 e5 chiaN3-peng5, koh u7 chit8 e5 ham7-khang, chiu7-si7 cha2 ti7-hia u7 choe7-choe7 iong2-kam2 e5 lang5, ui7-tioh8 beh tui3 Pek-li7-heng5 e5 chui2-chiN2, chhiuN7 chui2 lai5 hou7 Tai7-pit8 lim, ti3-kau3 hou7 lang5 phah-si2 e5 sou2-chai7.  Iu7-koh li7 to7-lou7 bo5 loa7 hng7, ma7-si7 u7 chit8 e5 sou2-chai7, chiu7-si7 cheng3 Iu5-thai3 lang5 khoaN3-choe3 seng3, put-chi2 teh siau3-liam7 e5, in-ui7 cha2 ti7-hia Nga2-kok u7 song3-sit i e5 oah8-mia7 e5 kng, si7 ui7-tioh8 “Liap8-kiat si2, bai5-chong3 ti7 I2-hoat-tai7 e5 lou7-piN, (au7-lai5 mia5 Pek-li7-heng5, chiu7-si7 hit e5 sou2-chai7).”
	Chong2-si7 Iok-sek kap Ma2-li7-a lai5 kau3 Pek-li7-heng5 e5 si5, in sim-lai7 sou2 te7-it khoa3-sim e5, chiu7-si7 hit e5 sou2 beh liam5-piN chiaN5 e5 koh-khah toa7 iau2-kin2 e5 tai7-chi3.  Iok-sek put-chi2 ti3-i3 si3-ke3 teh chhe7, thang hou7 Ma2-li7-a hioh-khun3 e5 sou2-chai7.  In-ui7 lou7-thau5 i2-keng kiaN5 hiah-nih8 hng7, Ma2-li7-a si7 chin sian7-thau5.  Siat-su2 si7 peng5-siong5 si5, chiu7 m7-bian2 hoan5-lo2 thang toa3 e5 sou2-chai7, in-ui7 Tang-iuN5 lang5 si7 put-chi2 chhin-chhiat gau5 ho2 khoan2-thai7 chhut-goa7 lang5, khoaN3 che choe3 si7 sin5-seng3 e5 gi7-bu7.  Chong2-si7 hit-si5 si7 kok-se3 tiau7-cha, chhut-goa7 lang5 si7 chin-choe7 chu7-chip8 ti7 siaN5-nih8.  Sou2-i2 na7 khah ban7 kau3 e5 lang5-kheh, bo5 lun7 ti7 sim2-mih8 sou2-chai7, a2-si7 kheh-koan2 ma7-si7 long2 bo5 pang5-keng thang hioh-khun3.
	In bo5 ui7 thang hioh-khun3, khiok be7 thang kong2 si7 sim2-mih8 lang5 e5 chho3-gou7.  In-ui7 tu5-khi3 ti7 I sou2 chhut-lai5 hit e5 se3-kai3 e5 siaN5-chhiuN5 e5 teng2-bin7, teh khoaN3 loh8-lai5 hiah e5 chong5-pai3 I e5 cheng3 thiN-sai3, i2-goa7 ti7 se3-kan to long2 bo5 lang5 chai I si7 chi7-chui7.  Sou2-i2 hiah e5 khia7-khi2 ti7 I sou2 hoaN-hi2 e5 se3-kai3 e5 lang5, long2 bo5 beh koe3-chek lan2, khiok si7 in kau3-giah8 thang ho2-chhio3, kong2, U2-tiu7 e5 Chu2 beh lim5-kau3 ti7 I sou2 chhong3-cho7 chit e5 soe3-soe3 e5 se3-kai3, koh ia7 bo5 chit8 ui7 pang5-keng thang choe3 I e5 lou7-eng7.
	In au7-lai5 u7 hoaN-hi2 siam2-pi7 khi3 ti7 soaN-piN, chit8 e5 cheng-siN sou2 teh khun3 e5 chu7-jian5 e5 tong7-khang e5 lai7-bin7.  Hit-si5 ti7-hia long2 bo5 u7 chhin-chhiat e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 thang pang-chan7 Ma2-li7-a, iu7-koh EN-a2 beh chhut-si3 e5 kan-khou2 to i2-keng kau3 ti7 chit e5 kou-tok8 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5.  Tui3 an2-ni, i chiu7 siN thau5-chiuN7 kiaN2, eng7 pou3 pau I, soa3 he7 I ti7 be2-cho5-lai7 kap sin-piN e5 cheng-siN choe3-he2 lai5 hiong2-siu7 I choe3 ang5 eN-a2 choe3 chhou e5 an-bin5.
	Chiong5-lai5 kiam2 bat u7 sim2-mih8 eN-a2, tiam3 ti7 pi2 chit e5 koh-khah ha7-chian7 e5 chong7-thai3 lai5 chhut-si3 ti7 chit e5 se3-kan mah?  Lan2 kiam2 bo5 in-ui7 an2-ni it-hoat thiaN3-thang I mah?  Siat-su2 I na7 lai5 chhut-si3 ti7 ong5-kiong, u7 choe7-choe7 kiong-lu2 thang khoan2-thai7 I, koh u7 choe7-choe7 che3-si-thau5 thang su-hau7 I, kiaN-liau2 hoan2-tng2 oe7 soa3 sun2-hai7 tioh8 I e5 sit8-chai7 e5 jin5-keh ia7 ku2 kaN2.  Chit e5 kho2-lin5, bo5 lang5 u7 chu3-i3--tioh8 e5 ang5 eN-a2, tiam3 ti7 hit ho7 bo5 lat8, tioh8 oa2-kho3 lang5 pang-chan7 e5 chong7-thai3, lai5 lim5-kau3 ti7 lan2, che su7-sit8 kah na2 chhin-chhiuN7 I u7 chiong pun2-sin long2 kau-thok lan2, teh theng3-hau7 lan2 lai5 thiaN3-sioh I, khiam3-eng7 lan2 lai5 hoaN-hi2 I.  Chhin-chhiuN7 tiam3 ti7 chit khoan2 oe7 kam2-tong7 lang5, oe7 giu2 lang5 e5 chu3-i3 e5 chong7-thai3, Ki-tok u7 chhut-si3 chiaN5-choe3 eN-a2 lai5 jip8 ti7 chit e5 se3-kan.
	Chong2-si7 lan2 i2-siong7 sou2 kong2 chiah-e5, put-ko3 u7 I e5 chhut-si3 e5 kou3-su7 e5 chit8 poaN3 na7-tiaN7.  Lan2 tioh8 oe7 ki3-tit cheng3 thiN-sai3 u7 soa3 chhut-hian7 ti7 chit e5 kou3-su7.  Chit nng7 e5 se3-kai3 long2 u7 hian2-chhut ti7 chit e5 kou3-su7 e5 sia2-chin e5 lai7-tiong.  Ng3-bang7 lan2 put-si5 oe7 ki3-tit chit e5 oan5-choan5 e5 sia2-chin, na7 bo5, kiaN-liau2 chit e5 kou3-su7 oe7 chho-gou7--khi3.
	Chhin-chhiuN7 cha2-khi2 si5 e5 jit8-thau5 e5 hoat-hian7 chit8 poaN, eng7 tan-sun5, peng5-siong5 e5 hoat-tou7, Siong7-te3 u7 ti7 chit e5 u2-tiu7 e5 lek8-su2 tiong, lai5 choe3 chhut chit8 e5 thang chhiN-kiaN e5 su7-kiaN7, chiu7-si7 u7 hou7 hit e5 Eng5-kng e5 Chu2 chhut-hian7 lai5 khia7-khi2 ti7 lang5 e5 tiong-kan.  Lan2 to7 toe7-bin7 sou2 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 e5, si7 kan-ta be2-tiau5, be2-cho5, cheng-siN, i2-kip8 chit8 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 kap chit8 e5 eng7 pou3 pau-teh e5 eN-a2 na7-tiaN7.  Ti7 chit tiong-kan lan2 long2 bo5 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 sim2-mih8 ki5-iN7 thang chhiN-kiaN e5 su7 ti7-teh.  Chong2-si7 lan2 tioh8 oe7 ki3-tit, ti7 au7-lai5, tui3 I sou2 siok8 hit e5 se3-kai3, u7 hian2-chhut chhan3-lan7 e5 kng, lai5 chio3 ti7 chit e5 kou3-su7 e5 choan5-keng2, chiu7-si7 ti7 be2-tiau5 e5 teng2-bin7, ti7 goa7-bin7 chhiN-siu3 kng-liang7 e5 sou2-chai7, u7 choe7-choe7 thian-peng kek8 toa7 e5 jiat8-nau7, lai5 hoaN-hi2 Ki-tok chhut-si3 choe3 eN-a2 lim5-kau3 se3-kan.
	Sou2-i2 lan2 tioh8 oe7 ki3-tit, an2-ni chiah si7 chit8 e5 oan5-choan5 e5 kou3-su7, chit8 e5 oan5-choan5 e5 sia2-chin.  Chit e5 oan5-choan5 e5 sia2-chin, chiu7-si7 teh piau2-si7 u7 chit8 e5 Sin5-seng3 e5 eN-a2, tui3 thiN-nih8 beh lim5 kau3 ti7 toe7-nih8 e5 si5, hiah e5 ti7 thiN-nih8 teh chiau3-kou3 I e5 cheng3 thiN-sai3, u7 ti7 goa7-bin7 teh hoaN-hi2 lai5 po2-hou7 I e5 chhut-si3.  Koh-chai3 lai5 kong2, tak8 pai2 lan2 na7 beh thak8 Ki-tok-toan7, lan2 tioh8 oe7 ki3-tit, I sou2 chhut-lai5 hit e5 se3-kai5 e5 su7.  Lan2 u7 sin3 hit e5 se3-kai3 si7 u7-iaN2.  Chong2-si7 lan2 e5 sim lou2-tun7, lan2 eng2-eng2 ai3 hut-liok8, tui3 an2-ni, lan2 sou2 oe7 e5 Ki-tok e5 siong7, eng2-eng2 ai3 sit-loh8 hit e5 tiong-sim tiam2.
	Ti7 Ki-tok-toan7 tiong, te7-it oe7 kam2-tong7 lan2 e5 sim e5, sit8-chai7 si7 hit cham7 teh ki3-chai3 hit e5 se3-kai3 e5 hian2-hian7 e5 su7.  Hit e5 im-gak8 e5 siaN-im u7 chaiN2-iuN7 chheng3 koaiN5 chhin-chhiuN7 hai2-eng2, pian3-moa2 ti7 thong Pek-li7-heng5 e5 bok8-tiuN5, lai5 gim5 toa7 hoaN-hi2 e5 ho2 siau-sit, hou7 cheng3 peh-siN3 long2 u7 hun7, ia7 tng peh-siN3 aN3 hi7-khang teh thiaN e5 si5, choe7-choe7 thian-peng u7 chaiN2-iuN7 hoaN-hi2 kau3 tong3 boe7 tiau5, hut-jian5 chhut-siaN lai5 gim5 hit e5 teng2-bin7 e5 se3-kai3 e5 chan3-bi2 e5 si, kong2,--- Ti7 Chi3-koaiN5 e5 ui7 eng5-kng kui ti7 Siong7-te3!
	Chong2-si7 lan2 na7 bo5 chhim-sin3 hit e5 se3-kai3, u7 put-si5 jiat8-jiat8 teh koan-sim ti7 lan2 e5 chit e5 se3-kai3, sui-jian5 tui3 hit e5 se3-kai3 u7 hian2-chhut sim2-mih8 ki5-iN7, a2-si7 sui2-sui2 e5 hian7-siong7, lan2 khoaN3-liau2 ma7-si7 bo5 sim2-mih8 oe7 giu2 lan2 e5 sim, khoaN3 choe3 bo5 heng3-bi7 e5 su7, sui-jian5 tui3 thiN-nih8 u7 thiN-sai3 chhut-hian7, ma7-si7 hoan2-tng2 ai3 khoaN3 choe3 chhin-chhiuN7 kui toa7 tin7 e5 hun5-bu7, lai5 teh jia-chah8 ti7 toe7-bin7 lan2 sou2 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 e5 be2-cho5, i2-kip8 EN-a2 e5 siong7.  Chit-tiap8 lan2 tek-khak m7-thang u7 an2-ni siuN7.  Lan2 na7-si7 bo5 beng5 hit e5 se3-kai3, a2-si7 khoaN3-khin hit e5 se3-kai3 sou2 hian2-hian7 e5 su7, put-ko3 si7 hou7 chit e5 oan5-choan5 e5 kou3-su7, piN3-choe3 chit8 e5 bo5 saN lian5-chiap, bo5 chhu3-su7 e5 kou3-su7.  In-ui7 hit e5 se3-kai3 e5 su7, m7-si7 kan-ta chhin-chhiuN7 lang5 teh choe3 bi2-biau7 e5 si sou2 teh khong-siong2 e5 na7-tiaN7, si7 Sin5-seng3 e5 su7-sit8, piN5-piN5 u7 kiat-lian5 ti7 chit e5 gin2-na2 e5 kou3-su7.  Hit e5 se3-kai3 e5 su7-sit8, sit8-chai7 si7 chit e5 pau kun e5 EN-a2 e5 kou3-su7 e5 chit8-pou7-hun7.  Chit nng7 e5 se3-kai3 , tek-khak tioh8 saN kiat-lian5, piN5-piN5 lai5 khoaN3-choe3 si7 sit8-chai7.  Lan2 tioh8 chhai2-chip8 chit nng7 e5 se3-kai3 e5 su7-sit8, chiah oe7 thang oan5-choan5 lai5 oe7 chit e5 sia2-chin.
	Chai7 Ia5-sou sou2 khoaN3 hit e5 se3-kai3, chiu7-si7 I e5 chou2-ke.  Sou2-i2 I u7 si5-siong5 choe3-he2 lai5 teh siuN7 chit nng7 e5 se3-kai3, oan2-jian5 chhin-chhiuN7 lan2 siong5-siong5 teh siau3-liam7 lan2 e5 kou3-hiong, i2-kip8 lan2 sou2 bat e5 peng5-iu2 chit poaN, I u7 siong5-siong5 kong2-khi2 thiN-nih8 e5 su7, ia7 u7 kong2-khi2 cheng3 thiN-sai3 i2-kip8 cheng3 sin5-leng5 e5 su7, I na7 tiam3 ti7 toe7-nih8 u7 khoaN3-tioh8 chit8 e5 soe3-han3 e5 gin2-na2 e5 si5, chiu7 iu5-goan5 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 ti7 thiN-nih8 hiah e5 teh chiau3-kou3 gin2-na2 e5 thiN-sai3,  I na7 tiam3 ti7 toe7-nih8 khoaN3-kiN3 chit8 e5 choe7-jin5 hoan2-hoe2 e5 si5, iu5-goan5 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 ti7 thiN-nih8, cheng3 thiN-sai3 e5 bin7-cheng5, u7 ui7-tioh8 i teh hoaN-hi2.  I u7 kam2-kak hit e5 se3-kai3 si5-siong5 pau-ui5 ti7 I e5 sin-piN, si5-siong5 koan-sim ti7 lan2 chit e5 se3-kai3.
	Lan2 ti7 cheng5 i2-keng u7 kong2, jin5-lui7 tiong Siong7-te3 tak8 pai2 e5 khe2-si7, i2-kip8 ti7 chit e5 se3-kai3 sou2 siu7 tak8 teng2 ho7 u7 the5-ko cheng-sin5-chiuN7 e5 su7, ti7 be7 chai ti7-chia  e5 i2-cheng5, chiu7 i2-keng heng-khi2 ti7 hit e5 se3-kai3.  Ti7 be7 hian2-hian7 ti7 chit peng5 e5 tai7-seng, ti7 hit peng5 tui3 ku2-ku2 chiu7 i2-keng chai-iaN2, sou2-i2 lan2 thang siuN7, chhin-chhiuN7 Eng2-oan2 e5 KiaN2 e5 Hoa3-sin, chit khoan2 toa7 e5 ke3-bou5, ti7 lan2 be7 chai e5 i2-cheng5, ti7 thiN-nih8, cheng3 thiN-sai3 un2-tang3 beh toa7-toa7 hat-chhai2 lai5 hoaN-hi2, ia7 kau3 au7-lai5 in ma7-si7 eng7 chong5-pai3 e5 liam7-thau5 lai5 hoaN-hi2 hit e5 bu2-tai5 u7 chhian-soa2 loh8-lai5 se3-kan, sou2-i2 lan2 chiah u7 thang khoaN3-kiN3 cheng3 thiN-sai3 chin hoaN-hi2, ti7 hit-am3 lai5 gim5 hap8-gi5 e5 koa, lai5 po3 toa7 hoaN-hi2 e5 ho2 siau-sit, hou7 cheng3-lang5 long2 u7 hun7 kong2, “Kin-a2-jit8 ti7 Tai7-pit8 e5 siaN5, i2-keng ui7-tioh8 lin2 siN chit8 e5 Chin2-kiu3 e5, chiu7-si7 Chu2 Ki-tok.”

Te7-2 chiuN	Chhu3-Lu2 Kang3-Tan3

Ui7-tioh8 chit e5 bun7-toe5, ti7 kun7-lai5 u7 chiaN5-choe3 it-poaN e5 gi7-lun7, ia7 siong5-siong5 siN-chhut put-an kap giau5-gi5 e5 liam7-thau5.  Sou2-i2 ti7-chia lan2 ai3 ke-sia2 chit8 chiuN, lai5 kan2-tan lun7-khi2 lan2 e5 Chu2 e5 Chhu3-lu2 kang3-tan3 e5 su7.
Tui3 chit e5 bun7-toe5, sit8-chai7 m7-si7 kan-ta bi7-sin3-chia2 teh giau5-gi5 hit e5 su7-sit8 na7-tiaN7, lian5 ti7 Ki-tok-tou5 e5 tiong-kan, to iu5-goan5 u7 choe7-choe7 lang5 teh chu2-tiuN kong2, che si7 bo5 koan-he7 ti7 lan2 teh sin3 Ia5-sou si7 Sin5-seng3, soa3 iau3-kiu5 chit chan5 tioh8 pang3 he7-teh, khoaN3-choe3 boe7 thang koat-teng7 e5 bun7-toe5, ia7 soa3 chu2-tiuN kango2, lan2 tioh8 tui3 lan2 e5 Sin3-keng lai5 san-tu5 chit ku3, “I tui3 Seng3 Sin5 e5 koan5-leng5 tau-thai, tui3 chai7-sek-lu2 Ma2-li7-a chhut-si3” e5 oe7 khi2--lai5, ng3-bang7 thang kiam2-chio2 lang5 e5 giau5-gi5.
Lan2 kiam2-chhai2 thang sin3-iong7 in, lai5 khoaN3 in e5 i3-su3 si7 seng5-sit8, iau2-ku2 lan2 ai3 chi2-si7 in chai, chit ho7 bo5 bun5-beng5 e5 thai3-tou7, si7 put-chi2 u7 sun2-hai7, koh u7 chho3-gou7 ti7-teh.  Lan2 bo5 u7 sim2-mih8 li2-iu5 thang kong2, che si7 si3-chiaN3 e5 su-siong2.  Ki5-sit8 chit ho7 su-siong2, kau3-be2 tiaN7-tioh8 si7 oe7 eng2-hiong2 ti7 lan2 teh sin3 Ia5-sou si7 Sin5-seng3.  Kau3-hoe7 hiah-nih8 tui3-tiong7 lai5 ki3-chai3 chit e5 su7-sit8 ti7 in e5 Sin3-keng, to m7-si7 bo5 in-toaN ti7-teh.  In-ui7 ke3-khi3 e5 lek8-su2, u7 chi2-si7 lan2 chai chit8-hang7 e5 ka3-si7, kong2, hoan7-na7 lang5 sit-loh8 Chu2 e5 Chhu3-lu2 kang3-tan3 e5 sin3-giong2, chiu7-si7 sit-loh8 Hoa3-sin e5 kau3-li2 e5 tiong-sim-chioh8.
Lun7 chit e5 toa7 e5 bun7-toe5, lan2 beh lai5 kan2-liok8 kong2, si7 chin ui5-lan5 e5 su7.  Put-ko3 chhiaN2 iong5-un2 goa2 lai5 chhi3-khoaN3, thau5 chit8 hang7, lai5 kong2-khi2 hit e5 lek8-su2-tek e5 cheng5-heng5, piau2-beng5 chit e5 kau3-li2, siaN2-su7 chiah oe7 lai5 he7 ti7 Sin3-keng e5 lai7-tiong; te7 ji7 hang7, lai5 gi7-lun7 ti7 kin-na2-jit8, lang5 u7 chaiN2-iuN7 teh hoan2-tui3, teh giau5-gi5 chit tiam2; te7 saN hang7, lan2 ai3 lai5 chu2-tiuN siaN2-su7 bo5 po2-siu2 chit-tiau5 e5 to7-li2, ti7 lan2 e5 sin3-giong2 e5 lai7-bin7, si7 be7 iong7-tit e5 in-toaN.
TaN lan2 thau5 chit8 hang7, lai5 lun7 hit e5 lek8-su2-tek e5 cheng5-heng5.  Tng lan2 e5 Chu2 chai7-se3 e5 tiong-kan, cheng3 hak8-seng si7 koat-toan3 m7-bat siuN7-tioh8 chit e5 bun7-toe5.  In na7-si7 iau2-be7 liau2-kai2 Ki-tok si7 Sin5, chu7-jian5 chit ho7 su7, in khoaN3-liau2 si7 put-hap8-li2, chin ki5-koai3, boe7 thang sin3-tit e5 su7.  Chiau3 Seng3-chheh sou2 kong2, Ma2-li7-a u7 “chiong it-chhe3 e5 su7 ki3 ti7 sim-nih8.”  Lan2 chai Ma2-li7-a si7 keng3-khian5, si7 koaN-gian5 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5, sou2-i2 hou7 lan2 thang sin3, kiam2-chhai2 tu5-khi3 tui3 kek8 sio2 pou7-hun7 e5 chi3-chhin e5 lang5 i2-goa7, Ma2-li7-a long2 bo5 lou7-chhut chit e5 tai7-chi3.  I beh thai3 oe7 leh?  Chhi3-siuN7 lang5 long2 iau2 teh khoaN3 Ia5-sou si7 chit8 e5 lang5 na7-tiaN7 e5 si5, chhin-chhiuN7 chit ho7 e5 bun7-toe5, i lai5 kham3-bat8 teh, long2 bo5 kong2-khi2, che kiam2 m7-si7 chin sui2, chu7-jian5 e5 thai3-tou7 mah?  Ma2-li7-a kiam2 oe7 boe7 ki3-tit i sou2 hun-iok e5, chin chhiN-kiaN e5 kan-khou2 e5 cheng5-keng2 mah?  Siat-su2 na7 m7-si7 Ma2-li7-a iu5-goan5 si7 i2-keng u7 liau2-kai2 Ki-tok si7 Sin5, i2-kip8 I e5 chhu3-lu2 kang3-tan3 e5 toa7 e5 i3-gi7, i kiam2 beh chiong chit ho7, chiau3 lang5 khoaN3 tiaN7-tioh8 si7 bo5 i3-su3, boe7 oe7 e5 keng-giam7, lai5 tui3 hit ho7 kau7 giau5-gi5 e5 se3-kai3 lou7-chhut mah?
Lan2 chai cheng3 hak8-seng ti7 khi2-thau5 teh kap Ia5-sou kau-poe5, long2 si7 khoaN3 I choe3 chit8 e5 lang5 na7-tiaN7.  Sit8-chai7 che beng5-beng5 ma7-si7 Siong7-te3 e5 i3-su3.  Ia5-sou iu5-goan5 si7 ai3 lang5 an2-ni khoan2-thai7 I.  I u7 chun2-choe3 chit8 e5 lang5, lai5 tit-tioh8 in e5 thiaN3-thang3, khim-giong2 kap chun-keng3 e5 sim.  Put-ko3 in e5 sim si7 u7 chiam7-chiam7 chin3-jip8 khah chhim, choe3 au7 soa3 siN-khi2 ki5-iN7 kap kiaN-hiaN5 e5 liam7-thau5, sim-lai7 soa3 put-chi2 be5-loan7, boe7-hiau2 I si7 chi7-chui7.  Cheng3 hak8-seng soa3 long2 m7-chai-iaN2 tioh8 chaiN-2iuN7 lai5 su-siuN2 I.  Ia5-sou ma7-si7 bo5 pang-chan7 in e5 khui3-lat8, put-tan3 si7 an2-ni, sim7-chi3 soa3 un2-bat8, bo5 ai3 lang5 chai I si7 Sin5.  Lian5 in u7 kam2-chhiok--tioh8 I e5 Sin5-seng3 e5 chit8-sut8-a2 e5 kng e5 si5, I ia7 m7-chun2 in lai5 kong2-khi2.  Lian5 ti7 pian3 iong5-mau7 e5 keng-giam7 au7, I ma7 iau2 teh hoan-hu3 in tioh8 cheng7-cheng7 theng3-hau7 kau3 ti7 “Jin5-chu2 tui3 si2-lang5 tiong koh khi2-lai5” e5 jit8, chiah thang kong2-khi2 I si7 Sin5.  Put-ko3 hit e5 si5 i2-keng peh-kun7 ti7 I e5 lim5-chiong, I chiah u7 piau2-beng5 pun2-sin kong2, “Lin2 tioh8 sin3 Siong7-te3, iah8 tioh8 sin3 goa2.”  “Goa2 kap goa2 e5 Pe7 si7 chit8-e5.”  “Seng3 Sin5 chiu7-si7 goa2 tui3 Pe7 sou2 chhe e5, beh lim5-kau3 lin2.”  “U7 chit8 jit8, goa2 beh lai5 sim2-phoaN3 oah8 lang5, si2 lang5.”
Chong2-si7 kau3 ti7 Ia5-sou e5 koh-oah8, keng-ke3 hit e5 o3-biau7 e5 si3-chap8 jit8, Seng-thian, koh Seng3 Sin5 lim5-kau3 liau2-au7, cheng3 hak8-seng chiah chiap-tioh8 chin hui-siong5 toa7 e5 khe2-si7, lai5 chap8-hun liau2-kai2 ti7 ki5-iN7 e5 saN ni5 ku2 tiam3 Pa-lek8-su-theng3 Hit e5 kap in choe3-he2 seng-oah8 e5, si7 chi7-chui7, chiu7-si7 beng5-pek8 tu2-tu2 si7 chiau3 e7-bin7 in sou2 kong2 e5.  “To7 u7 chiaN5-choe3 jiok8-the2 khia7-khi2 ti7 lan2 tiong-kan, u7 un-tian2 kap chin-li2 moa2-moa2, koh goa2 bat khoaN3-kiN3 I e5 eng5-kng, chhin-chhiuN7 Tok8-siN KiaN2 tui3 Pe7 sou2 tit e5 eng5-kng.”
Lun7 lang5 teh sin3 Ia5-sou si7 Sin5, che si7 choan5-jian5 bo5 koan-he7 ti7 I e5 chhu3-lu2 kang3-tan3 e5 su7-sit8.  In-ui7 ti7 cheng3 hak8-seng e5 tiong-kan, toa7 pou7-hun7 si7 long2 m7-chai-iaN2 chit e5 su7-sit8, ia7 sui-jian5 in long2 bo5 thiaN-kiN3 pi2 in sou2 keng-giam7 e5, koh khah cha2 e5 sim2-mih8 su7, in e5 sin3-giong2 ma7-si7 boe7 io5-choah, iu5-goan5 ma7-si7 oe7 hiau2-tit ko3-pek8 kong2, “Goan2 chai, Siong7-te3 e5 KiaN2 u7 lim5-kau3 se3-kan.”  Chit e5 su7-sit8 si7 ti7 ku2-ku2 e5 tiong-kan u7 giam5-giam5 kham3-bat8, put-ko3 kau3 ti7 it-poaN e5 khong-khi3 i2-keng pi7-pan7 pian7 thang seng5-siu7, hit-si5 chit e5 su7-sit8 chiah lou7-hian7, sou2-i2 chhi3-siuN7, hit si5 in e5 sin2-giong2 kiam2 m7-si7 chin7-chai7 kian-kou3 koh oan5-choan5 mah?  In-ui7 lun7 Chhu2-lu2 kang3-tan3 e5 su7, ti7 i2-cheng5 in khoaN3-liau2 si7 bo5 sim2-mih8 i3-su3 ti7-teh, chong2-si7 chit-tiap8 hit e5 i3-su3 si7 put-chi2 beng5.  Chit e5 su7-sit8 u7 tui3 I e5 Sin5-seng3 e5 o3-biau7, lai5 tu5-khi3 choe7-choe7 hun7-loan7 e5 bun7-toe5.  Chit e5 su7-sit8 si7 u7 ho5-hap8 ti7 I e5 hoa3-sin e5 su7-sit8, chhin-chhiuN7 so2-si5 e5 ho5-hap8 ti7 so2 e5 khoan2-sit chit8-poaN-iuN7.
Chu7-jian5 chit e5 kou3-su7, si7 tit8-chiap tui3 Ma2-li7-a, a2-si7 kan3-chiap tui3 Ma2-li7-a e5 chhin-lang5, toa7-bin7 Iok-han7, a2-si7 tui3 Ma2-li7-a hiah e5 keng3-khian5 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 phoaN7 lai5 thiaN-kiN3 e5.
