Choe3-chhou hak8-seng chaiN2-iuN7 lai5 thoan5-po3 hit e5 siau-sit, lan2 long2 m7-chai poaN3-hang7.  Tong-si5 e5 kau3-hoe7 sou2 boan2-chiok e5 cheng3-ku3 si7 sim2-mih8 khoan2, lan2 ma7-si7 long2 m7-chai.  Lan2 chi2-u7 chai-iaN2, “Ia5-sou e5 lau7-bu2 Ma2-li7-a u7 kap i e5 hiaN-ti7 saN-kap toa3.”  Koh chai-iaN2 ti7 bo5 kui2-ni5 e5 tiong-kan, chit e5 siau-sit u7 pian3-thoan5 ti7 choan5 Pa-lek8-su-theng3; iu7-koh chai-iaN2 chit e5 siau-sit, ti7 bo5 kui2-ni5 ku2, u7 piN3-choe3 chit8 e5 khau2-thoan5 ti7 in tiong-kan, ia7 chit e5 siau-sit chiaN5-choe3 khau3-thoan5 liau2-au7, Ma2-thai3 chiah giah8-pit lai5 ki3-chai3, ia7 Lou7-ka chiah soa3 ki3-chai3 koh khah siong5-se3 ti7 chheh-nih8.  Lan2 chi2-u7 chai tong-si5 e5 kau3-hoe7 u7 chhut-pan2 chiah e5 Hok-im-su lai5 piau2-beng5 in e5 sin3-giong2, soa3 chiong chit e5 sin3-giong2 lai5 phian-jip8 ti7 cha2-cha2 e5 Sin3-keng e5 lai7-bin7.  Ti7-chia u7 Lo5-ma2 lang5 oa2 ti7 Chu2-au7 100 ni5, in teh kiaN5 soe2-le2 e5 si5 sou2 teh eng7 e5 Sin3-keng, ti7 hit lai7-tiong, u7 chit8 ku3 teh kong2, “Tui3 Seng3 Sin5 lai5 hoai5-in7, tui3 chai7-sek-lu2 Ma2-li7-a lai5 chhut-si3.”  Ji5-hou7 ti7 tak8 si5-tai7 e5 kau3-hoe7 long2 bo5 pian3-oaN7, ia7 long2 bo5 iu5-tang7, u7 ki3-chai3 chit e5 su7-sit8 ti7 in e5 Sin3-keng, lai5 chhian2-beng5 I e5 Hoa3-sin e5 tiong-sim e5 ka3-si7.  Kau3 hian7-kim ti7 thong se3-kai3 tak8 sou2-chai7 e5 kau3-hoe7, to long2 si7 u7 ka3-si7 in e5 kiaN2-ji5, tioh8 sin3 I e5 hoa3-sin e5 to7-li2, soa3 kio3 in tioh8 oat8-liam7 kong2, “Goa2 sin3 Ia5-sou Ki-tok, i5-it e5 Chu2, chiu7-si7 tui3 Seng3 Sin5 e5 koan5-leng5 tau-thai, tui3 chai7-sek-lu2 Ma2-li7-a chhut-si3.”
Chit-tiap8 lan2 ai3 chiau3 si3-chiaN3 e5 sun7-su7 lai5 khoaN3 hak8-seng u7 chaiN2-iuN7 lai5 keng-giam7 I e5 Chhu3-lu2 kang3-tan3 e5 su7-sit8.  Cheng3 hak8-seng choe3-chhou si7 u7 tit-tioh8 toa7 e5 khak-sin3 lai5 keng-giam7--tioh8 Ki-tok e5 Sin5-seng3.  Tok8-tok8 lan2 u7 jin7 Ki-tok si7 Sin5, si7 Siong7-te3, hit si5 lan2 chiah u7 thang gi7-lun7 I e5 Chhu3-lu2 kang3-tan3 e5 bun7-toe5.  Lan2 na7-si7 bo5 u7 jin7 Ki-tok si7 Sin5, chu7-jian5 I e5 Chhu3-lu2 kang3-tan3 e5 su7, si7 khoaN3-choe3 bo5 i3-su3.  Lan2 chi2-u7 oe7 hiau2-tit lai5 chong5-pai3 hit e5 seng-thian e5 Ki-tok, lai5 khoaN3 I choe3 si7 Siong7-te3, hit si5 chiah oe7 tit-tioh8 chap8-hun e5 khak-sin3, lai5 beng5-pek8 Ma2-li7-a sou2 u7 thiaN-kiN3 hit e5 Sin5-seng3, koh sin5-pi3 e5 oe7, kong2, “Seng3 Sin5 beh lim5-kau3 li2, Chi3-koaiN5 e5, e5 koan5-leng5 beh ti3-im3 li2, sou2-i2 tui3 li2 siN e5, beh chheng choe3 Seng3, choe3 Siong7-te3 e5 KiaN2.”  Tui3 an2-ni, chhin-chhiuN7 so2-si5 e5 ho5-hap8 ti7 so2 e5 khoan2-sit, hit si5 I e5 Chhu3-lu2 kang3-tan3 e5 su7-sit8, lan2 chiah oe7 khoaN3-choe3 si7 u7 ho5-hap8 ti7 I e5 Sin5-seng3, u7 oan5-seng5 I e5 Sin5-seng3, chiaN5-choe3 hou7 lang5 oe7 thang sin3 tit e5 su7-sit8.
Ti7-si5 chit e5 su7 chiah hian2-jian5?  Chit e5 su7 m7-si7 keng-ke3 choe7-choe7 ni5 ku2, kau3 u7 si5-kan thang hoat-seng choe7-choe7 thoan5-soat e5 si5, chiah hian2-jian5.  M7-si7!  Chit e5 su7 si7 tu2-tu2 ti7 Chu2 koh-oah8 liau2, sui5-si5 hian2-jian5.  Tek-kok u7 chit8 ui7 hak8-chia2, kio3-choe3 Ha2-luh-na2-khuh (Adolf von Harnack), i si7 te7-it chai-bat goan5-si2 Ki-tok kau3 e5 lek8-su2, i pun2-sin khiok-si7 m7-sin3 Chhu3-lu2 kang3-tan3 e5 su7-sit8, iau2-ku2 u7 seng5-jin7 lai5 chu2-tiuN kong2, chit e5 Chhu3-lu2 kang3-tan3 e5 sin3-giong2, si7 oa2 te7-it se3-ki2 be2 tak8 sou2-chai7 e5 Ki-tok-tou5 kiong7-thong sou2 sin3 e5, sou2-i2 lan2 tioh8 seng5-jin7, chit e5 Chhu3-lu2 kang3-tan3 e5 sin3-giong2 si7 tui3 ti7 Chu2 koh-oah8 liau2 e5 si5 khi2, kau3 ti7 te7-it se3-ki2 be2 e5 tiong-kan, ti7 Pa-lek8-su-theng3 sou2 hoat-seng e5.
U7 sim2-mih8 lang5 thang choe3 lan2 e5 kan-cheng3?  Chu7-jian5 si7 khia7-khi2 ti7 hit si5-tai7 e5 lang5 thang choe3 lan2 e5 kan-cheng3.  In-ui7 hit si5-tai7 e5 lang5 chiah oe7 thang phoaN3-toan3 hit si5-tai7 e5 lek8-su2-tek e5 su7-sit8, i2-goa7 bo5 pat8 tiau5 lou7.  TaN lun7 I e5 Chhu3-lu2 kang3-tan3 e5 su7, lan2 chai hiah e5 khia7-khi2 ti7 hit si5-tai7 beh lai5 phoaN3-toan3 hit e5 cheng3-ku3 e5 lang5, si7 u7 chhim-sin3, sim7-chi3 soa3 sia2 hit e5 su7-sit8 ti7 in e5 chheh-nih8, lai5 chiaN5-choe3 u7 koan5-ui e5 chheh, kong2-khi2 in e5 Chu2 e5 kou3-su7.  Chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni, in khak-sit8 si7 u7 chhim-sin3, ma7 soa3 u7 sia2 beng5 chit e5 su7-sit8.
Ma2-thai3 kap Lou7-ka u7 seng5-jin7 in, put-ko3 si7 teh ki3-sut8 hit si5 e5 kau3-hoe7 e5 sin3-giong2, chiah u7 sia2 chit e5 Chhu3-lu2 kang3-tan3 e5 su7 ti7 in e5 Hok-im-su, soa3 ka7 in chhut-pan2, lai5 seng5-jin7 hiah e5 Hok-im-su si7 sit8-chai7 teh ki3-sit8 in e5 sin3-giong2 e5 chheh.  Lan2 kan-ta tui3 chit e5 sit8-cheng5, chiu7 i2-keng u7 kau3-giah8 e5 cheng3-ku3 ti7-teh.  Kho2-sioh lang5 choe7-choe7 si7 u7 hut-liok8 chit tiam2.  Che ki5-sit8 si7 u7 toa7 e5 chho-gou7 ti7-teh.  Lan2 na7 thak8 hit ho7 ti7-teh hoan2-tui3 Chhu3-lu2 kang3-tan3 e5 chheh liau2, kiam2-chhai2 oe7 siN-khi2 giau5-gi5 e5 sim, teh-beh siuN7 kong2, chaiN2-iuN7 kan-ta Ma2-thai3 kap Lou7-ka u7 kan-cheng3 chit e5 su7 na7-tiaN7, ia7 u7 si5 oe7 soa3 siuN7 kong2, in e5 chheh si7 kah na2 chhin-chhiuN7 teh sia2 in pun2-sin e5 hak8-soat, ng3-bang7 kau3-hoe7 thang ka7 in chiap-lap8.  Chhiat-chhiat ng3-bang7 lan2 bo5 u7 chit khoan2 e5 chho3-gou7 ti7-teh.  Lan2 tioh8 khak-sit8 chai, ki5-sit8 in put-ko3 si7 teh ki3-sut8 kau3-hoe7 e5 sin3-giong2 na7-tiaN7.  ChhiaN2 lan2 oe7 ki-tit e7-bin7 chit ku3 oe7: M7-si7 in-ui7 Chhu3-lu2 kang3-tan3 e5 su7-sit8 u7 ki3-chai3 ti7 Hok-im-su, sou2-i2 kau3-hoe7 chiah sin3.  Hoan2-tng2 si7 in-ui7 kau3-hoe7 u7 sin3 Chhu3-lu2 kang3-tan3 e5 su7-sit8, sou2-i2 in chiah u7 ki3-chai3 ti7 Hok-im-su.  Ti7 Ma2-thai3 kap Lou7-ka e5 poe3-au7 si7 u7 choan5 kau3-hoe7 ti7-teh.
Siat-su2 lan2 na7 sit8-chai7 oe7 ki3-tit i2-siong7 sou2 kong2 chit e5 sit8-cheng5, iah8 oe7 chiau3 lan2 e5 siong5-sek lai5 phoaN3-toan3, lan2 chiu7 khah m7-bian2 hui3-liau2 si5-kan lai5 siuN7, Ki-tok-tou5 sou2 teh hoai5-gi5, sou2 khoaN3 choe3 te7-it khun3-lan5 e5 bun7-toe5.  U7 Ki-tok-tou5 si7 bat teh pian7-pok kong2, thai3-tho2 Sin-iok ki5-thaN e5 tu3-chia2, tui3 I e5 Chhu3-lu2 kang3-tan3 e5 su7, long2 bo5 kan-cheng3 sim2-mih8?
Chit-tiap8, chhiaN2 iong5-un2 goa2 lai5 tho2-lun7 chit tiam2.  Lan2 chiam7-si5 ku2 m7-bian2 siuN7 hit khoan2 bo5 sin3-giong2 e5 lang5 e5 hoan2-tui3 e5 oe7.  Ki-tok-tou5 e5 tiong-kan u7 lang5 sou2 teh giau5-gi5, khoaN3 choe3 si7 te7-it thang chhiN-kiaN e5 khun3-lan5 e5 tiam2, chiu7-si7 kong2, Ma2-kho2 bo5 ki3-chai3 Chhu2-lu2 kang3-tan3 e5 su7-sit8, Iok-han7 ma7-si7 bo5.  Po2-lo5 ti7 i hiah-nih8 choe7 koan3 e5 phoe-sin3 e5 tiong-kan, lian5 chit8 tiuN ma7 bo5 teh kong2-khi2 chit e5 su7-sit8.  Che kiam2 m7-si7 teh am3-si7 lan2 chai, in si7 long2 bo5 sin3 I e5 Chhu3-lu2 kang3-tan3 e5 su7-sit8 mah?  U7-iaN2, lan2 na7-si7 bo5 chim-chiok siuN7, chit khoan2 e5 hoan2-tui3 e5 oe7, lan2 thiaN-liau2 si7 chhin-chhiuN7 chin thang chhiN-kiaN e5 khoan2.
Te7-it tai7-seng ai3 lan2 beng5-beng5 oe7 ki3-tit e5, chiu7-si7 kau3-hoe7 u7 chiap-lap8 Ma2-thai3 kap Lou7-ka e5 Hok-im-su, u7 seng5-jin7 in e5 Hok-im-su si7 sit8-chai7 teh ki3-sut8 in e5 sin3-giong2 e5 chheh, sou2-i2 tui3 chit e5 sit8-cheng5 lan2 thang chai, ti7 tak8 sou2-chai7 e5 Ki-tok-tou5, si7 long2 u7 sin3 I e5 Chhu2-lu2 kang3-tan3 e5 su7-sit8.  Na7-si7 an2-ni, Ma2-kho2 an3-choaN2 bo5 ki3-chai3?  Lan2 na7 hian-khui Ma2-kho2 e5 chheh, chiu7 chai i e5 toa7 bok8-tek, si7 chi2-u7 teh kong2-khi2 Ia5-sou e5 kong seng-gai5 na7-tiaN7.  Li2 khoaN3!  Ma2-kho2 tui3 thau5 chiu7-si7 kong2-khi2 Ia5-sou e5 Soe2-le2, i2-kip8 I ti7 Ka-li7-li7 thoan5-to7 e5 su7.  Ma2-kho2 si7 koat-toan3 bo5 kong2-khi2 khah cha2 e5 sim2-mih8 siau-sit.  Chong2-si7 lun7 Lou7-ka e5 bok8-tek, si7 chaiN2-iuN7?  Tu2-tu2 si7 chiau3 i pun2-sin sou2 kan-cheng3 e5 kong2, i si7 beh kan-cheng3 i e5 Chu2 “tui3 khi2-thau5 long2-chong2 e5 su7.”  Che chiu7-si7 kap Ma2-kho2 u7 toa7-toa7 koh-iuN7 e5 sou2-chai7.  Ki5-sit8 Ma2-kho2 si7 bo5 beh tui3 hit e5 siang7 khi2-thau5 kau3 ti7 siang7 lou7-be2 e5 su7-sit8, sui5 chit8 hang7 lai5 kan-cheng3 Ki-tok e5 choan5 seng-oah8.
TaN Iok-han7 siaN2-su7 bo5 kong2-khi2?  Lan2 m7-chai.  Chong2-si7 lan2 tioh8 oe7 ki3-tit, i khak-sit8 si7 u7 siong5-siong5 teh thak8 Ma2-thai3, i2-kip8 Lou7-ka e5 Hok-im-su, ia7 i ma7-si7 chai tong-si5 e5 kau3-hoe7 to long2 u7 chiap-lap8 I e5 Chhu3-lu2 kang3-tan3 e5 su7-sit8, iu7-koh i e5 bok8-tek chi2-u7 si7 beh pou2-chhiong ki5-u5 e5 Hok-im-su, chiah lai5 giah8 pit lai5 sia2 pat8 lang5 sou2 bo5 sia2-tioh8 e5 su7-sit8.  Chit tiam2 lan2 si7 i2-keng kong2 liau2.  Siat-su2 na7-si7 kong2 an2-ni, iau2 be7 u7 thang choe3 chap8-hun e5 in3-tap, chhiaN2 lan2 koh chu3-i3 chit8 hang7.  Iok-han7 chiu7-si7 tui3 thiN-nih8 e5 hong-bin7, m7-si7 tui3 toe7-nih8 e5 hong-bin7, lai5 teh khoaN3 Ki-tok e5 chhut-si3.  I khiok-si7 iu5-goan5 u7 teh ki3-chai3 Ki-tok e5 chhut-si3, put-ko3 i si7 bo5 kong2-khi2 Ia5-sou Ki-tok u7 chhut-si3 ti7 Iu5-thai3 e5 Pek-li7-heng5, hoan2-tng2 si7 u7 kong2, Ia5-sou u7 chaiN2-iuN7 tui3 hit e5 khah koaiN5 e5 se3-kai3, lai5 chhut-si3 ti7 chit e5 se3-kan.  Che chiu7-si7 i e5 thau5-su7 sou2 teh kang2-lun7 Ki-tok e5 chhut-si3 e5, ki5-sit8 tu2-tu2 si7 kap Ma2-thai3 i2-kip8 Lou7-ka e5 thau5-su7 saN it-ti3 ti7-teh.  Iok-han7 u7 kong2, “Ti7 khi2-thau5 u7 To7, To7 si7 kap Siong7-te3 saN-kap ti7-teh, To7 chiu7-si7 Siong7-te3…To7 u7 chiaN5 jiok8-the2 khia7-khi2 ti7 lan2 tiong-kan, koh goan2 bat khoaN3-kiN3 I e5 eng5-kng.”  Lan2 tui3 chit ku3 oe7, kiam2 thang kong2 Iok-han7 si7 chhin-chhiuN7 u7 teh hoan2-tui3 tong-si5 e5 kau3-hoe7 e5 sin3-giong2 mah?
Ia7 Po2-lo5 si7 an3-choaN2?  Kho2-sioh choe7-choe7 lang5 long2 boe7 ki3-tit thang siuN7 kong2, lun7 Ki-tok e5 seng-gai5 e5 su7, to si7 i i2-kip8 cheng3 su3-tou5 tak8-jit8 sou2 teh soat-kau3 e5, siaN2-su7 choan5-jian5 bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 Po2-lo5 u7 sia2 Ki-tok-toan7 le3?  Ki5-sit8 Po2-lo5 tui3 Ki-tok e5 seng-gai5 si7 u7 i e5 tiaN7-tioh8 e5 phiau-chun2 ti7-teh.  I chheng-ho7 chit e5 phiau-chun2 kong2, si7 “Goa2 e5 hok-im.”  Chhin-chhiuN7 u7 thoan5 kong2, “Lin2 tioh8 oe7 ki3-tit tui3 Tai7-pit8 e5 hou7-e3 sou2 chhut e5 Ia5-sou Ki-tok, I tui3 si2-lang5 tiong koh-oah8, tu2-tu2 chiau3 goa2 e5 hok-im.”
I tak8-jit8 to long2 si7 teh thoan5 hit e5 Hok-im, Ki-tok e5 seng-gai5, iau2 ku2 lan2 long2 bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 i u7 giah8 pit lai5 sia2 I e5 toan7-ki3.  sou2-i2 lan2 thang siuN, i teh soat-kau3 e5 tiong-kan, si7 long2 m7-bat thoan5 Chhu3-lu2 kang3-tan3 e5 to7-li2.  Che si7 bo5 thang giau5-gi5 e5 su7.  Chong2-si7 ti7 chia iau2 u7 chit8-hang7 chin tiong7-iau3, chin tu3-hian7 e5 su7-sit8, lan2 tioh8 oe7 ki3-tit.  Sui-jian5 Po2-lo5 si7 bo5 sia2 i e5 Hok-im-su, iau2 ku2 Po2-lo5 e5 hak8-seng, i sou2 chhin-bit8 e5 tang5-phoaN7 Lou7-ka, tng kap Po2-lo5 choe3-tin7 e5 si5, u7 sia2 chit8 pun2 Hok-im-su.  Lou7-ka kap Po2-lo5 tai7-ke saN chhin-bit8 teh kau-poe5 e5 hit kui2-ni5 e5 tiong-kan, i u7 nng7 koan3 e5 goan5-ko2 ti7-teh.  Chit8 koan3 si7 Po2-lo5 e5 thoan5-to7 e5 lu2-heng5 ki3, chiu7-si7 au7-lai5 i u7 chhut-pan2 chiaN5-choe3 Su3-tou5 Heng7-toan7.  Koh chit8 koan3, si7 koh khah po2-poe3, tiong7-iau3 e5, chiu7-si7 i ti7 au7-lai5 u7 chhut-pan2, chiaN5-choe3 i e5 Chu2 e5 toan7-ki3.  Lan2 thang sin3, Po2-lo5 u7 keng2-soan2 i lai5 choe3 hit e5 kang; ia7 thang sin3, Po2-lo5 u7 pang-chan7 Lou7-ka, u7 kap i saN-kap choe3 hit e5 kang; ia7 lan2 ma7-si7 chai chit-pun2 Hok-im-su u7 hian2-chhut Po2-lo5 e5 ka3-si7 ti7-teh.  Sou2-i2 chhou-tai7 kau3-hoe7 u7 chheng-hou chit-pun2 kio3-choe3 si7 Po2-lo5 e5 Hok-im-su.  Ti7-chia u7 te7-ji7 se3-ki2 nng7-ui7 e5 kau3-hu7, sou2 kan-cheng e5 oe7; chit8 ui7 si7 Gou2-luh (Gaul) e5 I5-le5-ni5 (Irenaeus), u7 kong2, “Lou7-ka u7 chiong Po2-lo5 sou2 thoan5 e5 Hok-im lai5 ki3-chai3 ti7 chheh-nih8;” koh chit8 ui7 si7 A-hui-li7-ka e5 Tek-to7-liong5 (Tertullian) u7 kong2, “Lou7-ka e5 lui7-piat khah siong5 si7 than3 Po2-lo5 e5.”  ChhiaN2 lan2 tioh8 oe7 ki3-tit, chit pun2 Lou7-ka Hok-im-su, chiu7-si7 tek8-piat8 u7 tui3-tiong7 Ia5-sou e5 Chhu3-lu2 kang3-tan3 e5 su7-sit!
Lan2 tui3 i2-siong7 sou2 kong2 e5 sit8-cheng5 lai5 khoaN3, thang chai sui-jian5 cheng3 phoe-sin3 e5 tiong-kan, long2 tiam7-tiam7 bo5 kong2-khi2 Chhu3-lu2 kang3-tan3 e5 su7-sit8, ma7 m7-si7 tiong7-iau3 e5 bun7-toe5.  Cheng3 phoe-sin3 si7 khah han2-tit lun7-khi2 Ki-tok e5 seng-gai5, in-ui7 cheng3 phoe-sin3 long2 si7 ui7-tioh8 tek8-piat8 e5 su7-iu5, teh gi7-lun7 ti7 hit-si5 tek8-piat8 hoat-seng e5 bun7-toe5, lai5 sia2 e5 tek8-piat8 e5 chheh.  Lun7 I e5 Chhu3-lu2 kang3-tan3 e5 su7, si7 beng5-beng5 long2 m7-bat choe3 bun7-toe5 hou7 lang5 teh gi7-lun7.  Sou2-i2 Po2-lo5 chiah long2 bo5 kong2-khi2 chit e5 su7-sit8.
I2-siong7 lan2 i2-keng kong2-khi2 Ki-tok-tou5 e5 hoai5-gi5-chia2, sou2 khoaN3 choe3 si7 te7-it khun3-lan5 e5 tiam2, chiu7-si7 lun7-khi2 Sin-iok Seng3-chheh khah choe7 e5 tu3-chia2 long2 si7 tiam7-tiam7 bo5 kong2-khi2 e5 su7.  Chhi3 mng7, che u7 kau3-giah8 ui5-hiam2 thang io5-choah lan2 e5 Seng3-keng mah?  Bian2 kong2 hiah e5 bo5 sin3-giong2 e5 lang5, si7 ai3 kan2-liok8 it-chhe3 e5 bun7-toe5, kong2, “Chhu3-lu2 kang3-tan3 si7 ti7 jin5-lui7 keng-giam7 tiong be7 bat tu2-tioh8 e5 su7.”  Chun2-choe3 u7 iaN2 lai5 kong2, Ki-tok ma7-si7 bo5 siong5-siong5 chhut-si3.  Seng3-chheh sou2 chu2-tiuN e5 si7 kong2, nng7 hang7 piN5-piN5 si7 siang7-si5 sou2 hoat-seng e5 su7-sit8; ia7 nng7 hang7 su7-sit8 si7 saN kiat-lian5 ti7-teh.  Chit ho7 oe7 khiok si7 boe7 thang tit-tioh8 hit ho7 bo5 sin3-giong2 e5 lang5 hoaN-hi2 thiaN, chong2-si7 che si7 u7 khui3-lat8 thang phah-phoa3 kap Ki-tok-tou5 sou2 beh saN cheng-pian7 e5 tiam2.  Lan2 si7 bo5 beh hit ho7 bo5 sin3-sim e5 lang5 saN-kap pian7-lun7.  In-ui7 lang5 na7 bo5 sin3 Ki-tok si7 Sin5, chu7-jian5 chit e5 bun7-toe5 chai7 i teh khoaN3, si7 bo5 i3-su3, si7 boe7 thang sin3 tit e5 su7.
TaN choe3-au7 lan2 ai3 lai5 kong2-khi2, bo5 po2-siu2 chit e5 ka3-si7 ti7 lan2 Ki-tok-tou5 e5 sin3-giong2 e5 lai7-bin7, si7 boe7 eng7-tit e5 li2-iu5.  U7 Ki-tok-tou5, khiok-si7 kek8 sio2-sou3 bat teh iau3-kiu5 kong2, lan2 tioh8 tui3 lan2 e5 Sin3-keng lai5 san-tu5 chit ku3, “I tui3 Seng3 Sin5 e5 koan5--leng5 tau5-thai, tui3 chai7-sek-lu2 Ma2-li7-a chhut-si3” e5 oe7 khi2-lai5, ng3-bang7 oe7 thang hou7 hiah e5 seng5-sit8 teh giau5-gi5 e5 lang5 khah peng5-an.
Lun7 khi2 lang5 ai3 giau5-gi5 I e5 Chhu3-lu2 kang3-tan3 e5 su7, khiok m7-si7 kun7-tai7 sin-sin e5 tai7-chi3.  Chit khoan2 giau5-gi5 sng3-si7 chu7 cha2-cha2 siat-lip8 kau3-hoe7 e5 si5, chiu7 i2-keng u7 lah.  Chhin-chhiuN7 chu7 cha2-cha2 chiu7 i2-keng u7 chit8 e5 iN7-toan-chia2, kio3-choe3 Khe2-lin2-sah-suh (Cerinthus), chiu7-si7 Iok-han7 sou2 teh kong-kek e5, i si7 i2-keng u7 teh giau5-gi5 chit tiam2.  Ji5-hou7 ti7 tak8 si5-tai7 ma7-si7 siong5-siong5 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 hit ho7 lang5 ti7-teh.  Hian7-kim chu7-jian5 ma7-si7 u7 nou3!  Put-ko3 ti7 chit tiong-kan u7 chit8 hang7 cheng-chha ti7-teh.  Cha2-cheng5 long2 si7 kau3-hoe7 goa7 e5 lang5, long2 si7 hiah e5 bo5 sin3 Ki-tok si7 Sin5 e5 lang5, ti7 teh giau5-gi5 pian7-pok I e5 Chhu3-lu2 kang3-tan3 e5 su7-sit8.  Sou2-i2 Ki-tok e5 Sin5-seng3 kap I e5 Chhu3-lu2 kang3-tan3 e5 su7-sit8, in long2 si7 saN-lian5 choe3-he2 teh pian7-pok.  In na7 m7-si7 piN5-piN5 chiap-lap8, chiu7-si7 piN5-piN5 ku7-choat8.  Chong2-si7 hian7-kim si7 khah ai3 pun-khui lai5 siuN7.  U7 e5 lang5 chit8-bin7 si7 u7 sin3 Ki-tok si7 Sin5, iah8 chit8-bin7 si7 chu2-chhiong3 Chhu2-lu2 kang3-tan3 e5 su5, si7 tioh8 pang3 he7 teh, khoaN3 choe3 si7 boe7 thang kai2-koat e5 bun7-toe5.
Chit khoan2 chhin-chhiat e5 ke3-bou5, choan-choan si7 ui7-tioh8 thiaN3-thang3 hoai5-gi5-chia2, chiah lai5 siuN7 e5, si7 ng3-bang7 Ki-tok-tou5 e5 sin5-keng hou7 lang5 khah khoai3 thang sin3.  Ki5-sit8 che si7 boe7-oe7 e5 su7.  Ki-tok-tou5 e5 Sin3-keng si7 koat-toan3 boe7 thang chhong3 hou7 i khah iong5-iN7 sin3.  In-ui7 Ki-tok-tou5 sou2 sin3 e5, chiu7-si7 choan5 u2-tiu7 kan choe3 te7-it thang chhiN-kiaN, ui5-lan5 sin3 e5 su7, chiu7-si7 sin3 kong2, Siong7-te3 u7 chiaN5-choe3 lang5!  To7 u7 chiaN5 jiok8-the2!
Lan2 ai3 lan2 e5 Sin3-keng, hou7 lang5 khah khoai3 thang sin3!  Boe7 lah!  Lan2 sou2 khoa3-lu7 e5, si7 hit ho7 chhin-chhiat e5 ke3-bou5, m7-si7 oe7 hou7 lang5 khah khoai3 sin3 lan2 e5 Sin3-keng, hoan2-tng2 si7 oe7 hou7 lang5 tu2-tioh8 koh khah oh-tit e5 bun7-toe5.  In-ui7 na7 an2-ni, au7-lai5 tek-khak beh u7 choe7-choe7 su-siuN2 ka koh gi7-lun7 kong2, chaiN2-iuN7 Siong7-te3 oe7 chiaN5-choe3 lang5?  Hoan7-na7 u7 chhim-tim5 e5 su-siuN2-ka tiaN7-tioh8 si7 oe7 tu2-tioh8 chit ho7 e5 bun7-toe5, ia7 soa3 ai3 chhut-lat8 chhi3-khoaN3 oe7-thang kai2-koat i boe7.  Chhin-chhiuN7 kou2-cha2 u7 chit8 e5 iN7-toan-chia2, si7 m7-jin7 Chhu3-lu2 kang3-tan3 e5 su7, ia7 i u7 chin7 sou2 oe7 e5 khui3-lat8 lai5 chhi3-khoaN3, siuN7 kong2, “Ti7 thiN-nih8 e5 Ki-tok, ti7 Kai-sat The5-pi2-liu5 e5 chap8-gou7 ni5, u7 tui3 hit e5 koaiN5-koaiN5 e5 sou2-chai7 loh8-lai5, chiong pun2-sin kap hit si5 oa2 saN-chap8 he3 e5 toe7-nih8 e5 Ia5-sou kiat-lian5 chiaN5-choe3 chit-the2.”  Chhin-chhiuN7 chit khoan2 e5 siat-siong2, beh lai5 pou2-chhiong Chhu3-lu2 kang3-tan3 e5 su7, lan2 siuN7 siaN2 khoan2?  Che si7 in choe3-sian7 e5 sou2-choe3, i2-goa7 u7 choe7-choe7 iN7-toan-chia2 u7 chhut-lat8 teh chhi3-khoaN3, chong2-si7 bo5 u7 khah ho2 e5 kai2-soat.  Chhi3-siuN7, kiam2 iau2 u7 sim2-mih8 khah ho2 e5 hoat-tou7 thang lai5 kan-cheng3 hou7 lang5 chit8-bin7 oe7 thang sin3 Ki-tok e5 Hoa3-sin, ia7 koh chit8-bin7 oe7 thang hui-jin7 I e5 Chhu3-lu2 kang3-tan3 e5 su7-sit8.  Chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni, lan2 teh kong2-khi2 ai3 chiong Sin3-keng chhong3 hou7 iong5-iN7 thang sin3, che ki5-sit8 si7 bo5 i3-gi7 e5 oe7.
Lan2 u7 thiaN-kiN3 lang5 teh kong2, sui-jian5 Ia5-sou sit8-chai7 si7 Iok-sek kap Ma2-li7-a lai5 siN e5 KiaN2, eng7 an2-ni, Siong7-te3 ma7-si7 oe7 thang lai5 oan5-seng5 I e5 Hoa3-sin e5 su7-giap8.  Chun2 choe3 u7-iaN2 lai5 kong2, chai7 Siong7-te3 khiok-si7 bo5 sou2 m7-oe7.  Chong2-si7 chit e5 Chhu3-lu2 kang3-tan3 e5 su7-sit8, to u7 lang5 teh choe3 cheng3, an3 choaN2-iuN7 lan2 kong2 boe7?  Chai7 Siong7-te3 che ma7-si7 iong5-iN7, thang eng7 an2-ni lai5 oan5-seng5 I e5 Hoa3-sin e5 su7-giap8.  Chong2-si7 chai7 lan2 che kiam2-si7 piN5-piN5 iong5-iN7 thang sin3 e5 su7 mah?  Goa2 teh ki5-koai3, an3-choaN2 lan2 ai3 ka-ki7 chhui-chhek Siong7-te3 e5 i3-su3?  Iah8 an3-choaN2 bo5 beh chiap-lap8 kau3-hoe7 i2-kip8 Seng3-chheh sou2 chu2-tiuN Siong7-te3 sou2 u7 choe3 e5 su7 mah?  Chhin-chhiuN7 so2-si5 e5 ho5-hap8 ti7 so2 e5 khoan2-sit, I e5 Chhu3-lu2 kang3-tan3 si7 u7 ho5-hap8 ti7 I e5 Hoa3-sin e5 su7-sit8, an3-choaN2 lan2 m7 sin3 mah?
Toan3-toan3 m7-thang!  Ki5-sit8 chit nng7 e5 kau3-li2, i e5 chun5-bong5 tiaN7-tioh8 si7 saN kiat-lian5.  Lan2 u7 keng-giam7-tioh8 choe7-choe7 e5 su7-sit8, long2 si7 piau2-si7 an2-ni.  In2 chit8 e5 le7 lai5 kong2, Tek-kok u7 chit8-ui7 Sin5-hak8-ka, i u7 ka3-si7 hak8-seng, chit8-bin7 sin3 Hoa3-sin e5 to7-li2, iah8 koh chit8-bin7 hui-jin7 Chhu3-lu2 kang3-tan3 e5 su7-sit8.  Chong2-si7 kiat-kiok8 hiah e5 hak8-seng, na7 m7-si7 piN5-piN5 po2-siu2 chit nng7 tiau5 e5 to7-li2, chiu7-si7 piN5-piN5 pang3-sak.  Chit8-peng5 e5 lang5 si7 na2 chin3-jip8 ti7 chhim e5 sou2-chai7, lai5 liau2-kai2 Ki-tok si7 Sin5, sim-lai7 tit-tioh8 toa7 e5 chhui-pek lai5 po2-siu2 I e5 Chhu3-lu2 kang3-tan3 e5 su7-sit8.  Koh chit8-peng5 e5 lang5 si7 piN5-piN5 ku7-choat8 chit nng7 tiau5 e5 to7-li2, soa3 chiaN5-choe3 chit8 e5 I5-it-sin5-lun7-chia2 (Unitanian).
Che si7 choe7-choe7 keng-giam7, sou2 u7 chi2-si7 lan2 chai e5 kiat-lun7.  Nng7 tiau5 e5 to7-li2, si7 kiaN5 siang7 tiau5 e5 un7-mia7.  Sou2-i2 lang5 na7 ai3 kian3-siat hit ho7 chiat-thiong e5 sin3-giong2, khng3 chiat-thiong e5 thai3-tou7, beh lai5 su-siuN2 Ki-tok-kau3, si7 hoan2-tng2 hou7 i piN3-choe3 bo5 lat8 e5 chong-kau3, koh ia7-si7 put-chi2 bo5 tho3-tong3 e5 hoat-tou7.
Chit-tiap8 ai3 lan2 m7-bian2 koh gi7-lun7 koan-he7 lan2 e5 Chu2 e5 hak8-soat, chhiaN2 saN-kap lai5 siuN7, lan2 sou2 thiaN3 e5 Chu2 e5 jin5-keh.  ChhiaN2 lan2 eng7 ki5-iN7 kap keng3-ui3 e5 liam7-thau5 lai5 siuN7 I e5 Hoa3-sin e5 o3-biau7 e5 to7-li2, chiu7-si7 kong2, To7 u7 chiaN5 jiok8-the2!  Siong7-te3 u7 chiaN5-choe3 lang5!  Hit e5 bat aN3-loh8 lai5 thiaN3 lan2, ia7 lan2 iu5-goan5 u7 thiaN3 I e5, chiu7-si7 Ki-tok, si7 Siong7-te3 e5 Eng2-oan2 e5 Seng3 KiaN2, si7 tui3 kou2-cha2 i2-lai5 pun2-u7 e5, chiap8-chiap8 tu3-hian7.  Chhi3-siuN7, chu7 cha2 sou2 keng-giam7 e5 Kiu3-chu2-tan3, tak8-pai2 na7 siuN7-tioh8 Ki-tok u7 chhut-si3 lai5 choe3 eN-a2, hit si5 ti7 hit e5 tan-sun5 e5 sin3-giong2 e5 lai7-tiong, kiam2 m7-si7 u7 khoai3-lok8 kap peng5-an ti7-teh mah?  Ke3-khi3 bo5 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 sim2-mih8, ti7 chiong-lai5 ma7-si7 bo5 u7 sim2-mih8 oe7-thang khi2-lai5 io5-choah chit e5 su7-sit8.  Nng7 chheng ni5 ku2, kau3-hoe7 sou2 kan-cheng3 e5, iu7-koh kau3-hoe7 eng2-oan2 sou2 beh soa3-chiap lai5 kan-cheng3 e5, chiu7-si7 kong2, “Goa2 sin3 I tok8-siN e5 KiaN2, lan2 e5 Chu2 Ia5-sou Ki-tok.  I tui3 Seng3 Sin5 e5 koan5-leng5 tau5-thai, tui3 chai7-sek-lu2 Ma2-li7-a chhut-si3.”



Te7-3 chiuN	Iu3-Lian5

	Lan2 tiong-kan choe7-choe7 lang5 ti7-teh thak8 sim2-mih8 ui2-jin5 e5 toan7-ki3 e5 si5, te7-it oe7 giu2 lan2 e5 sim e5 pou7-hun7, chiu7-si7 lun7 in iu3-lian5 e5 kou3-su7, choe3 gin2-na2 si5-tai7 bo5 sia5-khi3 e5 han5-tam5, ti7-teh toa7-han3 e5 tiong-kan e5 chu7-jian5, bo5 i3-sek e5 tam5-lun7, in e5 thau5-nau2 e5 hoat-tat8, i2-kip8 in e5 seng-oah8 chiong2-chiong2 e5 khoan2-sit8; in-ui7 lan2 ai3 tui3 ti7 hit e5 tiong-kan lai5 khoaN3 chhut in chiong-lai5 chiaN5-choe3 ui2-tai7 e5 tiau7-thau5.
	Lan2 siong5-siong5 ki5-koai3, soa3 sit-bang7 Hok-im-su thai3 oe7 long2 bo5 kong2-khi2 lan2 e5 Chu2 e5 iu3-lian5 e5 kou3-su7.  Kiam2-si7 chiah e5 Hok-im-su tu3-chia2 m7-chai-iaN2 mah?  An3-choaN2 I e5 lau7-bu2 Ma2-li7-a, to u7 kong2-khi2 I chhut-si3 e5 kou3-su7, thai3 oe7 bo5 iu5-goan5 tui3 lang5 kong2-khi2 I iu3-lian5 e5 su7-cheng5 mah?  Kiam2-chhai2 u7, ia7 ku2 kaN2, iah8 i tang5-chng e5 peng5-iu2, in-ui7 khah koan-sim ti7 in pun2-sin e5 soe3-kiaN2, soa3 boe7 ki3-tit thang thoan5 lan2 e5 Chu2 iu3-lian5 e5 su7-cheng5.  Iau2-ku2 khah toa7-bin7 si7 bo5 chiah tioh8.  In-ui7 cheng3 Hok-im-su, chiap8-chiap8 piau2-si7, Ma2-li7-a si7 kan-ta teh koan-chhat, teh kiaN-hiaN5, teh sam3-su chit e5 eN-a2 e5 chhut-si3 na7-tiaN7.  In u7 piau2-beng5 Ma2-li7-a si7 thiam5-cheng7, koaN2-gian5 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5, ti7 am3-am3 e5 tiong-kan, eng7 thiaN3-sim kap keng3-ui3 e5 liam7-thau5, lai5 teh sam3-su i hit e5 o3-biau7 e5 soe3-kiaN2, teh siuN7 Ia5-sou e5 ki5-chek-tek e5 chhut-si3; Tui3 an2-ni, u7 siN-khi2 chong3-giam5 e5 sim, m7-kaN2 lam7-sam2 kong2-khi2, put-ko3 chai ti7 Ia5-sou e5 thau5-cheng5, sou2 an-pai5 hit e5 koaiN5-koaiN5 e5 thian-hun7; chong2-si7 m7-chai tioh8 chaiN2-iuN7 I chiah oe7 thang oan5-seng5, tui3 an2-ni, sim-lai7 siong5-siong5 u7 ju5-loan7.  Ma2-li7-a u7 beng5-beng5 chai sou2 u7 tu2-tioh8 e5, si7 chin ki5-iN7 e5 su7, chhut-lat8 teh liau7-siong2, ng3-bang7 oe7 thang chiau3 i sou2 siuN7 e5 khoan2, na2 siuN7 na2 ki5-koai5, soa3 tiam7-tiam7 long2 bo5 kong2-khi2 sim2-mih8.  “Ma2-li7-a chiong chiah e5 oe7 ki3 tiau5-tiau5, siong5-siong5 teh siuN7.”  Chong2-si7 put-lun7 siaN2 khoan2, chiau3 khoaN3, lun7 lan2 e5 Chu2 e5 iu3-lian5 e5 su7, Ma2-li7-a si7 bo5 kong2 kau3 loa7 choe7.
	Lan2 chit-tiap8 boe7 bian2-tit ki5-koai3, ai3 lai5 siuN7 Ma2-li7-a ti7 khi2-thau5 m7-chai an3-choaN2 lai5 teh khoan2-thai7 Ia5-sou?  Ma2-li7-a kiam2 u7 phah-sng3 i e5 soe3-kiaN2 Ia5-sou si7 Sin5, si7 Siong7-te3 e5 Eng2-oan2 e5 KiaN2 mah?
	Chiau3 Hok-im-su sou2 ki3, si7 boe7 thang hou7 lan2 siuN7 Ma2-li7-a u7 jin7 Ia5-sou si7 Sin5.  Lan2 e5 li2-seng3 iu5-goan5 m7 iong5-un2 an2-ni.  In-ui7 Ma2-li7-a na7-si7 tui3 khi2-thau5 chiu7 u7 jin7 Ia5-sou si7 Sin5, an3-choaN2 Ia5-sou oe7 thang chhin-chhiuN7 chit8 e5 chu7-jian5 lang5 e5 gin2-na2, lai5 chin3-pou7 I tak8 hang7 e5 seng-oah8, hang5-hok8 ti7 I e5 pe7-bu2, ti3-hui7 kap sin-khu chiam7-chiam7 toa7, chhin-chhiuN7 ki5-u5 e5 gin2-na2 chit8 poaN, lai5 hou7 Siong7-te3 kap lang5 na2 thiaN3 I?  An3-choaN2 Ma2-li7-a oe7 thang in-ui7 Ia5-sou ian5-chhian5 ti7 Seng3-tian7, chiu7 ti7 cheng3 phok-su7 e5 bin7-cheng5 kaN2 lai5 chek-pi7 I mah?  An3-choaN2 Ma2-li7-a oe7 thang choan5-jian5 khoaN3-choe3 si7 i ka-ki7 e5 soe3-kiaN2 lai5 khoan2-thai7 I mah?  Na7-si7 lang5 i2-keng chai-iaN2 Ia5-sou si7 Sin5, tak8 e5 lang5 ti7 sim-lai7 tek-khak oe7 put-chi2 chhiN-kiaN, m7-kaN2 khoan2-thai7 I chhin-chhiuN7 chit8 e5 lang5.  Ia5-sou e5 ka-teng5 seng-oah8 si7 put-kho2-leng5, put-kho2 kai2 e5 su7.  I e5 Hoa3-sin e5 bok8-tek, un2-tang3 si7 kui ti7 khang-khang; in-ui7 I tek-khak tioh8 chiaN5-choe3 “Chin-sit8” e5 lang5, lai5 chiam7-chiam7 tiong2-toa7 ti7 I e5 jin5-keh-tek e5 seng-oah8.
	Bo5 lah!  Ma2-li7-a bo5 phah-sng3 Ia5-sou si7 Sin5.  Ma2-li7-a kan-ta u7 teh phah-sng3 Ia5-sou si7 hit e5 sou2 iok-sok beh lai5 e5 Bi2-sai3-a, m7-ku2 Iu5-thai3 lang5 lun7 Bi2-sai3-a e5 koan-liam7 si7 kek8-ki5 bo5 beng5.  Ma2-li7-a chai, Ia5-sou e5 ki5-chek-tek e5 chhut-si3, si7 piau2-beng5 I si7 u7 kap lang5 khah koh-iuN7.  Iau2-ku2 ti7 chit-tiap8, Ma2-li7-a si7 be7 liau2-kai2 Ia-sou si7 Sin5.  Chit e5 toa7 e5 pi3-bit8 e5 i3-su3, chi2-u7 kau3 ti7 khah au7-lai5 i chiah u7 liau2-kai2.
	Lian5 cheng3 hak8-seng iau2-be7 kun7 ti7 Ia5-sou e5 lim5-chiong e5 si5, to iu5-goan5 bo5 liau2-kai2 Ia5-sou si7 Sin5.  Chha-put-to thang kong2, ti7 I e5 choan5 seng-gai5 u7 kham3-bat8 I e5 Sin5-seng3.  In-ui7 tioh8 an2-ni, Ia5-sou chiah oe7 thang chiau3 lang5 e5 keng-giam7 lai5 tiong2-toa7, cheng3-lang5 thang ho2-taN2 khoan2-thai7 I, choe3 peng5-iu2 lai5 bat I, ia7 Pi2-tek chiah kaN2 oa2 lai5 chit-bun7 I, IOk-han7 lai5 khoa3 thau5-khak ti7 I e5 heng-cheng5, koh-chai3 soe3-han3 gin2-na2 chiah thang hong3-sim lai5 hou7 I pho7, cheng3 thiu-hiong3 e5, i2-kip8 chhiong-ki chiah thang lai5 kap I kong2-oe7, lai5 tit-tioh8 chong3-taN2.  Siat-su2 in tai7-ke na7 i2-keng liau2-kai2 Ia5-sou si7 Sin5, si7 Siong7-te3, i2-siong7 sou2 kong2 chiah e5 su7, beh thai3 oe7 ne3?
	Lan2 u7 khoaN3-kiN3, tng ti7 Ia5-sou na2 pek-kun7 ti7 lim5-chiong e5 si5, I u7 chiam7-chiam7 hian2-chhut I e5 Sin5-seng3 e5 pi3-bit8.  Lan2 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 ti7 cheng3 su3-tou5 e5 tiong-kan, chiam7-chiam7 u7 siN-khi2 ki5-iN7 kap kiaN-ui3 e5 liam7-thau5, lai5 teh su-siong2 I.  Lan2 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 in u7 siong5-siong5 chhiN-kiaN, chiap-chhiok--tioh8 hit e5 chin-li2 e5 chit8-sut-a2 e5 kng, ia7 soa3 siu7 chou2-chi2, m7-ai3 in kong2-khi2.  Chong2-si7 ki5-sit8 kau3 ti7 I koh-oah8 au7, Seng-thian kau3 ti7 I e5 eng5-kng e5 sou2-chai7, koh hit e5 iok-sok e5 Seng3 Sin5 lim5-kau3 liau2, hit-si5 in chiah u7 chap8-hun liau2-kai2 chit e5 thang chhiN-kiaN e5 o3-biau7 e5 i3-gi7.  Hit-si5 in chiah oat8-lin3-tng2 lai5 hoe5-siong2 kap I saN-kap kau-poe5 hit saN ni5 ku2 e5 ki3-ek, soa3 ki5-koai3 hit-si5 in e5 bak8-chiu thai3 oe7 hiah-nih8 hoe, be7 hiau2-tit in hian7-si5 sou2 bat e5 to7-li2, chiu7-si7 kong2, “To7 chiaN5 jiok8-the2, khia7-khi2 ti7 lan2 tiong-kan, u7 un-tian2 kap chin-li2 moa2-moa2.  Koh goan2 bat khoaN3-kiN3 I e5 eng5-kng, chhin-chhiuN7 Tok8-siN KiaN2, tui3 Pe7 sou2 tit e5 eng5-kng.”
	lan2 kiam2 thang eng7 kiaN-ui3 kap kin2-sin7 e5 thai3-tou7 lai5 koh chin3 chit8 pou7 mah?  Lan2 si7 khia7 ti7 seng3 e5 toe7, ti7 lan2 e5 bin7-cheng5 u7 choe7-choe7 eng2-oan2 e5 o3-biau7 ti7-teh.  Chong2-si7 lan2 boe7 jim2-tit bo5 lai5 su-siong2 I e5 cheng5-keng2.  Lan2 ai3 chin7 lan2 e5 khui3-lat8 lai5 siong2-siong7 I.  Chit e5 Sin5-tong5 tui3 I pun2-sin e5 i3-sek si7 siaN2 khoan2?
	Tioh8 oe7 ki3-tit, lan2 m7-thang kan-ta sin3 I e5 Sin5-seng3, ia7 tioh8 sin3 I e5 jin5-seng3.  In-ui7 Ia5-sou Ki-tok u7 chiaN5-choe3 “Chin-sit8” e5 lang5, tu5-khi2 ti7 lan2 sou2 u7 e5 gu5-chhun2, u-khu, i2-kip8 choe7-ok, i2-goa7 it-chhe3, I si7 long2 kap lan2 sio-siang7.  Ia5-sou choe3 gin2-na2 si7 choe3 jin5-lui7 e5 chit8 e5 gin2-na2.  Lan2 teh ki5-koai3, m7-chai kau3 ti7-si5 Ia5-sou chiah khi2-thau5 lai5 hian2-beng5 I sou2 u7 e5 khah ko-siong7 e5 i3-sek?  Kau3 ti7 si5 I chiah u7 kam2-kak--tioh8 ti7 I e5 sim-lai7 sou2 u7 hit e5 be7 thang kong2-chhut e5 chhim-chhim e5 leng5-kai3 e5 i3-sek?  Siong5-siong5 ti7 I e5 gin2-na2 sim e5 ki5-to2 e5 si5, u7 tit-tioh8 chit8-sut-a2 e5 am3-si7 lai5 beng5-pek8 I sou2 hut-liok8--khi3 e5 ui2-tai7 e5 su7, i2-kip8 kng-beng5 kap bi2-le7 e5 se3-kai3 e5 keng-giam7, chiu7-si7 chhiau-oat8 ti7 toe7-bin7 sou2 bat keng-giam7 e5.  Hit-si5 m7-chai ti7 I e5 sim-lai7 u7 siN-chhut kiaN-ui3 e5 liam7-thau5 a2-bo5?  Ia5-sou iau2 choe3 gin2-na2 e5 si5, m7-chai bat teh siuN7 I si7 chi7-chui7, bat teh chhi3-khoaN3 ai3 beh liau2-kai2 I e5 thian-hun7 kap I lim5-kau3 se3-kan e5 bok8-tek mah?
	Lan2 chai I chiaN5-choe3 lang5, chiu7-si7 u7 chiap-lap8 jin5-lui7 iu2-han7 e5 khui3-lat8, sou2-i2 I ti7 tiap-a2-ku2 u7 sit-loh8 I e5 chin-sit8 e5 ui-giam5, bo5 chap8-hun oe7 ki3-tit hit e5 Eng2-oan2 e5 se3-kai3.  Na7 bo5 an2-ni, I si7 boe7 thang chiaN5-choe3 “Chin-sit8” e5 lang5.  Tui3 ti7 chit tiam2, lan2 toa7-bin7 iau2 oe7 thang soat-beng5 khah siong5-soe3 chit8-sut-a2.  Ti7 kin-a2-jit8 e5 sim-li2-hak8, u7 chit8-tiau5 sim-sek e5 hak8-soat, kio3-choe3 chiam5-chai7 i3-sek, tui3 an2-ni u7 chi2-si7 lan2 chai, Ia5-sou e5 Sin5-seng3 e5 pi3-koat u7 chiam5-chai7 ti7 I e5 poaN3-chheN2 e5 cheng-sin5 chong7-thai3.  Put-ko3 I peng5-siong5 chhiN2-gou7 e5 i3-sek, si7 chit8 e5 chu7-jian5 lang5 e5 gin2-na2 e5 i3-sek.  Ti7 chit kui2-ni5 lai5, hak8-chia2 put-chi2 u7 kang2-kiu3 lan2 lang5 e5 poaN3 i3-sek e5 cheng-sin5 hian7-siong7, chai-iaN2 ti7 hit ho7 e5 cheng-sin5 hian7-siong7 e5 e7-bin7, u7 chek-chu7 choe7-choe7 sou2 boe7 ki3-tit--khi3 e5 ki3-ek ti7-teh, ia7 hiah e5 ki3-ek khah-siong5 na7 tu2-tioh8 tut8-jian5 e5 chhi3-kek e5 si5, chiu7 sui5-hang7 sui5-hang7 koh phu5 khi2-lai5 ti7 lan2 e5 i3-sek e5 lai7-tiong, koh-chai3 chit8-hang7 chit8-hang7 lai5 siuN7-tioh8.  Lan2 bat thak8-tioh8 u7 sim2-mih8 gin2-na2 phah-k-kiN3, hou7 chhat8 a2-si7 song3-hiong lang5 thau chhoa7 khi3, saN-kap tiam3 it-ji7-chap8 ni5 ku2, ti7 hit tiong-kan, tak8 pai2 na7 tu2-tioh8 chin toa7 e5 chhi3-kek e5 si5, khah siong5 oe7 siN-khi2 bo5 loa7 hun-beng5 e5 i3-sek, lai5 sio2-khoa2 oe7 ki3-tit cha2-cheng5 i e5 ko-siong7 e5 ka-teng5, sui2-sui2 e5 khoan5-keng2, i2-kip8 hit e5 bo5 loa7 hun-beng5 e5 lau7-bu2 e5 bin7-mau7.  Kiam2-chhai2 khia7-khi2 ti7 Na2-sat-lek8 chit e5 Sin5-tong5 Ia5-sou e5 i3-sek, sit8-chai7 u7 tam7-pok8 chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni, ia7 ku2 kaN2.
	Lan2 iong5-un2 chit khoan2 e5 siat-siong2, boh8-tit phah-sng3 si7 bo5 keng3-khian5 e5 su7.  Put-ko3 lan2 tek-khak si7 m7-kaN2 koh siuN chin3-cheng5 lai5 kong2-khi2 sim2-mih8.
	Put-lun7 siaN2-khoan2, Hok-im-su sou2 ki3 sui-si7 chio2, iau2-ku2 lan2 bian2 lun2-neh lai5 chhi3-khoaN3 bio5-sia2 I iu3-lian5 e5 cheng5-keng2, soa3 lai5 siong2-siong7 hit e5 khoan2-sit.  Lan2 thang tui3 lan2 sou2 bat I e5 khoan5-keng2 lai5 kang2-kiu3, soa3 eng7 keng3-khian5 e5 liam7-thau5 lai5 siong2-siong7.  Siat-su2 lan2 na7 oe7 khah koan-sim I ti7 au7-lai5 sou2 kong2 e5 oe7, chiu7 oe7 chhe7-tioh8 choe7-choe7 si7 I teh hoe5-siong2 I iu3-lian5 e5 su7-sit8.
	ChhiaN2 seng lai5 siuN7 Na2-sat-lek8.  Chit e5 Na2-sat-lek8 chiu7-si7 I e5 kou3-hiong, si7 ti7 toe7-bin7-chiuN7 te7-it sin5-seng3 e5 sou2-chai7, si7 I e5 iu3-lian5 i2-kip8 siau3-lian5 si5-tai7 it-chhe3 e5 ki3-ek e5 poe3-keng2.  Tui3 cheng3-lang5 put-si5 to hian2-beng5 I si7 Na2-sat-lek8 e5 Ia5-sou.  Ti7 Sip8-ji7-ke3 teng2 sou2 teng3 e5 cham2-tiau5 ia7-si7 chheng-hou I si7 Na2-sat-lek8 e5 Ia5-sou; I tui3 thiN-nih8 chhut-hian7 lai5 hou7 Tai7-sou3 e5 So2-lo5 khoaN3-kiN3, hit-si5 ia7-si7 kong2, “Goa2 chiu7-si7 Na2-sat-lek8 e5 Ia5-sou, li2 sou2 khun2-tiok8 e5.”
	Lan2 ai3 seng tam7-poh8 lai5 siuN7 Na2-sat-lek8 e5 cheng5-keng2.  U7 chit8 pak Pa-lek8-su-theng3 e5 toe7-tou5 thian2 khui-khui ti7 goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5.  Goa2 si7 che7 ng3 pak.  Sou2-i2 ti7 goa2 e5 to3-peng5 u7 lam5 sek e5 Toe7-tiong-hai2, chiaN3-peng5 u7 Iok-tan3 ho5, peng5-heng5 teh lau5.  ChhiaN2 oe7 ki3-tit, u7 chit8-tiau5 khoah-khoah e5 soaN-khiN tui3 Toe7-tiong hai2 chhut-hoat hoaiN5 ke3 tiong-iong Pa-lek8-su-theng3 e5 soaN-kok, thang3 kau3 Iok-tan3 ho5.  Chit tiau5 soaN-khIN,m si7 kio3-choe3 Ia5-su-liat8 (Jezreel) e5 soaN-khiN.  Chiong chit tiau5 soaN-khiN choe3 kai3-soaN3, pak-peng5 e5 thou2-toe7 si7 kio3-choe3 Ka-li7-li7.  TaN lan2 na7 khia7 ti7 chit tiau5 soaN-khiN e5 tiong-iong, bin7 ng3 pak-peng5, hit si5 lan2 thang khoaN3-kiN3 chit8-tiau5 to7-lou7, kio3-choe3 “Na2-sat-lek8 e5 to7-lou7,” u7 thang3 chiuN7 pak-peng5, tit8-tit8 jip8 soaN-nih8, kau3 ti7 hit e5 iN5-iN5 e5 chu7-jian5 e5 hi3-hng5 lai7.
	Ti7-hia sou2 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 hit e5 iN5-iN5 e5 chu7-jian5 e5 hi3-hng5, chiu7-si7 Ia5-sou choe3 gin2-na2 e5 si5, sou2 keng-ke3 e5 bu2-tai5.
	Lan2 ai3 lai5 siong2-siong7, ti7 hit e5 soe3-soe3 e5 bu2-tai5 e5 Ia5-sou e5 khoan2-sit.  Lan2 na7 hoe5-siong2 lan2 choe3 gin2-na2 e5 cheng5-keng2, chiu7 u7 thang choe3 chham-kho2 lai5 pang-chan7 lan2 khah bat I.  Ti7 goa2 e5 thak8-chheh keng, u7 koa3 chit8 pak toa7 e5 toe7-tou5, u7 oe7 hit e5 iN5-iN5 e5 chu7-jian5 e5 hi3-hng5 ti7-teh.  Sou2-i2 goa2 thang khoaN3-tioh8 cha2-si5 I sou2 khoaN3 e5 sio-siang7 e5 soaN-nia2, i2-kip8 soaN-khiN, kap hit e5 soe3-soe3 e5 soaN-lai7 e5 koe-a2, sou2 chek-chu7 choe7-choe7 peh8-sek e5 khia7-koe chhu3, koh ti7 hit e5 koe-a2 e5 au7-bin7, u7 ou-sek e5 lou2-kou2-chioh8.  Lan2 thang siong2-siong7, Ia5-sou ti7 soe3-han3 e5 si5, u7 si3-koe3 kiaN5-iu5 ti7 hit e5 tiong-kan.
	Ke3-khi3 sui-si7 tu2-tioh8 Tho2-ni2-ki5 lang5 e5 hui2-hoai7, iau2-ku2 kau3 ti7 kin-a2-jit8, hit e5 kong-keng2, toa7-pou7-hun7 si7 bo5 sim2-mih8 pian3-oaN7.  Chhin-chhiuN7 lan2 sou2 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 hit e5 oeh8-oeh8, oan-oan, oat8-oat e5 koe-lou7, khi2 ti7 siaN5-goa7 e5 khong3-ia2, a2-si7 hoe-hng5 lai7 e5 khia7-koe chhu3, i2-kip8 hit e5 chhiN-chhui3 e5 soaN-kok, chhun-thiN chit8-e7 kau3, si3-bin7 moa2-moa2 to si7 pek8-hap8, kim-lian5, mui5-kui3, peh8-sek e5 bou2-tan, kap ki5-u5 tak8 teng2-ho7 e5 ia2-hoe, long2 saN-chiN khui, chhan3-lan7 kau3-kek8, chiaN5-choe3 pak-peng5 e5 Pa-lek8-su-theng3 tiong te7-it sui2-keng2 e5 chit8-e5, che long2 si7 cha2 Ia5-sou sou2 u7 khoaN3 e5 kong-keng2.  Koh u7 chit8-tiau5 tng5-tng5 e5 soaN-lou7, chiu7-si7 I sou2 siong5-siong5 teh kiaN5 e5.  Ti7 siaN5-nih8 e5 au7-bin7, u7 chit8 e5 koaiN5-koaiN5 e5 soaN-a2, cha2 ti7 ho2 thiN e5 si5, I u7 khia7 ti7 hit e5 teng2-bin7 lai5 teh khoaN3 Tai7-pok soaN, Hi-pek-lun5 soaN, i2-kip8 So2-lo5 kap Iok-na2-tan si2 e5 Ki-pi2-a (Gilboa) soaN, ia7 soa3 tui3 hia lai5 khoaN3 hit e5 chhin-chhiuN7 chit8-pak e5 tou5 thian2 khui-khui e5 Ka-li7-li7 hong-hoe3 e5 soaN-lun5-a2, i2-kip8 saN-li7 hng7-hng7 hit e5 lam5-sek e5 Toe7-tiong-hai2.  Ti7 chit e5 bo5 pian3-oaN7 e5 Tang-iuN5 e5 se3-kai3, cha-bou2 gin2-na2 iau2 si7 siang7-khoan2 chhin-chhiuN7 cha2-si5 chit8 poaN, long2-si7 ti7 koe-lou7-nih8 teh soan-jiong2, ti7 chhan5-chng e5 chiN2-piN teh au5-kio3, ti7 lou7-nih8 e5 hiong-chhoan lang5 long2 kap cha2-si5 siang7-khoan2, si7 chheng7 hit ho7 hoe-ang5 liu2-lek8 e5 i-chiuN5, ti7 lou7-nih8 tai7-ke sek8-sai7 saN chheng2-an.  Si7 lah!  Koh u7 thiN-tiong e5 pe-chiau2, chiu7-si7 I sou2 bat in2-khi2 e5, chiong5-tiong u7 choe7-choe7 lan2 put-chi2 sek8-sai7 e5, chhin-chhiuN7 u7 poaN3-thiN-a2, tou7-koan, koh u7 teh pe-lai5 pe-khi3 ti7 soe3-tiau5 khoe-a2 e5 chioh8-thau5 teng2 e5 chek-leng5 (gu5-sai2 chiau2-a2), i2-kip8 kui toa7-tin7 teh pe e5 chhek-chiau2-a2, chiu7-si7 I sou2 teh kong2, sui-jian5 ti7 chhi7-tiuN5-nih8 nng7 chiah si7 tat8 u7 chit8-hun gun5, iau2-ku2 Siong7-te3 u7 teh chiau3-kou3 i.
	TaN beh lai5 siuN7 Na2-sat-lek8, I e5 kou3-hiong.  I u7 khia7-khi2 ti7 Na2-sat-lek8 e5 chit8 tiau5 e5 koe-nih8, tiam3 ti7 bak8-chhiuN7 e5 soe3-keng chhu3-a2-lai7, si7 chiaN5-choe3 chit8 e5 chu7-jian5 lang5 e5 gin2-na2, lai5 tiam3 ti7 chu7-jian5 lang5 e5 ka-teng5.  Ti7 hit e5 ka-teng5 tu5-khi2 Ia5-sou i2-goa7, iau2 u7 pat8 e5 gin2-na2 ti7-teh.  Lan2 oe7 ki3-tit, Na2-sat-lek8 e5 chhu3-piN bat hui2-pong3 I, m7-jin7 I si7 sian-ti lang5, in-ui7 long2 bat I e5 ka-teng5 si7 teh choe3-bak8, si7 khia7-khi2 ti7 in e5 keh-piah tiau5 e5 koe-a2 na7-tiaN7.  In u7 thi2-chhio3 I kong2, “Chit e5 kiam2 m7-si7 bak8-chhiuN7 e5 KiaN2 mah?  I e5 lau7-bu2 kiam2 m7-si7 kio3-choe3 Ma2-li7-a2, I e5 hiaN-ti7 Nga2-kok, Iok-se, Se-bun5, Iu5-tai7 mah?  I e5 chi2-be7 kiam2 bo5 long2 kap lan2 ti7-chia mah.”
	Lan2 ti7-chia m7-bian2 gi7-lun7 lang5 siong5-siong5 sou2 teh tho2-lun7 e5 bun5-toe5, kong2, hiah e5 gin2-na2 si7 Ma2-li7-a sou2 siN-e5, a2-si7 Iok-sek cheng5 u7 chhoa7 chit8 e5 lai5 siN e5 kiaN2 mah?  Liong2-peng5 khiok long2 u7 choe7-choe7 e5 gi7-lun7, put-ko3 long2 bo5 u7 phou2-pian3-tek thang hou7 cheng3-lang5 chiap-lap8 e5 kiat-lun7.  Put-lun7 siaN2-khoan2, chai7 lan2 chi2-u7 thang kau3-giah8 chai, u7 kui2-na7 e5 hiaN-ti7 chi2-be7 kap Ia5-sou saN-kap tiong2-seng5 ti7 hit e5 ka-teng5.
	Lan2 tioh8 bian2-kiong2 lan2 e5 sim-su, lai5 li7-khui hit e5 tui3 kou2-cha2 i2-lai5 pun2-u7, ia7 chiap8-chiap8 tu3-hian7 e5 Eng2-oan2 e5 KiaN2 e5 su-siuN2, saN-kap lai5 siuN7, soa3 lai5 hian2-beng5 choe3 chit8 e5 soe3-han3 gin2-na2 e5 Ia5-sou, u7 chaiN2-iuN7 khia7-khi2 ti7 Na2-sat-lek8 lai5 su-hau7 I e5 lau7-bu2, u7 khi3 kang-tiuN5 khioh khau-to hoe, soa3 lai5 khoaN3 I u7 chaiN2-iuN7 tiam3 ti7 choe7-choe7 gin2-na2 e5 tiong-kan, ti7 koe-chhi7-nih8 lai5 thit-tho5, hit ho7 gin2-na2 se3-kai3 e5 bo5 pian3-khoan2 e5 iu5-hi3.
	Ti7 gin2-na2 e5 se3-kai3 sou2 teh thit-tho5 e5 hoat-tou7, si7 bo5 sim2-mih8 pian3-khoan2, che m7-chai lan2 bat siuN7-tioh8 bo5?  Sui-si7 keng-ke3 kui2-na7 se3-ki2, iau2-ku2 ti7 gin2-na2 e5 se3-kai3 sou2 teh thit-tho5 e5, sou2 teh gim5 e5, si7 long2 bo5 hun-piat kou2-kim, tui3 Pa-piat e5 thah hit-si5, kau3 ti7 hian7-kim long2 si7 chit8-iuN7.  Sou2-i2 lan2 toa7-bin7 thang thiaN-tioh8 nng7 chheng ni5 cheng5 Na2-sat-lek8 e5 gin2-na2 sou2 teh gim5 e5 si, kong2:
	“Goan2 tui3 lin2 pun5 tat8-a2, lin2 bo5 thiau3-bu2;
	Goan2 bat pi-ai, lin2 bo5 tui5-heng.”
U7 chit8-jit8 Ia5-sou kap hak8-seng giam5-siok teh tam5-lun7 e5 si5, I u7 siuN7-tioh8 chit8 ku3 si, kong2, 	“Goan2 tui3 lin2 pun5 tat8-a2, lin2 bo5 thiau3-bu2; goan2 bat pi-ai, lin2 bo5 tui5-heng.”  Put-ko3 I si7 in2-khi2 soe3-han3 e5 si5 sou2 koan3-si3 teh gim5 e5 si e5 chit8 chat na7-tiaN7.  Kho2-sioh lan2 bo5 thang thiaN-kiN3 I eng7 sim2-mih8 tiau7 teh gim5, lan2 chi2-u7 thiaN-kiN3 Na2-sat-lek8 gin2-na2 sou2 teh gim5 e5 si7 e5 oe7 na7-tiaN7.  Goa2 tak8-pai2 khoaN3-tioh8 gin2-na2 ti7 koe-lou7-nih8 teh gim5-si, thit-tho5 e5 si5, bo5 chit8 pai2 bo5 siuN7-tioh8 chit ku3, i2-kip8 Ia5-sou teh thit-tho5 e5 cheng5-keng2.
	Toa7-bin7 I sou2 in2-khi2 e5 le7, si7 ti7 bo5 i3-sek e5 tiong-kan, tui3 I choe3 Gin2-na2 e5 ki3-ek lai5 tit-tioh8 e5, che lan2 u7 si5 kiaN-liau2 khah bo5 chu3-i3--tioh8.  Phi3-ju7 lai5 kong2, lan2 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 chit8 e5 Gin2-na2 bat soe3-ji7 chiong ka-lauh8 e5 chhek-chiau2-a2 hu5 chiuN7 siu7-nih8, ia7 sim-lai7 u7 kam2-chhiok--tioh8 Siong7-te3 e5 chiau3-kou3, soa3 siuN7 kong2, “Na7 m7-si7 Siong7-te3 e5 i3-su3, lian5 chit8 chiah soe3-soe3 e5 chhek-chiau2-a2 ia7 boe7 ka-lauh8 toe7.”  Lan2 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 chit8 e5 e5 choe3-kang lang5 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5, khia7-khi2 ti7 Na2-sat-lek8 soe3-keng e5 kang-tiuN5 lai7, u7 sit-loh8 chit8 e5 gun5-a2, chiu7-si7 i khoaN3-choe3 chin tat8-chiN5 e5, chiu7 “tiam2-teng, sau3-chhu3, khun5-khun5 chhe7 kau3-tioh8.”  Lan2 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 chit8 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5, teh niu5 saN-tau2 e5 mi7-hun2, lai5 pi7-pan7 chit8 le2-pai3 ku2 sou2 tioh8 khiam3-eng7 e5 mi7-pau.  Hit e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 e5 ka-teng5 si7 soe3-soe3, sou2-i2 saN-tau2 si7 kau3-giah8 thang choe3 chit8 le2-pai3 e5 lou7-eng7.  Hit e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 u7 lam7 tam7-poh8 kaN3 ti7 hit e5 tiong-kan.  Koh u7 chit8 e5 soe3-han3 gin2-na2 be7 pi2 chau3-thau5 khah koaiN5, u7 chhun i e5 chhiu2, chian7-tang chian7-sai, soa3 chiap8-chiap8 mng7 kong2, che si7 sim2-mih8, si7 an3-choaN2 choe3, si7 ui7-tioh8 siaN2 in-toaN chiah choe3.  Tng Ia5-sou teh kong2, “Thian-kok chhin-chhiuN7 kaN3, hu7-jin5-lang5 theh8-khi3 khng3 ti7 saN tau2 e5 mi7-hun2 e5 lai7-bin7, kau3 long2 hoat-kaN3,” hit-si5 lan2 thang phah-sng3, Ia5-sou u7 siuN7-tioh8 choe3 gin2-na2 e5 keng-giam7 chiah tioh8.  Lan2 khah siong5 u7 hut-liok8 choe7-choe7 gin2-na2 si5-tai7 hiah e5 khah toa7 chan5 e5 su7, iau2-ku2 chhin-chhiuN7 chit khoan2 soe3-soe3 hang7 e5 su7, tian-to3 si7 put-si5 khek ti7 sim-lai7!
	Chit e5 Gin2-na2 Ia5-sou lim5-kau3 se3-kan, m7-si7 u7 chiau5-pi7 e5 ti3-sek ti7-teh.  Lian5 koan-he7 I e5 chong-kau3 e5 bun7-toe5 ia7 tioh8 ai3 hak8-sip8.  chong2-si7 beh hak8-sip8 chit khoan2 bun7-toe5, i e5 kong-hau7, toa7-pou7-hun7 si7 chai7 beh hak8-sip8 e5 gin2-na2 e5 thau5-nau2, na7-si7 an2-ni, chhi3-siuN7, chit e5 Gin2-na2 Ia5-sou sou2 hak8-sip8 e5 siaN2-khoan2.
	Lun7 chong-kau3 I choe3-chhou e5 ti3-sek, bian2 kong2, si7 tui3 I e5 lau7-bu2 lai5 tit-tioh8 e5.  Sui-jian5 lan2 chai, Iu5-thai3 lang5 si7 lau7-pe7 teh tam-tng gin2-na2 it-chhe3 e5 chek-jim7, iau2-ku2 lun7 chong-kau3 e5 su7, tui3 Siong7-te3 e5 un-su3, beh hou7 thong se3-kai3 choe3 lau7-bu2 e5 lang5 lai5 tam-tng chit e5 su2-beng7.  Tak8-am2 Ma2-li7-a beh he7 eN-a2 Ia5-sou khi3 khun3 e5 si5, u7 ka3-si7 I ki5-to2, u7 tui3 I kong2-khi2 Pe7 Siong7-te3 e5 su7, koh ti7 i e5 sim-lai7 u7 eng7 choan5 cheng-sin5, lai5 su-siuN2 ti7 Ia5-sou e5 thau5-cheng5 sou2 an-pai5 e5 thian-hun7, chhi3-siuN7 hit ho7 si5-kan, si7 sin5-seng3 kau3 siaN2 khoan2!  Ma2-li7-a ah!  Cheng3 hu7-jin5-lang5 bo5 thang tam-tng li2 sou2 tam-tng--e5.  Ti7 cheng3 hu7-jin5-lang5 e5 tiong-kan, li2 u7 tit-tioh8 un-tian2!  Chin kho2-sioh, choe7-choe7 hu7-jin5-lang5 kap gin2-na2 bo5 u7 chit ho7 e5 keng-giam7!
	Iu5-thai3 lang5 tui3 ti7 gin2-na2 e5 chong-kau3 hun3-lian7, si7 tek8-piat8 put-chi2 u7 koan-sim ti7-teh.  Lian5 ti7 hit e5 iN7-kau3 e5 sou2-chai7, lau7-pe7 si7 iN7-kau3, lau7-bu2 si7 Iu5-thai3 e5 ka-teng5, lan2 oe7 ki3-tit hit e5 siau3-lian5 e5 The5-mou5-thai3 e5 ho2 siau-sit, kong2, “i tui3 soe3-han3 i2-keng bat hiah e5 Seng3-chheh.”  gin2-na2 tu2-tu2 teh oh8 kong2 oe7 e5 si5, chiu7 soa3 ka3-si7 in chong-kau3 e5 su7.  Ia5-sou u7 hak8-sip8 “Shema,” che tu2-tu2 si7 chhin-chhiuN7 lan2 e5 Sin3-keng.  Lun7 si, Ia5-sou u7 hak8-sip8 Siong7-te3 khah kan2-tan e5 Si-phian.  Lun7 lek8-su2, I u7 hak8-sip8 Siong7-te3 u7 chaiN2-iuN7 in2-chhoa7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 kou3-su7,  Lian5 ti7 I tu2-chiah soe3-soe3-han3, be7 hak8-sip8 sim2-mih8 e5 i2-cheng5, tak8 pai2 beh hoah8-jip8 mng5-lai7 e5 si5, put-si5 to u7 khoaN3-kiN3 hit e5 u7 sia2 Seng3-chheh e5 oe7, ut-teh e5 choa2, teng3 ti7 mng5-khia7, si7 teh piau2-beng5 Siong7-te3 u7 chiau3-kou3 I2-sek-liat8 ke e5 ki3-ho7.
	Chiu-ui5 it-chhe3 e5 su7-but8, long2 si7 ka3-si7 Ia5-sou chai-bat I e5 chong-kau3 e5 su7-sit8.  Bo5 lun7 si7 an-hioh-jit8 e5 saN-tng3, an-hioh-jit8 e5 teng-he2, mui2 le2-pai3-jit8 sou2 chhut-sek8 e5 hoe7-tng5, mui2 ni5 e5 chiok-tian2, siu-koah e5 choeh-ki5, chit8 chiu-kan e5 che3-jit8, siok8-choe7 e5 jit8, i2-kip8 PoaN5-ke3-choeh, chiu7-si7 cheng3-lang5 ti7 tak8 ni5 tioh8 li7-khui kou3-hiong, chiuN7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 sou2 teh hu3 e5 choeh, chhi3-siuN7 che chai7 Ma2-li7-a e5 kiaN2 Ia5-sou khoaN3-liau2 siaN2 khoan2!  Bo5 m7-si7 oe7 hou7 I siuN7-tioh8 Siong7-te3 e5 i3-su3 u7 hiah-nih8 un2-bat8 ti7 peng5-siong5 e5 seng-oah8.  Chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni, Ia5-sou u7 chiau3 lang5 e5 khoan2-sit chiam7-chiam7 toa7, jit8-jit8 iong2-chong3, ti3-hui7 chhiong-moa2, Siong7-te3 e5 un-tian2 kap I saN-kap ti7-teh.  “I e5 ti3-hui7 kap ni5-he3 na2 ke-thiN, Siong7-te3 kap lang5 na2 thiaN3 I.”
	Ia5-sou kau3 ti7 lak8 he3 e5 si5, chiau3 Iu5-thai3 lang5 e5 hong-siok8, tioh8 ai3 hu3 sui5-lang5 e5 siaN5-chhi7 e5 hoe7-tng5 e5 sio2-oh8, lai5 siu7 hiong-chhoan e5 liap8-pi2 e5 ka3-si7.  Tong-si5 Iu5-thai3 lang5 si7 put-chi2 khoaN3-tang7 chit ho7 e5 oh8-tng5.  Chiau3 kui-ku2, tak8 sou2-chai7 long2 tioh8 ai3 u7 oh8-tng5 thang hou7 gin2-na2 siu7 kau3-iok8.  Kau3 chap8-he3 ui5-chi2, long2 si7 eng7 Seng3-chheh choe3 kau3-kho-su lai5 hou7 in thak8.
	Chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni, lan2 thang siong2-siong7, Ia5-sou choe3 soe3-han3 gin2-na2 e5 si5, u7 kap I e5 hiaN-ti7 chi2-be7 saN chhoa7 chiuN7 oh8.  Iah8 thang siong2-siong7, I u7 choe3 gin2-na2 lai5 kap I e5 tang5-phoaN7 saN-kap choe7 ti7 phou-chng e5 toe7 e5 teng2-bin7, tai7-ke ui5 poaN3 iN5-heng5 ti7 sian-siN e5 bin7-cheng5, lai5 teh hak8-sip8 Siong7-te3 e5 Oe7.  Ah!  Lan2 khah siong5 si7 chin lou2-tun7 boe7-hiau2 ka3-si7 gin2-na2 bat Seng3-chheh!  Goa2 teh ki5-koai3 hiah e5 teh ka3-si7 Ia5-sou e5 lau7 liap8-pi2, m7-chai si7 sim2-mih8 khoan2-sit e5 lang5?
	Kau3 Ia5-sou khah oe7 hiau2 thak8 e5 si5, I sou2 chhin-kun7, liah8-choe3 si7 te7-it iau3-kin2 e5 chheh, chiu7-si7 Ku7-iok Seng3-chheh.  Iu5-thai3 lang5 e5 sian-siN u7 tui3 Seng3-chheh e5 tiong-kan, lai5 phian-chhip siok8 ti7 gin2-na2 sou2 tioh8 thak8, lai5 choe3 in e5 lou7-eng7, chhin-chhiuN7 Chhong3-se3-ki3 e5 kou3-su7 hit ho7.  Lan2 ai3 khah au7-lai5 chiah lai5 siuN7 chit pun2 Seng3-chheh tui3 ti7 chit e5 ti7-teh toa7-han3 e5 Gin2-na2 Ia5-sou e5 i3-gi7 kau3 siaN2 khoan2.  Ti7-chia, lan2 put-ko3 si7 ai3 toa7-toa7 lai5 chu2-tiuN, I ti7 soe3-han3 sou2 siu7 e5 kau3-iok8 e5 tiong-sim ki-chhou2, chiu7-si7 seng5-siu7 Seng3-chheh e5 kam2-hoa3.  Toa7 ng3-bang7 lan2 tak8 e5 ka-teng5 iu5-goan5 oe7 chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni!
	Chong2-si7 chai7 I teh khoaN3, ti7 Siong7-te3 e5 se3-kai3 it-chhe3 e5 hian7-siong7, bo5 m7-si7 seng3, koh thang choe3 ka3-si7 e5 lou7-eng7.  Lang5 e5 chhiu2 sou2 sia2 e5 Oe7 (Seng3-chheh) i2-goa7 ti7 Ia5-sou e5 sin-piN u7 chiau5-chng5 sui2 e5, m7-si7 lang5 e5 chhiu2 sou2 sia2 e5 Oe7 ti7-teh.  Hit e5 Oe7 chiu7-si7 Pe7 Siong7-te3 e5 toa7 chu7-jian5, bo5 kong2-oe7 e5 si-koa.  Tui3 chit e5 toa7 chu7-jian5, Pe7 Siong7-te3 u7 si5-siong5 teh tui3 Ia5-sou kong2-oe7.  Lan2 chai, Ia5-sou u7 tek8-piat8 e5 i3-sek, chai-iaN2 Siong7-te3 put-si5 kap I saN-kap ti7-teh.  Chin7-chai7 o3-biau7, sui2 koh ki5-koai3 e5 su7-sit8, chiu7-si7 lian5 Ia5-sou iau2-be7 u7 khui3-lat8 thang siuN7 e5 i2-cheng5, Siong7-te3 chiu7 i2-keng u7 kap chit e5 eN-a2 e5 sim-sin5 teh ong2-lai5.
	Goa2 giah8 bak8 lai5 khoaN3 tiau3 ti7 goa2 e5 thak8-chheh keng, hit e5 Na2-sat-lek8 e5 te7-tou5 e5 si5, goa2 sim-lai7 teh siuN7, choe3 Gin2-na2 e5 Ia5-sou u7 pian3 kiaN5 ti7 hit e5 chheng-chhai2 e5 soaN-io, Siong7-te3 sou2 hian2-hian7 e5 sui2-sui2 e5 chu7-jian5 e5 tiong-kan, lai5 koan-siong2 Siong7-te3 sou2 chhong3-cho7 e5 chhiN-chhui3 e5 soaN-nia2, chhio3-iong5 e5 khoe-chui2, i2-kip8 Siong7-te3 sou2 chhong3-cho7 e5 jit8-thau5, u7 chaiN2-iuN7 teh khi2-lai5 phou2-chio3 se3-kan, koh ia7 ti7 ang5-ang5 chhan3-lan7 lai5 chhia5-loh8 toa7-hai2 e5 chui2-tiong; soa3 lai5 khoaN3 Siong7-te3 sou2 chhong3-cho7 e5 hoe-bak8, chiau2-chiah, chau2-siu3, soa3 khoai3-lok8 lai5 thiaN3-sioh in, iah8 kam2-kak Pe7 u7 iu5-goan5 khoai3-lok8 lai5 thiaN3-sioh in.  Lan2 na7 khoaN3 ti7 khah au7-lai5, Ia5-sou teh in2-khi2 chu7-jian5-kai3 e5 mih8, it-chhe3 bo5 m7 hou7 lan2 kam2-kak Siong7-te3 si7 tiam3 ti7 ban7-mih8 e5 au7-bin7, teh khoaN3-kou3 ban7-mih8.  Siong7-te3 u7 thiaN3-thang3 hiah e5 teh tio5-thiau3 ti7 khong3-ia2 e5 soe3-soe3 chiah e5 iuN5-a2.  Siong7-te3 u7 khoaN3-kou3 hiah e5 sit-be5 kho2-lin5 e5 iuN5.  Siong7-te3 u7 teh iuN2-chhi7 thiN-tiong e5 pe-chiau2, in bo5 tioh8-boe5, bo5 phang2-cheh.  Siong7-te3 u7 teh chiau3-kou3 hit chiah ka-lauh8 toe7 e5 chhek-chiau2-a2.  SoaN-nih8 e5 chhau2-bak8, Siong7-te3 u7 hou7 i chheng7 kau3-giah8.  Siong7-te3 u7 chiau3 I e5 sim sou2 hoaN-hi2, lai5 chng-thaN7 soaN-nih8 e5 ia2-hoe, sou2-i2 “tng So2-lo5-bun5 kek8 hang5-ngou2 e5 si5, i sou2 chheng7 e5, m7-tat8-tioh8 chit ho7 hoe e5 chit8 lui2.”  Na2-sat-lek8 e5 choh-sit lang5, ia7 beh8-a2-chi2 ti7 hng5-nih8 e5 si5, choe3 Gin2-na2 e5 Ia5-sou khoaN3-kiN3, sui5-si5 beng5-pek8 ban7-mih8 e5 oah8-mia7 si7 chai7 ti7 Siong7-te3, iah8 hit e5 cheng2-chi2 e5 hoat-seng si7 chhin-chhiuN7 sin5-jiah e5 khoan2-sit, “khi2-thau5 si7 ng, au7-lai5 u7 sui7, koh au7-lai5, sui7 chiu7 kiat-chiaN5 gou2-kak.”
	Ti7 se3-kai3 tu5-khi2 Ia5-sou i2-goa7, kiam2 iau2 u7 pat8-e5 gin2-na2 bat hiong2-lok8 chu7-jian5, thiaN3-sioh chu7-jian5, iah8 ti7 chu7-jian5 e5 tiong-kan, hiah beng5 lai5 khoaN3-kiN3 Siong7-te3, kau3 chhin-chhiuN7 chit e5 Na2-sat-lek8 e5 Gin2-na2 mah?  Chhi3-siuN7, lan2 na7 oe7 thang chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni lai5 poe5-iuN2 lan2 e5 soe3-kiaN2, kiam2 m7-si7 chin ho2!  Na7 oe7-tit-thang khoaN3-kiN3 Siong7-te3 u7 teh un7-heng5 ti7 chu7-jian5, eng7 kiaN-ui3 e5 liam7-thau5 lai5 koan-khoaN3 chhiu7-bak8 teh puh-iN2, soa3 oe7 chai, lan2 na7 siong-hai7 chit8-chiah soe3-soe3 chiah e5 chiau2-a2, a2-si7 eng7 kha lai5 thun2-tah8 soaN-nih8 e5 hoe-bak8, si7 siat-tok8 lan2 e5 Chu2 Siong7-te3 e5 mia5, lan2 siuN7 siaN2 khoan2!  Chhi3-siuN7, ti7 gin2-na2 e5 chong-kau3 seng-oah8, na7 oe7 thang hou7 in oe7-hiau2 siuN7-tioh8 chit e5 chhin-chhiat e5 Siong7-te3, u7 chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni hiah-nih8 si5-siong5 teh chhin-kun7 ti7 in, che kiam2 m7-si7 chu7-jian5 chin thang hoaN-hi2 e5 su7!  Iau2-be7 u7 se3-kan e5 kan-khou2 kap choe7-ok e5 i3-sek, lai5 teh chhui-pek Ia5-sou e5 sim e5 i2-cheng5, khak-sit8 I si7 chit8 e5 heng7-hok-ji5, khia7-khi2 ti7 Na2-sat-lek8 lai5 hiong2-siu7 hit e5 chu7-iu5, tan-sun5 e5 iu3-lian5 e5 seng-oah8.



Te7-4 chiuN	Siau3-Lian5 Kap Seng5-Lian5

	Seng3-chheh u7 ki3-chai3 Ia5-sou ti7 siau3-lian5 si5-tai7, chap8-ji7 he3 e5 si5 sou2 tu2-tioh8 e5 chit8 e5 kou3-su7, lai5 phah-phoa3 hit e5 saN-chap8 ni5, tng5-tng5 e5 thiam5-cheng7 e5 lek8-su2.  Lan2 teh ki5-koaim3 m7-chai si7 u7 sim2-mih8 in-toaN ti7-teh?  M7-chai si7 u7 sim2-mih8 bok8-tek chiah lai5 teh kong2-khi2?  Kiam2-si7 u7 i3-su3 beh am3-si7, ti7 I e5 cheng-sin5 seng-oah8 e5 hoat-tat8-siong7 e5 chit8 choan2-ki mah?  Kiam2-chhai2 si7 teh am3-si7, ti7 hit-si5 Ia5-sou chiah chhou-chhou u7 i3-sek I e5 sin5-pi3 ia7 ku2 kaN2?
	Iu5-thai3 lang5 e5 gin2-na2, na7 kau3 chap8-ji7 he3, chiau3 in e5 kui-ku2, long2 hou7 in hak8-sip8 lut8-hoat e5 ka3-si7, lai5 chiaN5-choe3 “Lut8-hoat e5 KiaN2,” tu2-tu2 si7 chhin-chhiuN7 hian7-kim, bo5 lun7 sim2-mih8 Ki-tok-kau3 e5 thoan5-the2, u7 kiaN5 in e5 le2-sek lai5 hou7 gin2-na2, u7 hun7 ti7 kau3-hoe7 long2-chong2 e5 chek-jim7 chit8 poaN.  Chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni, I e5 iu3-lian5-ki5 i2-keng ke3-liau2.  I ti7 sim-lai7 si7 u7 kam2-kak chong-kau3-siong7 tiong7-tai7 e5 chek-jim7.  Chit-tiap8 I oe7 thang kap toa7-lang5 saN-=kap chiuN7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 hu3 choeh.  Sou2-i2 lan2 u7 thak8-tioh8 kong2, “Tak8-ni5 PoaN5-ke3-choeh e5 si5, I e5 pe7-bu2 khi3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, kau3 I chap8-ji7 he3 e5 si5, chiau3 choeh-ki5 e5 le7, long2 chiuN7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2.”
	Seng3-chheh tui3 chit-chan5, u7 khoaN3 put-chi2 tang7, sou2-i2 tui3 an2-ni, u7 giu2 lan2 e5 sim ai3 lai5 chu3-i3 chit tiam2.  Lan2 thang siong2-siong7, chit e5 seng3-cheng5 thiam5-cheng7, chhim-tim5 e5 Gin2-na2 Ia5-sou, ti7 ku2-ku2 e5 tiong-kan, u7 giah8 thau5 teh theng3-hau7 chit e5 ki-hoe7, chit-tiap8 I e5 sim-lai7 u7 put-chi2 siu7 toa7 e5 kam2-tong7, lai5 kap cheng3 Na2-sat-lek8 e5 sun5-le2-chia2 choe3-tin7 chhut-hoat, tui3 hit-tiau5 Na2-sat-lek8 e5 toa7 to7-lou7, ng3 hit e5 piN5-iuN5 tit8-tit8 loh8-khi3, ia7 chu3-i3 teh khoaN3 hiah e5 tui3 siang-chhe lou7 lai5 chiap-tin7 e5 choe7-choe7 e5 sin e5 thoan5-the2, tai7-ke keng-ke3 sian-chou2, i2-kip8 sian-ti lang5 sou2 bat lek8-ke3 e5 u7 lek8-su2 e5 sou2-chai7, jian5-au7 u7 kiaN5-kau3 ti7 Su7-liam7, tai7-ke chiu7 hioh-khun3 ti7-hia lai5 thiaN-kiN3 I2-li7-sa e5 su7-chek, iu7-koh beh kiaN5-ke3 Ki5-pi2-a e5 si5, u7 thiaN-kiN3 kong2, hit sou2-chai7 si7 So2-lo5 ong5 e5 kou3-hiong.  In tai7-ke na2 kiaN5 na2 teh gim5 hoaN-hi2 e5 chin3-heng5 koa --- Si-phian --- lai5 chheng-chan3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 Seng3-siaN5.

	Lan2 si7 chin oh8-tit siat-siong2, hiah e5 jiat8-sim e5 Iu5-thai3 e5 gin2-na2 e5 liam7-thau5; chiong5-tiong choe3 Gin2-na2 e5 Ia5-sou, choe3-chhou lai5 khoaN3-kiN3 Seng3 e5 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, hit-si5 I si7 kam2-siong2 siaN2-khoan2, si7 hou7 lan2 koh-khah be7-thang siat-siong2 tit e5!  Chiau3 I teh khoaN3, Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 m7-si7 chit8 e5 kok-bin5 e5 kiaN-siaN5 na7-tiaN7, ma7 m7-si7 chit8 e5 u7 siu7 choe7-choe7 lek8-su2 e5 ki3-ek sou2 chng-thaN7 e5 siaN5-chhi7 na7-tiaN7.  Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 si7 chit8 e5 Seng3 e5 SiaN5; u7 kiat-lian5 ti7 I e5 chong-kau3, I e5 ki5-to2, I e5 Seng3-chheh; ia7 u7 kiat-lian5 ti7 I e5 bin5-chok8 e5 lek8-su2 tiong choe3 te7-it sin5-seng3 e5 si5-ki5.  Cheng3 sun5-le2-chia2 hoah8-jip8 Tai7-ma2-sek siaN5 e5 si5, si7 i2-keng jip8 ti7 Siong7-te3 e5 Seng3 e5 SiaN5.
	Khak-sit8, chai7 Ia5-sou teh khoaN3, I jip8-siaN5 hit-jit8, si7 I it-seng sou2 tioh8 ki3-liam7 e5 jit8.  Ti7 hit chit8 le2-pai3 ku2 e5 tiong-kan, I un2-tang3 u7 siN-khi2 ki5-iN7 i2-kip8 keng3-ui3 e5 liam7-thau5.  Chhi3 siuN7, I jip8 ti7 I e5 Pe7 e5 Chhu3, choan5 se3-kai3 e5 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 sou2 chong5-hong7 keng3-pai3 e5 tiong-sim, hit e5 chong3-koan e5 tian7-tng5, hit si5 I e5 sim-sin5 m7-chai giam5-siok kau3 chaiN2-iuN7!  Chhi3-siuN7, I khoaN3-kiN3 kang2 pah-ban7 e5 kui toa7-tin7 e5 jiat8-sim, keng3-khian5 e5 Iu5-thai3 lang5, tui3 thiN-e7 tak8-kok chu7-chip8, lai5 chak ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 koe-chhi7, u7-e5 tah pou3-piN5 hioh-khun3 ti7 soaN-nih8, ia7 tai7-ke chu7-chip8 choe3-he2 eng7 tang5 chit8-iuN7 e5 sim, beh ti7 I e5 Seng3-tian7 lai5 hok8-sai7 Pe7, hit-si5 I khoaN3-kiN3 hit e5 kong-keng2, I e5 sim-koaN kiam2 bo5 chin hoaN-hi2 khoai3-lok8!  Bo5 giau5-gi5, hiah e5 khah lau7 e5 lang5 e5 tiong-kan, u7 e5 si7 gau5 keng-the2 lang5, gau5 khoaN3-khin lang5 e5 keng3-khian5, sou2-i2 bo5 kau3 loa7-nih8 siu7 kam2-tong7.  Chong2-si7 lang5 na7 m7-si7 tui3 chap8-ji7 he3 khi2, si7 boe7 siN-khi2 hit ho7 e5 sim-koaN!  Sou2-i2 khak-sit8 hit e5 kerng2-hong2, Ia5-sou khoaN3-liau2 si7 kam2-khai3 bu5-liong7!
	Ti7 hit e5 giam5-siok e5 am3-mi5, ti7 sui-lang5 e5 ka-teng5, kiam2-chhai2 u7 kui2-na7 e5 ka-teng5 choe3 chit8 e5 thoan5-the2, lai5 ti7 “Lau5-teng2” siu2 hit e5 tui3 kui2-na7 se3-ki2 i2-lai5, sou2 teh chi2-beng5 I e5 PoaN5-ke3-choeh e5 le2-sek, koh-chai3 chhi3-siuN7, I khoaN3-tioh8 chit e5 cheng5-keng2, hit-si5 e5 kam2-siong2 siaN2-khoan2?  Hit-si5 PoaN5-ke3-choeh e5 iuN5-ko i2-keng thai5, bo5 kaN3 e5 piaN2 kap phang-chhau2 i2-keng pai5 ti7 toh-nih8, u7 choe7-choe7 soe3-soe3 han3 e5 gin2-na2, toa7-bin7 Ia5-sou ia7-si7 u7 oa2 lai5 mng7 sou2 pai5-liat8 e5 le2-sek kong2, “Chit e5 le2-sek si7 sim2-mih8 i3-su3?”  Hit-si5 ti7 cheng3 tai7-ke e5 tiong-kan, te7-it lau7 e5 lang5, chiu7 chin giam5-siok lai5 in3 kong2, “Chit e5 chiu7-si7 Chu2 e5 PoaN5-ke3-choeh e5 le2-sek, lai5 siau3-liam7 cha2 Chu2 u7 poaN5-ke3 I2-sek-liat8 cheng3 kiaN2-sun e5 chhu3, lai5 chin2-kiu3 lan2 e5 ke.”  Khak-sit8 chhin-chhiuN7 chit khoan2 keng2-hong2, choe3 Gin2-na2 e5 Ia5-sou khoaN3-liau2, un2-tang3 siu7 toa7 kam2-tong7, lai5 siN-khi2 ki5-iN7 e5 liam7-thau5 chiah tioh8.

	TaN lai5 kong2-khi2 chiah e5 liap8-pi2 e5 su7.  In-ui7 u7 tam7-poh8 li2-iu5 ti7-teh, sou2-i2 lan2 chiah tioh8 tek8-piat8 lai5 kong2-khi2 I kap in tam5-lun7 e5 kou3-su7.
	Iu5-thai3 lang5 e5 keng-chheh (Talmud) u7 chi2-si7 lan2 chai, Seng3-tian7 e5 pheng5-gi7-oan5 (Sanhedrim), si7 khah-siong5 ti7 tak8-pai2 e5 choeh e5 si5, tioh8 ai3 lai5 che7 ti7 “Gim5-a2” e5 teng2-bin7 lai5 ka3-si7 peh-siN3.  In sou2 kong2 e5 si7 tan-sun5, phou2-thong e5 ka3-si7, tak8-lang5 thang lai5 thiaN, lai5 mng7.  U7 chit8 jit8, chit e5 Gin2-na2 Ia5-sou u7 khoaN3-tang khoaN3-sai, chin hi-han2 e5 khoan2, lai5 si3-ke3 kiaN5 ti7 hit e5 chong3-giam5 e5 thiaN-tng5, lai5 tit-tioh8 choe7-choe7 sin-ki5 e5 in3-siong7 khek ti7 sim-lai7, ia7 ti7 bo5 phah-sng3 e5 tiong-kan, I u7 kiaN5 lai5 khia7 ti7 hit e5 “Gim5-a2” e5 teng2-bin7!
	Tiap-a2-ku2 e5 tiong-kan, chit e5 Gin2-na2 Ia5-sou long2 bo5 teh siuN7 I e5 lau-bu2, peng5-iu2 i2-kip8 ki5-thaN it-chhe3 e5 su7.  Chit e5 siau3-lian5 Gin2-na2 Ia5-sou khia7 ti7-chia, sim-sin5 put-chi2 chhui3-ta him-bou7 ti3-hui7, to long2 bo5 boan2-chiok Na2-sat-lek8 hiah e5 bu5-ti e5 lau7 liap8-pi2 e5 ka3-si7.  Sim7-chi3 ti7 chit e5 “Gim5-a2” teng2, koh u7 cheng3 kok-bin5 e5 toa7 sian-siN, u7 chai-bat e5 lang5 choe7-choe7 ti7-teh, sou2-i2 u7 it-hoat siN-khi2 him-bou7 e5 sim.
	Lan2 thang siuN7, I u7 jiat8-sim ti7-teh thiaN, lai5 siu7 in e5 ka3-si7.  Kau3 hit am3, tak8 lang5 to long2 si3-soaN3 liau2, I kou-put-chiong ia7 tioh8 li7-khui in, lai5 si3-ke3 seh8-lai5 seh8-khi3 ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 koe-lou7-nih8, ia7 long2 be7 thang tu2-tioh8 sim2-mih8 peng5-iu2, sou2-i2 phah-sng3 u7 chhin-chhiat e5 hu7-jin5-lang5, ho2 khoan2-thai7 chit-e5 sit-be5 e5 Gin2-na2 Ia5-sou, u7 pi7-pan7 pang5-keng hou7 I hioh-khun3, pi7-pan7 mi7-pau hou7 I chiah8.  Keh cha2-khi2, I khun3-chhiN2, chiu7 koh-chai3 lai5 cha-hng e5 sou2-chai7, ia7 thiaN ia7 siuN7 in sou2 kong2 e5 to7-li2.  U7-si5 I ma7 soa3 jiat8-jiat8 lai5 chheng2-kau3 in.  Kau3 lou7-be2, hiah e5 lau7 liap8-pi2 soa3 put-chi2 u7 chu3-i3--tioh8 I, sim7-chi3 soa3 chin chhu3-bi7 ai3 kap I tam5-lun7, sou2-i2 au7-lai5 in "“ong2 ki5-koai3 I e5 chhang-mia5 kap I e5 in3-tap.”
	Tui3 ti7 pat8 sou2-chai7 lan2 sou2 chai-iaN2, lun7 gin2-na2 e5 thau5-nau2 e5 hoat-tat8, lan2 tek-khak bo5 thang kau3 loa7 ki5-thai7 Iu5-thai3 e5 liap8-pi2 e5 pang-chan7.  Hoan2-tng2 choe7-choe7 si7 koan-he7 gin2-na2 pun2-sin e5 iat-lek8.  Lian5 hiah e5 bo5-bi7 bo5-sou3 e5 sin5-hak8-chia2, kiam2-chhai2 u7 si5 ma7 iau2 oe7 ki3-tit in pun2-sin bat choe3 gin2-na2 e5 khoan2, sou2-i2 chhin-chhiuN7 Ia5-sou hit ho7 u7 khiau2-khi3, jiat8-seng5 e5 thau5-nau2 e5 gin2-na2, un2-tang3 si7 put-chi2 oe7 chhui-pek hiah e5 sian-siN e5 liong5-sim.  Ti7 hiah e5 Iu5-thai3 e5 liap8-pi2 e5 tiong-kan, u7 choe7-choe7 cin gau5 e5, m7-si7 kan-ta mia5 kong2 si7 sin5-hak8-chia2 na7-tiaN7.  Ti7 in tiong-kan u7 choe7-choe7 chhim-tim5 e5 su-siong2-ka, ko-siong7 e5 jin5-keh-chia2 ti7-teh.  Chhin-chhiuN7 liap8-pi2 Hi-le2-luh (Hillel), Siam2-mai2 (Shammai), i2-kip8 Po2-lo5 e5 Sian-siN Ka-ma2-liat8 (Gamaliel), chiah e5 sian-siN kau3 kin-a2-jit8, ti7 Iu5-thai3 e5 lek8-su2-tiong si7 hou7 lang5 chun-keng3 choe3 chong-kau3 su-siuN2 e5 te7-it ko-siong7 e5 chi2-to7-chia2.  Chiah e5 lang5 toa7-bin7 ti7 hit-jit8 u7 chhut-sek8 ti7 hit e5 “Gim5-a2” e5 teng2-bin7.  In-ui7 ti7 PoaN5-ke3-choeh e5 si5, in tek-khak si7 bo5 khiam3-sek8 chiah tioh8.
	Ti7 au7-lai5 tai7-khai3 Ia5-sou si7 bo5 kap liap8-pi2 kau-oaN7 i3-kian3 kau3 loa7-choe7.  Chong2-si7 chit-tiap8 tai7-ke cham2-jian5 u7 saN heng3-bi7 ti7-teh.  Cheng3 liap8-pi2 u7 chhut bun7-toe5 hou7 chit e5 Gin2-na2 Ia5-sou lai5 siuN7.  M7-chai Ia5-sou thiaN in e5 ka3-si7 liau2, u7 kam2-siong2 siaN2 khoan2?  M7-chai Ia5-sou u7 tui3 in chheng2-kau3 sim2-mih8 khoan2 e5 bun7-toe5 houN3?  Phah-sng3 u7 choe7-choe7 bun7-toe5, I si7 un2-tang3 ai3 chai, ki5-tiong chhin-chhiuN7 lun7-khi2 Siong7-te3 tui3 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 e5 ke3-ek8, a2-si7 lun7-khi2 Bi2-sai3-a e5 ng3-bang7, i2-kip8 PoaN5-ke3-choeh e5 i3-su3.  KIam2-chhai2 I ia7 u7 siuN7 kong2, an3-choaN2 Siong7-te3 to u7 hian2-chhut I e5 thiaN3, thai3 oe7 iu5-goan5 ti7 chit se3-kan u7 khou2-thang3, u7 choe7-ok ti7-teh, chit ho7 o3-biau7 e5 bun7-toe5, I un2-tang3 u7 mng7, ia7 ku2 kaN2.  Lan2 kiam2 m7-si7 chin ai3 thiaN I an3-choa2 lai5 mng7, ia7 an3-choaN2 lai5 in3 mah?  Siat-su2 chit e5 kou3-su7 na7-si7 u7 i3-su3, ai3 beh am3-si7, ti7 chit e5 Gin2-na2 Ia5-sou e5 seng-oah8 tiong e5 chit8 choan2-ki lai5 kong2, i2-siong7 lan2 sou2 teh siuN7 e5, sit8-chai7 si7 chin tiong7-iau3 e5 bun7-toe5.  Hok-im-su e5 tu3-chia2, eng-kai tioh8 ai3 sia2 beng5, put-ko3 Lou7-ka chi2-u7 si7 chai Ma2-li7-a sou2 chai e5 na7-tiaN7.  M7-ku2 Ma2-li7-a si7 tu2-tu2 in tam5-lun7 beh liau2 chiah jip8-khi3.  Lou7-ka si7 tui3 Ma2-li7-a lai5 tit-tioh8 chit e5 siau-sit.  Sou2-i2 chit e5 kou3-su7 thang kong2 si7 chin ui5-ham7, chin bo5 oan5-choan5 e5 kou3-su7.
	Lan2 si7 chhiat-chhiat ng3-bang7 hiah e5 khah lau2-lian7 e5 liap8-pi2 ti7-hia, u7-e5 beh u7 khui3-lat8 thang eng3 I e5 jiat8-jiat8 e5 su-siuN2 e5 iau3-kiu5.  Put-koan2 siaN2 khoan2, in khoaN3-liau2 si7 cham2-jian5 chhiN-kiaN I e5 chhang-mia5, chiu7 him-bou7 Ia5-sou lai5 tiam3 ti7 in e5 tiong-kan, lai5 thiaN lai5 mng7 teng2-teng2 e5 bun7-toe5, ti3-kau3 soa3 boe7 ki3-tit si5-kan tit8-tit8 teh ke3--khi3, ia7 Na2-sat-lek8 e5 sun5-le2-chia2, to long2 tng2-khi3 liau2.  Kau3 saN jit8 au7, Iok-sek kap Ma2-li7-a sim put-chi2 ju5-loan7, lai5 teh chhe7 I, au7-lai5 chhe7-tioh8 I ti7 tian7-nih8, “che7 ti7 hiah e5 sian-siN e5 tiong-kan, ia7 teh thiaN, ia7 teh mng7.”
	Hit-si5 Ma2-li7-a khoaN3-kiN3 I chiu7 “gong5-ngiah8,” toa7 bin7 si7 in-ui7 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 i hit e5 ui3-siau2-le2 e5 gin2-na2 Ia5-sou, u7 kap hiah e5 toa7 liap8-pi2 che7 choe3-he2 teh tam5-lun7.  Chong2-si7 lan2 thang phah-sng3, m7-si7 kan-ta in-ui7 an2-ni na7-tiaN7.  Ma2-li7-a u7 khoaN3-tioh8 chit e5 Gin2-na2 Ia5-sou chhin-chhiuN7 u7 hian2-chhut tam7-poh8 koh-iuN7 e5 iong5-mau7, I e5 bak8-chiu u7 hoat-chhut sin-iN7 e5 kong-chhai2 ti7-teh.  Ma2-li7-a si7 teh chhiN-kiaN, Ia5-sou un2-tang3 u7 keng-giam7--tioh8 sim2-mih8 ki5-iN7 e5 su7 chiah tioh8!
	Si7 lah!  Ia5-sou u7 keng-giam7--tioh8 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, I ka-ki7 e5 PoaN5-ke3-choeh, I e5 Pe7 e5 Seng3-tian7, kang2 pah ban7 lang5 phak-pai3 ti7 Siong7-te3 e5 bin7-cheng5, i2-kip8 kap liap8-pi2 saN-kap tam5-lun7 e5 cheng5-keng2.  Seng3-chheh tui3 ti7 lou7-be2 chit chan5 u7 put-chi2 khoaN3-tang7, sou2-i2 sui-jian5 bo5 ki3-chai3 kau3 loa7-nih8 siong5-se3, thang hou7 lan2 chai hit e5 cheng5-keng2, put-ko3 lan2 long2 bian2 giau5-gi5, chit e5 tai7-chi3 si7 I e5 chin iau3-kin2 e5 keng-giam7.  Put-koan2 siaN2-khoan2, chit e5 Gin2-na2 Ia5-sou ti7 i e5 sim-sin5 u7 tit-tioh8 sin-iN7 e5 keng-giam7 chiah tioh8.
	Seng3-chheh u7 ki3 Ia5-sou hu3 chit e5 thau5 chit8-pai2 e5 PoaN5-ke3-choeh e5 kou3-su7, lai5 phah-phoa3 I e5 siau3-lian5 si5-tai7, hit e5 tng5-tng5 thiam5-cheng7 e5 lek8-su2; khak-sit8 chit e5 kou3-su7 si7 u7 teh chi2-si7 I e5 seng-gai5 tiong e5 chit8 choan2-ki.

	Ma2-li7-a khian3-chek Ia5-sou, mng7 kong2, “KiaN2 ah, li2 siaN2-su7 khoan2-thai7 goan2 kau3 an2-ni mah?”  Chit ku3 kiam2 m7-si7 tong-jian5 e5 oe7 mah?  siat-su2 lai5 kong2, u7 sim2-mih8 hu7-jin5-lang5 hoan5-lo2 kui2-na7 jit8 ku2, lai5 chhe7 i sou2 sit-loh8 e5 soe3-kiaN2, sim-lai7 chhau3-sim-siuN7 tak8 teng2-ho7 e5 su7, au7-lai5 hut-jian5-kan chhe7-tioh8 i, khoaN3-kiN3 i e5 gin2-na2 sim-lai7 hoaN-hoaN hi2-hi2, long2 bo5 siuN7-tioh8 pe7-bu2 e5 kan-khou2, hit si5 choe3 pe7-bu2 e5 lang5, kiam2 m7-si7 tiaN7-tioh8 iu5-goan5 beh chiau3 an2-ni lai5 mng7 i e5 kiaN2 mah?  Choe3 lau7-bu2 e5 lang5 si7 chin kho2-lin5, su7-su7 si7 chin gau5 khoa3-lu7.  Ma2-li7-a si7 kap choe7-choe7 hu7-jin5-lang5 chit8 poaN, si7 boe7-oe7 li2-kai2 i e5 soe3-kiaN2 ti7 sim-lai7 sou2 teh oah8-tang7 e5 hit ho7 sin5-pi3 e5 su-siuN2.
	Ia5-sou tui3 I e5 lau7-bu2 sou2 in3 chit ku3 oe7, si7 lan2 thau5 chit8-pai2 thiaN-kiN3 I sou2 kong2 e5 oe7, u7 ki3-chai3 ti7 Seng3-chheh lai7 e5.  Tui3 I sou2 in3 chit ku3 oe7, hou7 lan2 thang chai, Ma2-li7-a sou2-siong5 u7 chaiN2-iuN7 eng7 sui2-sui2 e5 cheng-sin5 teh ka3-si7 Ia5-sou bat Pe7 Siong7-te3 e5 su7.  Chit ku3 u7 teh am3-si7, Ma2-li7-a toa7-bin7 si7 i2-keng u7 tui3 Ia5-sou kong2-khi2 I e5 sin5-pi3-tek e5 chhut-si3, i2-kip8 tui3 Siong7-te3 I sou2 u7 e5 tek8-piat8 e5 hoan-he7.  I chiu7-si7 in3 kong2, “SiaN2-su7 chhe7 goa2, kiam2 m7-chai goa2 eng-kai ti7 goa2 e5 Pe7 e5 chhu3 mah?”
	Chong2-si7 chit ku3 oe7, ki5-sit8 si7 iau2 u7 teh piau2-si7 koh khah chhim e5 i3-su3 ti7-teh.  I in3 an2-ni, si7 piau2-beng5 I i2-keng u7 sio2-khoa2 teh li7-khui Ma2-li7-a, si7 piau2-beng5 I u7 phau7 hit ho7 lian5 Ma2-li7-a to ia7-si7 boe7 thang li2-kai2 e5 su-siong2 ti7-teh.  Lan2 thang eng7 keng3-khian5 e5 liam7-thau5 lai5 chhui-siong2, chit-tiap8 Ia5-sou si7 i2-keng u7 thoat-chhut hit e5 Eng2-oan2 e5 se3-kai3 e5 poaN3 i3-sek e5 cheng-sin5 chong7-thai3, ti7 I e5 sim-lai7 i2-keng u7 kam2-chhiok--tioh8 chit8-sut-a2 e5 kng, lai5 beng5-pek8 I pun2-sin si7 u7 khah koh-iuN7 ti7 chiu-ui5 e5 lang5, u7 khah koh-iuN7 ti7 hiah e5 kap I choe3-he2 teh thit-tho5 e5 gin2-na2, i2-kip8 poe5-iuN2 I toa7-han3 e5 pe7-bu2.  Chit e5 Gin2-na2 Ia5-sou e5 cheng-sin5 e5 hoat-tat8, si7 chiam7-chiam7 e5 su7, lang5 sou2 boe7-thang khoaN3-kiN3 e5, si7 chhin-chhiuN7 chhun-thiN si5 e5 soe3-chang5 chhiu7 teh suh i e5 chhiu7-chiap khi2-lai5 teng2-bin7 chit8-poaN.  Khiok u7 si5 ti7 lang5 e5 cheng-sin5 e5 hoat-tat8-siong7, iu5-goan5 bat tu2-tioh8 choe7-choe7 pai2 e5 choan2-ki.  Lan2 na7-si7 hoe5-kou3 lan2 choe3 gin2-na2 e5 chong7-thai3, lan2 iu5-goan5 oe7 ki3-tit, kau3 ti7 chap8-ji7 he3 e5 tiong-kan, ma7-si7 u7 keng-giam7--tioh8 choe7-choe7 pai2 hit ho7 giam5-siok e5 choan2-ki, chiu7-si7 ti7 hit ho7 e5 si5-chun7, Siong7-te3 u7 ti7 am3-chiN7 e5 tiong-kan, lai5 hong2-bun7 lan2 siau3-lian5 lang5 e5 sim-sin5, ia7 lan2 e5 toa7-hiaN ma7 long2 m7-chai poaN3-hang7.  Chai7 hit ho7 phou2-thonglang5 e5 chap8-ji7 he3 e5 gin2-na2, to u7 hit khoan2 e5 keng-giam7, sou2-i2 lan2 khak-sin3, ti7 hit e5 u7 chong3-giam5 koh oe7 kam2-tong7 lang5 e5 PoaN3-ke3-choeh e5 chit8-chiu kan, chit e5 Sin5-tong5 Ia5-sou, si7 un2-tang3 tit-tioh8 chhim-chhim e5 keng-giam7 chiah tioh8.
	I e5 lau7-bu2 Ma2-li7-a tek-khak si7 u7 chit8-sut-a2 kan2-chhiok--tioh8 chit e5 su7-sit8, in-ui7 lan2 u7 thak8-tioh8 kong2, “In be7 hiau2-tit I sou2 ka7 in kong2 e5…..I e5 lau7-bu2 u7 chiong chiah e5 oe7 long2 ki3 ti7 sim-nih8.”  Chhin-chhiuN7 ti7 khah au7-lai5, lan2 sou2 oe7 thang khoaN3-kiN3 e5, lun7 I e5 lau7-bu2 e5 boe7-oe7 liau2-kai2 I e5 su7, ki5-sit8 m7-si7 kan-ta chit pai2 na7-tiaN7.  Ti7 khah au7-lai5 I put-si5 tioh8 kou-lip8, bo5 lang5 thang li2-kai2 I e5 sim-su, che si7 boe7 thang siam2-pi7 e5 su-sit8.  Chong2-si7 lian5 chit-tiap8, Ia5-sou to si7 tu2-chiah chap8-ji7 he3 na7-tiaN7, chiu7 i2-keng u7 sio2-khoa2 kam2-kak--tioh8 I e5 kou-tok8, bu5-liau5 e5 liam7-thau.  Che si7 Ia5-sou e5 kou-tok8 e5 seng-oah8 e5 khi2-goan5.
	Tui3 ti7 i2-siong7 sou2 kong2 chiah-e5, hou7 lan2 it-hoat ai3 chu3-i3 ti7 chit ku3 toe2-toe2 e5 oe7, chiu7-si7 kong2, “Ia5-sou chiu7 kap in loh8-khi3 kau3 Na2-sat-lek8, lai5 seng5-sun7 in.”  Siat-su2, Ia5-sou ia7 si7 chit8 e5 phou2-thong e5 chu7-jian5 lang5 e5 gin2-na2 lai5 kong2, chhin-chhiuN7 I hit ho7 u7 chhim-tim5 ko-siong7 e5 su-siuN2, i2-kip8 keng-giam7 ti7-teh, I un2-tang3 si7 khah bo5 i3-hiong3 ti7 hit ho7 bo5 chhu3-bi7 e5 hiong-chhoan e5 seng-oah8 chiah tioh8.  I kiam2 m7-si7 ai3 kap hiah e5 toa7 sian-siN saN-kap tiam3 ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 mah?  I kiam2 m7-si7 ai3 chu7 an2-ni tiam3 ti7 I e5 Pe7 e5 chhu3, lai5 hak8-sip8 choe3 “I e5 Pe7 e5 kang” e5 toa7 e5 ka3-si7 mah?  Siat-su2 I ko2-jian5 chu7 an2-ni tiam3 ti7-hia, bian2 giau5-gi5, lan2 ma2-si7 un2-tang3 oe7 siuN7-chhut choe7-choe7 ho2-thiaN koh keng3-khian5 e5 li2-iu5, thang lai5 pian7-beng5.  Chong2-si7 chit e5 Sin5-tong5 Ia5-sou chai, ia7 soa3 chi2-si7 lan2 chai, lang5 tan-sun5 lai5 sun7-hok8 pe7-bu2, chiong5-su7 hit ho7 bo5 khoaN3-oah8 e5 su7-giap8, ti7 Pe7 e5 bin7-cheng5 u7 si5 iau2 koh-khah si7 ko-siong7, sin5-seng3 e5 su7.  Lan2 si7 put-chi2 be7 jim2-siu7 jin5-seng bo5 khoaN3-oah8 e5 lou7-cham7; sou2-i2 khah ho2 lan2 tioh8 chai, hit khoan2 e5 lou7-cham7, si7 I sou2 beh tam-tng e5 thian-hun7.
	Chit-tiap8 chai7 Ia5-sou teh khoaN3, I e5 tan-sun5 e5 jit8-siong5 e5 seng-oah8, si7 teh choe3 “I e5 Pe7 e5 kang.”  In-ui7 I chit chun7, tu2-chiah si7 chap8-ji7 he3, ia7 I e5 tan-sun5 e5 ka-teng5 seng-oah8, i2-kip8 tui3 pe7-bu2 sou2 tioh8 chin7 e5 hau3-sun7, bo5 giau5-gi5, si7 choe3 ho2 e5 pi7-pan7, thang choe3 I chiong-lai5 e5 lou7-eng7.  Ti7 I e5 seng-oah8, bo5 u7 hui chu7-jian5 e5 keng-giam7, a2-si7 u7 thang hian2-chhut I si7 u7 toa7-lang5 e5 khi3-khai3, lai5 hou7 lang5 thiam2-mi7, a2-si7 kiaN-hiaN5 e5 khoan2-sit ti7-teh.  Chheng-lian5 e5 seng-oah8, i e5 hoat-tat8 si7 tioh8 u7 chu7-jian5, u7 kui-ku2, u7 khong-kian7, u7 oah8-khi3 e5 khoan2-sit.  Chit e5 choe3 Gin2-na2 e5 Ia5-sou, iu5-goan5 si7 ti7 bo5 lang5 chu3-i3--tioh8 e5 tiong-kan, chiam7-chiam7 lai5 tiong2-seng5 e5.  Toa7-bin7 chit-tiap8 I ma7-si7 m7-chai-iaN2 Siong7-te3 e5 i3-su3, si7 ai3 I ti7 au7-lai5 tioh8 chin7 I e5 gi7-bu7 lai5 chiau3-kou3 I e5 chiu2-koaN2 e5 lau7-bu2 Ma2-li7-a, sou2-i2 chiah lai5 in2-chhoa7 I khi3 tiam3 ti7 hit e5 phian-phiah e5 hiong-chhoan, lai5 hau3-sun7 I e5 si7-toa7-lang5 khah ke chap8-poeh ni5 ku2.  Chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni, ti7 I e5 sim-lai7 khng3 sin e5 bun7-toe5, ti7 I e5 bak8-chiu khng3 sin e5 ki5-koai3, chit e5 Gin2-na2 Ia5-sou u7 to3-tng2-khi3 in tau Na2-sat-lek8, ti7-hia lai5 tit-tioh8 hap8-gi5 e5 pi7-pan7, thang oan5-seng5 I lim5-kau3 se3-kan ui7-tioh8 lan2, i2-kip8 lan2 e5 Chin2-kiu3 e5 su7-giap8.



Te7-5 chi	uN	BAK8-CHHIUN7

	Lan2 chit-tiap8 sit8-chai7 si7 ai3 chin3-cheng5 lai5 siuN7 khah hng7 khi3 e5 su7.  Tui3 I to3-tng2-khi3 Na2-sat-lek8 liau2-au7, to i2-keng ke3-liau2 chap8-poeh ni5 ku2 lah.  Chong2-si7 lan2 ai3 koh chit8-pai2 lai5 khoaN3 I e5 kou3-hiong Na2-sat-lek8.  Chit e5 Sin5-tong5 Ia5-sou si7 i2-keng toa7-han3 seng5-lian5.  Iu7-koh hit e5 bak8-chhiuN7 Iok-han2, ma7-si7 i2-keng ke3-ong2.  Sou2-i2 hit e5 bo5 liau5 e5 koaN2-hu7 Ma2-li7-a, chhiu2 kan-ta pho7 i sou2 thiaN3 e5 KiaN2, put-si5 to na5-au5-kng2 tiN7, ti7-teh iu-chhiu5.  Ah!  Sit8-chai7 Ma2-li7-a tiam3 ti7 hit ho7 pi-siong e5 si5, Ia5-sou u7 thang tiam3 ti7 i e5 sin-piN si7 chin hok-khi3, ia7 m7 han7-tiaN7 ti7 chit-tiap8 na7-tiaN7, ti7 chiong-lai5 i tak8 pai2 kou-tok8 bo5 liau5 e5 si5, Ia5-sou u7 thang tiam3 ti7 i e5 sin-piN si7 chin ban7-heng7; in-ui7 Ia5-sou si7 chin gau5 hong7-iong2 I e5 lau7-bu2 Ma2-li7-a.  Li2 khoaN3, I sui-jian5 hou7 lang5 teng3 ti7 hit e5 chhiN-chham2 e5 Sip8-ji7-ke3 e5 si5, ia7-si7 ti3-i3 lai5 siau7-kai3 I e5 lau7-bu2 hou7 I sou2 chi3-chhin e5 hak8-seng Iok-han7, thang khoaN3-kou3 i, kong2, “Hu7-jin5-lang5 ah, khoaN3, li2 e5 kiaN2!  Koh tui3 hak8-seng kong2, khoaN3, li2 e5 lau7-bu2.”
	chiau3-khoaN3, Ia5-sou si7 u7 choe3 bak8 lai5 hong7-iong2 I e5 lau7-bu2 Ma2-li-a.  Kiam2-chhai2 I e5 hiaN-ti7 i2-kip8 chi2-be7 si7 long2 i2-keng hap8-hun liau2, sui-lang5 long2 u7 kian3-siat in sui-lang5 e5 ka-teng5.  Hiah e5 bat Ia5-sou e5 Na2-sat-lek8 lang5 u7 kan-cheng3 kong2, “Chit e5 kiam2 m7-si7 bak8-chhiuN7, Ma2-li7-a e5 kiaN2 mah?”  Chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni, lan2 thang siuN7, Ia5-sou ti7 be7 chhut-thau5 thoan5-kau3, siau3-lian5 e5 si5-tai7, si7 u7 chiaN5-choe3 chir8 e5 bak8-chhiuN7, lai5 than3 chiN5 hong7-iong2 I e5 chiu2-koaN2 e5 lau7-bu2 Ma2-li7-a.
	Chhi3-siuN7 Siong7-te3 e5 KiaN2, I e5 un-jiu5 kap khiam-sun3 kau3 chaiN2-iuN7!  Ia5-sou u7 chiaN5-choe3 chit8 e5 choe3 kang lang5, lai5 chin7 pun2-hun7 ti7 I e5 thau5-lou7, chiaN5-choe3 chit8 e5 bak8-chhiuN7, lai5 than3 chiN5 hong7-iong2 I e5 lau7-bu2 Ma2-li7-a.  Lan2 kiam2 m7-si7 ai3 chai-iaN2 Ia5-sou tui3 chit-giap8 kap kim-chiN5 si7 phau7 sim2-mih khoan2 e5 i3-kian3 mah?  ChhiaN2 lai5 siuN7 chit e5 bak8-chhiuN7 e5 tiam3, sou2 hian2-chhut e5 kui2-na7-hang7 e5 ka3-si7.  Ia5-sou si7 u7 choe3 gu5-le5-taN.  Lan2 thang khak-sin3, I sou2 choe3 e5, si7 put-chi2 ho2.  Hoan7-na7 u7 him-bou7 seng5-sit8, oe7 sin3-iong7 tit e5 chhiu2-lou7 e5 choh-sit lang5, un2-tang3 si7 ai3 beh lai5 chhe7 Ia5-sou, tui3 I boe2 in sou2 khiam3-eng7 e5 mih8 chiah tioh8.
	Chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni, Ia5-sou u7 ka3-si7 lan2 chai, ti7 Siong7-te3 e5 bin7-cheng5, u7 seng5-sit8 e5 lo5-tong7, sit8-chai7 si7 eng2-oan2 u7 ke3-tat8 ti7-teh.  Chu7-kou2 kip8-kim, lang5 long2 si7 khoaN3-khin chhou-kang.  Ia5-sou e5 chhu3-piN ma7-si7 thi2-chhio3 kong2, “Chit e5 kiam2 m7-si7 bak8-chhiuN7 mah?”  Cha2-si5 Ki-khe2-loh (Cicero) u7 kong2, “kun-bah lo5-tong7 e5 thau5-lou7 long2 si7 chhou-siok8, ha7-chian7.  Ti7 hit ho7 chhou-kang e5 sou2-chai7, bo5 u7 sim2-mih8 oe7 eng7-tit kio3-choe3 si7 ko-siong7 e5 su7 ti7-teh.”  Chhi3-siuN7, chit e5 choe3 chhouo-kang e5 Ia5-sou, u7 chaiN2-iuN7 hou7 it-chhe3 u7 seng5-sit8 e5 kang lai5 chiaN5-choe3 ko-siong7 e5 su7!  Sit8-chai7 hiah e5 che7 ti7 i2-nih8 teh choe3-bak8 e5 lang5, si7 thang  liah8 Ia5-sou choe3 in e5 Chu2 lai5 kap I kau-poe5.
	Ai3 lan2 ti7-chia lai5 chim-chiok siuN7, Ia5-sou chaiN2-iuN7 teh khoaN3 kim-chiN5 e5 bun7-toe5.  I tek-khak si7 u7 kau-chiap kim-chiN5 chiah tioh8.  I un2-tang3 si7 bat khi3 boe2 chha5-liau7, ia7 bat boe7 I sou2 choe3 e5 mih8-kiaN7, koh ma7-si7 bat ti7 tiam3-nih8 kap lang5-kheh boe2-boe7.  Sou2-i2 Ia5-sou u7 ka3-si7 lan2 chai, bo5 lun7 si7 choe3 sim2-mih8 khoan2 e5 seng-li2, kau3-giah8 si7 oe7 thang hou7 i chiaN5-choe3 seng3 e5 su7.  Chhiu2 theh8 kim-chiN5, to m7-si7 u7 pi2 giah8 ai3-kok e5 to-kiam3 khah ha7-chian7, iu7-koh siau3-kui7 ma7-si7 oe7 thang chheng-khi3, bo5 u7 chho3-gou7, thang chiaN5-choe3 Siong7-te3 e5 seng3-toaN5.
	ChhiaN2 koh ian5-chhian5 tiap-a2-ku2, lai5 siuN7 ti7 hit e5 kang-tiuN5 lai7 e5 chit-hang7 e5 su7-sit8.  Lan2 thang phah sng3 u7 choe7-choe7 soe3-soe3 han3 e5 gin2-na2, long2 m7-kiaN, ho2-taN2 jip8-khi3 hit e5 kang-tiuN5 khioh khau-to-hoe, ia7 hiah e5 gin2-na2 un2-tang3 chin thiaN3 Ia5-sou.  Tu2-tu2 si7 chiau3 Hok-im-su sou2 kong2, “Siong7-te3 kap lang5 long2 thiaN3 I.”  Lan2 khak-sin3, gin2-na2 si7 long2 chin thiaN3 I.  Iu7-koh chit e5 bak8-chhiuN7 Ia5-sou un2-tang3 ma7-si7 chin gau5 thiaN3 hiah e5 soe3-soe3 han3 e5 gin2-na2, ai3 in lai5 chhe7 I chiah tioh8.  Bo5 giau5-gi5, I un2-tang3 koaiN3-si3 gau5 kong2 ho2 thiaN e5 kou3-su7 hou7 in thiaN; in-ui7 ti7 au7-jit8 lan2 to u7 khoaN3-kiN3 I siong5-siong5 tui3 soe3-han3 gin2-na2 kong2-khi2 ho2 thiaN e5 kou3-su7, sou2-i2 lan2 oh-tit siuN7, I ti7 khah cha2 chit-tiap8, long2 m7-bat kong2-khi2.  Khak-sit8 u7 choe7-choe7 gin2-na2 lai5 ti7 I e5 kang-tiuN5 oe7 pi2 ti7 hoe7-tng5-nih8 sou2 beh siu7 e5 chong-kau3 kau3-iok8, si7 koh-khah u7 thang tit-tioh8 ka3-si7, lai5 chai-bat Siong7-te3 e5 thiaN3 kap I e5 chiau3-kou3.

	Ia5-sou e5 u7-pi7 e5 si5-kan, i2-keng pek-kun7 ti7 lou7-be2, hit si5 I e5 sim-lai7 u7 chun5 sim2-mih8 khoan2 e5 toa7 e5 su-siong2, lan2 m7-kaN2 chin3-cheng5 lai5 chhui-siong2.  Put-ko3, lan2 kan-ta thang phah-sng3, I ti7 jit8-si5 si7 che7 ti7 i2-nih8 teh choe3 bak8, kau3 mng2-pou, jit8 beh am3 e5 si5, chiu7 peh-chiuN7 khi3 Na2-sat-lek8 e5 soaN-lun5-a2 e5 teng2-bin7, ti7 hia thiam5-cheng7 lai5 bek8-siong2 I e5 o3-biau7 e5 chiong-lai5, kiam2-chhai2 ia7 chhin-chhiuN7 ti7 khah au7-lai5 e5 khoan2-sit, u7 tiam3 ti7 soaN-teng2, “thong-mi5 ki5-to2 Siong7-te3.”
	Lan2 thang siong2-siong7, I long2 bo5 teh koan-sim ti7 I pun2-sin e5 su7, long2 bo5 lang5 chit8-khek ku2, choan-choan ai3 kap I e5 Pe7 saN-kap kau-poe5.  Lan2 thang siuN7, I tak8-jit8 long2 u7 teh su-bou7 hiah e5 bat siu7 toa7 e5 kam2-tong7 e5 bong7-siong2 ka, si-ong, i2-kip I e5 tang5-chok8 e5 sian-ti lang5 e5 su7-chek.  Ti7 chiah e5 jit8, Ia5-sou lai5 siuN7 chit ho7 e5 su7 si7 chin hap8-gi5.  Lan2 na7 si7 u7 chhim-chhim lai5 siuN7 Ia5-sou chaiN2-iuN7 u7 chun-keng3 Ku7-iok e5 Seng3-chheh, chiu7 chi2-u7 tui3 an2-ni lan2 thang it-hoat siN-khi2 ai3 thak8 Seng3-chheh e5 sim.  I si7 chi2-u7 thang thak8 hit pun2 hian7-kim choe7-choe7 lang5 sou2 ai3 khoaN3-khin e5 Ku7-iok e5 Seng3-chheh.  I u7 chi2-si7 lan2 chai-iaN2 sim2-mih8 sou2-chai7 si7 Ku7-iok Seng3-chheh e5 bo5 oan5-choan5 e5 tiam2, soa3 in2-chhoa7 lan2 lai5 bat hit e5 khah ko-siong7 e5 i3-gi7.  Put-ko3 ti7 I e5 it-seng, Ku7-iok Seng3-chheh si7 choe3 I e5 kau3-iok8 e5 Seng3-chheh, ia7-si7 choe3 I e5 thoan5-to7 e5 Seng3-chheh.  I si7 u7 chan3-seng5 hit tiong-kan e5 kun-pun2 e5 to7-li2.  I si7 u7 chiap-lap8 Ku7-iok Seng3-chheh, khoaN3-choe3 si7 teh u7-pi7 I pun2-sin e5 chheh, ia7 ka3-si7 hak8-seng tioh8 tui3 Ku7-iok Seng3-chheh lai5 chhe7-chhut I e5 su7-sit8.  I si7 u7 eng7 Ku7-iok Seng3-chheh lai5 pian7-hou7 I e5 su2-beng7, soa3 lai5 chhian2-beng5 Sip8-ji7-ke3 e5 o3-biau7.  Put-tan3 si7 an2-ni, I u7 chiong hit e5 lai7-bin7 e5 to7-li2 lai5 iuN2-chhi7 I pun2-sin e5 cheng-sin5 seng-oah8, ia7 tak8-pai2 ti7 I e5 seng-oah8 e5 toa7 gui5-ki e5 si5, Ku7-iok Seng3-chheh si7 u7 choe3 I e5 khui3-lat8 lai5 hu5-chhi5 I; in-ui7 I si7 u7 seng5-jin7 Ku7-iok Seng3-chheh si7 Siong7-te3 e5 giam5-siok e5 Oe7.
	Chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni, hit e5 thiam5-cheng7 u7-pi7 e5 si5-kan, soa3-chiap tit8-tit8 ke3--khi3, kau3 “Ia5-sou chhut-thau5 e5 si5, iok-liok8 saN-chap8 he3.”  Kiat-kiok8 I e5 cheng-sin5 e5 choan2-ki si7 i2-keng kun7 lah, I e5 si5-ki5 si7 i2-keng kau3 lah!
	Tng hit-si5 ti7 choan5 Pa-lek8-su-theng3 e5 lang5 long2 u7 toa7 io5-choah, toa7 siu7 kam2-tong7.  In-ui7 hit e5 thiam5-cheng7 e5 gou7 se3-ki2 i2-keng ke3-khi3 liau2, ti7 chit-tiap8 u7 chit8 e5 sian-ti kio3-choe3 KiaN5 soe2-le2 e5 Iok-han7 u7 koh heng-khi2 ti7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 tiong-kan.  Cheng3-lang5 tai7-ke toa7-siaN long2 teh mng7 kong2, “Li2 si7 I2-li7-a mah?”  In-ui7 chiau3 Iu5-thai3 lang5 it-poaN e5 sin3-giong2, I2-li7-a si7 tioh8 koh lai5, ia7 I2-li7-a na7 lai5, hit-si5 in sou2 teh theng3-hau7 e5 Bi2-sai3-a si7 i2-keng kau3 ti7 mng5-khau2.
	KiaN5 soe2-le2 e5 Iok-han7, u7 chhim-chhim io5-choah hiah e5 teh theng3-hau7, teh liau5-bang7 e5 kok-bin5, lai5 tui3 in kong2, “Lin2 tioh8 hoan2-hoe2!  In-ui7 Bi2-sai3-a beh lai5 lah!  Siong7--te3 e5 kok kun7 lah!  goa2 si7 hong7-chhe ti7 I e5 bin7-cheng5, lai5 thoe3 I pi7-pan7 lou7.”
	Hit e5 siau-sit u7 io5-choah thoan5 kau3 ti7 Iok-tan3 goa7 chhit-chap8 eng-li2 e5 chiu-ui5.  Choe7-choe7 e5 hiong-chhoan lang5 long2 oe-oe khoeh-khoeh chu7-chip8 lai5 thiaN Iok-han7 sou2 kan-cheng3 e5 oe7, soa3 toa3 choe7-choe7 siau-sit tng2-khi3 sui5-lang5 e5 sou2-chai7.  Choan5 Na2-sat-lek8 e5 lang5 ma7-si7 long2 io5-choah khi2--lai5.  Tai7-ke long2 bo5 teh kong2 pat8-mih8 su7.
	Ia5-sou ma7 u7 thiaN-kiN3, koh u7 liau2-kai2 hit e5 i3-gi7.  Tui3 an2-ni, I ti7 chit8-am3 u7 choe3-au7, eng2-oan2 lai5 pang3-he7 choe3 bak8 e5 khi3-khu7.  Che chiu7-si7 hit e5 tng5-tng5 thiam5-cheng7 e5 u7-pi7 e5 si5-ki5 e5 chiong-be2.
	“Hit si5 Ia5-sou tui3 Ka-li7-li7 kau3 Iok-tan3, chiu7-kun7 Iok-han7, beh tui3 i siu7 soe2-le2.”


Te7  III Koan3 Thau5 Chit-Ni5


Te7-1 chiuN	Soe2-Le2

	Tiap-a2 tiap-a2(**tiap8-a2)-ku2 koh lai5 hoe5-kou3 ti7 saN-chap8 ni5 cheng5 e5 u7 chit8 jit8, Ma2-li7-a siu7 thiN-sai3 ko3-ti liau2-au7, “i u7 khi2-sin koaN2-kin2 khi3 soaN-toe7 Iu5-thai3 chit8 e5 siaN5, jip8 Sat-ka-li7-a e5 chhu3, chheng2-an I2-li7-sa-pek.  I2-li7-sa-pek chit8-e7 thiaN-kiN3 Ma2-li7-a chheng2-an, thai-in7 ti7 pak-tou2-lai7 e5 eN-a2 chiu7 tio5-thiau3, “ kah na2 chhin-chhiuN7 teh tui3 i e5 Chu2 piau2-si7 keng3-i3 chit8 poaN.”
	Chit nng7 e5 gin2-na2 si7 siang7 ti7 hit kui2 geh8-jit8 lai7 chhut-si3 e5.  Lan2 ti7 i2-cheng5 teh siuN7 tiam3 ti7 Na2-sat-lek8 iu3-lian5 e5 Ia5-sou, hit-si5 lan2 u7 hut-liok8, bo5 siuN7-tioh8 ti7 Hi-pek-lun5 soaN-teng2 hit e5 lau7 che3-si e5 chhu3-lai7, iau2 hit e5 gin2-na2 e5 su7.
	Ti7 lan2 e5 Chu2 e5 toan7-ki3 e5 tiong-kan, Iok-han7 si7 put-chi2 tiong7-iau3 e5 jin5-but8.  I si7 ti7 hit e5 tng5-tng5 e5 sian-ti e5 lek8-su2 tiong choe3 au7 e5 sian-ti, put-chi2 tu3-hian7 koh kou-tok8, chhin-chhiuN7 soaN-chiam chhut-hian7 ti7 I2-sek-liat8 ke3-khi3 e5 lek8-su2 e5 chui2-peng5 soaN3-bin7, lai5 kan-cheng3 Siong7-te3 e5 Chi2-i3, soa3 chi2-si7 Chu2 teh-beh lai5 e5 Jit8.
	Iok-han7 si7 kau3-giah8 ui2-tai7, tu2-tu2 chiau3 Ia5-sou sou2 kong2, hu7-jin5-lang5 sou2 siN e5, chiong5-tiong be7 u7 heng-khi2 khah toa7 ti7 KiaN5 soe2-le2 e5 Iok-han7; i si7 thang hou7 lan2 eng7 choan5 chit8 chiuN, a2-si7 kui2-na7 chiuN lai5 kang2-lun7 i e5 su7-chek.  Chong2-si7 lan2 ti7-chia boe7 thang an2-ni choe3, lan2 e5 bak8-chiu tioh8 si5-siong5 chu3-bak8 ti7 hit e5 tiong-sim e5 jin5-but8.  Hit e5 i2-goa7, kan-ta ai3 choe3 hit e5 siong7 e5 lou7-eng7, lai5 sio2-khoa2 bio5-sia2 chiu7 kau3-giah8.  U7 thiaN-kiN3 kong2, bou2 ui2-tai7 e5 ge7-sut8 ka, bat oe7 Choe3-au7 e5 Boan2-chhan e5 tou5, ti7 hit-si5 na7 u7 lang5 oa2--lai5, chi2-u7 chu3-bak8 ti7 hiah e5 kek8 sio2-khoa2 bi2-biau7 e5 tiam2; i chiu7 chek-si5 eng7 chhat-pit lai5 chhat hit ui7 khi2--lai5, in-ui7 lian5 tiap-a2(**tiap8-a2)-ku2 to ia7 m7-ai3 lang5 bo5 chu3-i3--tioh8 Ki-tok e5 siong7.
	Lun7 Ia5-sou e5 siau3-lian5 si5-tai7, lan2 bo5 sim2-mih8 chai, chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni lun7 Iok-han7 e5, lan2 ia7 si7 koh-khah m7-chai.  Chit nng7 lang5 e5 u7-pi7 si5-tai7 si7 khah koh-iuN7.  Lun7 Ki-tok, I si7 kap lan2 choan5-jian5 siang7 khoan2, chhin-chhiuN7 lan2 tai7-ke e5 chit8 e5, kap tak8 teng2-ho7 e5 lang5 choe3-he2 siu7 iong2-iok8, bit8-chiap ti7 hiong-chhoan e5 seng-oah8.  Chong2-si7 chit e5 pi-chian7 e5 sian-hong, si7 ti7 kou-tok8 e5 tiong-kan lai5 tiong2-seng5 e5.
	Lan2 thang siong2-siong7, i si7 chit8 e5 thiam5-cheng7, kou-tok8 e5 gin2-na2, chhin-chhiuN7 lang5 ti7 ni5-lau7 sou2 tit-tioh8 e5 kou-kiaN2 chit8 poaN, su7-su7 khah cha2 u7 toa7-lang5 e5 khi3-khai3, si7 bo5 hiaN-ti7, bo5 chi2-be7, bo5 thit-tho5 phoaN7,  a2-si7 peng5-iu2, kan-ta tui3 pe7-bu2 lai5 hiau2-ngou7 pun2-sin e5 thian-chit, sim-lai7 ai3 thiam5-cheng7, ai3 ka-ki7 chit8 lang5, ti7 kui2-na7 jit8 e5 tiong-kan, si3-koe3 kiaN5 ti7 soaN-ia2 hiong-chhoan, lai5 chhim-su lai5 bek8-siong2 teng2-teng2 e5 tai7-chi3.
	Ti7 seng5-lian5 si5-tai7, lan2 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 i si7 choe3 chit8 e5 un2-su7, khia7-khi2 ti7 soaN-kan, li7 hng7-hng7 bo5 lang5 sou2 kau3 e5 sou2-chai7; si7 chit8 e5 jiat8-sim ka, u7 bong7-siong2 ka e5 gan2-kong ti7-teh; si7 chit8 e5 kim3-iok8 ka, pun2-sin bo5 kap lang5 lian5-lok8, ku7-choat8 hap8-gi5 e5 khoai3-lok8, lai5 kim3-chiah8, chham2-hoe2, khek-ki2, chheng7 lok8-to5 mng5, chiah8 soaN-ia2 e5 chhau2-meh kap ia2-bit8.
