I put-si5 to-teh bek8-siong2 i e5 tang5-chok8 cheng3 sian-ti lang5 e5 oe7, chiu7-si7 Siong7-te3 chioh in e5 chhui3 lai5 thoan5 hou7 cheng3-lang5 e5.  In e5 giam5-siok e5 seng-oah8, in teh khian3-chek lang5 e5 choe7-ok, kio3-chhiN2 lang5 hoan2-hoe2, si7 put-chi2 u7 lat8, oe7 giu2 i hit ho7 seng3-chit e5 lang5 e5 sim.  Chong2-si7 che tui3 ti7 cheng3 sian-ti e5 chheh tiong, sou2 oe7 toat8 i e5 sim-sin5 hit ho7 tiong-sim su-siong2 lai5 khoaN3, put-ko3 si7 chhin-chhiuN7 hit e5 goa7-heng5 e5 kun2-ian7 ji5-i2.  Ki5-sit8 hit e5 su-siong2 e5 o3-biau7 e5 he7-thong2, koan3-chhoan3 ti7 poeh se3-ki2 cheng3 sian-ti e5 tiong-kan e5, si7 teh ng3-bang7 chit8 e5 Ng5-kim e5 Si5-tai7, Siong7-te3 kok e5 lim5-kau3, si7 teh ng3-bang7 ti7 chiong-lai5 u7 chit8 jit8, beh u7 chit8 e5 ui2-tai7 sou2 beh lai5--e5 e5 lim5-kau3.  I u7 tui3 cheng3 sian-ti e5 chham3-gu2. lai5 chou-chit i chiong-lai5 e5 ng3-bang7.  Chong2-si7 chin oh-tit e5 su7.  In-ui7 u7 khun3-lan5, hok8-chap8, saN mau5-tun2 e5 sou2-chai7 ti7-teh.  Phi3-ju7 lai5 kong2, lian5 I2-sai3-a e5 chheh, si7 i sou2 te7-it hoaN-hi2 e5, iu5-goan5 boe7 thang pang-chan7 i kau3 loa7-choe7.  In-ui7 hit e5 chheng-hou kio3-choe3 “Sin5-biau7 e5, Bou5-su7 e5, Chi3-koaiN5 e5 Siong7-te3, I e5 kok heng-ong7, eng2-eng2 thai3-peng5” e5 Bi2-sai3-a, iu5-goan5 si7 tioh8 “hou7 lang5 che3-ap, chhin-chhiuN7 iuN5 hou7 lang5 khan beh khi3 thai5, Ia5-ho5-hoa hou7 lan2 choe7-ok chek-moa2 i e5 sin.”  Sit8-chai7 si7 hok8-chap8 e5 bun7-toe5.  Lun7 Hit e5 sou2 beh lai5 e5 Bi2-sai3-a e5 su7!
	I chai pun2-sin si7 chin ki5-biau7, kap Hit e5 sou2 beh lai5 e5 u7 saN koan-lian5 ti7-teh.  Lan2 bian2 giau5-gi5, i e5 lau7-pe7 un2-tang3 m7 ka7 i kong2, ti7 i beh chhut-si3 e5 si5, thiN-sai3 sou2 po3 e5 siau-sit, chiu7-si7 kong2, “i beh eng7 I2-li7-a e5 sim-sin5 kap chai5-leng5 kiaN5 choe3-thau5 ti7 Chu2 e5 bin7-cheng5.”  Chit ku3 oe7, chai7 i si7 put-chi2 u7 giam5-siok e5 i3-su3 ti7-teh.  In-ui7 i chai, cha2 e5 sian-ti lang5 u7 chham3-gu2 kong2, “Goa2 beh chhe-khian2 I2-li7-a ti7 I e5 bin7-cheng5.”  Chhin-chhiuN7 it-poaN e5 lang5 choe3 si teh gim5 e5 khoan2, i chhim chai “u7 chit8-jit8, I2-li7-a beh koh-chai3 lai5, iah8 i na7 chhut-hian7, hit si5 Bi2-sai3-a chiu7 kiaN5 kau3 ti7 mng5-khau2.”  Bo5 ki5-koai3, chai7 chit e5 lang5 teh khoaN3, jin5-seng si7 giam5-siok, chin-kiam3 e5 su7.  Kau3 u7 theng5-tou7, i i2-keng u7 kam2-kak pun2-sin e5 thian-hun7, tiaN7-tioh8 si7 tioh8 choe3 Bi2-sai3-a e5 chiu2-kiN peng, iah8 i i2-keng u7 koan-sim teh ng3-bang7, teh theng3-hau7 I “chhin-chhiuN7 chiu2-kiN e5 lang5, ng3-bang7 thiN-kng.”
	Lan2 put-chi2 chu3-bak8 i hit ho7 pi-chham2 e5 heng5-chong7; sou2 chheng7 si7 hit ho7 chhou-ia2 e5 i-chiuN5, sou2 tiam3 si7 ti7 Si2-hai2, bo5 lang5 kau3 e5 sou2-chai7.  Put-si5 tioh8 kou-tok8 , lai5 teh su-siong2 i e5 khun3-lan5 e5 bun7-toe5, siong5-siong5 tu2-tioh8 giau5-gi5 kau3 sit-chi3, lai5 cheng-chian3 ti7 i e5 sim-lai7.  Bo5 chit8 lang5 beh bian2-le7 i, chheng-chan3 i.  Ki5-sit8 i choan5-jian5 bo5 kou3-tioh8 ka-ki7.  “Goa2 chi2-u7 si7 ti7 khong3-ia2 teh kio3 e5 e5 siaN.”  I bo5 ui7-tioh8 pun2-sin lai5 tou(**tou5)-bou5 sim2-mih8, ia7 bo5 tit-tioh8 sim2-mih8.  I put-ko3 si7 khui-mng5 hou7 pat8-lang5 jip8 na7-tiaN7.  I si7 ui2-tai7 e5 lang5, teh ka7 lang5 kiaN5 soe2-le2, chong2-si7 ka-ki7 koat-toan3 m7-bat siu7 soe2-le2.  I bo5 thang chhin-chhiuN7 pat8-lang5 thang tit-tioh8 kap Ia5-sou saN kau-poe5 e5 khoai3-lok8.  Pat8-lang5 long2 teh jip8 ti7 i sou2 soan-thoan5 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 kok, iau2-ku2 ti7 hit si5, i tioh8 siu7-hai7 ti7 kaN-gak8 e5 lai7-bin7.
	Sit8-chai7 i si7 pi-chham2, kou-tok8 e5 lang5.  Chong2-si7 Siong7-te3 khah siong5 si7 chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni teh hun3-lian7 i choe3-toa7 e5 sian-ti i2-kip8 soat-kau3-chia2.  Tui3 ti7 i e5 thiam5-cheng7, tan-sun5, sin3-giong2 Siong7-te3 e5 sim, u7 pang-chan7 i thiat-toe2 lai5 jiat8-sim, khak-sin3 i e5 su2-beng7, soa3 choan5-jian5 bo5 kiaN lang5 e5 bin7-sek, tui3 an2-ni hou7 i chiaN5-choe3 hap8-gi5, lai5 pi7-pan7 i e5 Chu2 e5 lou7 e5 lang5.  Tui3 ti7 i e5 thiam5-cheng7 e5 seng-oah8, hou7 i u7 it-hoat kam2-kak Siong7-te3 u7 sit8-chai7 ti7-teh, hou7 i it-hoat beng5-pek8 Bi2-sai3-a sou2 tui3 hia lai5 hit e5 Bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 e5 se3-kai3.
	Kiat-kiok8 i e5 si5 i2-keng kau3.  Lan2 u7 thak8-tioh8 kong2, “The5-pi2-liu5 Kai-sat che7-ui7 e5 chap8-gou7 ni5, pun2-tiu Pi2-liap8-to, choe3 Iu5-thai3 e5 chong2-tok, Hi-lut8 choe3 Ka-li7-li7 hun-hong e5 jin5-kun, i e5 hiaN-ti7 Hui-lek8 choe3 I2-thou2-li7-a kap Pek-liap8-kho2-ni5 toe7-hng hun-hong e5 jin5-kun, Lu7-sat-liap8 choe3 A-pi2-ni5 hun-hong e5 jin5-kun, A-na2 kap Kai-a-hoat choe3 che3-si-thau5 e5 si5, Sat-ka-li7-a e5 kiaN2 Iok-han7 ti7 khong3-ia2-nih8, Siong7-te3 e5 oe7 kau3 ti7 i.  I chiu7 kau3 Iok-tan3 ho5 e5 si3-hng, thaon5 hoan2-hoe2 e5 soe2-le2, hou7 lang5 tit-tioh8 sia3-choe7, chhin-chhiuN7 sian-ti I2-sai3-a e5 chheh sou2 ki3 e5 oe7 kong2, U7 teh kio3 ti7 khong3-ia2 e5, i e5 siaN kong2: Pi7-pan7 Chu2 e5 lou7, siu tit8 I e5 sio2-lou7.

	Iok-han7 sou2 chiap-chhiok--tioh8 e5, long2 si7 chhiN-chham2, siu7 jiu2-lin2 e5 peh-siN3.  Hiah e5 oan3-hun7 in e5 lang5 e5 chhiu2, u7 chin chan5-jim2 khoa3 ti7 in e5 keng-thau5 teng2.  Tu2-chiah sou2 in2-khi2 hiah e5 lang5-mia5, long2 u7 hian2-chhut hit e5 cheng5-heng5.  The5-li2-liu5 Kai-sat  si7 chit8-e5 choan-che3 e5 jin5-kun.  Pun2-tiu Pi2-liap8-to si7 pi2 i2-cheng5 e5 cheng3-hu2 koh khah gau5 biau2-si7 in it-chhe3 e5 chong-kau3 siong7 e5 bun7-toe5.  Che3-si-thau5 bo5 chin7-chit, siu7 it-poaN kong-jian5 e5 hui2-pong3, toa7 to-sou3 e5 bin5-chiong3 iu5-goan5 si7 oh-tit thang ng3-bang7 u7 sim2-mih8 khah ho2 e5 sou2-chai7.  Peh-siN3 kap che3-si si7 long2 siang7-khoan2.  Pa-lek8-su-theng3 si7 i2-keng song3-sit i e5 ng3-bang7.  Cha2-si5 I2-sek-liat8 e5 cheng-sin5 si7 i2-keng si2--khi3.  Hit e5 oah8-mia7 e5 i5-it e5 ki3-ho7, chi2-u7 hian2-chhut ti7 pak-peng5 hiah e5 Kok-chui7 tong2, i2-kip8 ti7 Ka-li7-li7 hit e5 chu7-iu5 e5 soaN-toe7 sou2 u7 hiah e5 chok-loan7 e5 Tok8-lip8 tong2 e5 tiong-kan; in e5 sim oan3-hun7 goa7-kok lang5, lai5 choe3-thau5 koan2-hat in, soa3 teh ng3-bang7 cha2-si5 Ia5-ho5-hoa choe3 in e5 Ong5, hit e5 seng7-tai7 e5 jit8 e5 sit8-hian7.  Chin7-chai7 chhu3-bi7 e5, chiu7-si7 oe7 thang khoaN3-kiN3 ti7 hiah e5 poan7-tou5 e5 tiong-kan, u7 chit8 e5 si7 Ia5-sou e5 hiaN-ti7, kio3-choe3 Se-bun5, tui3 an2-ni lang5 chheng i si7 Jiat8-sim tong2 e5 Se-bun5.  Chiah e5 lang5 put-si5 si7 hou7 cheng3-hu2 sou2 teh chhau-hoan5 e5.  In ai3 eng7 to-kiam3 lai5 heng-khi2 goa7-heng5 e5 Siong7-te3 kok, ki5-sit8 hoan7-na7 kiah8-to e5, beh tui3 to lai5 si2.  Chong2-si7 in koat-toan3 bo5 loe2-chi3, ng3-bang7 ti7 u7 chit8-jit8 Siong7-te3 e5 kok tek-khak beh sit8-hian7.
	Ti7 hit ho7 chhiN-chham2 e5 chong7-thai3, hit khoan2 ng3-bang7, chiau3-khoaN3 si7 ki5-iN7 e5 su7, iau2-ku2 si7 u7 khui-khoah pian3-thoan5 ti7 cheng3 peh-siN3 e5 tiong-kan.  Tu2-chiah khiok goa2 u7 sia2 kong2, “Cha2-si5 I2-sek-liat8 e5 cheng-sin5 si7 i2-keng si2--khi3.”  Chong2-si7 che si7 kan-ta chiau3 sou2 khoaN3 e5 i3-su3 na7-tiaN7.  Tui3 piau2-bin7 lai5 khoaN3, si7 i2-keng si2--khi3, si7 siu7 lang5 ap-pek, iau2-ku2 si7 chhin-chhiuN7 tang-thiN si5 sng-seh teng2 kou-ta5 e5 chhiu7 chit8-poaN, ti7 hit e5 e7-bin7 u7 chhim-chhim kiong5-tai7 e5 ng3-bang7, ai3 tit-tioh8 chiong-lai5 e5 chin2-kiu3 ti7-teh.  Hit e5 ng3-bang7, kiN3-na7 u7 tu2-tioh8 sim2-mih8 tut8-jian5 e5 chhi3-kek e5 si5, si7 oe7 chin2-chok kau3 ti7 tak8 lang5 e5 sim-toe2.
	Ti7 I2-sek-liat8 lek8-su2 tiong, te7-it tu3-hian7 koh si7 te7-it thang chhiN-kiaN e5, chiu7-si7 ti7 chit e5 si5-tai7, choan5 Iu5-thai3 e5 se3-kai3, sou2 hian2-chhut hit e5 thiam5-cheng7, koh kin2-tiuN ti7-teh ki5-thai7 e5 cheng-sin5.  Be7 u7 sim2-mih8 kok-bin5 ti7 in e5 lek8-su2, bat hian2-chhut chhin-chhiuN7 Bi2-sai3-a  tu2-tu2 beh lim5-kau3, hit-si5 e5 Iu5-thai3-kau3 sou2 hian2-chhut e5 hian7-siong7, hiah gau5 giu2 lang5 e5 sim, hou7 lang5 chhiN-kiaN.  In-ui7 siang7 lou7-be2 teh kan-cheng3 Hit e5 sou2 beh lai5--e5, e5 sian-ti e5 chham3-gu2, i2-keng ke3-liau2 gou7-pah ni5 ku2, ti7 hit tiong-kan ia7 long2 iau2-be7 u7 sim2-mih8 tong7-cheng7.
	Tng hit-si5, lan2 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 KiaN5 soe2-le2 Iok-han7 chhou-chhou chhut-thau5, “cheng3-lang5 sim-lai7 chiu7 teh gi7-lun7, Iok-han7 kiam2-chhai2 si7 Ki-tok.”  Lan2 ia7 u7 thiaN-kiN3 cheng3-lang5 te7-it tai7-seng jiat8-jiat8 lai5 mng7 i kong2, “ChhiaN2 ka7 goan2 kong2, Li2 si7 I2-li7-a lai5 beh pi7-pan7 lou7 e5 mah?  Li2 si7 Ki-tok mah?  Li2 si7 hit e5 sou2 beh lai5 e5 mah?”  Chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni, lan2 oe7 kam2-kak lan2 si7 khia7-khi2 ti7 chit8 e5 jiat8-chhiat teh ng3-bang7 e5 khong-khi3 e5 tiong-kan.
	Tu2-tu2 ti7 chit e5 si5-chun7, hut-jian5 tui3 khong3-ia2 u7 siaN au5-kio3 kong2, “Siong7-te3 e5 kok kun7 lah!”
	Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 u7 chiam7-chiam7 io5-choah khi2--lai5.  U7 chin thang chhiN-kiaN e5 hong-bun5, chhin-chhiuN7 tui3 khong-tiong teh khi2.  Ti7-chia ti7-hia long2 teh tam5-lun7 hit e5 khia7-khi2 ti7 soaN-kan e5 seng3-chia2, hit e5 o3-biau7 e5 jin5-but8, i oan2-jian5 si7 chhin-chhiuN7 it-poaN e5 lang5 sou2 teh liau5-bang7 e5 I2-li7-a, sou2 chheng7 si7 Lok8-to5-mng5, sou2 ha5 ti7 io-nih e5, si7 phe5-e5 toa3.  U7 lang5 u7 tu2-tioh8 hiah e5 ti7 soaN-tiuN5 thiaN-kiN3 Iok-han7 kong2 to7-li2 e5.  Au7-lai5 ti7 tiap-a2(**tiap8-a2)-ku2 e5 tiong-kan, ti7 siaN5-nih8 u7 siu7 kam2-tong7 e5 siaN teh hoat-chhut, au5-kio3 kong2, “Goan2 u7 thiaN-kiN3, u7 khoaN3-kiN3 i.  I si7 I2-li7-a koh to3-tng2 lai5!  I teh khian3-chek lan2 e5 choe7!  I teh kio3-chhiN2 lang5 tioh8 hoan2-hoe2!  I teh thoan5-po3 Siong7-te3 e5 kok!  I teh kong2-khi2 koan-he7 Hit e5 sou2 beh lai5 e5, e5 chhiN-kiaN e5 su7!”

	Ti7 chit geh8-jit8 e5 tiong-kan, choan5 Iu5-thai3 toe7 long2 io5-choah khi2--lai5.  Ti7 tak8 tiau5 lou7 oe-oe khoeh-khoeh, u7 choe7-choe7 sun5-le2-chia2, koaN2-kin2 beh khi3 Iok-tan3-ho5 chiu7-kun7 i, chiu7-si7 u7 ta-pou, cha-bou2, u7 siaN5-nih8 lang5, hiong-chhoan lang5, u7 seng-li2 lang5, u7 thiu-hiong3 e5, u7 pou7-peng, u7 choh-sit lang5, u7 keng-hak8-su7, u7 liap8-pi2.  Chiu7-si7 ke3-liau2 ku2-ku2 Ia5-sou ia7 iau2 u7 koh the5-khi2 hit si5 lang5 chaiN2-iuN7 siu7 kam2-tong7, chin3-cheng5 kau3 Iok-tan3 e5 cheng5-keng2, kong2, “Lin2 cheng5 chhut-khi3 khong3-ia2, beh khoaN3 sim2-mih8?”

	Pa-lek8-su-theng3 chit-tiap8 si7 chin giam5-siok, siu7 kam2-tong7 e5 si5-chun7.  Hit e5 hian7-siong7 si7 chhin-chhiuN7 lan2 sou2 bat keng-giam7--ke3.  Ti7 Ui2-lek8-su7 (Wales), Ai3-ni2-lan5 (Ireland), i2-kip8 ti7 Bi2-kok (America), bat u7 choe7-choe7 pai2 khoaN3-kiN3 hit ho7 siu7 kam2-tong7 kau3 oe7 thiu-choah e5 hian7-siong7, ti7 kui2 na7 geh8-jit8 e5 tiong-kan, ti7 tak8 sou2-chai7 long2 si7 thiaN-kiN3 lang5 teh hoan2-hoe2, teh ki5-to2, long2 si7 teh chong-kau3 kong5.  Au7-lai5 hit e5 kam2-tong7 liam5-piN bo5--khi3, kiat-kiok8 m7-si7 u7 loa7-nih8 ku2-tng5 e5 kong-hau7 ti7-teh.
	Chong2-si7 ti7 chit nng7 chan5 e5 tiong-kan, ia7 u7 toa7 cheng chha ti7-teh.  Iok-han7 m7-si7 kan-ta kio3 lang5 lai5 hoan2-hoe2 na7-tiaN7.  Koh chin3 chit8 pou7 chiu7-si7 chiong chit e5 hoan2-hoe2 beh choe3 hit e5 sou2 beh lai5 e5 toa7 e5 su7-kiaN7 e5 pi7-pan7, chhin-chhiuN7 cha2-si5 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 ti7 Se-nai2-soaN ka-ki7 chheng-khi3, pi7-pan7 sim lai5 thiaN Siong7-te3 e5 siaN chit8 poaN.  Chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni, Iok-han7 kio3 lang5 hoan2-hoe2, si7 bit8-chiap koan-lian5 ti7 Bi2-sai3-a e5 chhut-hian7, sou2-i2 Iu5-thai3 lang5 u7 chit8 ku3 siok8-gu2 teh kong2, “siat-su2 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 na7 u7 chit8 jit8 sit8-chai7 hoan2-hoe2, Tai7-pit8 e5 kiaN2 un2-tang3 beh lim5-kau3.”
	Chit e5 soat-kau3-chia2 Iok-han7, eng7 giam5 e5 oe7 toa7 siaN au5-kio3 kong2, “Lin2 tioh8 hoan2-hoe2, in-ui7 Siong7-te3 e5 kok kun7 lah.  Lin2 phah-sng3 chit e5 teh-beh lai5 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 kok, si7 khin-khoai3 e5 su7 mah?  Lin2 phah-sng3 lin2 tiam3 ti7 bo5 hoan5-lo2 an-jian5 e5 chong7-thai3, ka-ki7 i2-keng pi7-pan7 pian7 lah mah?  Lin2 tioh8 hoan2-hoe2!  Lin2 tioh8 hoan2-hoe2!  Chit-tiap8 si7 lin2 e5 bin5-chok8 e5 choan2-ki.  Pou2-thau5 si7 i2-keng he7 ti7 chhiu7-thau5.  KiN3-na7 chhiu7 bo5 kiat ho2 ke2-chi2 e5, chiu7 chho3 i, hiat loh8 he2.  Tioh8 pang3-sak lin2 e5 ke2-ho2, ke2-choe3, bo5 seng5-sit8 e5 sim!  Tioh8 kiat-hap8 ti7 hoan2-hoe2 e5 ke2-chi2.  In-ui7 Bi2-sai3-a teh-beh lai5.  I e5 chhiu2 theh8 poa3-ki, beh chiong I hit-tiuN5 e5 beh8 it-chin7 poa3, siu i jip8-chhng; chong2-si7 beh8-hiuN7 chiu7 eng7 be7 hoa e5 he2 sio i.  Boh8-tit ka-ki7 phah-sng3 kong2, U7 A-pek-liap8-han2 choe3 goan2 e5 Pe7; in-ui7 Siong7-te3 oe7 tui3 chiah e5 chioh8-thau5 chhut kiaN2-sun hou7 A-pek-liap8-han2.”
	Iok-han7 koh kan-cheng3, kong2, “M7-si7!  Goa2 m7-si7 Bi2-sai3-a.  Goa2 m7-si7 sian-ti.  Goa2 chiu7-si7 teh kio3 ti7 khong3-ia2 e5, i e5 siaN kong2, ‘Siu-tit8 Chu2 e5 lou7.  I i2-keng khia7-khi2 ti7 lin2 tiong-kan, lin2 m7-bat I.  I chiu7-si7 te3-be2 goa2 lai5 e5, chiu7 thau2 I e5 oe5-toa3, goa2 iah8 boe7 kham-tit.  Goa2 chi2-u7 hong7-chhe lai5 pi7-pan7 lin2 e5 sim, thang kui ti7 I, sou2-i2 goa2 lai5 eng7 chui2 ka7 lin2 kiaN5 soe2-le2, hou7 lin2 hoan2-hoe2; chong2-si7 I beh eng7 Seng3 Sin5, eng7 he2 ka7 lin2 kiaN5 soe2-le2.”
	Iok-han7 tui3 chit8 sou2-chai7 soa2 ke3 chit8 sou2-chai7, sun7 hit tiau5 ho5 tit8-tit8 chiuN7 pak khi2--khi3, iau2-ku2 jit8-jit8 na2 ke-thiN kui toa7 tin7 e5 lang5 lai5 te3 i.  I kau3 chit8 sou2-chai7 kio3-choe3 Pek-tai7-ni5, li7 Na2-sat-lek8 u7 ji7-chap8 eng-li2 e5 lou7, hit-si5 u7 chit8 e5 thiam5-cheng7 siau3-lian5 e5 Na2-sat-lek8 e5 hiong-chhoan lang5, tui3 soaN-lou7 tit8-tit8 loh8--khi3 khia7 ti7 cheng3-lang5 e5 tiong-kan, lang5 long2 bo5 chu3-i3--tioh8.
	Hit jit8 Ia5-sou sou2 khoaN3-kiN3 e5, si7 chit e5 cheng5-keng2.  Chiu7-si7 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 chit e5 jiat8-sim ka, i e5 bak8-chiu u7 beng5-liang7, bin7-mau7 ia3-lan2, khia7 ti7 hoaN7-teng2 lai5 thou2-lou7 i e5 sim-pak.  Ti7 i e5 sin-piN u7 kui toa7 tin7 siu7 kam2-tong7 e5 peh-siN3, chiong5-tiong u7 e5 si7 teh kong2 ki-chhi3 e5 oe7, u7-e5 si7 teh mng7, u7-e5 si7 sim-lai7 hun7-loan7 teh ki5-koai3, toa7-pou7-hun7 e5 lang5 si7 chim3 ti7 chong-kau3 kam2-cheng5 e5 pho-long7 tiong, na5-au5-kng2 tiN7, lai5 hoe2-gou7 in e5 choe7-ok.  Hit jit8 kek8 toa7 tin7 e5 lang5 chu7-chip8, chiau3 sou2 ki3-chai3 e5 kong2, “Hit-si5 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, thong Iu5-thai3, i2-kip8 Iok-tan3 ho5 e5 si3-hng e5 cheng3-lang5 chhut-lai5, chiu7-kun7 i; ti7 Iok-tan3 ho5 tui3 i siu7 soe2-le2, jin7 in e5 choe7.”  Che si7 Ia5-sou hit jit8 sou2 khoaN3-kiN3 e5 cheng5-keng2.
	Jit8 ke3 jit8, I chu3-bak8 khoaN3 in.  Ji5-hou7 tng u7 chit8 jit8 cheng3-lang5 e5 soe2-le2 long2 chheng-chho2, Iok-han7 ka-ki7 teh khia7 e5 si5, Ia5-sou ka-ki7 kiaN5 oa2 khi3 chui2-piN chiu7-kun7 i.  Lanthang2 chim-chiok lai5 siong2-siong7, I tu2 oa2-khi3 e5 si5, KiaN5 soe2-le2 e5 Iok-han7 e5 bin7, un2-tang3 si7 hut-jian5 chin chhiN-kiaN, hian2-chhut giam5-siok e5 thai3-tou7, u7 ki5-koai3, hun7-loan7, gong5-ngiah8 e5 bin7-sek.  Au7-lai5 i put-chi2 chhiN-chin lai5 hoat-chhut hit e5 jiat8-seng5, kiaN-ui3 e5 chit-bun7, mng7 kong2, “Chit e5 si7 chi7-chui7?”
	Choe3 gin2-na2 e5 si5, in tek-khak u7 siong-hoe7 chiah tioh8, chong2-si7 kau3 seng5-lian5 e5 tiong-kan, beng5-beng5 si7 bo5, in-ui7 Iok-han7 u7 kong2, “Goa2 m7-bat I.”  Toa7-bin7 i si7 m7-chai-iaN2 Bi2-sai3-a si7 i2-keng lim5-kau3 ti7 toe7-bin7-chiuN7, a2-si7 I teh-beh hut-jian5-kan eng7 koan5-leng5 kap eng5-kng tui3 thiN-nih8 loh8--lai5.  Chong2-si7 ti7 chit e5 Lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5, i khak-chhiat u7 siu7 kam2-tong7 kau3 ti7 sim-te2.  Iok-han7 chai ti7 i e5 bin7-cheng5, chit e5 Lang5 e5 lai7-bin7, u7 hit ho7 gau5 kam2-tong7 lang5 e5 ki5-iN7 e5 lat8 ti7-teh.
	Au7-lai5, Ia5-sou giah8 bak8 tit8-tit8 khoaN3 i e5 bin7.  Au7-lai5, i chiah chai-iaN2 lah! i chiah chai-iaN2 lah!  Ia5-sou chiu7-si7 i ti7 kui2-na7 ni5 bo5 liau5 e5 tiong-kan, sou2 teh theng3-hau7 e5, ti3-i3 aN3 i e5 hi7-khang sou2 teh soe3-ji7 beh thiaN I e5 kha-pou7 e5.  Chit-tiap8 chai, I chiu7-si7 Bi2-sai3-a, I2-sek-liat8 lang5 sou2 teh hi-bong7 e5 lah, I taN lim5-kau3 lah!
	Lan2 thang siong2-siong7, hit-si5 Iok-han7 e5 cheng-sin5 e5 hun7-loan7 kau3 chaiN2-iuN7!  I e5 sim-lai7 chhiN-kiaN, hang5-hok8, tut8-jian5 pian3-oaN7 i e5 siaN-im.  Tu2-a2-chiah i si7 chhin-chhiuN7 u7 koan5-peng3 e5 khoan2, lai5 khian3-chek Hoat-li7-sai3 lang5 kiau-ngou7 e5 sim, kong2, “Tok8-choa5 e5 lui7 ah, chi7-chui7-a2 chi2-si7 lin2 siam2-pi7 chiong-lai5 e5 siu7-khi3 ah?”  chong2-si7 chit-tiap8 i sou2 u7 iong2-kam2, sou2 u7 e5 khak-sin3, long2-chong2 song3-sit--khi3.  I kong2, “An3-choaN2?  Goa2 hap8-kai tioh8 tui3 li2 siu7 soe2-le2, li2 hoan2-tng2 chiu7-kun7 goa2 mah?”
	Chong2-si7 Ia5-sou eng7 un-jiu5 e5 thai3-tou7 lai5 chhiaN2 i chiap-soa3 chin7 i e5 chit-hun7, ka7 I kiaN5 soe2-le2.  U7-iaN2!  Ia5-sou bo5 khiam3-eng7 tioh8 siu7 soe2-le2 lai5 hoan2-hoe2 choe7.  Put-ko3 chit e5 soe2-le2 si7 piau2-beng5 I tui3 chit-tiap8 khi2 beh jip8 ti7 kiu3 leng5 e5 kang e5 i3-su3.  Ia5-sou ai3 kap hiah e5 choe3 te7-it pi-chian7 e5, saN-kap sun7-than3 chit e5 le2-sek.  “TaN chhiaN2 un2 goa2, in-ui7 lan2 hap8-gi5 tioh8 an2-ni, lai5 chin7 long2-chong2 e5 gi7.”  Tui3 an2-ni, Iok-han7 u7 un2 I.  Iok-han7 chiu7 hoaN7-chhiu2 ti7 I e5 teng2-bin7, hou7 I kui7-loh8 ti7 chui2-nih8.  Tui3 hit-tiap8 khi2, I chiu7 chiap-lap8 I e5 chit-hun7.  I e5 su seng-gai5 chiu7 i2-keng soah.  Sin e5 si5-ki5 i2-keng khai-si2.  Tui3 Na2-sat-lek8 e5 kang-tiuN5 chhut-lai5 chit e5 pi-chian7 e5 hiong-chhoan lang5, tui3 hit-tiap8 khi2 si7 chiaN5-choe3 Siong7-te3 e5 Bi2-sai3-a.
	Au7-lai5 in u7 tu2-tioh8 chit8 chan5 koat-toan3 bo5 boe7 ki3-tit--khi3 e5 su7, chiu7-si7 Ia5-sou i2-keng siu7 soe2-le2, tui3 chui2 chiuN7--lai5 teh ki5-to2, kiam2-chhai2 si7 teh ki5-to2 I sou2 te7-it hoaN-hi2 hit e5 ki5-to2-bun5, kong2, “Pe7 ah.  Goan7 Li2 e5 kok lim5-kau3, Li2 e5 chi2-i3 chiaN5 ti7 toe7-nih8, chhin-chhiuN7 ti7 thiN-nih8,” hit-si5 thiN hut-jian5 khui, in u7 khoaN3-kiN3 Siong7-te3 e5 Sin5, chhin-chhiuN7 chiN2-a2 kang3-lim5 ti7 Ia5-sou e5 teng2-bin7; koh u7 thiaN-kiN3 tui3 thiN u7 siaN, chiu7-si7 Siong7-te3 e5 siaN, kong2, “Chit e5 si7 goa2 sou2 thiaN3 e5 KiaN2, goa2 sou2 hoaN-hi2 e5.”  Iok-han7 khak-sit8 ti7 chit-tiap8 u7 chai-iaN2 i u7 khoaN3-tioh8 Ki-tok.
	Ti7 khah au7-lai5, Iok-han7 hou7 lang5 koaiN-kaN e5 si5, ti7 hit e5 ou-am3 sit-i3 e5 sun3-kan, i tui3 Ia5-sou khiok si7 bat keng-giam7--tioh8 tiap-a2(**tiap8-a2)-ku2 e5 gi5-sim.  Ti7 i si2 liau2-au7, i e5 hak8-seng tiong chit8 e5 oe7 ki3-tit in e5 sian-siN u7 chaiN2-iuN7 bat chhe-khian2 nng7 e5 hak8-seng lai5 mng7 Ia5-sou kong2, “Sou2 beh lai5 e5 , si7 li2 mah? a2-si7 goan2 tioh8 koh ng3-bang7 pat8 lang5 ah?”  Chong2-si7 ti7-teh ka7 Ia5-sou kiaN5 soe2-le2 e5 si5, i chiu7 long2 bo5 giau5-gi5.  Ia5-sou siu7 soe2-le2 liau2-au7, i u7 giam5-siok lai5 tui3 i e5 theng3-chiong3 kong2, “U7 khia7 ti7 lin2 tiong-kan e5, lin2 m7-bat I.”  Au7-lai5 Ia5-sou siu7-chhi3 liau2-au7, hit-si5 i ia7 koh-chai3 khoaN3-kiN3 I, ia7 u7 au5-kio3 kong2, “Li2 khoaN3, Siong7-te3 e5 IuN5-ko!”



Te7-2 chiuN	Siu7-Chhi3

	“Hit-si5 Ia5-sou hou7 Seng3 Sin5 chhoa7 kau3 khong3-ia2, beh siu7 Mou5-kui2 chhi3.”  Che tu2-tu2 si7 siu7 soe2-le2 liau2 e5 su7.  Lan2 u7 thiaN-kiN3 kong2, hit e5 cheng5-keng2 chiu7-si7 goa7-bin7 e5 khoan5-keng2, i2-kip8 lai7-bin7 e5 keng-giam7 u7 chek-si5 pian3-oaN7.  Chiu7-si7 tui3 Soe2-le2 kau3 ti7 Siu7-chhi3.  Tui3 Kng kau3 ti7 Am3.  I khoaN3-kiN3 thiN khui, u7 thiaN-kiN3 Pe7 e5 siaN liau2, u7 tit8-tit8 hou7 Seng3 Sin5 chhoa7 kau3 khong3-ia2 beh siu7 Mou5-kui2 chhi3.
	Hok-im-su tui3 chit chan5 u7 put-chi2 tui3-tiong7, che si7 teh piau2-si7 chit chan5 m7-si7 kan-ta ngou2-jian5 e5 su7, si7 ti7 Ia5-sou seng-gai5 tiong chit8 e5 giam5-siok, koh si7 te7-it tiong7-tai7 e5 choan2-ki, che si7 kau3-giah8 beng5 e5 su7-sit8.  Chiau3 khoaN3, I u7 chhim-chhim teh siuN7 I e5 tiong7-tai7 e5 su2-beng7, sim-lai7 u7 khou2-thang3, u7 be5-loan7, teh tui-chhe7 thang siam2-pi7 e5 lou7, iah8 Sat-tan3 thang kiaN e5 khui3-lat8, u7 kap I teh saN cheng-chian3, ai3 in2-iu2 I, ai3 chhoa7 I jip8 ti7 phian-lou7, lai5 li7-khui I sou2 eng-kai kiaN5 e5 lou7-cham7.  I chiaN5-choe3 lang5, ai3 beh kian3-siat Siong7-te3 e5 Kok, tioh8 u7 chhin-chhiuN7 lang5 e5 khoan2-sit, ai3 tai7-seng kap Mou5-kui2 e5 kok e5 khui3-lat8 kau-chian3, soa3 lai5 khah-iaN5 i chiah oe7 eng7-tit.
	U7 chit8 jit8, lan2 e5 Chu2 u7 tui3 kui2 mia5 e5 hak8-seng lai5 kong2-khi2 chit e5 Siu7-chhi3 e5 kou3-su7.  Toa7-bin7 lun7 hit e5 chhim-o3 e5 sou2-chai7 si7 poaN5-ke3 in sou2 oe7 thang li2-kai2 e5.  Toa7-bin7 ui7-tioh8 an2-ni, I u7 eng7 kan2-tan e5 hoat-tou7 lai5 kong2 hou7 in thiaN.  Chong2-si7 sui-jian5 si7 eng7 kan2-tan e5 hoat-tou7, lan2 ma7-si7 iau2 teh giau5-gi5 kiaN-liau2 in thiaN-liau2 si7 kah na2 chhin-chhiuN7 lan2 e5 khoan2.  In thiaN-liau2 kiam2 u7 chap8-hun thau3-thiat.  Phah-sng3 in ma7 u7 piau2-si7 in e5 boe7 li2-kai2, lai5 chheng2-kau3, ai3 I e5 chi2-si7, chhin-chhiuN7 teh lun7 tui3 ThiN-nih8 loh8-lai5 e5 oah8-mia7 piaN2 hit e5 o3-biau7 e5 ka3-si7, hit si5 e5 chong7-thai3 chit8 poaN (Iok-han7 6 chiuN).  Lan2 khiok-si7 bo5 thiaN-kiN3 kong2 an3-choaN2.  Kiam2-chhai2 si7 in-ui7 ai3 lan2 pun2-sin lai5 kho2-chhat chit e5 su7 ia7 ku2 kaN2.  Sou2-i2 lan2 tioh8 ai3 tng-bin7 ti7-chia lai5 siuN7 chit e5 bun7-toe5.

	Lan2 tai7-seng ai3 tui3 chit nng7 e5 lan5-toe5 lai5 chhut-hoat.  Lan2 kiam2-tioh8 chiau3 sou2 u7 ki3-chai3 e5 chit8-tiam2, chit8-uih8 lai5 thak8, chiu7-si7 kong2, ti7 khong-tiong u7 thiaN-kiN3 phaiN2-sin5 e5 siaN-im, u7 khoaN3-kiN3 chit8 e5 ou-ou u7 koan5-peng3 e5 oah8-mih8, lai5 chhoa7 Ia5-sou ti7(**e5) jiok8-the2 kau3 ti7 soaN-teng2, Seng3-tian7 e5 be2-liu mah?  A2-si7 thang kong2, chit e5 kou3-su7 put-ko3 si7 I teh bio5-sia2 Pun2-sin e5 cheng-sin5-chiuN7 kau-chian3 e5 keng2-hong2 mah?  Siat-su2 lan2 na7 soe3-ji7 lai5 koan-chhat hit e5 Siu7-chhi3 e5 chong7-hong2, lan2 chi3-chio2 oe7-thang siong2-siong7, u7 chit8 lang5 kou-tok8 bo5 liau5 tiam3 ti7 khong3-ia2, bo5 lang5 sou2 kau3 e5 chioh8-tong7, chiam5-su bek8-siong2, ti7 si3-chap8-jit8 ku2, kin2-sin7 lai5 ti2-khong3 hit e5 teh chhi3-lian7 I e5 sim-sin5 e5 bo5 heng5 phaiN2-sin5 e5 khui3-lat8, chhim-chhim lai5 siuN7 I e5 su2-beng7, chiong Sat-tan3 tui3 I sou2 the5-si7 hit ho7 khoaN3 si7 thang chiap-lap8, ki5-sit8 si7 phaiN2 e5 ke3-ek8, it-it khoaN3-phoa3 i e5 chin-siong3, toan3-jian5 ka7 i ku7-choat8.  Na7-si7 chiau3 an2-ni khoaN3, lan2 tiong-kan u7 lang5 beh kam2-kak si7 khah chu7-jian5, khah chhin-chhiuN7 lan2 pun2-sin sou2 bat keng-giam7 e5 khoan2-sit ia7 bo5 tek-khak.
	Lun7 chit nng7 khoan2 e5 thai3-tou7, chai7 Ia5-sou sit8-chai7 si7 siang7 chit8-iuN7, in-ui7 chu7-jian5 I un2-tang3 seng5-jin7 ti7 I e5 sin-piN u7 phaiN2 e5 mih8, hek8-chia2 si7 u7 heng5 e5, a2-si7 bo5 heng5 e5 ti7-teh.  Siat-su2 lan2 na7 seng5-jin7 ti7 I e5 sim-lai7 sou2 siu7 it-chhe3 e5 siaN-im, khoaN3-choe3 si7 chin-sit8 e5 chhi3, iu7-koh hiah e5 siaN-im, m7-si7 tui3 I e5 bo5 choe7 e5 sim-sin5 hoat-chhut, si7 tui3 goa7-bin7 jip8-lai5 e5, bo5 lun7 ta2-loh8 chit8 khoan2 e5 siat-siong2, goa2 siuN7 to long2 oe7 thang chiap-lap8.

	Na7-si7 an2-ni, lan2 boe7 bian2-tit ai3 chek-si5 chin3-cheng5 koh lai5 siuN7 chit8 e5 iau2 koh-khah tiong7-tai7 e5 bun7-toe5.  Lan2 e5 Chu2 Ia5-sou to bo5 choe7, thai3-tho2 oe7 tu2-tioh8 Mou5-kui2 e5 chhi3 mah?  Chai7 lan2 e5 keng-giam7, Siu7-chhi3 si7 teh piau2-beng5 ti7 lan2 e5 lai7-tiong u7 phaiN2 e5 seng3-chit oe7 in3-tap chhi3 e5 iu2-hek8.  M7-ku2 Ia5-sou e5 jin5-seng3 si7 bo5 choe7, tui3 an2-ni, kiam2-chhai2 lang5 beh siuN7 I sou2 siu7 e5 chhi3, put-ko3 si7 chit8 cheng2 e5 bou5-gi2-chian3, bo5 u7 sit8-chai7 e5 gui5-hiam2 ti7-teh.
	Toan3-jian5 m7-si7!  Na7-si7 I sou2 siu7 e5 chhi3, m7-si7 sit8-chai7, lan2 tu2-tioh8 chhi3 e5 si5, chiu7 bo5 thang tit-tioh8 an-ui3.  Lan2 e5 chhi3 khak-sit8 m7-si7 chit8 cheng2 e5 bou5-gi2-chian3.  Lan2 chai lan2 sou2 siu7 e5 chhi3 si7 oe7 hou7 lan2 kau3 ti7 si2-bo5.  Seng3-chheh sou2 chi2-si7 lan2 chai chit e5 Sin5-seng3 e5 Sengl3?-chia2, chhiu2-nih8 sou2 theh8 e5 chian3-kah, na7-si7 to-chhiuN chhak8 be7 phoa3 e5, an2-ni si7 u7 sim2-mih8 li7-ek thang choe3 lan2 e5 bian2-le7?  Chit8 jit8 bat u7 chit8 e5 bi7-sin3-chia2, koh si7 u7 su-siuN2 e5 lau7-toa7-lang5, tui3 goa2 kong2, “Siat-su2 lin2 sou2 hok8-sai7 e5 Ki-tok si7 Sin5, chiu7 I sou2 siu7 e5 chhi3 si7 bo5 thang an-ui3 goa2.”  Sit8-chai7 si7 chin oh-tit in3-tap kau3 hou7 chit e5 lang5 oe7 hoaN-hi2 chiap-lap8.  Put-ko3 tui3 chit ku3 oe7, lan2 chai chit e5 lau7-toa7-lang5 u7 chin-sit8 e5 sim, him-bou7 ti7 ka-ki7 e5 sin-piN oe7 tit thang chhe7-tioh8 chit8 e5 oah8-oah8, sit8-chai7 bat chin chhiN-chham2 tu2-tioh8 chhi3-lian7, chhin-chhiuN7 i pun2-sin sou2 bat keng-giam7--e5 e5 peng5-iu2, ng3-bang7 thang chiaN5-choe3 chit8 e5 gau5 e5 toa7-hiaN lai5 tong5-cheng5 i, pang-chan7 i e5 it-seng.
	Chong2-si7 lan2 ai3 mng7, chit e5 bo5 choe7 e5 Ki-tok sit8-chai7 oe7 tu2-tioh8 chhi3 mah?  Seng3-chheh si7 u7 beng5-beng5 kan-cheng3 kong2, Si7!  I u7 sit8-chai7 tu2-tioh8 chhi3.
	Chit-tiap8 chhiaN2 lai5 siuN7 chit e5 bun7-toe5.  Lan2 sui-si7 kong2, I bo5 choe7, ki5-sit8 hit e5 i3-su3 m7-si7 kong2, choe7-ok e5 in2-iu2 koat-toan3 be7 hian2-chhut ti7 I e5 bin7-cheng5, ia7 m7-si7 kong2, I koat-toan3 be7 kam2-kak--tioh8 in2-iu2.  Hit e5 i3-su3 chi2-u7 si7 kong2, I koat-toan3 m7-kheng2 hok8-chiong5 choe7 e5 in2-iu2, sui-si7 gu7-tioh8 in2-iu2, I e5 sim-chi3 ka -ki7 oe7 khia7-chai7.  Lan2 na7 kong2, ti7 sim-lai7 u7 beng5-beng5 kam2-kak--tioh8 in2-iu2 tui3 goa7-bin7 teh jip8-lai5, kap ti7 sim-lai7 u7 choe7-ok e5 ou-tiam2, u7 i3-su3 ai3 beh hok8-chiong5 i, chit nng7 hang7 si7 u7 thian-ian e5 cheng-chha ti7-teh.  Sou2-i2 chhi3 thang kong2 si7 long2 bo5 u7 chit8 sut-a2 m7-ho2 e5 su7.  Lang5 na7 chin-sit8 lai5 hoe5-kou3 ti7 it-seng sou2 te7-it thang khoa-khau2, te7-it khoai3-lok8 thang siau3-liam7 e5, chiu7-si7 u7 khah-iaN5 ti7 chhi3 e5 su7.  Ah!  Khiok u7-iaN2, kho2-sioh lan2 bo5 u7 chiap8-chiap8 tit-tioh8 hit ho7 e5 keng-giam7!
	Put-ko3 chai7 lan2 u7 chhim-chhim keng3-khian5 e5 liam7-thau5 e5 lang5, si7 m7-kaN2 siuN7 lan2 e5 Chu2 chin-chiaN3 bat tu2-tioh8 chhi3 e5 in2-iu2.  Che si7 in-ui7 lan2 bo5 chap8-hun liau2-kai2, I u7 choan5-jian5 khiam-pi ka-ki7 lai5 chiaN5-choe3 lang5 e5 in-toaN.  Lan2 chu7-jian5 tioh8 si5-siong5 oe7 ki3-tit I si7 Chin-sit8 e5 Sin5 (Very God), iau2-ku2 ma7-si7 tioh8 chhut-lat8 chu2-tiuN I si7 ui7-tioh8 lan2 tai7-ke i2-kip8 lan2 e5 chin2-kiu3, lai5 chiaN5-choe3 Chin-sit8 e5 Lang5 (Very Man).  Hit e5 khah-iaN5 chhi3 e5, si7 Lang5 e5 Ia5-sou; m7-si7 Sin5 e5 Ia5-sou.  Lan2 e5 Thau5-lang5 khiam-pi lim5-kau3 se3-kan kap Mou5-kui2 kau-chian3, hit si5 I u7 pang3-he7 I sou2 u7 e5 kian-kou3 chhan3-lan7 e5 chian3-kah ti7 lan2 e5 sin-piN, chiaN5-choe3 lan2 e5 tang5-phoaN7, thng3 chhiah-kha kap lan2 pai5 tang5-liat8 lai5 kau-chian3.  I si7 bo5 chit8-sut-a2 khah koh-iuN7 ti7 pat8-lang5, su7-su7 si7 chhin-chhiuN7 lan2 chit8 poaN, sit8-chai7 u7 tu2-tioh8 chhi3.
	Lan2 oe7 liau2-kai2 I sou2 siu7 e5 chhi3, a2-si7 be7, chhiaN2 poah chit8-piN, put-ko3 Seng3-chheh to u7 chi2-si7 lan2 chai, Ia5-sou si7 u7 chhu2 lang5 e5 seng3-cheng5, kap lang5 siang7-khoan2, u7 it-chhe3 hap8-gi5 e5 iok8-bong7, chu7-jian5 e5 kheng-hiong3 ti7-teh; chiah e5 chai7 lan2 khiok si7 choe3 choe7-ok e5 mng5-lou7.  I u7 chhin-chhiuN7 lan2 chit8 poaN, oe7 pek-chhiat kam2-kak iau-go7 e5 kan-khou2, chhin-chhiuN7 ti7 Sip8-ji7-ke3 teng2, I ui7-tioh8 chhui3-ta e5 kan-khou2 u7 ai3 tho2 beh lim-chui2.  I e5 sin-the2 ia7-si7 chin gau5 kam2-kak thang3-thiaN3; chhin-chhiuN7 ti7 Khek-se-ma2-ni5, I e5 sim-sin5 iu-chhiu5 kau3 chhin-chhiuN7 sim-koaN beh phoa3-lih8.  “Siat-su2 na7 oe7 choe3-tit,” I kong2 chit-ku3, si7 piau2-beng5 ti7 hit si5 I chu7-jian5 u7 tu2-tioh8 in2-iu2, ai3 beh siam2-pi7 chiah e5 su7.
	Chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni, lan2 beng5-beng5 chai, I bo5 choe7 e5 jin5-seng3 ia7-si7 be7 thang siam2-pi7 chhi3 e5 chhiN-chham2; ia7 hit e5 cheng-chian3 khah-siong5 si7 chin kek-liat8; put-ko3 I si7 chi2-u7 eng7 sit8-chai7 e5 lou2-lek8 lai5 khah-iaN5.  Seng3-chheh chaiN2-iuN7 kong2?  “In-ui7 I i2-keng siu7 khou2-lan7 lai5 tu2-tioh8 chhi3, chiu7 oe7 pang-chan7 chiah e5 siu7-chhi3 e5 lang5.”  “In-ui7 lan2 sou2 u7 e5 che3-si-thau5, m7-si7 boe7-oe7 the2-thiap lan2 long2-chong2 e5 loan2-jiok8; chiu7-si7 hoan7-su7 piN5-piN5 u7 siu7-chhi3, chong2-si7 bo5 hoan7-choe7.”  Ti7-chia sou2 kong2 chiah-e5, m7-si7 Ia5-sou choe3-chhou sou2 siu7 e5 chhi3, iah8 m7-si7 choe3-au7 e5 chhi3.  Ki5-sit8 ti7 i2-cheng5 I e5 choan5 seng-oah8 si7 chhin-chhiuN7 lan2 chit8 poaN, iu5-goan5 u7 tu2-tioh8 chhi3.  Ti7 au7-lai5 I e5 choan5 seng-oah8 ma7-si7 an2-ni.  Li2 khoaN3 Seng3-chheh si7 ki3-chai3 kong2, hit-si5 Sat-tan3 chi2-u7 “chiam7-si5” li7-khui I.  Lian5 ti7 khek-se-ma2-ni5 hng5 e5 si5, chhi3 iu5-goan5 si7 kap I saN-kap ti7-teh.  “Goa2 e5 Pe7 ah, na7 oe7 choe3-tit, tioh8 hou7 chit e5 poe li7-khui goa2.”  I beh lim5-chiong e5 si5, u7 tui3 hak8-seng kong2 chit8 ku3 put-chi2 oe7 kam2-tong7 lang5 e5 oe7, chiu7-si7 kong2, “lin2 chiu7-si7 siong5-siong5 kap goa2 ti7 chhi3-lian7 tiong e5.”  Chong2-si7 I put-si5 to tek-seng3.
	Chai7 lan2 sou2 u7 e5 pin5-jiok8 e5 ti3-sek, si7 chi2-u7 oe7 thang li2-kai2 kau3 chia ji5-i2.
	Chit-tiap8 ai3 oat8 lin3-tng2 lai5 siuN7 chit e5 kou3-su7.  Lan2 thang siong2-siong7, Ia5-sou ti7 hit-jit8 tui3 Iok-tan3 ho5 khi2-lai5 e5 si5, I e5 sim-sin5 si7 kam2-khai3 bu5-liong7!  I u7 keng-ke3 cheng-sin5-chiuN7 choe3-ko e5 choan2-ki, chiu7-si7 I u7 thiaN-kiN3 tui3 thiN-nih8 loh8--lai5 e5 SiaN, u7 tit-tioh8 Seng3 Sin5 e5 seng3-piat, chhiau chu7-jian5 khui3-lat8 e5 i3-sek, lai5 khai-si2 I it-seng e5 ke3-ek8, soa3 liau2-kai2 beh choe3 “I e5 Pe7 e5 kang,” si7 chin tiong7-tai7 e5 su7-giap8.
	Au7-lai5, I chiu7 bo5 than3 pun2-sin e5 i3-su3, chi2-u7 tan-sun5 sun7-hok8 tui3 Pe7 sou2 chhut hit e5 Sin5-seng3 e5 i3-su3 lai5 kiaN5, chiu7-si7 “u7 hou7 Seng3 Sin5 chhoa7 khi3 khong3-ia2 beh siu7 Mou5-kui2 chhi3.”
	Chhin-chhiuN7 ti7 hit khoan2, ti7 I e5 sim-sin5, kam2-cheng5, u7 ke3-thau5 nau7-tong7 e5 chong7-thai3 e5 si5, I boe7 bian2-tit ai3 siam2-pi7 cheng3-lang5, ka-ki7 chit8 e5 lai5 su-siuN2 teng2-teng2 e5 su7.  Lan2 thang siong2-siong7, I u7 ka-ki7 chit8 lang5 li7-khui hiah e5 khia7 ti7 hoaN7-teng2 kui tin7 e5 cheng3-lang5, tui3 hit e5 oan-oan oat-oat e5 lou7, tit8-tit8 chiuN7--khi2-khi3 kau3 ti7 soaN-nih8 chhiu7-na5 e5 tiong-kan.  I thong mi5 si3-ke3 kiaN5-lai5 kiaN5-khi3, choe3-au7 u7 chhe7-tioh8 chit8 ui7 bo5 lang5 sou2 kau3 e5 chioh8-tong7, ia2-siu3 sou2 tiam3 e5 tong7-hiat8, ka-ki7 chit8 lang5 lai5 che7 ti7-hia.
	Lou7-ka u7 kong2, I si7 choan5-jian5 ka-ki7 chit8 e5 ti7-hia.  “Seng3 Sin5 chhoa7 I ti7 khong3-ia2-nih8 si3-chap8 jit8 ku2, hou7 Mou5-kui2 chhi3.”  Goa2 ai3 lan2 chu3-i3 ti7 hit si3-chap8 jit8 e5 su7.  Lan2 tiong-kan choe7-choe7 lang5 chha-put-to long2 hut-liok8 hit si3-chap8 jit8 kan e5 su7, kan-ta siuN7 hiah e5 si5-jit8 ke3-liau2, chiah sou2 tu2-tioh8 e5 chhi3 na7-tiaN7.  Che sit8-chai7 u7 chho3-gou7 ti7-teh.  Lan2 na2 gian2-kiu3 chiu7 na2 oe7 thang liau7-siong2, hit si3-chap8 jit8 chiu7-si7 I e5 cheng-sin5 e5 tou3-cheng e5 choe3-ko tiam2, ti7 hit e5 thang kiaN-hiaN5 e5 si3-chap8 jit8 ku2, I e5 cheng-sin5 chong7-thai3, si7 kau3-giah8 e5 kin2-tiuN, ti3-kau3 I soa3 m7-chai-iaN2 I bo5 mih8 thang chiah8.  Lan2 kiam2 oe7 thang sio2-khoa2 lai5 siong2-siong7 ti7 hit si3-chap8 jit8 kan I sou2 keng-giam7 e5 cheng-sin5 kin2-tiuN e5 chong7-thai3 mah?
	Lan2 e5 cheng-sin5 na7-si7 tu2-tioh8 chin chhiN-kiaN, chin kin2-tiuN e5 si5, lan2 eng2 ai3 boe7 ki3-tit chiu-ui5 it-chhe3 e5 su7-but8, ma7 soa3 boe7 ki3-tit long2 bo5 chiah8 sim2-mih8.  Siat-su2 lan2 na7 khoaN3-kiN3 hit e5 lang5 hut-jian5 chhiN2-gou7, chai iau, hit-si5 lan2 kiam2 bo5 phah-sng3 i e5 kin2-tiuN e5 cheng-sin5 si7 i2-keng chiam7-chiam7 pang3-sang--khi3 mah?  Seng3-chheh sou2 ki3-chai3 chit e5 iu2-hek8 e5 kou3-su7, chiu7-si7 teh am3-si7 hit e5 kin2-tiuN e5 cheng-sin5 i2-keng u7 pang3-sang, tui3 hit e5 jiat8-jiat8 kin2-tiuN e5 cheng-sin5, tut8-jian5 chhiN2-gou7, koh-chai3 hok8-to3 peng5-siong5 e5 cheng-sin5 chong7-thai3 lah.  Ki5-sit8 hit si3-chap8 jit8 ku2, kin2-tiuN e5 cheng-sin5 seng-oah8 i2-keng soah, I chiah khi2-thau5 chai iau ai3 him-bou7 beh chiah8.  Hit si3-chap8 jit8 tek-khak si7 chin thang kiaN-hiaN5 e5 si5-kan, u7 hou7 I kiaN chit8-e7, I u7 chim-chiok siuN7, ng3-bang7 thang liau2-kai2 hit e5 i3-su3.  Chit e5 kou3-su7 si7 chi2-si7 lan2 chai, ti7 chit e5 khui-khoah, sin5-pi3-tek e5 cheng-sin5 se3-kai3, u7 choe7-choe7 bo5 heng5, phaiN2 e5 khui3-lat8 tiam3 ti7 lan2 e5 sin-piN, teh kap lang5 kau-chian3, ia7 teh kap Siong7-te3 kau-chian3.  Lan2 thang liau7-siong2 tui3 ti7 hit si3-chap8 jit8 e5 seng-oah8, u7 hou7 I ke-thiN chit8 hang7 sin e5 ki5-kiu5 lai5 he7 ti7 I sou2 hoaN-hi2 e5 Ki5-to2-bun5, kong2,  “Boh8-tit chhoa7 goan2 jip8 ti7 chhi3, tioh8 kiu3 goan2 chhut hit e5 phaiN2 e5.”
	Ti7 hit si3-chap8 jit8 ku2, Ia5-sou u7 chu-chu siuN7 kah sin5--khi3, hit e5 sin5-pi3-tek e5 cheng-sin5-chiuN7 e5 tou3-cheng siaN2-khoan2, I koat-toan3 boe7-thang tui3 lan2 lang5 kong2-khi2.  Lan2 thang phah-sng3 hit e5 cheng5-keng2 si7 boe7-thang eng7 lan2 sou2 oe7 hiau2-tit e5 khiuN-khau2 lai5 kong2-khi2.  Lan2 thang ho2-taN2 chhui-toan3, ti7 hit si3-chap8-jit8 I e5 cheng-sin5 bo5 u7 toe7-bin7-chiuN7 hian7-sit8 e5 i3-sek ti7-teh, si7 li7-khui hng7-hng7, jip8 ti7 hit e5 bu5-han7 e5 leng5-kai3, khia7-khi2 ti7 hit e5 chin thang chhiN-kiaN, bo5 hioh-khun3, chham2-khok e5 kau-chian3 e5 tiong-kan.  I siong5-siong5 si7 chhiau-oat8 lan2 sou2 bat oe7-kau3 e5.  Iau-go7 e5 i3-sek si7 thau5 chit8-e5 ki3-ho7 piau2-beng5 I koh hok8-to3 toe7-bin7-chiuN7 hian7-sit8 e5 i3-sek.  Kiam2-chhai2 chi2-u7 tui3 chit si5 khi2, I sou2 siu7 e5 chhi3, chiah si7 lan2 sou2 li2-kai2 oe7 kau3 e5 pou7-hun7.
	Hit si3-chap8-jit8 kin2-tiuN e5 seng-oah8 ke3-liau2, lan2 thak8-tioh8 kong2 I chiah chai iau.  Lan2 khiok long2 m7-bat u7 hit ho7 kek8-ki5 iau-go7 e5 keng-giam7.  Hiah e5 bat choe7-choe7 jit8 bo5 chiah8 sim2-mih8 e5 lang5, u7 tui3 lan2 kong2-khi2 hit e5 him-bou7 ai3-chiah8 mih8 e5 sim, si7 chin7-chai7 pek-chhiat boe7 thang theng3-hau7--tit.  Ia5-sou khah m7-si7 chhin-chhiuN7 KiaN5 soe2-le2 e5 Iok-han7 koan3-lian7 kim3-iok8.  Ti7 chit si5-khek I e5 khong-kian7 e5 jiok8-the2, un2-tang3 tong3 long2 boe7 tiau5, him-bou7 ai3 chiah8.  Ti7 hit e5 i3-sek bo5 loa7 beng5 e5 si5, chai7 pak-tou2 chin iau e5 lang5, si3-soaN3 ti7 sin-piN e5 chioh8-thau5, eng2-eng2 ai3 khoaN3-choe3 si7 mi7-pau.  Koh toa7-bin7 ti7 hit ho7 chhiN-kiaN cheng-sin5 song3-sit e5 si5, eng2 ai3 siN-khi2 put kian7-choan5 e5 cheng-sin5 chong7-thai3 lai5 giau5-gi5 it-chhe3.  I u7 iau-go7 kau3 sim-sin5 ia3-lan2 bo5 lat8.  I ka-ki7 kap Mou5-kui2 saN-kap tiam3.  Lan2 chai ti7 hit khoan2 cheng-sin5 kin2-tiuN kou-tok8 e5 si5, si7 oe7 siN-khi2 gi5-sim, khoaN3 it-chhe3 e5 ho2-su7, si7 chin thang giau5-gi5, m7-kaN2 liah8-choe3 si7 sit8-chai7.

	Ti7 Seng3-chheh sou2 ki3, Mou5-kui2 thau5-chit8 pai2 lai5 chhi3 I chiu7-si7 mng7 kong2, “Siat-su2 Li2 na7-si7 Siong7-te3 e5 KiaN2.” Li2 kiam2-si7?  Hit e5 chhou-ia2 jiat8-kong5 e5 KiaN5 soe2-le2 e5 Iok-han7, kiam2 bo5 chho3-gou7 mah?  Tui3 thiN-nih8 sou2 hoat-chhut hit e5 SiaN, i2-kip8 Seng3 e5 ChiN2-a2, kiam2 m7-si7 tui3 cheng-sin5 chhok-kak sou2 ti3 e5 mah?  Iau2-be7 chhut-hoat lai5 choe3 chit e5 kang, iau2-be7 in2-chhoa7 lang5 kiaN5 ti7 phian-lou7 e5 tai7-seng, tioh8 chhi3-giam7 Li2 pun2-sin!  Tioh8 chhi3-khoaN3, lian5 ti7 iau-go7 i2-kip8 si2-bo5 e5 si5, Li2 oe7-thang kiu3 pun2-sin a2-boe7?  Siong7-te3 e5 KiaN2 ah!  Siat-su2 Li2 si7 Siong7-te3 e5 KiaN2, tioh8 beng7-leng7 chiah e5 chioh8-thau5 piN3-choe3 piaN2.
	Ia5-sou siaN2-su7 bo5 than3 Mou5-kui2 e5 i3-su3 lai5 choe3?  Chhou-chhou khoaN3 liau2, che si7 chhin-chhiuN7 u7 li2-khi3, bo5 m7-tioh8 e5 su7.  Kiam2-chhai2 chit e5 si7 I thau5-chit8 pai2 kam2-kak--tioh8 hit e5 bo5 han7-liong7 e5 khui3-lat8 lai5 teh in2-iu2 I.  An3-choaN2-iuN7 ti7 chit-si5 I bo5 hoat-hui I e5 chhiau chu7-jian5 e5 khui3-lat8 mah?  Ti7 khah au7-lai5, I to u7 hoat-hui I e5 khui3-lat8 lai5 pian3-piaN2 iuN2-chhi7 kui toa7-tin7 e5 lang5, lai5 pian3 chui2 piN3-choe3 chiu2.  An3-choaN2 chit-tiap8 bo5 beh neh?
	Ti7 chit e5 chhi3-nih8 u7 chin li7-hai7 e5 sou2-chai7 ti7-teh.  Eng7 hit ho7 beng5-beng5 si7 phaiN2 e5 su7, lai5 beh iu2-hek8 I, si7 gu5-chhun2 e5 sou2-choe3.  Lan2 long2 kam2-kak lan2 sou2 tu2-tioh8 te7-it hui3-khi3 e5 chhi3, chiu7-si7 tu2-tioh8 in2-iu2 lan2, lai5 kiu5 hit-ho7 ho2 e5 su7, hit si5 lan2 eng2-eng2 ai3 phian-sim mng7 kong2: “Chit e5 su7 kiam2-si7 chho3-gou7 mah?”
	Sui-jian5 Ia5-sou si7 put-chi2 iau-go7 kau3 sim-sin5 chin hui-siong5 ai3 chiah8, iau2-ku2 I chai chit e5 tai7-chi3 si7 m7 eng-kai tioh8 choe3 e5.  An3-choaN2?  Lan2 chi2-u7 thang eng7 keng3-khian5 lai5 chhui-chhek hit e5 in-toaN.  I sou2 siu7 chit e5 tang7 e5 chhi3, kiam2 m7-si7 Seng3 Sin5 chhoa7 khi3 siu7 e5, na7-si7 an2-ni, I kiam2 thang siam2-pi7 mah?  I kiam2 thang ui7-tioh8 I ka-ki7, i2-kip8 ka-ki7 e5 khoai3-lok8 lai5 su2-iong7 hit ho7 beh choe3 pat8-lang5 e5 lou7-eng7 e5 khui3-lat8 mah?  I kiam2 m7-si7 tioh8 choan5-jian5 hang5-hok8 ti7 Pe7 e5 chiau3-kou3, bo5 kho3 ka-ki7 e5 khui3-lat8 lai5 kiu3 I pun2-sin mah?  Ui7-tioh8 ai3 choe3 lan2 e5 bian2-le7, I u7 kam-goan7 khiam-pi lai5 chhu2 loan2-jiok8 e5 jin5-seng3 e5 chong7-thai3; tui3 an2-ni, I si7 boe7-thang kiaN5 sin5-jiah lai5 kiu3 ka-ki7, ti3-kau3 lai5 pho3-hoai7 I lim5-kau3 se3-kan e5 bok8-tek.  Che si7 I kap lan2 u7 cheng-chha e5 sou2-chai7.  Siat-su2 I chit-tiap8 na7 than3 Mou5-kui2 e5 i3-su3 lai5 choe3, lan2 beh siuN7, an3-choaN2 I bo5 chiap8-chiap8 kiaN5 sin5-jiah thang kiu3 ka-ki7 thoat-li7 song3-hiong, khiam3-kheh, m7-bian2 bo5 chhu3 thang khia7, m7-bian2 choe3 chit8 e5 bo5 thang khoa3 thau5-khak e5 kho2-lin5 song3-hiong e5 Jin5-chu2 mah?  An3-choaN2 I bo5 siam2-pi7 Khek-se-ma2-ni5-hng5 e5 chhiN-chham2 mah?  An3-choaN2 I bo5 chin2-kiu3 pun2-sin lai5 thoat-chhut ti7 lim5-chiong e5 si5, sou2 pai5 ti7 I e5 bin7-cheng5, hit e5 siang7 chit8-iuN7 e5 chhi3 mah?  “Li2 na7-si7 Siong7-te3 e5 KiaN2, tioh8 kiu3 ka-ki7, tioh8 tui3 Sip8-ji7-ke3 loh8--lai5.”
	Bo5!  I u7 chin2-kiu3 pat8 lang5.  Chong2-si7 bo5 kiu3 ka-ki7, bo5 lun7 hit si5 a2-si7 hian7-kim.  Ia5-sou sin3, siat-su2 seng-oah8 na7 oe7-thang bian2 ham7-loh8 ti7 chho3-gou7, chiu7 si2 na7 thang.  I ti7 i2-cheng5 koat-toan3 be7 bat chhin-chhiuN7 chit-tiap8 e5 chiap-kun7 ti7 si2 e5 toe7-kai3.  Chit-tiap8 I si7 beh go7-si2 e5 Ki-tok.
	Lan2 na7-si7 bo5 beh choat8-tui3 hok8-chiong5 Siong7-te3 Seng3 e5 chi2-i3, lan2 iu5-goan5 u7 choe7-choe7 ho2 e5 ki-hoe7, thang hou7 pun2-sin tit-tioh8 khah khoaN3-oah8, khah khoai3-lok8, tit-tioh8 khah choe7 e5 chiN5-gun5, chiaN5-choe3 pu3-u7, oe7-thang siat-pi7 khah ho2-soe3, lai5 li7-ek lan2 e5 ka-teng5.  Lan2 long2-si7 kong2, “Lang5 tek-khak tioh8 oah8.”  Chong2-si7 chit e5 tek-seng3 e5 Ia5-sou, tui3 khong3-ia2 e5 sou2-chai7 ka7 lan2 kong2, “Goa2 i2-keng u7 keng-ke3 lah.  Tioh8 oh8 Goa2!  Tioh8 oh8 hit e5 si2 ti7 chian3-tiuN5 e5 kian7-lam5-ji5.  Lang5 bo5 pit-iau3 tioh8 oah8.  Lang5 leng7-khou2(**leng5-kho2) si2, si7 khah-ho2 oah8-teh lai5 poe7-biu7 si3-chiaN3 e5 lou7.”

	Chit-tiap8 ai3 lai5 siuN7 te7-ji7 e5 chhi3.  Ia5-sou u7 tui3 sin3 Siong7-te3, tui3 Seng3-chheh e5 oe7 lai5 khah-iaN5.  Chit-tiap8 hit e5 phaiN2 e5, u7 eng7 Ia5-sou pun2-sin e5 kun-ku3 lai5 ti7-tng I.  Keng3-jian5 li2 u7 hit ho7 e5 sin3-sim, taN tioh8 hian2-chhut hit e5 sin3 hou7 goa2 khoaN3.  Tioh8 ti7 sou2 chu7-chip8 chiah e5 che3-si i2-kip8 chham-pai3-chia2 e5 bin7-cheng5, lai5 tui3 Tian7-nih8 e5 chhu3-teng2-be2 tio5--loh8-khi3.  An2-ni chiu7 u7 thang piau2-si7 li2 oan5-choan5 e5 sin3-sim.  An2-ni chiu7 u7 ui-giam5 thang piau2-beng5 Bi2-sai3-a e5 ki3-ho7, in-ui7 ti7 Ku7-iok u7 ki3-chai3 kong2, “I beh ui7-tioh8 li2, beng7-leng7 I e5 thiN-sai3, in beh hu5 li2, bian2-tit li2 e5 kha tak-tioh8 chioh8.”
	Lun7 chit e5 chhi3 lan2 beh an3-choaN2-iuN7 lai5 kai2-sek?  Kiam2-si7 Sat-tan3 chin-chiaN3 chhoa7 Ia5-sou ti7 jiok8-the2 chiuN7-khi3 ti7 Tian7-nih8 e5 chhu3-teng2-be2 mah?  Lan2 khiok-si7 kau3-giah8 thang chai sin5-leng5-kai3 e5 khui3-lat8 si7 oe7-thang hian2-chhut chit ho7 tai7-chi3.  A2-si7 lan2 thang kong2, chit e5 kou3-su7 si7 teh piau2-beng5 ti7 I e5 sim sou2 siu7 e5 chhim-chhim e5 cheng-sin5-chiuN7 e5 chhi3 e5 keng2-hong2 mah?
	Bo5 giau5-gi5, I i2-keng chu-chu teh siuN7 I it-seng e5 ke3-ek8.  I ti7-teh siuN7 e5 si5, u7 tu2-tioh8 chit8 e5 toa7 e5 chhi3.  In-ui7 I chai I u7 chhiau chu7-jian5 e5 khui3-lat8.  I tioh8 chaiN2-iuN7 choe3 chiah si7 choe3 ho2 e5 hoat-tou7, thang lai5 kian3-siat Siong7-te3 e5 kok e5 hok-khi3, ti7 chit e5 kho2-lin5 lo5-khou2 e5 se3-kai3?  I tioh8 hoan-hu3 cheng3 thiN-sai3, kap I saN-kap ko-ku2 thiN-kok e5 kun-ki5 mah?  I tioh8 hian2-chhut sin5-jiah e5 khui3-lat8, hou7 lang5 thang chek-si5 kui-sun7 mah?  Cheng3 peh-siN3 long2 teh theng3-hau7 beh khoaN3 sin5-jiah, thang choe3 cheng3 I si7 Bi2-sai3-a.  In-ui7 in na7 m7-si7 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 sin5-jiah, chiu7 bo5 beh chiap-lap8 I.  Lan2 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 cheng3-lang5 ti7 au7-jit8 chit8-pai2 ke3 chit8-pai2, to long2-si7 teh iau3-kiu5 tui3 thiN-nih8 lai5 e5 sin5-jiah.  Chit-tiap8 I tioh8 tui3 in lai5 hian2-beng5 hit e5 boe7-thang pian7-pok--tit e5 sin5-jiah, lai5 choe3 I e5 chong-kau3 e5 kong2-ko3, hou7 lang5 khoaN3-liau2 siu7 kam2-tong7 mah?  I tioh8 ai3 chiaN5-choe3 chit8 e5 gau5 kiaN5 ki5-iN7 e5 koan5-leng5 e5 lang5, lai5 chhut-thau5 mah?  I na7-si7 ko2-jian5 tui3 koaiN5-koaiN5 e5 sou2-chai7 tio5--loh8-khi3 ti7 cheng3 chham-pai3-chia2 e5 tiong-kan, a2-si7 eng7 sim2-mih8 sin5-jiah e5 hoat-tou7 lai5 chhut-hoat eng3 in peh-siN3 e5 iau3-kiu5, I un2-tang3 beh tit-tioh8 toa7 e5 hoan-geng5, peh-siN3 beh choe5-siaN hat-chhai2, hoaN-hi2 kah na2 siau2 chit8-poaN, ia7 I beh tui3 Seng3-tian7 chhut-khi3, u7 kui toa7-tin7 e5 lang5 beh te3 I, si7 chhin-chhiuN7 khai2-soan5 e5 heng5-kun, beh soa3-chiap kiaN5 choe7-choe7 e5 sin5-jiah, ke-thiN toa7 e5 eng5-kng, cheng3-lang5 beh phak-pai3 ti7 I e5 bin7-cheng5, lai5 hang5-hok8 ti7 I e5 koan5-ui.
	Hit e5 chhi3 e5, u7 oa2-lai5 ti7 I e5 hi7-khang-piN, soe3-siaN kong2, “Li2 e5 ki-hoe7 kau3 lah.  Siong7-te3 e5 KiaN2 ah, Li2 na7-si7 Siong7-te3 e5 KiaN2, Li2 tioh8 tio5--loh8-khi3.  Tioh8 piau2-beng5 hit e5 Chi3-koaiN5 e5 u7 teh ui7 li2.  TaN tioh8 eng7 li2 e5 koan5-leng5 lai5 kian3-siat, li2 sou2 phah-sng3 beh chiok-hok jin5-lui7 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 kok.  Tui3 an2-ni, bian2 sim2-mih8 kan-khou2, m7-bian2 hoan5-lo2 oe7 ian5-chhian5 kau3 loa7-ku2; tui3 an2-ni, li2 beh liam5-piN tat8 kau3 li2 e5 bok8-tek (Goal).”
	Chai7 Jin5-chu2, che kiam2 m7-si7 sit8-sit8 chai7-chai7 e5 chhi3 mah?  Bian2 kong2, chit e5 chhi3 m7-si7 ui7-tioh8 I pun2-sin e5 chhi3.  Lian5 Sat-tan3 iu5-goan5 to chai-iaN2, eng7 ko3-jin5-tek e5 khoai3-lok8 kap eng5-kng si7 boe7-thang lai5 in2-iu2 I.  Chi2-u7 si7 lan2, chiah oe7 siu7 hit-ho7 chhou-siok8 e5 in2-iu2.  Chong2-si7 Ia5-sou kiam2 m7-si7 ai3 khah-kin2 lai5 kian3-siat Siong7-te3 e5 kok, lai5 hou7 chit e5 kho2-lin5, lo5-khou2, choe7-ok e5 se3-kai3, tit-tioh8 hok-khi3!  Ia5-sou tek-khak u7 siuN7-tioh8 chit khoan2 sin5-jiah e5 ke3-ek8, na7 bo5, I chiu7 bo5 liah8 chit khoan2 choe3 si7 iu2-hek8.  Chi3-chio2 un2-tang3 ti7 tiap-a2(**tiap8-a2)-ku2 e5 tiong-kan, chit e5 iu2-hek8 u7 chhui-pek I e5 sim.
	Chong2-si7 Ia5-sou chai, kam2-than3 e5 sim kap sin3-giong2 e5 sim si7 u7 cheng-chha ti7-teh.  Eng7 sin5-jiah lai5 hou7 lang5 chhiN-kiaN, bo5 tek-khak si7 khah u7 li7-ek.  Ia5-sou lai5 se3-kan, m7-si7 beh eng7 I e5 koan5-leng5, si7 beh eng7 I e5 thiaN3-thang3 lai5 tit-tioh8 lang5.  I hong7-chhe si7 beh hian2-beng5 Siong7-te3 e5 thiaN3-thang3, jin5-chu5, i2-kip8 hi-seng e5 sim.  Siat-su2 an2-ni, na7-si7 boe7-thang tit-tioh8 lang5, chiu7 i2-goa7 bo5 hoat-tou7 thang tit-tioh8.  Sou2-i2 u7 nng7 hang7 e5 hoat-tou7, pai5 ti7 I e5 bin7-cheng5, I tioh8 ai3 soan2-tek8.  It, si7 ia3-lan2 e5 lou7, si7 sit-bang7, ian5-chhian5, siu7-khou2, Sip8-ji7-ke3 e5 lou7.  Ji, si7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 ku2-ku2 sou2 teh ng3-bang7 e5 lou7, chiu7-si7 Bi2-sai3-a beh tui3 Tian7-nih8 e5 Seng3-sou2 lai5 khai2-soan5 chhoa7 in chhut e5 lou7.
	Ia5-sou u7 keng2-soan2 I sou2 beh kiaN5 e5 lou7.
	I siuN7 hit e5 iong5-iN7 choe3 e5 sin5-jiah e5 iu2-hek8, bian2 kong2 tioh8 ku7-choat8.  Chong2-si7 siat-su2 si7 eng-kai tioh8 chin7 e5 lou7, I un2-tang3 bo5 ian5-chhian5, chek-si5 lian5 tui3 Seng3-tian7 e5 be2-liu to hoaN-hi2 lai5 tio5--loh8-khi3.  Chong2-si7 na7 bo5 beng5-beng5 chai hit e5 si7 eng-kai tioh8 chin7 e5, lai5 kiaN5 an2-ni, I si7 liah8-choe3 teh thiau-chian3 Siong7-te3 lai5 chhe thiN-sai3 po2-hou7 I.  Sou2-i2 Ia5-sou kong2, “U7 ki3-chai3 kong2, li2 m7-thang chhi3 Chu2 li2 e5 Siong7-te3.”

	“Mou5-kui2 koh chhoa7 I chiuN7 kek8 koaiN5 e5 soaN, eng7 thiN-e7 ban7 kok kap in e5 eng5-kng hou7 I khoaN3.”  Kiam2-chhai2 lan2 thang chiau3 sou2 ki3-chai3 e5 khoan2 lai5 thak8, “hek8-si7 tiam3 ti7 sinpkhu, a2-si7 bo5 tiam3 ti7 sin-khu,” Sat-tan3 ko2-jian5 u7 chhoa7 lan2 e5 Chu2 chiuN7 kek8 koaiN5 e5 soaN, eng7 ki5-iN7 e5 leng5-lek8, chiong thiN-e7 ban7 kok kap in e5 eng5-kng hou7 I khoaN3.
	Chong2-si7 khak toa7-bin7 chit ku3 e5 i3-su3, si7 teh piau2-beng5 Ia5-sou u7 ui7-tioh8 beh kian3-siat Siong7-te3 e5 kok, lai5 chhim-chhim siuN7 I chiong-lai5 sou2 phau7 e5 ke3-ek8, hit si5 ti7 I e5 thau5-nau2 lai7 u7 siuN7-tioh8 in Iu5-thai3 lang5 e5 Bi2-sai3-a e5 bong7-siong2, ng3-bang7 cheng3 iN7-pang e5 se3-kai3 lai5 hang5-hok8 I, thang koan2-hat thong thiN-e7.  Chit-tiap8 ti7 I e5 bin7-cheng5, u7 hian2-chhut sou2 iok-sok beh hou7 I e5 ong5-kok ti7-teh.  I long2 bo5 siuN7-tioh8 I sou2 tiam3 e5 soa-bou5 kan-ta teh siuN7 se3-kan e5 eng5-kng.  I u7 chu-chu teh siuN7 chin-choe7 hang7 e5 su7, chiu7-si7 teh siuN7 hit e5 chhan3-lan7, sui2-sui2 long2-chong2 e5 se3-kai3, i2-kip8 hit e5 tou-chhi7, ong5-kiong, kun-tui7, pu3-u7, i2-kip8 hiah e5 u7 mia5-siaN, u7 khui3-lat8 e5 cheng3 peh-siN3, kap hiah e5 khiam-pi lai5 pai3 chhong3-cho7 in e5 Chu2 e5 bin7-cheng5 e5 cheng3-lang5.
	I ai3 sit8-hian7 I e5 bong7-siong2, ng3-bang7 thang chiong heng7-hok i2-kip8 ko-siong7 e5 su7-giap8, lai5 khi2-cho7 ti7 chit e5 phaiN2 e5 se3-kai3!  Ia5-sou na7 choe3 Ong5, chit e5 se3-kai3 si7 chin eng5-kng!  Chong2-si7 beh an3-choaN2 chiah thang seng5-chiu7 chit e5?  Sat-tan3 u7 kong2, “Li2 na7 phak-loh8 pai3 goa2, chiah e5 long2 beh hou7 li2.”
	Lan2 tioh8 beng5-beng5 chai, I u7 siu7 in2-iu2 lai5 choe3 hit ho7 siok8 ti7 phaiN2 e5 heng5-tong7.  Kiam2-chhai2 I u7 chhin-chhiuN7 Mou5-han2-bek8-tek e5 khoan2, siuN7 ai3 eng7 po7-lek8 lai5 kian3-siat Siong7-te3 e5 kok.  A2-si7 khah toa7-bin7 si7 Mou5-kui2 u7 chhi3 I, kong2, “Li2 na7-si7 kap chit nse3-kan hiah e5 khah toa7-liap8 e5 lang5 saN-kap tho3-hiap8, a2-si7 kap Lo5-ma2 e5 koan5-se3; kap keng-hak8-su7, i2-kip8 Hoat-li7-sai3 lang5 saN-kap kiat-tong2, Li2 e5 kok un2-tang3 si7 bo5 oh-tit, si7 khoai3-khoai3 thang sit8-hian7.  Se3-kan it-chhe3 toa7 e5 un7-tong7, to long2 si7 eng7 an2-ni lai5 oan5-seng5.  Chi2-u7 si7 chit hoat, chiah thang tit-tioh8 se3-kai3 e5 eng5-kng.”  Ti7 kin-a2-jit8 choe7-choe7 u7 jin5-khi3 e5 soat-kau3-chia2, tek-khak iu5-goan5 u7 siu7-tioh8 chit khoan2 e5 in2-iu2, sim-lai7 ia7 bat siuN7 , kong2, “Goa2 tioh8 lai5 sio2-khoa2 kap hiah e5 u7 se3-lek8 e5 lang5 tho3-hiap8, kap in choe3 ho2 peng5-iu2; ia7 it-poaN e5 phian-kian3 khah-ho2 boh8-tit phah-phoa3; goa2 sou2 chhim-sin3 u7 kui2 tiam2 tiong7-iau3 e5 chin-li2, khah ho2 m7-bian2 siuN chhut-lat8 kan-cheng3, kiam2-chhai2 an2-ni choe3, si7 khah u7 li7-ek Siong7-te3, thang tit-tioh8 khah toa7 e5 se3-lek8, hou7 cheng3-lang5 khah ai3 lai5 thiaN goa2 e5 oe7, thang khah u7 kong-hau7, lai5 soan-thoan5 chong-kau3 e5 to7-li2.”
	Mou5-kui2 tui3 Ia5-sou sou2 kong2 e5, toa7-pou7-hun7 si7 chin-sit8 e5 oe7, u7 li2-khi3 ti7-teh.  Siat-su2 lan2 na7 kam-goan7 hang5-hok8 Mou5-kui2 e5 ke3-ek8, lan2 un2-tang3 oe7 tit-tioh8 se3-kai3 e5 kui2 pou7-hun7, i2-kip8 in e5 eng5-kng.  Phak-teh pai3 goa2!  Kin-jit8 e5 kau3-hoe7, ma7-si7 bo5 siong5-siong5 gau5 siam2-pi7 chit khoan2 e5 chhi3; kau3-hoe7 si7 khah ai3 kap se3-kan hiah e5 chiau3 khoaN3 si7 u7 se3-lek8 e5 lang5 saN tho3-hiap8, saN the5-he5, teh ng3-bang7 tui3 an2-ni thang lai5 “khah-iaN5 se3-kai3.”
	Chong2-si7 Ia5-sou koat-toan3 bo5 beh kap phaiN2 e5 se3-kai3 saN-kap tho3-hiap8.  Siong7-te3 kok e5 sit8-hian7, si7 eng7 thiaN3-thang3, hi-seng, khek-ki2, khiam-pi, bo5 ti2-khong3 e5 hoat-tou7 lai5 chin3-heng5, ia7 i e5 chin3-heng5 si7 ban7-ban7 lo5-khou2 e5 su7.  Siong7-te3 e5 kok si7 ku2-tng5 tioh8-boa5 e5 kang.  Siong7-te3 e5 kok si7 tioh8 ai3 keng-ke3 sou2 se3-ki2 chiah oe7 thang oan5-seng5.  Lian5 kin-a2-jit8, sui-si7 keng-ke3 2000 ni5 e5 ku2, ma7 sit8-hian7 iau2-be7 chit8 poaN3.  Put-ko3 lan2 sin3, ti7 chiong-lai5 tek-khak oe7 sit8-hian7.  Chit se3-kan e5 cheng3 pang-kok, tek-khak oe7 pian3-chiaN5 lan2 e5 Siong7-te3 i2-kip8 lan2 e5 Chu2 e5 Seng3-kok, I tek-khak choe3 Ong5, koan2-hat thiN-e7 kau3 tai7-tai7 bo5 chin7.  Sat-tan3 u7 chiong i hit e5 iong5-iN7 piN5-thaN2 e5 lou7, lai5 pai5 ti7 I e5 bin7-cheng5 in2-iu2 I, kio3 I kan-ta hui3-liau2 sio2-khoa2 e5 cheng-sin5, phak-pai3 i chit8-e7, chiu7 thang bian2 kiaN5 hit ehi5am-iau3, khun3-lan5 e5 gi7-bu7 e5 lou7-cham7.  Chong2-si7 Ia5-sou long2 bo5 chiap-lap8 hit ho7 e5 in2-iu2.
	“Sat-tan3 the3-khi3; in-ui7 u7 kki3-chai3 kong2, Tioh8 pai3 Chu2 li2 e5 Siong7-te3; tok8-tok8 hok8-sai7 I na7-tiaN7.”

	Chit-tiap8 lun7 Ia5-sou sou2 siu7 e5 chhi3, lan2 i2-keng saN-kap siuN7 chheng-chho2.  Ti7-chia ai3 saN-kap lai5 khoaN3 u7 sim2-mih8 thang choe3 lan2 e5 ka3-si7.
	(1) Lan2 e5 Chu2, chiu7-si7 hou7 lan2 thang ko3-pek8 lan2 e5 sit-pai7 e5, si7 oe7 tong5-cheng5 ti7 lan2 sou2 siu7 e5 chhi3, in-ui7 I “hoan7-su7 piN5-piN5 u7 siu7-chhi3, chong2-si7 bo5 choe7.”  Sui-jian5 I si7 bo5 hang5-hok8 choe7-ok, iau2-ku2 bo5 in-ui7 an2-ni, chiu7 khah boe7 tong5-cheng5 lan2 e5 loan2-jiok8.  Chit-tiap8 chhiaN2 lai5 siuN7 chit tiam2.  Phi3-ju7 lai5 kong2, u7 saN e5 hiaN-ti7 chin7-lat8 beh peh-chiuN7 soaN-be2-liu, hiam2-iau3 e5 sou2-chai7.  Hit e5 seng3-li7 e5 choe3 ko-tiam2, si7 u7 chit8 pah kham2.  Goa2 peh kau3 50 kham2 chiu7 bo5 lat8, soah--khi3.  goa2 e5 ji7-hiaN u7 chhut-lat8 phihN8-phihN8-chhoan2, kiong5-kiong5 peh kau3 70 kham2 chiah sit-pai7.  I oe7-thang tong5-cheng5 goa2.  I ia7 chai-iaN2 goa2 e5 kan-khou2.  Chong2-si7 goa2 e5 toa7-hiaN tiam3 goan2 e5 sin-piN ma7-si7 phihN8-phihN8-chhoan2, teh kou2-bu2 goan2, ia7 i ka-ki7 m7-kheng2 soah.  Jit8 i2-keng teh-beh am3, chong2-si7 I soa3-chiap teh hun3-tou3, koaN7 lau5 moa2-bin7, cheng5-khui3 m7-hu3 au7-khui3, chong2-si7 I bo5 hioh-khun3.  Kau3-be2 I u7 tek-seng3, lai5 keng-ke3 khun2-pek kap lo5-khou2.  I kiam2 boe7-thang chhin-chhiuN7 hit e5 sit-pai7 e5 ji7-hiaN, hiah-nih8 gau5 tong5-cheng5 goa2 mah?  I sou2 siu7 e5 kan-khou2, si7 pi2 goan2 nng7 lang5 khah choe7 lah.
	(2) I si7 oe7 thang choe3 ji7-hiaN sou2 boe7-thang choe3 e5, chiu7-si7 I u7 chi2-si7 lan2 chai, lan2 un2-tang3 oe7 tek-seng3.  Che si7 te7-ji7 hang7 e5 ka3-si7, thang kou2-bu2 lan2, kam2-tong7 lan2, hou7 lan2 thang khah-iaN5 ti7 sou2 siu7 e5 chhi3.  Tek-seng3 e5 Ia5-sou, tui3 khong3-ia2 u7 khui siaN ka7 lan2 kong2, “Goa2 e5 loan2-jiok8, hoan5-bun7, siu7-chhi3 e5 hiaN-ti7 ah!  tioh8 chin3-cheng5 lai5 khah-iaN5!  In-ui7 lin2 oe7 tek-seng3 lah.  Bo5 u7 sim2-mih8 li2-iu5 thang kong2 lin2 si7 boe7-thang khah-iaN5.  Lin2 boe7-thang khah-iaN5, si7 tui3 ti7 lin2 u7 sit-taN2 e5 ian5-kou3.  Lin2 siuN ke3-thau5 kiaN5-hiaN5 lai5 kang2-lun7 chhi3 e5 khui3-lat8, i2-kip8 hit e5 sit-pai7 e5 chhiN-chham2 e5 cheng5-keng2.  Hit ho7 oe7, si7 kam2-cheng5-tek e5 oe7.  He si7 bo5 tam2-liong7 e5 tam5-lun7.  He si7 bo5-iaN2 e5 tai7-chi3.  Tioh8 choe3 chin-sit e5 lang5!  Tioh8 eng7 goa2 e5 khui3-lat8 lai5 chhi3 khoaN3 mai7.  Goa2 i2-keng u7 chiaN5-choe3 lang5, lai5 piau2-beng5 jin5-seng3 si7 u7 khui3-lat8 kau3 chaiN2-iuN7.  Goa2 u7 tiam3 ti7 lin2 e5 sin-piN, chhin-chhiuN7 chit8 e5 bo5 thang i-oa2 e5 lang5, chi2-u7 tan-sun5 sin3 Siong7-te3 lai5 cheng-chian3.  Goa2 sou2 tu2-tioh8 e5 cheng-chian3, pi2 lin2 sou2 beh siu7 e5 koh-khah si7 u7 bu5-han7-liong7 e5 khun3-lan5 ti7-teh.  Iau2-ku2 Goa2 u7 khah-iaN5.  Goa2 ti7 toa7 e5 cheng-chian3 u7 khah-iaN5, chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni, lin2 ti7 khah-sio2 e5 , iu5-goan5 oe7 khah-iaN5.”
	Tui3 an2-ni, Mou5-kui2 u7 li7-khui I, u7 thiN-sai3 lai5 su-hau7 I.  Che si7 teh piau2-beng5 I e5 kho2-lin5 e5 cheng3 lou5-pok8, tak8-pai2 khah-iaN5 Mou5-kui2 e5 chhi3 liau2-au7, iu5-goan5 u7 thiN-sai3 beh lai5 su-hau7 in.



Te7-3 chiuN	Choe3-Chhou e5 Hak8-Seng

	Koh ke3 chit8 le2-pai3.  Chit-tiap8 lan2 sou2 ai3 chu3-bak8 e5, m7-si7 ti7 hit e5 bo5 lang5 kau3 e5 khong3-ia2 kap Mou5-kui2 teh kau-chian3 e5 Ia5-sou, si7 hit e5 cheng-sin5 i2-keng chhiN2-gou7, thoat-chhut kin2-tiuN e5 seng-oah8, hok8-to3 phou2-thong e5 cheng-sin5 lai5 kap phou2-thong lang5 teh saN-kap kau-poe5 e5 Ia5-sou.  I si7 chin i3-ai3 khia7-khi2 ti7 Ka-li7-li7 lai5 kap hiah e5 tan-sun5, ho2 kau-poe5 e5 choh-sit-lang5 saN-kap ong2-lai5.
	Kai-chai3 hit e5 ni5-lau7 e5 Iok-han7 si7 chin ho2 ki3-ti5, na7 bo5, lan2 si7 oe7 sit-loh8 hit e5 Siu7-chhi3 au7 chit chiu-kan te7-it u7 chhu3-bi7 e5 kou3-su7, chiu7-si7 teh kong2-khi2 Ia5-sou chhe7-tioh8 choe3-chhou e5 hak8-seng e5 jit8 e5 kou3-su7.  Ma2-thai3, Ma2-kho2, i2-kip8 Lou7-ka long2 si7 kong2-khi2 ti7 Chu2 e5 seng-gai5 tiong hiah e5 tiong7-iau3 e5 su7-kiaN7na7-tiaN7.  In long2 u7 ki3-chai3 kiong7-tong5 e5 lek8-su2, i2-kip8 chhou-tai7 kau3-hoe7 sou2 liu5-thoan5 e5 kiong7-tong5 e5 Hok-im.  Chong2-si7 ti7 in e5 kou3-su7, u7 lang3 choe7-choe7 cham7 bo5 kong2-khi2.  Lan2 ti7-chia sou2 beh kong2 chit chan5 si7 in sou2 hut-liok8 e5 tiam2.  In ki3-chai3 hit e5 Siu7-chhi3 e5 kou2-su7 liau2, chiu7 long2 soa3-chiap kong2-khi2 Ia5-sou ti7 Ka-li7-li7 e5 thoan5-to7 e5 su7, iau2-ku2 ti7 hit tiong-kan sou2 u7 tu2-tioh8 e5, in si7 long2 bo5 ki3-chai3 poaN3-hang7.
	Chong2-si7 hit e5 tiam3 ti7 hng7-hng7 I2-hut-sou2 e5 lau7 hak8-seng Iok-han7, u7 hian-khui chiah e5 Hok-im-su, ia7 thak8-liau2 bo5 sim2-mih8 boan2-chiok, ti7 i e5 sim-lai7 na2 teh pou2-chhiong ti7 hiah e5 kou3-su7 tiong sou2 lang3-khiah e5 sou2-chai7.  I thak8-tioh8 Siu7-chhi3 e5 kou3-su7 liau2, hit si5 lan2 thang liau7-siong2 i u7 chhut-siaN kong2, Ai ah!   in long2 hit-liok8 Siu7-chhi3 au7 hiah e5 ki5-iN7 e5 kui2-jit8 ku2 e5 kou3-su7!  I thak8-tioh8 Ia5-sou hian2-jian5 chhut-thau5 chio hak8-seng lai5 tam-tng chit-hun7, hit si5 i ti7 sim-lai7 chin ki5-koai3, siuN7 kong2, In thai2 oe7 long2 bo5 kong2-khi2 goan2 tong-si5 chaiN2-iuN7 kap I sek8-sai7 e5 cheng5-keng2.
	Iok-han7 u7 choe7-choe7 pat8-lang5 sou2 bo5 e5, thang siau3-liam7 e5 ki3-ek, in-ui7 i ti7 Ia5-sou e5 sin-piN, u7 thang tit-tioh8 choe7-choe7 chin sui2 e5 ki3-ek.  I ti7 sim-lai7 siong5-siong5 siuN7 tioh8 hiah e5 su7, soa3 lai5 kong2 hou7 cheng3-lang5 thiaN, ia7 soa2 chiong hiah e5 sui2-sui2 e5 ki3-ek lai5 ki3-chai3 ti7 i e5 Hok-im-su e5 lai7-bin7.
	Ti7 i long2-chong2 e5 ki3-ek e5 tiong-kan, te7-it tu3-hian7 e5, chiu7-si7 oe7 ki3-tit ti7 gou7-chap8 ni5 cheng5 e5 u7 chit8-e7-pou, iok-liok8 si3-tiam2 cheng e5 si5 sou2 keng-giam7 e5, chiu7-si7 i ti7 hit si5 chiah chhou-chhou kiN3-tioh8 i e5 Chu2 e5 bin7.  Hit jit8 si7 i it seng e5 ki3-liam7 jit8.  I tek-khak bo5 hut-liok8 hit jit8 e5 keng-giam7.  I u7 chiong Ia5-sou Siu7-chhi3 au7 chit8 chiu-kan e5 su7 long2 chho2-ko2 khi2-lai5, iah8 hit e5 ki3-liam7 jit8 si7 choe3 hit chit8 chiu-kan e5 tou5 e5 tiong-sim.  Sit8-chai7 chin chhu3-bi7, lan2 thang kong2, hit jit8 toa7-bin7 si7 lan2 e5 pai3-lak8, in e5 an-hioh-jit8.  In-ui7 i u7 ki3-chai3 tui3 hit jit8 khi2, lian5-lian5 si3-jit8 ku2 sou2 tu2-tioh8 e5 su7, iah8 soa3 kong2-khi2 chiah e5 jit8 liau2-au7, koh ke3 saN-jit8 ti7 Ka-li7-li7 e5 Ka-na2 u7 hun-in e5 ian5-siah8.  Hit-tiap8 Iu5-thai3 lang5 e5 hong-siok8, si7 tiaN7-tioh8 ti7 pai3-saN choe3 hun-in.  Sou2-i2 lan2 thang tui3 pai3-saN sng3 to3-tng2, kau3 chin3-cheng5 le2-pai3 e5 pai3 si3, lai5 siuN7 hit tiong-kan sou2 tu2-tioh8 e5 su7-sit8.

	ChhiaN2 chu3-i3 lai5 khoaN3 i sou2 pai5-liat8 e5 cheng5-keng2.  thau5 chit8-jit8 si7 pai3-si3.  Iok-han7 si7 kap i e5 sian-siN KiaN5 soe2-le2 e5 Iok-han7 saN-kap ti7 Pek-tai7-ni5.  I u7 kap chit8 kun5 e5 siau3-lian5 e5 tang5-phoaN7, chiu7-si7 u7 khng3 him-bou7 khah ko-siong7 e5 sim e5, tai7-ke kap kui toa7-tin7 e5 cheng3-lang5 tui3 Ka-li7-li7 loh8-lai5 thiaN chit e5 sin e5 sian-ti Iok-han7 e5 ka3-si7.  In chek-si5 te3 i lai5 choe3 i e5 hak8-seng, soa3 chu7 an2-ni tiam3 ti7 i e5 sin-piN, kau3 tho2-hai2 e5 si5-ki5 chiah koh to3-khi3 Ka-li7-li7.
	KiaN5 soe2-le2 e5 Iok-han7 e5 thoan5-to7, u7 put-chi2 io5-choah Pa-lek8-su-theng3 e5 choan5-toe7, ti3-kau3 hou7 khia7-khi2 ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 Hoat-li7-sai3 lang5 khoaN3-choe3 iau3-kin2, u7 chhe tai7-piau2 lai5 tham3-mng7 i.  Ti7 hit e5 pai3-si3, toa7-bin7 si7 Ia5-sou tui3 khong3-ia2 to3-tng2--lai5 e5 chin3-cheng5 jit8, hiah e5 su3-chia2 u7 chiau5-kau3.  Chit e5 toa7 e5 Soan-kau3-su choan5-jian5 eng7 seng5-sit8, bo5 un2-moa5 e5 thai3-tou7 lai5 chih-chiap in.  Khiok I ma7-si7 long2 bo5 sim2-mih8 su7 thang un2-bat8.
	“ChhiaN2 ka7 goan2 kong2, Li2 si7 chi7-chui7?”
	“Goa2 m7-si7 Ki-tok.”
	“Che si7 chaiN2-iuN7?  Li2 si7 I2-li7-a mah?”
	“M7-si7.”
	“Li2 su7 hit e5 sian-ti mah?”
	“M7-si7.”
	“Na7-si7 an2-ni, Li2 si7 chi7-chui7? hou7 goan2 thang he5-hok chhe goan2 e5.  Li2 tioh8 kong2 ka-ki7 si7 chi7-chui7?”
	“Goa2 chiu7-si7 teh kio3 ti7 khong3-ia2 e5, i e5 siaN, kong2, Siu tit8 Chu2 e5 lou7, chhin-chhiuN7 sian-ti I2-sai3-a sou2 kong2 e5.”
	“Li2 na7 m7-si7 Ki-tok, iah8 m7-si7 I2-li7-a, iah8 m7-si7 hit e5 sian-ti, chaiN2-iuN7 kiaN5 soe2-le2 ah?”
	“Goa2 eng7 chui2 kiaN5 soe2-le2; u7 khia7 ti7 lin2 tiong-kan e5, lin2 m7-bat I.”

	“Keh jit8,” KiaN5 soe2-le2 e5 Iok-han7 u7 kap kui2 mia5 e5 ti-ki2, saN-kap teh khia7 e5 si5, hut-jian5 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 Ia5-sou, tui3 lak8 le2-pai3 cheng5 I sou2 un2-bat8 hit e5 soaN-io e5 lou7 chhut--lai5, ng3 in tai7-ke chin3-cheng5 teh kiaN5.  I e5 kiaN5-tah8 si7 chin-chiaN3 ia3-sian7 e5 khoan2, hit si3-chap8 jit8 ku2 thang chhiN-kiaN e5 kin2-tiuN e5 cheng-sin5, iau2 u7 hian2-chhut ti7 I e5 bin7-mau7; ti7 I e5 bak8-chiu iau2 u7 hian2-chhut pat8 se3-kai3 e5 kong-chhai2 ti7-teh.  KiaN5 soe2-le2 e5 Iok-han7 khak-sit8 ti7 i2-cheng5 u7 teh ki5-koai3, tau3-ti2 Ia5-sou si7 un2-bat8 khi3 ti7 ta2-loh8.  Chit-tiap8 i chek-si5 jin7-tit I, chiu7 eng7 jiat8-jiat8 kiong-keng3 e5 thai3-tou7 lai5 po3 i e5 tang5-phoaN7, kong2, “Li2 khoaN3, Siong7-te3 e5 IuN5-ko, chiu7-si7 tam-tng se3-kan e5 choe7 e5.  Chit e5 chiu7-si7 goa2 sou2 bat kong2 e5.  Goa2 bat khoaN3-kiN3 Seng3 Sin5 chhin-chhiuN7 chiN2-a2 tui3 thiN kang3-loh8 hioh ti7 I e5 teng2-bin7.  Goa2 bat khoaN3-kiN3, soa3 lai5 kan-cheng3 chit e5 si7 Siong7-te3 e5 KiaN2.”
	Chit e5 I2-hut-sou2 e5 lau7 kam-tok, koh chit8 pai2 kam2-kak--tioh8 siau3-lian5 e5 khi3-khai3, in-ui7 i u7 koh siuN7-tioh8 cha2-si5 chhou-chhou khoaN3-kiN3 Ia5-sou hit-si5 i e5 sim siu7 kam2-tong7 kau3 chaiN2-iuN7.  In-ui7 i chai i sou2 khoaN3-kiN3 e5, si7 ti7 ku2-ku2 e5 tiong-kan I2-sek-liat8 lang5 sou2 teh him-bou7 theng3-hau7 e5, si7 beh tam-tng se3-kan e5 choe7, taN lan2 e5 tang7-taN3 e5.

	Iok-han7 koh chin3-cheng5 lai5 hoe5-siong2 hit si5 e5 ki3-ek, chiu7-si7 kong2, koh keh-jit8, chiu7-si7 in e5 an-hioh-jit8, ti7 hit e7-pou Iok-han7 u7 kap i e5 tang5-phoaN7 An-tek-liat8 teh tam5-lun7 in e5 sian-siN e5 su7, un2-tang3 ia7 si7 teh tam5-lun7 Ia5-sou e5 su7, hit si5 Ia5-sou u7 tu2-tu2 beh kiaN5 ke3 khoe-kiN5 e5 lou7.  Lan2 thang siong2-siong7 KiaN5 soe2-le2 e5 Iok-han7, sim-lai7 un2-tang3 u7 siu7 kam2-tong7, chiah lai5 khan i e5 siau3-lian5 e5 tang5-phoaN7 e5 chhiu2, pi2 kong2, “Li2 khoaN3!  Siong7-te3 e5 IuN5-ko!”  Siong7-te3 e5 IuN5-ko!  In iau2-be7 khoaN3-kiN3 Siong7-te3 e5 IuN5-ko siu7 teng3 ti7 Kok-kok-thaN e5 i2-cheng5, chu7-jian5 si7 boe7 thang liau2-kai2 hit e5 long2-chong2 e5 i3-gi7.  Chong2-si7 in e5 sim u7 chhut tui3 tut8-jian5 e5 chhiong-tong7, ho2-taN2 lai5 te3 I, chiu7-si7 “u7 nng7 e5 hak8-seng thiaN i sou2 kong2, chiu7 te3 Ia5-sou.”  Toa7-bin7 si7 in-ui7 KiaN5 soe2-le2 e5 Iok-han7 khiok iau2 si7 u7 ko3-jin5-tek e5 ai3-cheng5 ti7-teh, chong2-si7 hit e5 ai3-cheng5 si7 boe7 thang kim3-chi2 in te3 Ia5-sou.  Iok-han7 chi2-u7 si7 choe3 i e5 Chu2 e5 sian-hong na7-tiaN7.
	Hit nng7 e5 siau3-lian5 e5 tho2-hai2 lang5, beh chhut-hoat loh8-khi3 khoe-kiN5, hit si5 lan2 thang siong2-siong7, in un2-tang3 si7 chin ui3 siau2-le2, kiaN-kiaN, chin m7 koaiN3-si3 e5 khoan2, chit8 sim hoaN-hi2 ai3 kap Ia5-sou kong2-oe7, ia7 chit8 sim kiaN-hiaN5 m7-kaN2.  Ia5-sou chit8-e7 thiaN-kiN3 in e5 kha-pou7 siaN, chiu7 oat8-thau5 khoaN3-kiN3 in teh te3 I, chhin-chhiuN7 ti7 tak8 si5-tai7, I u7 oat8-thau5 lai5 khoaN3 hiah e5 him-bou7 ai3 te3 I, iau2-ku2 bo5 tam2-liong7 e5 hak8-seng chit8 poaN.  I eng7 chhin-chhiat, bian2-le7 e5 oe7 lai5 mng7 in kong2, “Lin2 teh chhe7 sim2-mih8?”  Ia5-sou kong2 chit ku3, kiam2-chhai2 I e5 i3-su3 si7 teh chhi3 in, ai3 hoan3-khi2 in e5 sim, lai5 ka-ki7 sim2-mng7 in sou2 teh chhe7 e5.  Ia5-sou si7 ai3 in chai-iaN2.  Ia5-sou si7 bo5 iau3-kin2 lang5 e5 gu5-gong7, loan2-jiok8, lou2-tun7, i2-kip8 ki5-thaN, put-ko3 kan-ta ai3 lang5 ti7 sim-lai7 oe7 hiau2 kam2-kak, kong2, “Goa2 si7 teh chhe7 Siong7-te3.  goa2 si7 ai3 hok8-sai7 Li2.”
	Chit nng7 e5 siau3-lian5 e5 hiong-chhoan lang5 thiaN-liau2 si7 chin chhiN-kiaN, chin hun7-loan7, ti3-kau3 boe7 hiau2-tit tioh8 chaiN2-iuN7 in3, soa3 mng7 kong2, “Liap8-pi2, Li2 si7 tiam3 ti7 ta2-loh8?”  Ah!  Ia5-sou chai-iaN2 in e5 khiam3-kheh.  I chiu7 ka7 in kong2, “Lin2 lai5 chiu7 oe7 khoaN3-kiN3.”  I chiu7 chhoa7 in kau3 I sou2 toa3 hit e5 m7-chiaN5-mih8, soe3-soe3 e5 chhu3-a2; hit jit8 in u7 kap Ia5-sou saN-kap toa3.  Iok-han7 e5 ki3-ek si7 put-chi2 beng5; hoe5-kou3 poaN3-se3-ki2 cheng5 e5 su7 kau3 chin siong5-se3 kong2, “hit-si5 iok-liok8 si3-tiam2 cheng.”  ChaiN2-iuN7 i oe7-thang hut-liok8 hit-si5 e5 cheng5-keng2?  In ti7 hit-jit8 e5 am3 thau5-a2, kan-ta kap Ia5-sou saN-kap tiam3 ti7-hia, soa3 siu7-tioh8 I e5 kan2-tan e5 khoan2-thai7, ia7 soa3 chu7-iu5 lai5 kap I tam5-lun7, mng7 I tang, mng7 I sai, lai5 thiaN I e5 ka3-si7, ia7 hit-si5 I un2-tang3 u7 tui3 in kong2-khi2 koan-he7 I e5 sim tioh8 chaiN2-iuN7 ui7-tioh8 jin5-lui7 e5 choe7-ok lai5 kan-khou2, i2-kip8 tui3 ti7 Siong7-te3 kok I jiat8-jiat8 e5 ke3-ek8 kap hi-bong7 e5 su7, ti7 au7-lai5 in siuN7-tioh8 hit-si5 e5 cheng5-keng2, kiam2 m7-si7 kam2-khai3 bu5-liong7!  Ia5-sou u7 tong5-cheng5 in, ti3-kau3 u7 hoan3-khi2 in hoaN-hi2 lai5 ui3-ui3 kong2-khi2 in e5 chi3-khi3.  Lan2 khak-sin3 I thiaN-liau2 un2-tang3 u7 tui3 in kong2, toa7-bin7 I e5 khoan2 tu2-tu2 si7 ai3 kong2 an2-ni ia7-ku2-kaN2, “u7 chit8-jit8 goa2 ai3 lin2 nng7 lang5, khia7 ti7 goa2 e5 sin-piN lai5 pang-chan7 goa2.”  Chit-ho7 oe7 si7 gau5 chhui-pek lang5 e5 sim, oe7 in2-chhoa7 lang5, hoat-hui lang5 sou2 u7 e5 ho2 e5 pou7-hun7.
	Chhi3 siuN7 chit nng7 e5 siau3-lian5 lang5, ti7 hit e5 moa2-thiN-chhiN e5 am3-mi5, li7-khui I to3-tng2 khi3 in tau, hit-si5 in e5 sim-koaN un2-tang3 chin ki5-koai3 koh chin jiat8, un2-tang3 sim-sim liam7-liam7 to si7 teh su-siong2 hit e5 sin e5 peng5-iu2.  “Lan2 un2-tang3 te3 I, ia7 koh beh te3 I kau3 si2.”  Hit e5-hng in khoaN3 choan5 se3-kai3 si7 long2 pian3-oaN7 liau2-liau2, it-chhe3 bo5 m7 oaN7 choe3 sin.

	Iok-han7 kong2, hit am3 khi3 chhe7 Ia5-sou e5, “Ki5-tiong chit8 e5 si7 Se-bun5, Pi2-tek e5 hiaN-ti7 An-tek-liat8.”  Iau2 hit e5 si7 i pun2-sin, i si7 khiam-pi m7-kaN2 kong2.  An-tek-liat8 ti7 hit am3 kap Ia5-sou kau-poe5 liau2, sim-lai7 kam2-kak bu5-siong7 e5 hoaN-hi2 khoai3-lok8, chiu7 chek-si5 khi3 chhe7 i e5 hiaN-ti7.  “Se-bun5! Goan2 i2-keng tu2-tioh8 Bi2-sai3-a (hoan-ek8 chiu7-si7 Ki-tok) lah ne7!”  Goan2 m7-si7 kan-ta tui3 Kia5 soe2-le2 e5 Iok-han7 thiaN-kiN3 na7-tiaN7.  goan2 pun2-sin si7 i2-keng u7 tu2-tioh8 I.  Chit ho7 e5 khak-sin3 si7 tui3 ti7 hit am3 in u7 kap Ia5-sou choe3-he2 sou2 tit-tioh8 e5.  Lang5 tui3 pun2-sin e5 sim-toe2 e5 keng-giam7, oe7 thang khak-sin3 lai5 kong2, goan2 i2-keng u7 tu2-tioh8 Ki-tok, hit-ho7 lang5 chin-chai3 u7 hok-khi3!  Chong2-si7 na5 oe7-thang koh in2-chhoa7 pat8 lang5 lai5 chiu7-kun7 I, hit ho7 e5 lang5 si7 koh-khah u7 hok-khi3!
	Chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni, “Antek-liat8 chiu7 chhoa7 Se-bun5 chiu7-kun7 Ia5-sou.”  Che chiu7-si7 hit e5 so3-seng3, chhiong-tong7-tek, to-cheng5 khoai3 tioh8-tak e5 Pi2-tek, jip8 I e5 kun5 e5 khoan2-sit.  Pi2-tek tu2-tu2 lai5 e5 si5, Ia5-sou khoaN3-kiN3 i, chiu7 sui(**sui5)-si5 ka7 i ho7 sin e5 mia5.  Kiam2-chhai2 si7 in-ui7 Pi2-tek u7 ka-ki7 kian3-siau3, tam7-poh8 sit-chi3 chai-iaN2 i e5 seng3 khoai3 tin2-tang7, gau5 io5-choah.  Ia5-sou chit8-e7 khoaN3-kiN3 i, sui5-si5 liau2-kai2 i e5 sim-cheng5.  “Iok-han7 e5 kiaN2 Se-bun5 ah, goa2 long2 bat li2.  Li2 chit-tiap8 sui-jian5 si7 loan2-jiok8, iau2-ku2 u7 chit8-jit8 li2 beh chiaN5-choe3 iong2-chong3 e5 lang5.  U7 chit8-jit8, li2 beh chheng-choe3 Ki-hoat, chiu7-si7 chioh8-poaN5.”  Che si7 piau2-beng5 Chu2 e5 gau5 chong3 lang5 e5 taN2, eng7 thiaN3-thang3 e5 tong7-chhat-lat8, gau5 khoaN3 kau3 lang5 e5 chiong-lai5.
	Iok-han7 chit-tiap8 iau2 si7 oe7 ki3-tit hiang3 tang5(**tang)-si5-a2 e5 cheng5-keng2.  Pi2-tek khiok-si7 chu7 cha2-cha2 chiu7 i2-keng ke3-sin, khi3 tiam3 hit e5 leng5-kai3 kap i e5 Chu2 saN-kap khia7-khi2, ia7 chit e5 lau7 hak8-seng hit-tiap8 iau2-ku2 oe7 ki3-tit Ia5-sou chhou-chhou teh khoaN3 Pi2-tek, hit-si5 I e5 bak8-chiu e5 khoan2-sit, si7 sio-siang7 ti7 saN-ni5-au7 e5 u7 chit8-jit8, koh chit8 pai2 lai5 “Oat8-thau5 khoaN3 Pi2-tek, iah8 Pi2-tek chiu7 chhut-khi3 goa7-bin7, toa7 thi5-khau3,” hit-si5 e5 khoan2.

	Keh-jit8, Ia5-sou beh-khi3 Ka-li7-li7, lou7-nih8 ai3 tui3 Ka-na2 keng-ke3.  Ti7 hit-tiau5 chhiong3-koan3 to7-lou7 e5 tiong-kan, chit cham7 si7 chin sui2, liong2-peng5 u7 chu7-jian5 e5 keng2-ti3.  Ia5-sou beh chhut-hoat khi3 Ka-li7-li7, lou7-nih8 I tioh8 hioh-khun3 ti7 Ka-na2 lai5 hu3-hun-in e5 ian5-siah8.  Hit-si5 u7 saN-e5 hak8-seng kap I choe3-tin7 khi3, in-ui7 in e5 chhu3 long2 si7 ti7 hit e5 keh-piah, ia7 koh iu5-goan5 siu7 pheng3-chhiaN2 tioh8 khi3 hu3 hit e5 hun-in.  Ti7 hit e5 lou7-tiong, Ia5-sou u7 tu2-tioh8 Hui-lek8.  Lan2 thang ho2-taN2 kong2, Ia5-sou si7 i2-keng bat i.  Hui-lek8 u7 chit8-ui7 put-chi2 chhin-bit8 e5 peng5-iu2, kio3-choe3 Na2-tan3-giap8, tiam3 ti7 Ka-na2.  Lan2 thang chhui-toan3 chit e5 Na2-tan3-giap8 si7 chit8 e5 keng3-khian5 e5 Iu5-thai3 lang5, i e5 seng3-cheng5 si7 ai3 thiam5-cheng7, ai3 bek8-siong2, ia7 ai3 siong5-siong5 kap Siong7-te3 kau-poe5.  I kap Hui-lek8 un2-tang3 khah siong5 choe3-he2 saN-kap tam5-lun7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 tui3 chiong-lai5 sou2 teh ng3-bang7 e5 su7.
	Hui-lek8 e5 sim boe7 tan2-tit thang koaN2-kin2 kau3 Ka-na2, lai5 chhe7-tioh8 i e5 peng5-iu2 Na2-tan3-giap8.
	“Na2-tan3-giap8 ah, Mou5-se ki3 ti7 lut8-hoat, kap chiah e5 sian-ti sou2 ki3 e5, goan2 i2-keng tu2-tioh8 I.”
	“I si7 chi7-chui?”
	“Chiu7-si7 Iok-sek e5 kiaN2, Na2-sat-lek8 lang5, Ia5-sou.”
	Chong2-si7 Na2-tan3-giap8 sim-lai7 khng3 giau5-gi5.  I bo5 teh liau5-bang7 Bi2-sai3-a, beh chiau3 chit khoan2 lang5 sou2 liau7 boe7-tioh8 e5 hoat-tou7 lai5 chhut-hian7.  Toa7-bin7 i si7 lau7 toa7-lang5, siuN ke3-thau5 soe3-ji7, bo5 khoai3-khoai3 lai5 thiaN chit e5 siau3-lian5 lang5 sou2 kong2 e5 oe7, lai5 hoah8 i e5 kha khi3 chhe7 Ia5-sou.  I eng7 tong-si5 hit ho7 teh biau2-si7 lang5 e5 siok8-gu2, lai5 in3 kong2, “Na2-sat-lek8 kiam2-oe7 chhut sim2-mih8 ho2-mih8 mah?”
	Hui-lek8 bo5 ai3 kap i saN pian7-lun7.  I chi2-u7 kong2, “Lai5 khoaN3!”  Si7 lai5 khoaN3!  Lan2 tui3 hiah e5 giau5-gi5 Ia5-sou e5 lang5 te7-it ho2 e5 in3-tap, chiu7-si7 chit khoan2 e5 oe7.  Hui-lek8 sim-lai7 teh siuN7, lang5 na7 lai5 kiN3-tioh8 Ia5-sou, bun7-toe5 chiu7 kai2-koat.  Lang5 na7 oa2-lai5 khoaN3 Ia5-sou chit8-e7, thiaN Ia5-sou kong2 chit8-ku3, hit e5 kong-hau7 si7 khah iaN5 it-chhe3 e5 pian7-lun7.  sou2-i2 Hui-lek8 u7 chhoa7 Na2-tan3-giap8 chhut-lai5 kiN3 pat8 e5 hak8-seng.  “Ia5-sou khoaN3-kiN3 Na2-tan3-giap8 chiu7-kun7 I” (koh chit8-pai2 chu3-i3 ti7 Iok-han7, chaiN2-iuN7 koh teh hoe5-siong2 Chu2 e5 bak8-chiu e5 khoan2-sit), chiu7 chi2 i kong2, “Li2 khoaN3, chin-chiaN3 si7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5, sim bo5 khui2-khiat e5.”
	Ia5-sou chit8-e7 khoaN3 i, chiu7 tit-tioh8 Na2-tan3-giap8, hou7 i e5 sim-sin5 chek-si5 kap I kiat-lian5.  In-ui7 ti7 lang5 e5 lai7-bin7 u7 hit ho7 ti-kak e5 pun2-leng5 ti7-teh, tui3 chit e5 pun2-leng5 ti7 choan5 se3-kai3 hoan7-na7 u7 seng5-sit8 e5 lang5, tai7-ke chiah khoai3-khoai3 siong-thong kok lang5 e5 i3-chi3.
	Na2-tan3-giap8 u7 ian5-chhian5 tiap-a2(**tiap8-a2)-ku2, chiu7 mng7 kong2, “Tui3 ta2-loh8 bat goa2?”
	“Ah, goa2 long2 bat li2.  Hui-lek8 iau2-be7 kio3 li2, li2 ti7 bu5-hoa-ko2 chhiu7 kha, goa2 i2-keng khoaN3-kiN3 li2 lah.”
	Na2-tan3-giap8 thiaN hit ku3 oe7 liau2, oe7 hiah kam2-tong7 i e5 sim, si7 in-ui7 u7 tam7-poh8 li2-iu5 ti7-teh.  I m7-si7 kan-ta ui7-tioh8 chai-iaN2 Ia5-sou u7 hit ho7 chhiau chu7-jian5 e5 ti3-hui7, lai5 chai-iaN2 i u7 tiam3 ti7 bu5-hoa-ko2 chhiu7 kha teh thak8 Seng3-chheh, sou2-i2 chiah hiah hoaN-hi2 lai5 piau2-si7 hit e5 kek8 ki5-iN7, seng5-sit8, oan5-choan5 e5 sin3-hok8.  Put-ko3 lan2 thang lai5 siuN7 hit e5 in-toaN.  Phi3-ju7 lai5 kong2, lan2 na7 siam2-pi7 khi3 ti7 bu5-hoa-ko2 chhiu7-e7, am3-am3 bo5 lang5 khoaN3-kiN3 e5 sou2-chai7, u7 chhim-chhim keng-giam7 cheng-sin5-chiuN7 e5 choan2-ki, lai5 ka-ki7 chit8 lang5 kap Siong7-te3 saN-kap ti7-teh; iu7-koh lan2 tui3 khoaN3-tioh8 Ia5-sou e5 bin7-mau7, i2-kip8 thiaN-tioh8 I e5 oe7 lai5 chai-iaN2 I long2 chai lan2 tiam3 ti7 hit e5 pi3-bit8 e5 sou2-chai7 ti7 sim-lai7 sit8-chai7 sou2 teh siuN7, sou2 teh ng3-bang7 e5, sim7-chi3 soa3 toa7-toa7 tong5-cheng5 lan2, ti7 hit-si5 lan2 un2-tang3 beh chin chhiN-kiaN, oe7 piN5-piN5 kap Na2-tan3-giap8 siang7-khoan2, eng7 hit ho7 thang kiaN-hiaN5, u7 li2-kai2 e5 oe7 lai5 au5-kio3 kong2, “Liap8-pi2, li2 chiu7-si7 Siong7-te3 e5 KiaN2!  I2-sek-liat8 e5 Ong5!”
	Si7 lah!  Ia5-sou si7 Siong7-te3 e5 KiaN2!  Chong2-si7 chit tiap8 I si7 khah ai3 un2-bat8 I e5 Sin5-seng3, khah ai3 khoaN3 choe3 chhin-chhiuN7 in e5 chit8-e5, lai5 kap chiah e5 siau3-lian5 e5 peng5-iu2 saN-kap kau-poe5.  Sou2-i2 I u7 eng7 I it-seng sou2 te7-it ai3 e5, hit-ku3“Jin5-chu2”e5 chheng-hou, i3-su3 si7 phou2-thong lang5 e5 kiaN2, lai5 in3-tap i, kong2, “Goa2 sit8-sit8 ka7 lin2 kong2, Lin2 beh khoaN3-kiN3 thiN khui, Siong7-te3 e5 thiN-sai3 chiuN7-loh8 ti7 Jin5-chu2 e5 teng2-bin7.”  Chit e5 in3-tap tu2-tu2 si7 sim2-mih8 i3-su3, lan2 si7 bo5 thang khoai3-khoai3 liau2-kai2.  Put-ko3 lan2 chai keng3-khian5 e5 Iu5-thai3 lang5, si7 koaiN3-si3 ti7 tak8 jit8 hian-khui Ku7-iok e5 Seng3-chheh, lai5 bek8-siong2 hit tiong-kan kui2 cham7 e5 to7-li2.  Sou2-i2 lan2 thang phah-sng3, Na2-tan3-giap8 ti7 hit cha2-khi2, tiam3 bu5-hoa-ko2 chhiu7-e7, si7 tu2-tu2 teh sam3-su Nga2-kok e5 iN7-siong7, i2-kip8 ti7 hit e5 lau5-thui teh chiuN7-loh8 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 thiN-sai3 e5 su7.  Kiam2-chhai2 Ia5-sou e5 oe7, si7 tui3-tui3 ti7 i sou2 thak8 e5, tui3 an2-ni hou7 Na2-tan3-giap8 it-hoat chhim-sin3, chai-iaN2 khia7 ti7 i e5 bin7-cheng5 chit e5 Ia5-sou, si7 oe7 bat i e5 sim-lai7 tak8 hang7 e5 sim-su.

Lan2 ai3 siuN7-tioh8 chit e5 lau7 hak8-seng u7 chaiN2-iuN7 eng7 keng3-ui3 e5 liam7-thau5 lai5 ki3-tit cha2 siau3-lian5 si5-tai7 e5 su7.  Lan2 ai3 siuN7-tioh8 Siong7-te3 u7 chaiN2-iuN7 chhu2 lang5 e5 iuN7-siuN3, lai5 ka3-si7 chiah e5 siau3-lian5 lang5 li2-kai2 chong-kau3.  I e5 hoat-tou7 si7 bo5 eng7 li2-khi3 lai5 lun7-cheng3 Siong7-te3, ma7 bo5 kong2-khi2 choe7-jin5 e5 un7-mia7 siaN2 khoan2, lai5 phah chhiN-kiaN in e5 sim, chi2-u7 si7 eng7 thiaN3-thang3 kap in choe3 peng5-iu2, lai5 hou7 in bat I.  Choan5 Hok-im e5 lek8-su2 u7 am3-si7 lan2 chai, Ia5-sou u7 chin ki5-iN7 e5 khip-in2-lat8 ti7-teh.  Lang5 na7 u7 seng5-sit8, chiu7 thang tui3 ti-kak e5 pun2-leng5 lai5 hoan-geng5 I.  lai5 thiaN3-thang3 I.  Cheng3 hak8-seng be7 bian2-tit u7 hit ho7 e5 keng-giam7.

	Cha2 si7 an2-ni, chiu7 hian7-kim ma7-si7.  Chiah e5 siau3-lian5 e5 hak8-seng, si7 choe3 tak8 si5-tai7 bu5-sou3-ban7 e5 lang5 e5 tai7-piau2, piau2-beng5 lan2 long2 si7 tui3 ti7 lan2 sou2 u7 hit e5 ti-kak e5 pun2-leng5, i2-kip8 I e5 jin5-keh e5 khip-in2-lat8 lai5 kun7-oa2 I.  Sit8-chai7 Ia5-sou put-si5 to u7 thang tit-tioh8 hit ho7 khiam-sun3, seng5-sit8 e5 lang5 lai5 kun7-oa2 I, bo5 m7-si7 in-ui7 an2-ni.  Lan2 khiok si7 boe7 thang chhin-chhiuN7 in e5 khoan2, lai5 tiam3 ti7 I e5 sin-piN, iau2-ku2 kiam2-chhai2 lan2 na7 eng7 ki5-to2 lai5 kang2-kiu3 lan2 chit pun2 e5 Ki-tok-toan7, sim-lai7 chin-chiaN3 ai3 beh bat I, hit si5 lan2 e5 sim-sin5 iu5-goan5 oe7 chhin-chhiuN7 chiah e5 siau3-lian5 lang5 chit8 poaN, un2-tang3 oe7 hou7 I giu2--khi3, soa3 lai5 sin3-kho3 I, iah8 chhiat-chhiat ng3-bang7 oe7 thang sio2-khoa2 lai5 oh8 I e5 khoan2-sit.
	Chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni, siat-su2 lan2 ti7 sim-lai7 na7-si7 i2-keng bat I, lan2 ti7-chia tioh8 koh chai-iaN2, iau2 u7 chit8-hang7 iau3-kin2 e5 kau3-hun3 hian2-chhut ti7 chit e5 kou3-su7 e5 piau2-bin7.  Cha2-si5 chiah e5 hak8-seng teh khui-khoah I e5 chong-kau3 e5 hoat-tou7, chi2-u7 si7 chio peng5-iu2 lai5 bat Ia5-sou ji5-i2.  Siat-su2 lan2 tak8-lang5 na7 oe7 chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni lai5 choe3, Siong7-te3 Kok e5 sit8-hian7, si7 liam5-piN e5 su7.  Goa2 ti7 teng2-jit8, chhau3-tu2-kham2 u7 thak8-tioh8 chit8 e5 khah-cha2 e5 lang5 sou2 tu3 e5 chheh, ti7 i e5 chheh-nih8 u7 ki3-chai3 chit8 hang7 khah ki5-koai3, thang chhiN-kiaN e5 ki3-su7 kong2, “Siat-su2 tui3 kin-ni5 khi2, kan-ta u7 100 e5 chin-sit8 e5 Ki-tok-tou5, koat-sim ti7 tak8-ni5 ku2 beh kok-kok in2-chhoa7 chit8 e5 peng5-iu2 lai5 bat i e5 Chu2, chiu7 choan5 se3-kai3 ti7 25 ni5 ku2 si7 long2 beh hang5-hok8 ti7 Chu2 e5 kha-e7.”  Goa2 khi2-thau5 thak8 liau2 bo5 sim2-mih8 beh sin3, chong2-si7 goa2 giah8 pit chit8-e7 sng3-khoaN3, to sit8-chai7 u7 iaN2.  Kin-ni5 100, me5-ni5 200, au7-ni5 400, 800, 1600, chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni, tak8 ni5 tit-tioh8 ka-pe7.  Kau3 25 ni5 au7 si7 thang tit-tioh8 16 ek lang5, chhiau-ke3 choan5 se3-kai3 e5 jin5-khau2.  Peng5-iu2 in2-chhoa7 peng5-iu2, tang5-phoaN7 in2-chhoa7 tang5-phoaN7, lau7-bu2 in2-chhoa7 soe3-kiaN2.  Ah!  Hu7-jin5-lang5 ah, Siong7-te3 u7 chiok-hok lin2, sit8-chai7 chha-put-to si7 chi2-u7 lin2 u7 teh choe3 chit e5 kang na7-tiaN7.  sit8-chai7 chha-put-to tak8 e5 choe3 lau7-bu2 e5 lang5 long2 him-bou7 i e5 soe3-kiaN2 lai5 bat Ia5-sou.  Kin-a2-jit8 Siong7-te3 e5 Seng3-kok, si7 tui3 hu7-jin5-lang5 e5 khui3-lat8, u7 chin3-pou7 kau3 chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni.


Te7-4 chiuN	Ka-Na2 e5 Hun-In

	Ke3 saN-jit8 au7, chiu7-si7 ke3-lai5 e5 pai3-saN, Ia5-sou u7 khi3 chit8 e5 hiuN-sia7 hu3 hun-in e5 ian5-siah8.  Chit e5 hun-in si7 u7 hian2-chhut tiong7-iau3 e5 hau7-ko2, put-chi2 u7 eng2-hiong2 ti7 I e5 it-seng e5 su7-giap8.  Iok-han7 ti7 hit jit8 u7 kap Ia5-sou choe3-tin7 khi3, u7 kong2, “e7-saN jit8 ti7 Ka-li7-li7 e5 Ka-na2, u7 hun-in e5 ian5-siah8; Ia5-sou e5 lau7-bu2 ti7-hia; Ia5-sou kap I e5 hak8-seng ia7 hou7 in chhiaN2 khi3 hu3 ian5-siah8.”
	Lan2 hian-khui Seng3-chheh khoaN3-liau2 chai-iaN2 Ia5-sou e5 lau7-bu2 si7 chu2-iau3 e5 tong-su7-chia2, koh chai3 khoaN3 I e5 lau7-bu2 u7 teh khoa3-lu7 in e5 siat-pi7, lai5 hoan-hu3 chhe-eng7 e5 lang5, sou2-i2 tui3 chiah e5 su7-sit8 hou7 lan2 thang chhui -li2, chit e5 hun-in beng5-beng5 si7 I e5 chhin-chok8 lai7 e5 hun-in.  Na7 m7-si7 sin-niu5, chiu7-si7 sin-kiaN2-sai3 si7 Ia5-sou e5 kun7-chhin.  Lan2 thang siong2-siong7, hit jit8 chit e5 sin-niu5 un2-tang3 u7 ti3 sui2 koh phek-peh8 e5 phe3, ia7 chhah chhiN-chhui3 e5 chhiu7-ki, sim-lai7 put-chi2 hoaN-hi2, put-chi2 tek-i3, in-ui7 Ia5-sou u7 lai5 hu3 i e5 hun-in.  Toa7-bin7 tui3 soe3-han3 e5 si5, i chiu7 bat Ia5-sou, in-ui7 in e5 chhu3 saN-li7 chi2-u7 si3-eng-li2 e5 lou7-cham7.  Kiam2-chhai2 i choe3 gin2-na2 e5 si5, bat kap choe7-choe7 gin2-na2 phoaN7 choe3-he2 lai5 Ia5-sou e5 kang-tiuN5, thiaN Ia5-sou kong2 kou3-su7 ia7 ku2 kaN2, sou2 i2 chit e5 hap8-hun-sek si7 i e5 hoaN-hi2 e5 jit8, i chin him-bou7 i e5 chhin-lang5 Ia5-sou chhut-sek8, in-ui7 i put-chi2 chun-keng3 I, thiaN3-thang3 I, khoaN3 I choe3 chit8 e5 toa7-hiaN, iu7-koh in-ui7 Ia5-sou chit-tiap8 i2-keng chiaN5-choe3 tui3 Siong7-te3 sou2 chhe-lai5 e5, chit e5 chhut-mia5 e5 sian-siN, tui3 an2-ni i it-hoat him-bou7 Ia5-sou lai5 chhut-sek8, thang eng5-kng i e5 hap8-hun-sek, thang lai5 khoaN3-kiN3 i e5 heng7-hok, ia7 ng3-bang7 thang tit-tioh8 I e5 chiok-hok.
	Ia5-sou ko2-jian5 u7 chhut-sek8 i e5 hap8-hun-sek.  I ti7 sim-lai7 put-si5 u7 chun5 ui2-tai7 e5 su-siuN2, ke3-ek8 kap chek-jim7, chai-iaN2 I si7 beh lai5 tam-tng jin5-lui7 e5 un7-mia7, sou2-i2 chiah hoaN-hi2 lai5 seng5-siu7 in e5 chiau-thai7。Tui3 an2-ni, Ia5-sou put-chi2 hoaN-hi2 lai5 hu3 in-e5 hun-in.
	U7 choe7-choe7 lang5 teh siuN7 kong2, Ia5-sou si7 choe3 chit8 e5 kek8 giam5-siok, hu7 gi7-bu7 lang5, khi3 hu3 hit e5 hun-in, oan2-jian5 chhin-chhiuN7 chit8 e5 u7 ui-giam5 e5 bok8-su beh khi3 hu3 lang5 e5 hun-in, thang soa3 eng7 keng3-khian5 e5 oe7 lai5 khou2-khng3 lang5-kheh.  Toan3-toan3 m7-si7!  Tui3 hit khoan2 e5 thai3-tou7, Ia5-sou si7 kek8 put chu7-jian5, kek8 m7-ai3, si7 boe7 oe7 tong5-cheng5.  I chhut-sek8 hit e5 hun-in, si7 in-ui7 I u7 hoaN-hi2 hun-in.  Ti7 se3-kan bo5 chit8-lang5 bat chhin-chhiuN7 Ia5-sou e5 khoan2, u7 hiah-nih8 khoai3-lok8 jin5-seng.  I sit8-chai7 si7 chin thiaN3-thang3 jin5-seng, I si7 u7 hiong2-siu7 tak8 ho7 e5 khoai3-lok8.  I si7 u7 liah8 chu7-jian5 choe3 khoai3-lok8.  I si7 u7 khoaN3 soe3-han3 gin2-na2 choe3 khoai3-lok8.  I si7 u7 hoaN-hi2 kap lang5 choe3 peng5-iu2 saN kau-poe5, chai-iaN2 che si7 bo5 boe7 eng7-tit e5 su7.  I si7 put-chi2 hoaN-hi2 ai3 kap sia7-hoe7 e5 lang5 saN-kap choe3-he2 kau-poe5, lai5 hoaN-hi2 ke3-jit8; tek8-piat8 tui3 hiah e5 kho2-lin5 e5, koh khah si7 an2-ni, ti3-kau3 Hoat-li7-sai3 lang5 soa3 chheng I choe3 tham-chiah8 houN3-chiu2 e5, thiu-hiong3 e5, i2-kip8 choe7-jin5 e5 peng5-iu2.  U7 iaN2 chit e5 oe7 si7 oan3-hun7 hui2-pong3 e5 oe7, chong2-si7 u7 chit8-tiam2 lan2 thang chu3-i3, chiu7-si7, siat-su2 na7 m7-si7 I sit8-chai7 si7 u7 chin hoaN-hi2, lai5 kap sia7-hoe7 e5 lang5 saN-kap kau-poe5, soa3 eng7 hoaN-hi2 e5 sim lai5 hiong2-siu7 I e5 saN-tng3, chiu7 koat-toan3 bo5 u7 chit ho7 hui2-pong3 e5 oe7 chiah tioh8.

	Sit8-chai7 Ia5-sou na7-si7 kau3 hia, khoai3-lok8 chiu7 te3 kau3 hia, in-ui7 I pun2-sin si7 put-chi2 khoai3-lok8 e5 lang5.  I ti7 hun-in e5 ian5-toh si7 chin hoaN-hi2, lai5 kong2 lai5 chhio3.  I sim-lai7 si7 put-chi2 him-bou7 ai3 kap cheng3-lang5 choe3-he2.  I si7 siong5-siong5 ai3 po-chiong2 hiah e5 sit-chi3 e5 lang5.  I kong2, An li2 e5 sim, si7 goa2; m7-bian2 kiaN!  ChaiN2-iuN7? chu7-jian5 in-ui7 I pun2-sin si7 khoai3-lok8 e5 lang5.  Kin-a2-jit8 ti7 se3-kan te7-it khoai3-lok8 e5, chiu7-si7 hiah e5 oe7 eng7 ho2 lai5 li7-ek pat8-lang5 e5, sim-lai7 siong5-siong5 khoai3-lok8 lai5 giong2-bong7 Siong7-te3, lai5 oan5-choan5 sin3-kho3 Siong7-te3 e5 lang5, chiu7-si7 hiah e5 ti7 sim-lai7 u7 khng3 bu5 han7-liong7 e5 lok8-koan e5 lang5, lai5 khak-sit8 chai in u7 choe3-au7 e5 seng3-li7, ia7 chai, si2 chiu7-si7 teng5-chai3 chhut-si3 ti7 hit e5 khah hong-seng7 e5 se3-kai3, iu7-koh chai-iaN2 choe7-ok ti7 u7 chit8-jit8 beh eng2-oan2 biat8-bo5.  Siat-su2 lan2 na7-si7 u7 oh8 Ia5-sou e5 khoan2, lan2 tak8-lang5 tiaN7-tioh8 si7 oe7 chiaN5-choe3 heng7-hok khoai3-lok8 e5 lang5.
	Put-tan3 si7 an2-ni, I it-seng sou2 hoaN-hi2 e5, chiu7-si7 ai3 pang-chan7 hiah e5 bo5 sin5-seng3 e5 lang5, chiaN5-choe3 sin5-seng3; sim bo5 peng5-an e5, chiaN5-choe3 u7 peng5-an.  Iu7-koh I u7 kam2-kak, ti7 teng2-bin7 hit e5 bu5-han7 e5 heng7-hok e5 sim5-seng3 e5 se3-kai3, si7 u7 jiat8-jiat8 eng7 tong5-cheng5 e5 sim teh khoaN3-kou3 I.  I ti7-teh hoaN-hi2 chit8 e5 choe7-jin5 hok8-to3 si3-chiaN3 e5 seng-oah8 e5 si5, I si7 iu5-goan5 u7 thiaN-tioh8 Siong7-te3 e5 cheng3 thiN-sai3 ti7-teh hoaN-hi2 khoai3-lok8 e5 siaN.
	Goa2 teh ki5-koai3, m7-chai lan2 it-poaN tui3 ta2-loh8 lai5 siuN7 kong2, Ia5-sou si7 iu-chhiu5 e5 bin7-mau7 e5 lang5.  Chhin-chhiuN7 chit ho7 e5 khoaN3-hoat, tek-khak m7-si7 chhut tui3 Hok-im-su e5 kou3-su7.  Lan2 thang liau7 chit ho7 e5 khoaN3-hoat, si7 chhut tui3 I2-sai3-a e5 u7-gian5, in-ui7 ti7-hia u7 teh kong2-khi2 “I siong5-siong5 tu2-tioh8 kan-khou2; sim-lai7 toa7 hoan5-lo2.”  U7 choe7-choe7 ui2-tai7 e5 bi2-sut8-ka, put-si5 to teh oe7 hit khoan2 iu-chhiu5 e5 bin7-mau7 e5 Ia5-sou; tui3 an2-ni, lan2 ai3 than3 hit e5 khoan2, lai5 thak8 Ia5-sou it-seng e5 kou3-su7; ki5-sit8 che si7 ke3-thau5 e5 sou2-chai7 ti7-teh.  U7 iaN2!  I u7 tam-tng lan2 e5 kan-khou2, taN lan2 e5 piN7-thiaN3.  Lan2 ai3 eng7 thiaN3-thang3, kam2-sia7 e5 sim, lai5 seng5-jin7 chit-tiam2.  Chong2-si7 thoe3 pat8-lang5 lai5 kan-khou2, lai5 si2, to m7-si7 kong2, tui3 an2-ni chiu7 oe7 hoe3-bo5 hit e5 ui2-tai7 e5 sim-sin5 sou2 u7 e5 hoaN-hi2 kap khoai3-lok8.  M7-si7 chai7 hit-khoan2 jiat8-sim kam-goan7 pang3-sak ka-ki7 e5 lang5 teh khoaN3, hi-seng e5 heng5-ui5 chiu7-si7 chit8 hang7 e5 khoai3-lok8.  Chhi3-mng7, ti7 chian3-tiuN5 pun2-sin kap si2 choe3 peng5-iu2 e5 peng, oe7-hiau2 tong5-cheng5 hiah e5 tioh8-siong e5, lai5 kng i tng2-lai5 khan3-hou7, hit-si5 i e5 sim-sin5 kiam2 u7 iu-chhiu5?  Sou2-i2 goa2 teh siuN7, Ia5-sou oe7 thang thoe3 pat8 lang5 lai5 si2, sit8-chai7 si7 hou7 Ia5-sou e5 lai7-bin7 seng-oah8 ke-thiN chit8 hoan e5 hoaN-hi2 khoai3-lok8 chiah tioh8.
