In-ui7 i u7 ki3-chai3 tui3 hit jit8 khi2, lian5-lian5 si3-jit8 ku2 sou2 tu2-tioh8 e5 su7, iah8 soa3 kong2-khi2 chiah e5 jit8 liau2-au7, koh ke3 saN-jit8 ti7 Ka-li7-li7 e5 Ka-na2 u7 hun-in e5 ian5-siah8.  Hit-tiap8 Iu5-thai3 lang5 e5 hong-siok8, si7 tiaN7-tioh8 ti7 pai3-saN choe3 hun-in.  Sou2-i2 lan2 thang tui3 pai3-saN sng3 to3-tng2, kau3 chin3-cheng5 le2-pai3 e5 pai3 si3, lai5 siuN7 hit tiong-kan sou2 tu2-tioh8 e5 su7-sit8.

	ChhiaN2 chu3-i3 lai5 khoaN3 i sou2 pai5-liat8 e5 cheng5-keng2.  thau5 chit8-jit8 si7 pai3-si3.  Iok-han7 si7 kap i e5 sian-siN KiaN5 soe2-le2 e5 Iok-han7 saN-kap ti7 Pek-tai7-ni5.  I u7 kap chit8 kun5 e5 siau3-lian5 e5 tang5-phoaN7, chiu7-si7 u7 khng3 him-bou7 khah ko-siong7 e5 sim e5, tai7-ke kap kui toa7-tin7 e5 cheng3-lang5 tui3 Ka-li7-li7 loh8-lai5 thiaN chit e5 sin e5 sian-ti Iok-han7 e5 ka3-si7.  In chek-si5 te3 i lai5 choe3 i e5 hak8-seng, soa3 chu7 an2-ni tiam3 ti7 i e5 sin-piN, kau3 tho2-hai2 e5 si5-ki5 chiah koh to3-khi3 Ka-li7-li7.
	KiaN5 soe2-le2 e5 Iok-han7 e5 thoan5-to7, u7 put-chi2 io5-choah Pa-lek8-su-theng3 e5 choan5-toe7, ti3-kau3 hou7 khia7-khi2 ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 Hoat-li7-sai3 lang5 khoaN3-choe3 iau3-kin2, u7 chhe tai7-piau2 lai5 tham3-mng7 i.  Ti7 hit e5 pai3-si3, toa7-bin7 si7 Ia5-sou tui3 khong3-ia2 to3-tng2--lai5 e5 chin3-cheng5 jit8, hiah e5 su3-chia2 u7 chiau5-kau3.  Chit e5 toa7 e5 Soan-kau3-su choan5-jian5 eng7 seng5-sit8, bo5 un2-moa5 e5 thai3-tou7 lai5 chih-chiap in.  Khiok I ma7-si7 long2 bo5 sim2-mih8 su7 thang un2-bat8.
	“ChhiaN2 ka7 goan2 kong2, Li2 si7 chi7-chui7?”
	“Goa2 m7-si7 Ki-tok.”
	“Che si7 chaiN2-iuN7?  Li2 si7 I2-li7-a mah?”
	“M7-si7.”
	“Li2 su7 hit e5 sian-ti mah?”
	“M7-si7.”
	“Na7-si7 an2-ni, Li2 si7 chi7-chui7? hou7 goan2 thang he5-hok chhe goan2 e5.  Li2 tioh8 kong2 ka-ki7 si7 chi7-chui7?”
	“Goa2 chiu7-si7 teh kio3 ti7 khong3-ia2 e5, i e5 siaN, kong2, Siu tit8 Chu2 e5 lou7, chhin-chhiuN7 sian-ti I2-sai3-a sou2 kong2 e5.”
	“Li2 na7 m7-si7 Ki-tok, iah8 m7-si7 I2-li7-a, iah8 m7-si7 hit e5 sian-ti, chaiN2-iuN7 kiaN5 soe2-le2 ah?”
	“Goa2 eng7 chui2 kiaN5 soe2-le2; u7 khia7 ti7 lin2 tiong-kan e5, lin2 m7-bat I.”

	“Keh jit8,” KiaN5 soe2-le2 e5 Iok-han7 u7 kap kui2 mia5 e5 ti-ki2, saN-kap teh khia7 e5 si5, hut-jian5 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 Ia5-sou, tui3 lak8 le2-pai3 cheng5 I sou2 un2-bat8 hit e5 soaN-io e5 lou7 chhut--lai5, ng3 in tai7-ke chin3-cheng5 teh kiaN5.  I e5 kiaN5-tah8 si7 chin-chiaN3 ia3-sian7 e5 khoan2, hit si3-chap8 jit8 ku2 thang chhiN-kiaN e5 kin2-tiuN e5 cheng-sin5, iau2 u7 hian2-chhut ti7 I e5 bin7-mau7; ti7 I e5 bak8-chiu iau2 u7 hian2-chhut pat8 se3-kai3 e5 kong-chhai2 ti7-teh.  KiaN5 soe2-le2 e5 Iok-han7 khak-sit8 ti7 i2-cheng5 u7 teh ki5-koai3, tau3-ti2 Ia5-sou si7 un2-bat8 khi3 ti7 ta2-loh8.  Chit-tiap8 i chek-si5 jin7-tit I, chiu7 eng7 jiat8-jiat8 kiong-keng3 e5 thai3-tou7 lai5 po3 i e5 tang5-phoaN7, kong2, “Li2 khoaN3, Siong7-te3 e5 IuN5-ko, chiu7-si7 tam-tng se3-kan e5 choe7 e5.  Chit e5 chiu7-si7 goa2 sou2 bat kong2 e5.  Goa2 bat khoaN3-kiN3 Seng3 Sin5 chhin-chhiuN7 chiN2-a2 tui3 thiN kang3-loh8 hioh ti7 I e5 teng2-bin7.  Goa2 bat khoaN3-kiN3, soa3 lai5 kan-cheng3 chit e5 si7 Siong7-te3 e5 KiaN2.”
	Chit e5 I2-hut-sou2 e5 lau7 kam-tok, koh chit8 pai2 kam2-kak--tioh8 siau3-lian5 e5 khi3-khai3, in-ui7 i u7 koh siuN7-tioh8 cha2-si5 chhou-chhou khoaN3-kiN3 Ia5-sou hit-si5 i e5 sim siu7 kam2-tong7 kau3 chaiN2-iuN7.  In-ui7 i chai i sou2 khoaN3-kiN3 e5, si7 ti7 ku2-ku2 e5 tiong-kan I2-sek-liat8 lang5 sou2 teh him-bou7 theng3-hau7 e5, si7 beh tam-tng se3-kan e5 choe7, taN lan2 e5 tang7-taN3 e5.

	Iok-han7 koh chin3-cheng5 lai5 hoe5-siong2 hit si5 e5 ki3-ek, chiu7-si7 kong2, koh keh-jit8, chiu7-si7 in e5 an-hioh-jit8, ti7 hit e7-pou Iok-han7 u7 kap i e5 tang5-phoaN7 An-tek-liat8 teh tam5-lun7 in e5 sian-siN e5 su7, un2-tang3 ia7 si7 teh tam5-lun7 Ia5-sou e5 su7, hit si5 Ia5-sou u7 tu2-tu2 beh kiaN5 ke3 khoe-kiN5 e5 lou7.  Lan2 thang siong2-siong7 KiaN5 soe2-le2 e5 Iok-han7, sim-lai7 un2-tang3 u7 siu7 kam2-tong7, chiah lai5 khan i e5 siau3-lian5 e5 tang5-phoaN7 e5 chhiu2, pi2 kong2, “Li2 khoaN3!  Siong7-te3 e5 IuN5-ko!”  Siong7-te3 e5 IuN5-ko!  In iau2-be7 khoaN3-kiN3 Siong7-te3 e5 IuN5-ko siu7 teng3 ti7 Kok-kok-thaN e5 i2-cheng5, chu7-jian5 si7 boe7 thang liau2-kai2 hit e5 long2-chong2 e5 i3-gi7.  Chong2-si7 in e5 sim u7 chhut tui3 tut8-jian5 e5 chhiong-tong7, ho2-taN2 lai5 te3 I, chiu7-si7 “u7 nng7 e5 hak8-seng thiaN i sou2 kong2, chiu7 te3 Ia5-sou.”  Toa7-bin7 si7 in-ui7 KiaN5 soe2-le2 e5 Iok-han7 khiok iau2 si7 u7 ko3-jin5-tek e5 ai3-cheng5 ti7-teh, chong2-si7 hit e5 ai3-cheng5 si7 boe7 thang kim3-chi2 in te3 Ia5-sou.  Iok-han7 chi2-u7 si7 choe3 i e5 Chu2 e5 sian-hong na7-tiaN7.
	Hit nng7 e5 siau3-lian5 e5 tho2-hai2 lang5, beh chhut-hoat loh8-khi3 khoe-kiN5, hit si5 lan2 thang siong2-siong7, in un2-tang3 si7 chin ui3 siau2-le2, kiaN-kiaN, chin m7 koaiN3-si3 e5 khoan2, chit8 sim hoaN-hi2 ai3 kap Ia5-sou kong2-oe7, ia7 chit8 sim kiaN-hiaN5 m7-kaN2.  Ia5-sou chit8-e7 thiaN-kiN3 in e5 kha-pou7 siaN, chiu7 oat8-thau5 khoaN3-kiN3 in teh te3 I, chhin-chhiuN7 ti7 tak8 si5-tai7, I u7 oat8-thau5 lai5 khoaN3 hiah e5 him-bou7 ai3 te3 I, iau2-ku2 bo5 tam2-liong7 e5 hak8-seng chit8 poaN.  I eng7 chhin-chhiat, bian2-le7 e5 oe7 lai5 mng7 in kong2, “Lin2 teh chhe7 sim2-mih8?”  Ia5-sou kong2 chit ku3, kiam2-chhai2 I e5 i3-su3 si7 teh chhi3 in, ai3 hoan3-khi2 in e5 sim, lai5 ka-ki7 sim2-mng7 in sou2 teh chhe7 e5.  Ia5-sou si7 ai3 in chai-iaN2.  Ia5-sou si7 bo5 iau3-kin2 lang5 e5 gu5-gong7, loan2-jiok8, lou2-tun7, i2-kip8 ki5-thaN, put-ko3 kan-ta ai3 lang5 ti7 sim-lai7 oe7 hiau2 kam2-kak, kong2, “Goa2 si7 teh chhe7 Siong7-te3.  goa2 si7 ai3 hok8-sai7 Li2.”
	Chit nng7 e5 siau3-lian5 e5 hiong-chhoan lang5 thiaN-liau2 si7 chin chhiN-kiaN, chin hun7-loan7, ti3-kau3 boe7 hiau2-tit tioh8 chaiN2-iuN7 in3, soa3 mng7 kong2, “Liap8-pi2, Li2 si7 tiam3 ti7 ta2-loh8?”  Ah!  Ia5-sou chai-iaN2 in e5 khiam3-kheh.  I chiu7 ka7 in kong2, “Lin2 lai5 chiu7 oe7 khoaN3-kiN3.”  I chiu7 chhoa7 in kau3 I sou2 toa3 hit e5 m7-chiaN5-mih8, soe3-soe3 e5 chhu3-a2; hit jit8 in u7 kap Ia5-sou saN-kap toa3.  Iok-han7 e5 ki3-ek si7 put-chi2 beng5; hoe5-kou3 poaN3-se3-ki2 cheng5 e5 su7 kau3 chin siong5-se3 kong2, “hit-si5 iok-liok8 si3-tiam2 cheng.”  ChaiN2-iuN7 i oe7-thang hut-liok8 hit-si5 e5 cheng5-keng2?  In ti7 hit-jit8 e5 am3 thau5-a2, kan-ta kap Ia5-sou saN-kap tiam3 ti7-hia, soa3 siu7-tioh8 I e5 kan2-tan e5 khoan2-thai7, ia7 soa3 chu7-iu5 lai5 kap I tam5-lun7, mng7 I tang, mng7 I sai, lai5 thiaN I e5 ka3-si7, ia7 hit-si5 I un2-tang3 u7 tui3 in kong2-khi2 koan-he7 I e5 sim tioh8 chaiN2-iuN7 ui7-tioh8 jin5-lui7 e5 choe7-ok lai5 kan-khou2, i2-kip8 tui3 ti7 Siong7-te3 kok I jiat8-jiat8 e5 ke3-ek8 kap hi-bong7 e5 su7, ti7 au7-lai5 in siuN7-tioh8 hit-si5 e5 cheng5-keng2, kiam2 m7-si7 kam2-khai3 bu5-liong7!  Ia5-sou u7 tong5-cheng5 in, ti3-kau3 u7 hoan3-khi2 in hoaN-hi2 lai5 ui3-ui3 kong2-khi2 in e5 chi3-khi3.  Lan2 khak-sin3 I thiaN-liau2 un2-tang3 u7 tui3 in kong2, toa7-bin7 I e5 khoan2 tu2-tu2 si7 ai3 kong2 an2-ni ia7-ku2-kaN2, “u7 chit8-jit8 goa2 ai3 lin2 nng7 lang5, khia7 ti7 goa2 e5 sin-piN lai5 pang-chan7 goa2.”  Chit-ho7 oe7 si7 gau5 chhui-pek lang5 e5 sim, oe7 in2-chhoa7 lang5, hoat-hui lang5 sou2 u7 e5 ho2 e5 pou7-hun7.
	Chhi3 siuN7 chit nng7 e5 siau3-lian5 lang5, ti7 hit e5 moa2-thiN-chhiN e5 am3-mi5, li7-khui I to3-tng2 khi3 in tau, hit-si5 in e5 sim-koaN un2-tang3 chin ki5-koai3 koh chin jiat8, un2-tang3 sim-sim liam7-liam7 to si7 teh su-siong2 hit e5 sin e5 peng5-iu2.  “Lan2 un2-tang3 te3 I, ia7 koh beh te3 I kau3 si2.”  Hit e5-hng in khoaN3 choan5 se3-kai3 si7 long2 pian3-oaN7 liau2-liau2, it-chhe3 bo5 m7 oaN7 choe3 sin.

	Iok-han7 kong2, hit am3 khi3 chhe7 Ia5-sou e5, “Ki5-tiong chit8 e5 si7 Se-bun5, Pi2-tek e5 hiaN-ti7 An-tek-liat8.”  Iau2 hit e5 si7 i pun2-sin, i si7 khiam-pi m7-kaN2 kong2.  An-tek-liat8 ti7 hit am3 kap Ia5-sou kau-poe5 liau2, sim-lai7 kam2-kak bu5-siong7 e5 hoaN-hi2 khoai3-lok8, chiu7 chek-si5 khi3 chhe7 i e5 hiaN-ti7.  “Se-bun5! Goan2 i2-keng tu2-tioh8 Bi2-sai3-a (hoan-ek8 chiu7-si7 Ki-tok) lah ne7!”  Goan2 m7-si7 kan-ta tui3 Kia5 soe2-le2 e5 Iok-han7 thiaN-kiN3 na7-tiaN7.  goan2 pun2-sin si7 i2-keng u7 tu2-tioh8 I.  Chit ho7 e5 khak-sin3 si7 tui3 ti7 hit am3 in u7 kap Ia5-sou choe3-he2 sou2 tit-tioh8 e5.  Lang5 tui3 pun2-sin e5 sim-toe2 e5 keng-giam7, oe7 thang khak-sin3 lai5 kong2, goan2 i2-keng u7 tu2-tioh8 Ki-tok, hit-ho7 lang5 chin-chai3 u7 hok-khi3!  Chong2-si7 na5 oe7-thang koh in2-chhoa7 pat8 lang5 lai5 chiu7-kun7 I, hit ho7 e5 lang5 si7 koh-khah u7 hok-khi3!
	Chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni, “Antek-liat8 chiu7 chhoa7 Se-bun5 chiu7-kun7 Ia5-sou.”  Che chiu7-si7 hit e5 so3-seng3, chhiong-tong7-tek, to-cheng5 khoai3 tioh8-tak e5 Pi2-tek, jip8 I e5 kun5 e5 khoan2-sit.  Pi2-tek tu2-tu2 lai5 e5 si5, Ia5-sou khoaN3-kiN3 i, chiu7 sui(**sui5)-si5 ka7 i ho7 sin e5 mia5.  Kiam2-chhai2 si7 in-ui7 Pi2-tek u7 ka-ki7 kian3-siau3, tam7-poh8 sit-chi3 chai-iaN2 i e5 seng3 khoai3 tin2-tang7, gau5 io5-choah.  Ia5-sou chit8-e7 khoaN3-kiN3 i, sui5-si5 liau2-kai2 i e5 sim-cheng5.  “Iok-han7 e5 kiaN2 Se-bun5 ah, goa2 long2 bat li2.  Li2 chit-tiap8 sui-jian5 si7 loan2-jiok8, iau2-ku2 u7 chit8-jit8 li2 beh chiaN5-choe3 iong2-chong3 e5 lang5.  U7 chit8-jit8, li2 beh chheng-choe3 Ki-hoat, chiu7-si7 chioh8-poaN5.”  Che si7 piau2-beng5 Chu2 e5 gau5 chong3 lang5 e5 taN2, eng7 thiaN3-thang3 e5 tong7-chhat-lat8, gau5 khoaN3 kau3 lang5 e5 chiong-lai5.
	Iok-han7 chit-tiap8 iau2 si7 oe7 ki3-tit hiang3 tang5(**tang)-si5-a2 e5 cheng5-keng2.  Pi2-tek khiok-si7 chu7 cha2-cha2 chiu7 i2-keng ke3-sin, khi3 tiam3 hit e5 leng5-kai3 kap i e5 Chu2 saN-kap khia7-khi2, ia7 chit e5 lau7 hak8-seng hit-tiap8 iau2-ku2 oe7 ki3-tit Ia5-sou chhou-chhou teh khoaN3 Pi2-tek, hit-si5 I e5 bak8-chiu e5 khoan2-sit, si7 sio-siang7 ti7 saN-ni5-au7 e5 u7 chit8-jit8, koh chit8 pai2 lai5 “Oat8-thau5 khoaN3 Pi2-tek, iah8 Pi2-tek chiu7 chhut-khi3 goa7-bin7, toa7 thi5-khau3,” hit-si5 e5 khoan2.

	Keh-jit8, Ia5-sou beh-khi3 Ka-li7-li7, lou7-nih8 ai3 tui3 Ka-na2 keng-ke3.  Ti7 hit-tiau5 chhiong3-koan3 to7-lou7 e5 tiong-kan, chit cham7 si7 chin sui2, liong2-peng5 u7 chu7-jian5 e5 keng2-ti3.  Ia5-sou beh chhut-hoat khi3 Ka-li7-li7, lou7-nih8 I tioh8 hioh-khun3 ti7 Ka-na2 lai5 hu3-hun-in e5 ian5-siah8.  Hit-si5 u7 saN-e5 hak8-seng kap I choe3-tin7 khi3, in-ui7 in e5 chhu3 long2 si7 ti7 hit e5 keh-piah, ia7 koh iu5-goan5 siu7 pheng3-chhiaN2 tioh8 khi3 hu3 hit e5 hun-in.  Ti7 hit e5 lou7-tiong, Ia5-sou u7 tu2-tioh8 Hui-lek8.  Lan2 thang ho2-taN2 kong2, Ia5-sou si7 i2-keng bat i.  Hui-lek8 u7 chit8-ui7 put-chi2 chhin-bit8 e5 peng5-iu2, kio3-choe3 Na2-tan3-giap8, tiam3 ti7 Ka-na2.  Lan2 thang chhui-toan3 chit e5 Na2-tan3-giap8 si7 chit8 e5 keng3-khian5 e5 Iu5-thai3 lang5, i e5 seng3-cheng5 si7 ai3 thiam5-cheng7, ai3 bek8-siong2, ia7 ai3 siong5-siong5 kap Siong7-te3 kau-poe5.  I kap Hui-lek8 un2-tang3 khah siong5 choe3-he2 saN-kap tam5-lun7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 tui3 chiong-lai5 sou2 teh ng3-bang7 e5 su7.
	Hui-lek8 e5 sim boe7 tan2-tit thang koaN2-kin2 kau3 Ka-na2, lai5 chhe7-tioh8 i e5 peng5-iu2 Na2-tan3-giap8.
	“Na2-tan3-giap8 ah, Mou5-se ki3 ti7 lut8-hoat, kap chiah e5 sian-ti sou2 ki3 e5, goan2 i2-keng tu2-tioh8 I.”
	“I si7 chi7-chui?”
	“Chiu7-si7 Iok-sek e5 kiaN2, Na2-sat-lek8 lang5, Ia5-sou.”
	Chong2-si7 Na2-tan3-giap8 sim-lai7 khng3 giau5-gi5.  I bo5 teh liau5-bang7 Bi2-sai3-a, beh chiau3 chit khoan2 lang5 sou2 liau7 boe7-tioh8 e5 hoat-tou7 lai5 chhut-hian7.  Toa7-bin7 i si7 lau7 toa7-lang5, siuN ke3-thau5 soe3-ji7, bo5 khoai3-khoai3 lai5 thiaN chit e5 siau3-lian5 lang5 sou2 kong2 e5 oe7, lai5 hoah8 i e5 kha khi3 chhe7 Ia5-sou.  I eng7 tong-si5 hit ho7 teh biau2-si7 lang5 e5 siok8-gu2, lai5 in3 kong2, “Na2-sat-lek8 kiam2-oe7 chhut sim2-mih8 ho2-mih8 mah?”
	Hui-lek8 bo5 ai3 kap i saN pian7-lun7.  I chi2-u7 kong2, “Lai5 khoaN3!”  Si7 lai5 khoaN3!  Lan2 tui3 hiah e5 giau5-gi5 Ia5-sou e5 lang5 te7-it ho2 e5 in3-tap, chiu7-si7 chit khoan2 e5 oe7.  Hui-lek8 sim-lai7 teh siuN7, lang5 na7 lai5 kiN3-tioh8 Ia5-sou, bun7-toe5 chiu7 kai2-koat.  Lang5 na7 oa2-lai5 khoaN3 Ia5-sou chit8-e7, thiaN Ia5-sou kong2 chit8-ku3, hit e5 kong-hau7 si7 khah iaN5 it-chhe3 e5 pian7-lun7.  sou2-i2 Hui-lek8 u7 chhoa7 Na2-tan3-giap8 chhut-lai5 kiN3 pat8 e5 hak8-seng.  “Ia5-sou khoaN3-kiN3 Na2-tan3-giap8 chiu7-kun7 I” (koh chit8-pai2 chu3-i3 ti7 Iok-han7, chaiN2-iuN7 koh teh hoe5-siong2 Chu2 e5 bak8-chiu e5 khoan2-sit), chiu7 chi2 i kong2, “Li2 khoaN3, chin-chiaN3 si7 I2-sek-liat8 lang5, sim bo5 khui2-khiat e5.”
	Ia5-sou chit8-e7 khoaN3 i, chiu7 tit-tioh8 Na2-tan3-giap8, hou7 i e5 sim-sin5 chek-si5 kap I kiat-lian5.  In-ui7 ti7 lang5 e5 lai7-bin7 u7 hit ho7 ti-kak e5 pun2-leng5 ti7-teh, tui3 chit e5 pun2-leng5 ti7 choan5 se3-kai3 hoan7-na7 u7 seng5-sit8 e5 lang5, tai7-ke chiah khoai3-khoai3 siong-thong kok lang5 e5 i3-chi3.
	Na2-tan3-giap8 u7 ian5-chhian5 tiap-a2(**tiap8-a2)-ku2, chiu7 mng7 kong2, “Tui3 ta2-loh8 bat goa2?”
	“Ah, goa2 long2 bat li2.  Hui-lek8 iau2-be7 kio3 li2, li2 ti7 bu5-hoa-ko2 chhiu7 kha, goa2 i2-keng khoaN3-kiN3 li2 lah.”
	Na2-tan3-giap8 thiaN hit ku3 oe7 liau2, oe7 hiah kam2-tong7 i e5 sim, si7 in-ui7 u7 tam7-poh8 li2-iu5 ti7-teh.  I m7-si7 kan-ta ui7-tioh8 chai-iaN2 Ia5-sou u7 hit ho7 chhiau chu7-jian5 e5 ti3-hui7, lai5 chai-iaN2 i u7 tiam3 ti7 bu5-hoa-ko2 chhiu7 kha teh thak8 Seng3-chheh, sou2-i2 chiah hiah hoaN-hi2 lai5 piau2-si7 hit e5 kek8 ki5-iN7, seng5-sit8, oan5-choan5 e5 sin3-hok8.  Put-ko3 lan2 thang lai5 siuN7 hit e5 in-toaN.  Phi3-ju7 lai5 kong2, lan2 na7 siam2-pi7 khi3 ti7 bu5-hoa-ko2 chhiu7-e7, am3-am3 bo5 lang5 khoaN3-kiN3 e5 sou2-chai7, u7 chhim-chhim keng-giam7 cheng-sin5-chiuN7 e5 choan2-ki, lai5 ka-ki7 chit8 lang5 kap Siong7-te3 saN-kap ti7-teh; iu7-koh lan2 tui3 khoaN3-tioh8 Ia5-sou e5 bin7-mau7, i2-kip8 thiaN-tioh8 I e5 oe7 lai5 chai-iaN2 I long2 chai lan2 tiam3 ti7 hit e5 pi3-bit8 e5 sou2-chai7 ti7 sim-lai7 sit8-chai7 sou2 teh siuN7, sou2 teh ng3-bang7 e5, sim7-chi3 soa3 toa7-toa7 tong5-cheng5 lan2, ti7 hit-si5 lan2 un2-tang3 beh chin chhiN-kiaN, oe7 piN5-piN5 kap Na2-tan3-giap8 siang7-khoan2, eng7 hit ho7 thang kiaN-hiaN5, u7 li2-kai2 e5 oe7 lai5 au5-kio3 kong2, “Liap8-pi2, li2 chiu7-si7 Siong7-te3 e5 KiaN2!  I2-sek-liat8 e5 Ong5!”
	Si7 lah!  Ia5-sou si7 Siong7-te3 e5 KiaN2!  Chong2-si7 chit tiap8 I si7 khah ai3 un2-bat8 I e5 Sin5-seng3, khah ai3 khoaN3 choe3 chhin-chhiuN7 in e5 chit8-e5, lai5 kap chiah e5 siau3-lian5 e5 peng5-iu2 saN-kap kau-poe5.  Sou2-i2 I u7 eng7 I it-seng sou2 te7-it ai3 e5, hit-ku3“Jin5-chu2”e5 chheng-hou, i3-su3 si7 phou2-thong lang5 e5 kiaN2, lai5 in3-tap i, kong2, “Goa2 sit8-sit8 ka7 lin2 kong2, Lin2 beh khoaN3-kiN3 thiN khui, Siong7-te3 e5 thiN-sai3 chiuN7-loh8 ti7 Jin5-chu2 e5 teng2-bin7.”  Chit e5 in3-tap tu2-tu2 si7 sim2-mih8 i3-su3, lan2 si7 bo5 thang khoai3-khoai3 liau2-kai2.  Put-ko3 lan2 chai keng3-khian5 e5 Iu5-thai3 lang5, si7 koaiN3-si3 ti7 tak8 jit8 hian-khui Ku7-iok e5 Seng3-chheh, lai5 bek8-siong2 hit tiong-kan kui2 cham7 e5 to7-li2.  Sou2-i2 lan2 thang phah-sng3, Na2-tan3-giap8 ti7 hit cha2-khi2, tiam3 bu5-hoa-ko2 chhiu7-e7, si7 tu2-tu2 teh sam3-su Nga2-kok e5 iN7-siong7, i2-kip8 ti7 hit e5 lau5-thui teh chiuN7-loh8 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 thiN-sai3 e5 su7.  Kiam2-chhai2 Ia5-sou e5 oe7, si7 tui3-tui3 ti7 i sou2 thak8 e5, tui3 an2-ni hou7 Na2-tan3-giap8 it-hoat chhim-sin3, chai-iaN2 khia7 ti7 i e5 bin7-cheng5 chit e5 Ia5-sou, si7 oe7 bat i e5 sim-lai7 tak8 hang7 e5 sim-su.

Lan2 ai3 siuN7-tioh8 chit e5 lau7 hak8-seng u7 chaiN2-iuN7 eng7 keng3-ui3 e5 liam7-thau5 lai5 ki3-tit cha2 siau3-lian5 si5-tai7 e5 su7.  Lan2 ai3 siuN7-tioh8 Siong7-te3 u7 chaiN2-iuN7 chhu2 lang5 e5 iuN7-siuN3, lai5 ka3-si7 chiah e5 siau3-lian5 lang5 li2-kai2 chong-kau3.  I e5 hoat-tou7 si7 bo5 eng7 li2-khi3 lai5 lun7-cheng3 Siong7-te3, ma7 bo5 kong2-khi2 choe7-jin5 e5 un7-mia7 siaN2 khoan2, lai5 phah chhiN-kiaN in e5 sim, chi2-u7 si7 eng7 thiaN3-thang3 kap in choe3 peng5-iu2, lai5 hou7 in bat I.  Choan5 Hok-im e5 lek8-su2 u7 am3-si7 lan2 chai, Ia5-sou u7 chin ki5-iN7 e5 khip-in2-lat8 ti7-teh.  Lang5 na7 u7 seng5-sit8, chiu7 thang tui3 ti-kak e5 pun2-leng5 lai5 hoan-geng5 I.  lai5 thiaN3-thang3 I.  Cheng3 hak8-seng be7 bian2-tit u7 hit ho7 e5 keng-giam7.

	Cha2 si7 an2-ni, chiu7 hian7-kim ma7-si7.  Chiah e5 siau3-lian5 e5 hak8-seng, si7 choe3 tak8 si5-tai7 bu5-sou3-ban7 e5 lang5 e5 tai7-piau2, piau2-beng5 lan2 long2 si7 tui3 ti7 lan2 sou2 u7 hit e5 ti-kak e5 pun2-leng5, i2-kip8 I e5 jin5-keh e5 khip-in2-lat8 lai5 kun7-oa2 I.  Sit8-chai7 Ia5-sou put-si5 to u7 thang tit-tioh8 hit ho7 khiam-sun3, seng5-sit8 e5 lang5 lai5 kun7-oa2 I, bo5 m7-si7 in-ui7 an2-ni.  Lan2 khiok si7 boe7 thang chhin-chhiuN7 in e5 khoan2, lai5 tiam3 ti7 I e5 sin-piN, iau2-ku2 kiam2-chhai2 lan2 na7 eng7 ki5-to2 lai5 kang2-kiu3 lan2 chit pun2 e5 Ki-tok-toan7, sim-lai7 chin-chiaN3 ai3 beh bat I, hit si5 lan2 e5 sim-sin5 iu5-goan5 oe7 chhin-chhiuN7 chiah e5 siau3-lian5 lang5 chit8 poaN, un2-tang3 oe7 hou7 I giu2--khi3, soa3 lai5 sin3-kho3 I, iah8 chhiat-chhiat ng3-bang7 oe7 thang sio2-khoa2 lai5 oh8 I e5 khoan2-sit.
	Chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni, siat-su2 lan2 ti7 sim-lai7 na7-si7 i2-keng bat I, lan2 ti7-chia tioh8 koh chai-iaN2, iau2 u7 chit8-hang7 iau3-kin2 e5 kau3-hun3 hian2-chhut ti7 chit e5 kou3-su7 e5 piau2-bin7.  Cha2-si5 chiah e5 hak8-seng teh khui-khoah I e5 chong-kau3 e5 hoat-tou7, chi2-u7 si7 chio peng5-iu2 lai5 bat Ia5-sou ji5-i2.  Siat-su2 lan2 tak8-lang5 na7 oe7 chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni lai5 choe3, Siong7-te3 Kok e5 sit8-hian7, si7 liam5-piN e5 su7.  Goa2 ti7 teng2-jit8, chhau3-tu2-kham2 u7 thak8-tioh8 chit8 e5 khah-cha2 e5 lang5 sou2 tu3 e5 chheh, ti7 i e5 chheh-nih8 u7 ki3-chai3 chit8 hang7 khah ki5-koai3, thang chhiN-kiaN e5 ki3-su7 kong2, “Siat-su2 tui3 kin-ni5 khi2, kan-ta u7 100 e5 chin-sit8 e5 Ki-tok-tou5, koat-sim ti7 tak8-ni5 ku2 beh kok-kok in2-chhoa7 chit8 e5 peng5-iu2 lai5 bat i e5 Chu2, chiu7 choan5 se3-kai3 ti7 25 ni5 ku2 si7 long2 beh hang5-hok8 ti7 Chu2 e5 kha-e7.”  Goa2 khi2-thau5 thak8 liau2 bo5 sim2-mih8 beh sin3, chong2-si7 goa2 giah8 pit chit8-e7 sng3-khoaN3, to sit8-chai7 u7 iaN2.  Kin-ni5 100, me5-ni5 200, au7-ni5 400, 800, 1600, chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni, tak8 ni5 tit-tioh8 ka-pe7.  Kau3 25 ni5 au7 si7 thang tit-tioh8 16 ek lang5, chhiau-ke3 choan5 se3-kai3 e5 jin5-khau2.  Peng5-iu2 in2-chhoa7 peng5-iu2, tang5-phoaN7 in2-chhoa7 tang5-phoaN7, lau7-bu2 in2-chhoa7 soe3-kiaN2.  Ah!  Hu7-jin5-lang5 ah, Siong7-te3 u7 chiok-hok lin2, sit8-chai7 chha-put-to si7 chi2-u7 lin2 u7 teh choe3 chit e5 kang na7-tiaN7.  sit8-chai7 chha-put-to tak8 e5 choe3 lau7-bu2 e5 lang5 long2 him-bou7 i e5 soe3-kiaN2 lai5 bat Ia5-sou.  Kin-a2-jit8 Siong7-te3 e5 Seng3-kok, si7 tui3 hu7-jin5-lang5 e5 khui3-lat8, u7 chin3-pou7 kau3 chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni.



Te7-4 chiuN	Ka-Na2 e5 Hun-In

	Ke3 saN-jit8 au7, chiu7-si7 ke3-lai5 e5 pai3-saN, Ia5-sou u7 khi3 chit8 e5 hiuN-sia7 hu3 hun-in e5 ian5-siah8.  Chit e5 hun-in si7 u7 hian2-chhut tiong7-iau3 e5 hau7-ko2, put-chi2 u7 eng2-hiong2 ti7 I e5 it-seng e5 su7-giap8.  Iok-han7 ti7 hit jit8 u7 kap Ia5-sou choe3-tin7 khi3, u7 kong2, “e7-saN jit8 ti7 Ka-li7-li7 e5 Ka-na2, u7 hun-in e5 ian5-siah8; Ia5-sou e5 lau7-bu2 ti7-hia; Ia5-sou kap I e5 hak8-seng ia7 hou7 in chhiaN2 khi3 hu3 ian5-siah8.”
	Lan2 hian-khui Seng3-chheh khoaN3-liau2 chai-iaN2 Ia5-sou e5 lau7-bu2 si7 chu2-iau3 e5 tong-su7-chia2, koh chai3 khoaN3 I e5 lau7-bu2 u7 teh khoa3-lu7 in e5 siat-pi7, lai5 hoan-hu3 chhe-eng7 e5 lang5, sou2-i2 tui3 chiah e5 su7-sit8 hou7 lan2 thang chhui -li2, chit e5 hun-in beng5-beng5 si7 I e5 chhin-chok8 lai7 e5 hun-in.  Na7 m7-si7 sin-niu5, chiu7-si7 sin-kiaN2-sai3 si7 Ia5-sou e5 kun7-chhin.  Lan2 thang siong2-siong7, hit jit8 chit e5 sin-niu5 un2-tang3 u7 ti3 sui2 koh phek-peh8 e5 phe3, ia7 chhah chhiN-chhui3 e5 chhiu7-ki, sim-lai7 put-chi2 hoaN-hi2, put-chi2 tek-i3, in-ui7 Ia5-sou u7 lai5 hu3 i e5 hun-in.  Toa7-bin7 tui3 soe3-han3 e5 si5, i chiu7 bat Ia5-sou, in-ui7 in e5 chhu3 saN-li7 chi2-u7 si3-eng-li2 e5 lou7-cham7.  Kiam2-chhai2 i choe3 gin2-na2 e5 si5, bat kap choe7-choe7 gin2-na2 phoaN7 choe3-he2 lai5 Ia5-sou e5 kang-tiuN5, thiaN Ia5-sou kong2 kou3-su7 ia7 ku2 kaN2, sou2 i2 chit e5 hap8-hun-sek si7 i e5 hoaN-hi2 e5 jit8, i chin him-bou7 i e5 chhin-lang5 Ia5-sou chhut-sek8, in-ui7 i put-chi2 chun-keng3 I, thiaN3-thang3 I, khoaN3 I choe3 chit8 e5 toa7-hiaN, iu7-koh in-ui7 Ia5-sou chit-tiap8 i2-keng chiaN5-choe3 tui3 Siong7-te3 sou2 chhe-lai5 e5, chit e5 chhut-mia5 e5 sian-siN, tui3 an2-ni i it-hoat him-bou7 Ia5-sou lai5 chhut-sek8, thang eng5-kng i e5 hap8-hun-sek, thang lai5 khoaN3-kiN3 i e5 heng7-hok, ia7 ng3-bang7 thang tit-tioh8 I e5 chiok-hok.
	Ia5-sou ko2-jian5 u7 chhut-sek8 i e5 hap8-hun-sek.  I ti7 sim-lai7 put-si5 u7 chun5 ui2-tai7 e5 su-siuN2, ke3-ek8 kap chek-jim7, chai-iaN2 I si7 beh lai5 tam-tng jin5-lui7 e5 un7-mia7, sou2-i2 chiah hoaN-hi2 lai5 seng5-siu7 in e5 chiau-thai7。Tui3 an2-ni, Ia5-sou put-chi2 hoaN-hi2 lai5 hu3 in-e5 hun-in.
	U7 choe7-choe7 lang5 teh siuN7 kong2, Ia5-sou si7 choe3 chit8 e5 kek8 giam5-siok, hu7 gi7-bu7 lang5, khi3 hu3 hit e5 hun-in, oan2-jian5 chhin-chhiuN7 chit8 e5 u7 ui-giam5 e5 bok8-su beh khi3 hu3 lang5 e5 hun-in, thang soa3 eng7 keng3-khian5 e5 oe7 lai5 khou2-khng3 lang5-kheh.  Toan3-toan3 m7-si7!  Tui3 hit khoan2 e5 thai3-tou7, Ia5-sou si7 kek8 put chu7-jian5, kek8 m7-ai3, si7 boe7 oe7 tong5-cheng5.  I chhut-sek8 hit e5 hun-in, si7 in-ui7 I u7 hoaN-hi2 hun-in.  Ti7 se3-kan bo5 chit8-lang5 bat chhin-chhiuN7 Ia5-sou e5 khoan2, u7 hiah-nih8 khoai3-lok8 jin5-seng.  I sit8-chai7 si7 chin thiaN3-thang3 jin5-seng, I si7 u7 hiong2-siu7 tak8 ho7 e5 khoai3-lok8.  I si7 u7 liah8 chu7-jian5 choe3 khoai3-lok8.  I si7 u7 khoaN3 soe3-han3 gin2-na2 choe3 khoai3-lok8.  I si7 u7 hoaN-hi2 kap lang5 choe3 peng5-iu2 saN kau-poe5, chai-iaN2 che si7 bo5 boe7 eng7-tit e5 su7.  I si7 put-chi2 hoaN-hi2 ai3 kap sia7-hoe7 e5 lang5 saN-kap choe3-he2 kau-poe5, lai5 hoaN-hi2 ke3-jit8; tek8-piat8 tui3 hiah e5 kho2-lin5 e5, koh khah si7 an2-ni, ti3-kau3 Hoat-li7-sai3 lang5 soa3 chheng I choe3 tham-chiah8 houN3-chiu2 e5, thiu-hiong3 e5, i2-kip8 choe7-jin5 e5 peng5-iu2.  U7 iaN2 chit e5 oe7 si7 oan3-hun7 hui2-pong3 e5 oe7, chong2-si7 u7 chit8-tiam2 lan2 thang chu3-i3, chiu7-si7, siat-su2 na7 m7-si7 I sit8-chai7 si7 u7 chin hoaN-hi2, lai5 kap sia7-hoe7 e5 lang5 saN-kap kau-poe5, soa3 eng7 hoaN-hi2 e5 sim lai5 hiong2-siu7 I e5 saN-tng3, chiu7 koat-toan3 bo5 u7 chit ho7 hui2-pong3 e5 oe7 chiah tioh8.

	Sit8-chai7 Ia5-sou na7-si7 kau3 hia, khoai3-lok8 chiu7 te3 kau3 hia, in-ui7 I pun2-sin si7 put-chi2 khoai3-lok8 e5 lang5.  I ti7 hun-in e5 ian5-toh si7 chin hoaN-hi2, lai5 kong2 lai5 chhio3.  I sim-lai7 si7 put-chi2 him-bou7 ai3 kap cheng3-lang5 choe3-he2.  I si7 siong5-siong5 ai3 po-chiong2 hiah e5 sit-chi3 e5 lang5.  I kong2, An li2 e5 sim, si7 goa2; m7-bian2 kiaN!  ChaiN2-iuN7? chu7-jian5 in-ui7 I pun2-sin si7 khoai3-lok8 e5 lang5.  Kin-a2-jit8 ti7 se3-kan te7-it khoai3-lok8 e5, chiu7-si7 hiah e5 oe7 eng7 ho2 lai5 li7-ek pat8-lang5 e5, sim-lai7 siong5-siong5 khoai3-lok8 lai5 giong2-bong7 Siong7-te3, lai5 oan5-choan5 sin3-kho3 Siong7-te3 e5 lang5, chiu7-si7 hiah e5 ti7 sim-lai7 u7 khng3 bu5 han7-liong7 e5 lok8-koan e5 lang5, lai5 khak-sit8 chai in u7 choe3-au7 e5 seng3-li7, ia7 chai, si2 chiu7-si7 teng5-chai3 chhut-si3 ti7 hit e5 khah hong-seng7 e5 se3-kai3, iu7-koh chai-iaN2 choe7-ok ti7 u7 chit8-jit8 beh eng2-oan2 biat8-bo5.  Siat-su2 lan2 na7-si7 u7 oh8 Ia5-sou e5 khoan2, lan2 tak8-lang5 tiaN7-tioh8 si7 oe7 chiaN5-choe3 heng7-hok khoai3-lok8 e5 lang5.
	Put-tan3 si7 an2-ni, I it-seng sou2 hoaN-hi2 e5, chiu7-si7 ai3 pang-chan7 hiah e5 bo5 sin5-seng3 e5 lang5, chiaN5-choe3 sin5-seng3; sim bo5 peng5-an e5, chiaN5-choe3 u7 peng5-an.  Iu7-koh I u7 kam2-kak, ti7 teng2-bin7 hit e5 bu5-han7 e5 heng7-hok e5 sim5-seng3 e5 se3-kai3, si7 u7 jiat8-jiat8 eng7 tong5-cheng5 e5 sim teh khoaN3-kou3 I.  I ti7-teh hoaN-hi2 chit8 e5 choe7-jin5 hok8-to3 si3-chiaN3 e5 seng-oah8 e5 si5, I si7 iu5-goan5 u7 thiaN-tioh8 Siong7-te3 e5 cheng3 thiN-sai3 ti7-teh hoaN-hi2 khoai3-lok8 e5 siaN.
	Goa2 teh ki5-koai3, m7-chai lan2 it-poaN tui3 ta2-loh8 lai5 siuN7 kong2, Ia5-sou si7 iu-chhiu5 e5 bin7-mau7 e5 lang5.  Chhin-chhiuN7 chit ho7 e5 khoaN3-hoat, tek-khak m7-si7 chhut tui3 Hok-im-su e5 kou3-su7.  Lan2 thang liau7 chit ho7 e5 khoaN3-hoat, si7 chhut tui3 I2-sai3-a e5 u7-gian5, in-ui7 ti7-hia u7 teh kong2-khi2 “I siong5-siong5 tu2-tioh8 kan-khou2; sim-lai7 toa7 hoan5-lo2.”  U7 choe7-choe7 ui2-tai7 e5 bi2-sut8-ka, put-si5 to teh oe7 hit khoan2 iu-chhiu5 e5 bin7-mau7 e5 Ia5-sou; tui3 an2-ni, lan2 ai3 than3 hit e5 khoan2, lai5 thak8 Ia5-sou it-seng e5 kou3-su7; ki5-sit8 che si7 ke3-thau5 e5 sou2-chai7 ti7-teh.  U7 iaN2!  I u7 tam-tng lan2 e5 kan-khou2, taN lan2 e5 piN7-thiaN3.  Lan2 ai3 eng7 thiaN3-thang3, kam2-sia7 e5 sim, lai5 seng5-jin7 chit-tiam2.  Chong2-si7 thoe3 pat8-lang5 lai5 kan-khou2, lai5 si2, to m7-si7 kong2, tui3 an2-ni chiu7 oe7 hoe3-bo5 hit e5 ui2-tai7 e5 sim-sin5 sou2 u7 e5 hoaN-hi2 kap khoai3-lok8.  M7-si7 chai7 hit-khoan2 jiat8-sim kam-goan7 pang3-sak ka-ki7 e5 lang5 teh khoaN3, hi-seng e5 heng5-ui5 chiu7-si7 chit8 hang7 e5 khoai3-lok8.  Chhi3-mng7, ti7 chian3-tiuN5 pun2-sin kap si2 choe3 peng5-iu2 e5 peng, oe7-hiau2 tong5-cheng5 hiah e5 tioh8-siong e5, lai5 kng i tng2-lai5 khan3-hou7, hit-si5 i e5 sim-sin5 kiam2 u7 iu-chhiu5?  Sou2-i2 goa2 teh siuN7, Ia5-sou oe7 thang thoe3 pat8 lang5 lai5 si2, sit8-chai7 si7 hou7 Ia5-sou e5 lai7-bin7 seng-oah8 ke-thiN chit8 hoan e5 hoaN-hi2 khoai3-lok8 chiah tioh8.
	Chiau3 lang5 e5 i3-su3 lai5 kong2, I ti7 it-seng oe7-thang khah-iaN5 se3-kan, si7 in-ui7 I e5 sim-lai7 put-si5 u7 hoaN-hi2 khoai3-lok8.  I koat-toan3 si7 bo5 sit-loh8 chit-ho7 e5 sim.  Lian5 ti7 kek8 pi-chham2 e5 jit8, I ma7-si7 bo5 sit-loh8.  Iau2-be7 khi3 Khek-se-ma2-ni5 hng5 e5 saN tiam2 cheng cheng5, I ma7 iau2-koh hou7 cheng3 hak8-seng lai5 siuN7-tioh8 in ti7 i2-cheng5 sou2 u7 e5 khoai3-lok8 e5 seng-oah8, iu7-koh I e5 choe3-au7 e5 ng3-bang7, iu5-goan5 si7 ai3 in beng5-pek8, lian5 I li7-khui in khi3 liau2-au7, ti7 se3-kan I sou2 u7 e5 hoaN-hi2, to iu5-goan5 beh kap in ti7-teh, hou7 in thang tit-tioh8 koh khah chhiong-seng7 u7 hoaN-hi2 moa2-moa2 e5 seng-oah8.  Sit8-chai7 Ia5-sou khah-cha2 ti7 se3-kan kap I e5 hak8-seng teh kau-poe5 e5 tiong-kan sou2 tit-tioh8 e5 hoaN-hi2, si7 ti7 chit se3-kan be7-bat u7 lang5 keng-giam7--tioh8 e5.  I pun2-sin u7 chit8 jit8 bat tui3 I e5 hak8-seng kong2, iah8 lan2 thang siuN7, tek-khak si7 eng7 chhio3 gi7-gi7 e5 bin7-mau7 lai5 kong2, “Lan2 si7 chhin-chhiuN7 hu2-hu7, ti7 sin-hun e5 lu2-heng5 tiong, Lan2 si7 kap sin-kiaN2-sai3 saN-kap ti7-teh e5 ho7-chhoa7 e5.”  U7 hit-ho7 bin7 tai3 iu-chhiu5 e5 Hoat-li7-sai3 lang5 lai5 mng7 Ia5-sou kong2, “Li2 e5 hak8-seng bo5 kim3-chiah8, si7 chaiN2-iuN7?”  Ia5-sou chiu7 ka7 in kong2, “Goan2 m7-bian2 kim3-chiah8, ai-siong; goan2 tai7-ke si7 chin khoai3-lok8; sin-kiaN2-sai3 kap ho7-chhoa7 e5 lang5 saN-kap ti7-teh, ho7-chhoa7 e5 lang5 kiam2 oe7 ai-siong mah?  Tok8-tok8 si5-jit8 beh kau3, sin-kiaN2-sai3 tui3 in tiong-kan bo5--khi3, hit-si5 in chiu7 beh kim3-chiah8.  Chit-tiap8 tioh8 theng3-hau7 kau3 hit e5 si5 kau3, chiah thang kim3-chiah8 ai-siong.”  M7-si7!  Ia5-sou m7-si7 hit-ho7 iu-chhiu5 e5 bin7-mau7 e5 lang5.  Chiau3 lan2 sou2 chai, I e5 jin5-keh put-si5 u7 khip-in2-lat8; m7-ku2 iu-chhiu5 e5 bin7-mau7 khah-siong5 si7 bo5 kah loa7 u7 khip-in2 e5 lat8 ti7-teh.  Lan2 m7-ai3 u7 hit khoan2 e5 bin7-mau7, I ma7-si7 m7-ai3.  Lian5 tui3 hak8-seng I ia7-si7 hoaN-hi2 an2-ni ka7 in kong2, “Lin2 kim3-chiah8 e5 si5, boh8-tit chhin-chhiuN7 ke2-ho2 e5 lang5 tai3 iu-iong5,”

	Ia5-sou si7 Siong7-te3.  Lan2 na7 khoaN3-kiN3 Ia5-sou si7 chin khoai3-lok8 khi3 hu3 hun-in e5 ian5-siah8, hit-si5 lan2 thang tui3 Ia5-sou lai5 chai-iaN2 Siong7-te3 e5 chhin-chhiat e5 seng3-chit kau3 ta2-loh8.  Siong7-te3 e5 sim si7 u7 hoaN-hi2 lan2 lang5 e5 hun-in.  Siong7-te3 e5 sim si7 u7 hoaN-hi2 lang5 tit-tioh8 khoai3-lok8.  Ti7 Ka-li7-li7 e5 Ka-na2, lan2 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 chit e5 Eng2-oan2 e5 Ki-tok, kek8 chiau3 chu7-jian5, chiau3 lang5 e5 khoan2, hoaN-hi2 lai5 chhut-sek8 hit e5 hiong-chhoan lang5 soe3-soe3 e5 hun-in, ia7 u7 tong5-cheng5 in nng7 e5 ai3-jin5 ti7 hun-in e5 hoaN-hi2, soa3 chin3 chit8-pou7. ai3 lan2 ti7 sim-nih8 oe7 siuN7 kong2, Che si7 Siong7-te3 e5 thai3-tou7.  Che si7 Siong7-te3 e5 sim-i3.  Siong7-te3 chu7-jian5 si7 put-chi2 koan-sim ti7 lan2 e5 chiaN5-seng3, lan2 e5 seng3-kiat.  Chong2-si7 m7-si7 chhin-chhiuN7 hit-ho7 ui-giam5 e5 bok8-su, kan-ta koan-sim ti7 kau3-hoe7, soat-kau3, tian2-le2, khah bo5 koan-sim ti7 jin5-seng e5 khoai3-lok8 e5 tai7-chi3.  Lan2 e5 Pe7 Siong7-te3 si7 u7 koan-sim ti7 I e5 cheng3 kiaN2-ji5 it-chhe3 sou2 u7 sim-sek e5 su7.  I si7 u7 hun7 ti7 jin5-lui7 it-chhe3, siok8 ti7 seng3-kiat kap khoai3-lok8 e5 su7.  I si7 u7 seng3-piat chiok-hok it-chhe3 jin5-lui7 e5 koan-he7.  I si7 u7 chhu3-bi7 ti7 khong-tiong e5 pe-chiau2, soaN-nih8 e5 ia2-hoe, ti7 chhau2-pou teh thiau3-bu2 e5 soe3-chiah iuN5-a2, ti7 chhi7-tiuN5 teh thit-tho5 e5 gin2-na2, i2-kip8 lau7-bu2 tui3 eN-a2 sou2 hian2-chhut hit e5 jin5-chu5 e5 sim, i2-kip8 siau3-lian5 e5 sin-niu5, ui3 siau2-le2 teh m7-kaN2 kiN3 sin-kiaN2-sai3 e5 bin7.  Siong7-te3 si7 ai3 lan2 oe7-hiau2 khoai3-lok8 jin5-seng.  Siong7-te3 u7 chhong3-cho7 im-gak8, ge7-sut8, thang hou7 lan2 tit-tioh8 khoai3-lok8.  Siong7-te3 u7 hou7 lan2 oe7-hiau2 kong2 chhio3-khoe e5 oe7, thang pang-chan7 lan2 khah khoai3 kiaN5 jin5-seng kham-khiat8 e5 lou7-cham7.  Hoan7-na7 oe7 hou7 lang5 e5 sim chiaN5-choe3 khoai3-lok8 hit-ho7 bo5 sia5-khi3 e5 kong2-chhio3, si7 teh kiaN5 ti7 ThiN-nih8 e5 Pe7 Siong7-te3 e5 chi2-i3.  Lan2 kiam2 bo5 siuN7 kong2, chong-kau3 ki5-sit8 si7 kek8 tan-sun5, sui2 e5 su7 mah?  Siat-su2 lan2 na7-si7 eng7 Ia5-sou e5 kian3-kai2 lai5 hak8-sip8 i, lan2 kiam2 bo5 siuN7 kong2, chong-kau3 si7 koh-khah oe7 giu2 soe3-han3 gin2-na2 e5 sim e5 su7 mah?

	In e5 hun-in si7 u7 tu2-tioh8 chin hui3-khi3 e5 su7.  ChhiaN2 oe7 ki3-tit, chit e5 si7 choh-sit lang5 e5 hun-in.  Chu2-ka si7 song3-hiong e5 lang5, beh lai5 khui hun-in e5 ian5-siah8, chiN5 cham2-jian5 si7 u7 khah an5.  Sou2-i2 ian5-siah8 kiaN5 kau3 tiong-cham7 e5 si5, u7 tu2-tioh8 theng5-chi2 e5 kan-khou2.  In-ui7 tut8-jian5-kan hoat-kian3--tioh8 chiu2 bo5 kau3-giah8.  U7 lang5 kiam2-chhai2 beh kong2, che put-ko3 si7 sio2-khoa2 e5 su7.  Iau2-ku2 hu7-jin5-lang5 chiu7 bo5 beh an2-ni phah-sng3.  Bo5 lun7 siaN2 khoan2, Ka-na2 hit e5 sin-niu5 sim-lai7 un2-tang3 ma7 bo5 beh siuN7 kong2 si7 sio2-khoa2 su7.  I chai, i i2-kip8 sin-kiaN2-sai3 ti7 cheng3 peng5-iu2 e5 bin7-cheng5 si7 chin kian3-siau3.  Ia5-sou ma7-si7 bo5 kong2 che si7 sio2-khoa2 e5 su7.  Ia5-sou chai, chu2-ka e5 lang5 si7 khah ai3 u7 the2-bian7, iah8 chai, ti7 hit ho7 si5-chun7 bo5 kau3-giah8 thang ho2 khoan2-thai7 lang5-kheh, si7 chin kian3-siau3.
	Ia5-sou e5 lau7-bu2 aN3 ti7 I e5 hi7-khang piN, soe3-soe3 siaN tui3 I kong2 --- goa2 teh liau7, chi2-u7 Iok-han7 u7 thiaN-kiN3 na7-tiaN7 --- “In bo5 chiuq2 lah.”
	Kiam2 si7 Ma2-li7-a him-bou7 ai3 khoaN3 I kiaN5 sin5-jiah mah?  Lan2 khiok si7 boe7 thang kong2 an3-choaN2, I to iau2-be7 kiaN5 sim2-mih8 sin5-jiah, iu7-koh lan2 un2-tang3 beh siuN7 sin5-jiah si7 siok8 ti7 khah ko-siong7 e5 si5 chiah tioh8 kiaN5 e5, khah m7-si7 ti7 ian3-sek8 e5 si5 lai5 kiaN5 e5 su7.  Kiam2-chhai2 tui3 Iok-sek ke3-sin liau2-au7, Ma2-li7-a tak8 pai2 u7 tu2-tioh8 khun3-lan5, chiu7 koaiN3-si3 oa2-kho3 I lai5 kai2-koat, sou2-i2 chit-tiap8 chu7-jian5 ia7 ai3 lai5 khoaN3 I.  Ma2-li7-a chai-iaN2 I un2-tang3 oe7 tau3 khoa3 sim, siat-su2 I na7 oe7 thang choe3, tiaN7-tioh8 si7 oe7 eng7 hoat-tou7 lai5 pang-chan7 in.  Kiat-kiok8 lai5 kong2, lian5 lan2 na7 u7 tu2-tioh8 sim2-mih8 khun3-lan5, lai5 chhe7 Ia5-sou, tui3 I kong2-khi2, lai5 kiu5 I e5 pang-chan7, che to m7-si7 m7-ho2 e5 sin3-giong2.
	Put-ko3 Ia5-sou tui3 I e5 lau7-bu2 sou2 in3-tap e5 oe7, u7 piau2-beng5 ti7 I e5 sim-lai7, chai-iaN2 lau7-bu2 teh chhui-pek I lai5 kiaN5 sin5-jiah.  I sou2 in3-tap hit ku3 oe7, chiau3 lan2 sou2 hoan-ek8 e5, thiaN-liau2 si7 cham2-jian5 khah keh8-hi7 e5 khoan2,  “Hu7-jin5-lang5 ah, goa2 kap li2 u7 sim2-mih8 kan-siap8.”  Chong2-si7 lan2 chi2-u7 si7 thak8-tioh8 I e5 piau2-bin7-chiuN7 e5 oe7 na7-tiaN7, lan2 bo5 thiaN-tioh8 I sou2 in3-tap e5 khau2-im, a2-si7 I e5 bak8-chiu e5 piau2-hian7 e5 khoan2-sit, in-ui7 che si7 cham2-jian5 u7 koan-he7 ti7 hit e5 i3-su3.  Ia5-sou kio3 I e5 lau7-bu2 kong2, Hu7-jin5-lang5 ah, si7 chhin-chhiuN7 chin phaiN2 thiaN e5 khoan2, chong2-si7 ki5-sit8, che si7 peng5-siong5 teh chheng-hou e5 hoat-tou7.  Li2 khoaN3! lian5 ti7 hit ho7 teh piau2-si7 chun-keng3 kap thiaN3-thang3 e5 si5, to iu5-goan5 si7 chheng-hou an2-ni.  Lan2 oe7 ki3-tit A-kou2-su-tok ia7 u7 eng7 an2-ni lai5 chheng-hou lu2-ong5 Khu-le2-o-pa-to-lah (Cleopatra).  Ti7 kou2-cha2 e5 kui3-chok8 kai-kip, iu5-goan5 si7 eng7 siang7 chit khoan2 e5 chheng-hou.  Tui3 hit e5 ti7 bong7-nih8 teh thi5-khau3 e5 Boat8-tai7-liap8 e5 Ma2-li7-a, Ia5-sou iu5-goan5 chiau3 an2-ni chheng-hou i.  Iu7-koh lan2 oe7 ki3-tit, I tui3 Sip8-ji7-ke3 lai5 tui3 I e5 lau7-bu2 sou2 lau5 lim5-chiong e5 ui5-gian5, ma7-si7 kong2, “Hu7-jin5-lang5 ah, khoaN3, li2 e5 kiaN2.”  Ki5-sit8 lan2 ma7-si7 chai-iaN2, Ma2-li7-a long2 bo5 chit8-sut-a2 u7 m7 hoaN-hi2, a2-si7 u7 sun2-hai7--tioh8 i e5 kam2-cheng5.  Ma2-li7-a kau3-giah8 u7 liau2-kai2, chai-iaN2 I u7 tong5-cheng5 e5 sim ti7-teh.  Siat-su2 Ma2-li7-a bo5 liau2-kai2 lai5 kong2, ia7 si7 u7 sin3-iong7 I, sou2-i2 kan-ta tui3 chhe-eng7 e5 kong2, “Hoan7-na7 I ka7 lin2 kong2 e5, lin2 tioh8 kiaN5 i.”
	M7-si7!  Ia5-sou m7-si7 bo5 the2-thiap I e5 lau7-bu2 Ma2-li7-a.  Put-ko3 I an2-ni in3 i, si7 ai3 hou7 i chai, in nng7 lang5 e5 koan-he7, si7 i2-keng u7 pian3-oaN7.  Ma2-li7-a chit-tiap8 tek-khak si7 boe7 thang khoan2-thai7 I chhin-chhiuN7 cha2, “Ia5-sou kap in loh8-khi3 Na2-sat-lek8, lai5 seng5-sun7 in.” hit si5 e5 khoan2.  Chit-tiap8 I si7 u7 toa7 e5 su2-beng7 tioh8 chin7.  Chit-tiap8 I si7 u7 phau7 choe7-choe7 e5 sim-su, si7 Ma2-li7-a sou2 boe7 thang liau2-kai2 tong5-i3 e5.  In e5 bu2-kiaN2 e5 koan-he7, si7 boe7 thang kan-siap8.  Chu7-jianche5 si7 i choe3 lau7-bu2 oh-tit liau2-kai2 e5 oe7, si7 chit8 pai2 ke3 chit8 pai2, siuN7 boe7 liau2-kai2 e5 oe7.  Chit-tiap8 Ma2-li7-a un2-tang3 si7 iau2 oe7 ki3-tit Ia5-sou choe3 gin2-na2 e5 si5, tui3 i sou2 in3 hit ku3 oe7.  “Kiam2 m7-chai, goa2 eng-kai ti7 goa2 e5 Pe7 e5 chhu3 mah?”

Chiau3-khoaN3 Ia5-sou u7 chiam7-si5  ku2, ian5-chhian5 siuN7 bo5 ai3 kiaN5 sim2-mih8 sin5-jiah.  Lan2 thang siuN7, I khi3 hu3 chit e5 hun-in, chiau3-khoaN3 si7 bo5 chhun7-pan7 beh kiaN5 sin5-jiah chiah tioh8, an2-ni siuN7, kiam2-si7 u7 put keng3-khian5 e5 sou2-chai7 mah?  I to hoaN-hi2 seng5-siu7 iu2-han7 e5 jin5-seng3, chu7-jian5 I un2-tang3 bo5 pit-iau3 tioh8 put-si5 koan-sim ti7 be7 kau3 e5 su7.  Lan2 u7 thak8-tioh8 kong2, I u7 bat tu2-tioh8 hit ho7 chin bo5 an3-sng3 e5 tai7-chi3.  Siat-su2 chit e5 tai7-chi3 si7 m7-si7 I e5 pun2-i3, lan2 thang kong2, che si7 ti7 tut8-jian5 e5 tiong-kan, koaN2-kin2 lai5 koat-sim lai5 kiaN5 e5.  I chit-tiap8 sng3-si7 iau2-be7 chhut-hoat I e5 kong seng-gai5, tu2-tu2 si7 teh-beh chin3-cheng5 khi3 na7-tiaN7.  sou2-i2 I na7-si7 eng7 sin5-jiah lai5 chhut-hoat, kiaN-liau2 si7 chhin-chhiuN7 teh ke3 Lu2-bi2-kou2 ho5 (Rubicon), si7 mou7-hiam2 e5 su7, tiaN7-tioh8 si7 oe7 chek-si5 in2-chhoa7 I kiaN5 kau3 ti7 Kok-kok-thaN e5 lou7-cham7, lai5 tu2-tioh8 toa7 e5 oah8-mia7 e5 cheng-chian3.  I ti7 sim-lai7 tiap-a2(**tiap8-a2)-ku2 teh siuN7 kong2, chit-tiap8 lai5 kiaN5 sin5-jiah kiam2-si7 Pe7 e5 chi2-i3, kiam2-si7 tioh8 lai5 hian2-chhut thiaN3-thang3 e5 sim, lai5 kiu3 I e5 peng5-iu2 bian2 ti3-kau3 kian3-siau3 mah?  Lan2 ti7 hit khoan2 chhiong-tong7, khah-siong5 oe7 tit-tioh8 chai Siong7-te3 e5 chi2-i3 sou2 kau-tai7 lan2 tioh8 choe3 e5 su7.
Ia5-sou ti7 tiap-a2(**tiap8-a2)-ku2 e5 tiong-kan, siuN7 liau2 chiu7 koat-sim beh kiaN5 sin5-jiah.  Ti7 chit8 le2 pai3 cheng5, I si7 u7 ku7-choat8 Mou5-kui2 e5 chhi3, bo5 beh pian3 chioh8 piN3-choe3 piaN2, lai5 kiu3 I pun2-sin thoat-li7 iau-go7.  Chong2-si7 chit-tiap8 I si7 u7 hoaN-hi2, chiong chui2 pian3-choe3 chiu2, lai5 kiu3 I e5 peng5-iu2 bian2 ti3-kau3 kian3-siau3.  Sit8-chai7 che si7 Siong7-te3 e5 thai3-tou7.
Ia5-sou chiu7 ka7 chhe-eng7 e5 kong2, “Eng7 chui2 hou7 i moa2 ang3!”  In chiu7 hou7 i moa2 kau3 ang3-khau2.  Koh ka7 in kong2, TaN tioh8 iuN2 i, phang5 hou7 chiang2-li2 ian5-toh e5 lang5.  In chiu7 phang5 hou7 i.  Chiang2-li2 ian5-toh e5 lang5 chhi3 lim i, chai-iaN2 si7 chui2 pian3-choe3 chiu2, chong2-si7 m7-chai tui3 ta2 loh8 lai5, (lan2 choe7-choe7 lang5 tit-tioh8 Siong7-te3 e5 un-su3, iu5-goan5 si7 chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni, long2 bo5 mng7 khoaN3 si7 tui3 ta2-loh8 lai5), chi2-u7 tui3 sin-kiaN2-sai3 kong2, “Tok8-tok8 li2 lau5 chiu2 kau3 ti7 chit-tiap8.”
Lan2 phah-sng3 hit nng7 e5 siau3-lian5 e5 sin-kiaN2-sai3 kap sin-niu5, beh khoai3-khoai3 lai5 boe7 ki3-tit in Piau2-e5, ui7-tioh8 in ti7 ian5-siah8 e5 tiong-kan, sou2 kiaN5 chit e5 su7 mah?  Sit8-chai7 chin kho2-sioh ti7 hit-jit8 bo5 lang5 thang tui3 hit e5 Ka-na2 e5 sin-niu5 lai5 kong2-khi2, in e5 hun-in si7 beh chiaN5-choe3 choan5 se3-kai3 e5 lek8-su2 tiong, te7-it chhut-mia5 e5 hun-in, soa3 kong2, ti7 2000 ni5 au7 lang5 un2-tang3 beh kang2-kiu3 chit e5 kou3-su7, lai5 beng5-pek8 che si7 Siong7-te3 thau5 chit8-pai2 tui3 lang5 lai5 hian2-hian7 I pun2-sin.
Chit e5 hun-in thang kong2 si7 ti7 Ia5-sou e5 lek8-su2 tiong e5 chit8 choan2-ki, hit e5 i3-su3 m7-si7 kan-ta teh piau2-beng5 tui3 chit-tiap8 khi2, I u7 chhut-hoat I e5 kong seng-gai5, iu5-goan5 soa3 teh piau2-beng5 I tui3 lang5 khi2-thau5 lai5 hian2-chhut I pun2-sin si7 chi7-chui7.  sou2-i2 Iok-han7 chiah kong2, “Chit e5 thau5 chit8-pai2 e5 sin5-jiah, Ia5-sou kiaN5 ti7 Ka-li7-li7 e5 Ka-na2, lai5 hian2-chhut I e5 eng5-kng.  I e5 hak8-seng chiu7 sin3 I.”

Chit e5 si7 Ia5-sou sou2 kiaN5 e5 “thau5 chit8-pai2 e5 sin5-jiah.” sou2-i2 lan2 ti7 chia lai5 kang2-lun7 Chu2 Ia5-sou e5 sin5-jiah e5 bun7-toe5, chiau3 khoaN3 si7 chin tu2-hap8.  U7 lang5 siuN7, sin5-jiah hoan2-tng2 si7 chiaN5-choe3 Hok-im-su tiong e5 that-gai7 chioh8.  Siat-su2 sin5-jiah na7 oe7-thang theh8--khi2-lai5, tai7-ke si7 oe7 khah khoai3 lai5 sin3 Hok-im.  Kiam2-chhai2!  Chong2-si7 cheng3 Hok-im-su e5 tu3-chia2, m7-si7 ui7-tioh8 beh hap8 lang5 e5 sin3-sim e5 lou7-eng7, chiah lai5 sia2 in e5 chheh.  In chi2-u7 si7 chiau3 sou2 chai e5 su7-sit8 lai5 sia2-beng5 na7-tiaN7.  Chai7 in khak-sit8 si7 bo5 choe3 that-gai7 chioh8.
Ti7 chap8-kau2 se3-ki2 e5 chu7-jian5 kho-hak8, khah siong5 si7 ai3 chu2-chhiong3 kong2, “Chu7-jian5 e5 se3-kai3, si7 chiau3 it-teng7 e5 hoat-chek teh un7-choan2.  Sit8-chai7 long2 bo5 u7 khoaN3-tioh8 sim2-mih8 sin5-jiah chham-chhap ti7 hit tiong-kan.  Sou2-i2 na7-si7 lun7 sin5-jiah e5 su7, lan2 sui-si7 boe7 thang kong2 khak-sit8 e5 oe7, siang7 chio2-chio2 to tioh8 khng3 giau5-gi5 e5 thai3-tou7.”  Chong2-si7 ji7-chap8 se3-ki2 e5 kho-hak8, si7 cham2-jian5 u7 khah khiam-pi, u7 ko3-pek8 kong2, kho-hak8 put-ko3 si7 chai-bat ti7 hian7-siong7 e5 se3-kai3 lian5-lian5 sou2 hoat-seng e5 su7-sit8 na7-tiaN7.  Lun7-khi2 ban7-mih8 e5 goan5-thau5, a2-si7 hian7-siong7 se3-kai3 e5 poe3(**poe7)-au7, hit e5 Sim-i3 (Will), kho-hak8 si7 choan5-jian5 m7-chai.  Sit8-chai7 lai5 kong2, u7 hoat-seng chit8 hang7 e5 su7-but8, chiu7 tek-khak u7 hit e5 goan5-in.  It-tan3 u7 Goan5-in, chiu7 tek-khak ti7 hit e5 au7-bin7 u7 chit8 e5 Sim-i3 ti7-teh chiah tioh8.  Siat-su2 lan2 na7 oe7 thang seng5-jin7 chhin-chhiuN7 Hoa3-sin hit ho7 tok8-it bu5-ji7 e5 su7-sit8, kho-hak8 un2-tang3 si7 iu5-goan5 beh seng5-jin7 sin5-jiah chiah tioh8.  Chai7 hit ho7 u7 keng3-khian5, u7 chun5 ki5-iN7 e5 kam2-liam7 e5 lang5 teh khoaN3 chit e5 u2-tiu7 si7 o3-biau7, sin5-pi3 liau2-liau2.  Chhin-chhiuN7 Bi2-kok e5 si-jin5 (Walt Whitman) u7 kong2, “Chiau3 goa2 teh khoaN3, bo5 chit8 hang7 m7-si7 sin5-jiah.  Chai7 goa2, bo5 lun7 si7 kng, si7 am3, tak8 si5-khek to si7 sin5-jiah.”
Sin5-jiah u7 an3-choaN2 teh hian2-chhut I e5 eng5-kng?  sin5-jiah si7 piau2-beng5 I si7 Chu7-jian5 e5 Chu2-chaiN2.  Lan2 phah-sng3 hiah e5 hak8-seng ti7 hit si5, boe7 chap8-hun liau2-kai2 hit e5 i3-su3 chiah tioh8.  In-ui7 in chi2-u7 chiah kap I sio-bat bo5 loa7 ku2.  Chong2-si7 Iok-han7 chit-tiap8 si7 u7 keng-giam7--tioh8 Ia5-sou e5 Sip8-ji7-ke3, i2-kip8 I e5 koh-oah8, iu7-koh ti7 gou7-chap8 ni5 ku2 e5 tiong-kan, u7 bek8-siong2 i e5 Chu2 e5 seng-oah8.  I chit-tiap8 i2-keng khak-sit8 chai Ia5-sou si7 chi7-chui7, I u7 sia2 kong2, “I ti7 khi2-thau5 kap Siong7-te3 saN-kap ti7-teh.  Ban7-mih8 tui3 I lai5 chhong3-cho7; kiN3-na7 siu7 chhong3-cho7 e5, bo5 chit8 hang7 m7-si7 tui3 I lai5 chhong3-cho7.”  Ia5-sou u7 chhong3-cho7 se3-kan ban7 hang7 e5 mih8, u7 hou7 ban7-mih8 thang tit-tioh8 siu-seng5, iu7-koh ti7 tak8 si5-tai7, ti7 tak8 sou2-chai7 e5 phu5-to5-hng5, ma7 u7 teh hou7 chui2 pian3 choe3 chiu2.
Goa2 oe7 ki3-tit, bat u7 chit8 jit8 lu2-heng5 ti7 Sui7-se kok e5 Lo5-ni5 (Rhone) e5 soaN-khiN, hit-si5 sim-lai7 u7 kam2-siong2-tioh8 Ka-na2 e5 sin5-jiah.  Hit-si5 tu2-tu2 si7 u2-ki5.  Hit e5 soaN-io, soaN-kham3, tak8 ui7 long2 si7 phu5-to5 liau2-liau2.  Hou7-chui2 put-chi2 toa7, piaN3-loh8 ti7 phu5-to5-hng5.  Ti7 bo5 kui2 geh8-jit8 e5 tiong-kan, ban2 phu5-to5 e5 lang5 u7 lai5, iah8 khoaN3-kiN3 i2-cheng5 sou2 loh8 e5 hou7-chui2, taN i2-keng long2 si7 pian3-choe3 chiu2.  Hit e5 phu5-to5 chiu2, chiu7 hoat-sang3 kau3 ti7 thong se3-kai3 tak8 sou2-chai7 e5 ian3-sek8, iah8 chiang2-li2 ian5-toh e5 lang5 chhi3 lim i, chong2-si7 m7-chai tui3 ta2-loh8 lai5.  In kan-ta kong2, “Chit e5 bi7 chin7-chai7 tiN, koh chin u7 phang-thau5.  Che long2 si7 koan-he7 ti7 jit8-thau5 e5 iam7-jiat8, phu5-to5 e5 seng3-chit, i2-kip8 koan-he7 ti7 soaN-toe7 e5 tek8-piat8 e5 hoa3-hak8 chok-iong7.”  In si7 chi2-u7 bat kau3 chia na7-tiaN7.  In si7 boe7 thang koh chin3-cheng5 lai5 kong2 siaN2 khoan2.  Ki5-sit8 Siong7-te3 put-si5 to teh kiaN5 sin5-jiah ti7 lan2 e5 beh8-hng5, ma7-si7 put-si5 teh hou7 chui2 pian3 choe3 chiu2 ti7 lan2 e5 phu5-to5-hng5; sit8-chai7 lan2 long2 bo5 kam2-kak--tioh8 ti7 lan2 e5 sin-piN sou2 u7 phou2-thong e5 su7-sit8 e5 tiong-kan, u7 chit khoan2 chong3-giam5 e5 eng5-kng ti7-teh.
Sin5-jiah e5 i3-gi7 si7 teh ka3-si7 lan2 chai, hit e5 chong3-giam5 e5 eng5-kng u7 put-si5 pau-ui5 ti7 lan2 e5 sin-piN.  Chi3-toa7 e5 cho7-but8 Chu2, u7 eng7 sin5-jiah e5 hoat-tou7 ti7 tiap-a2(**tiap8-a2)-ku2 e5 tiong-kan lai5 piau2-si7 I pun2-sin, hou7 lan2 oe7 ki3-tit, sui-jian5 lan2 bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 sin5-jiah e5 si5, I si7 iu5-goan5 si5-siong5 teh choe3 kang.  Sin5-jiah put-ko3 si7 teh hian2-chhut hit e5 un2-bat8 e5 eng5-kng.  Ki5-iN7 e5 su7, put-ko3 si7 teh piau2-beng5 hou7 lan2 chai, peng5-siong5 e5 su7 iu5-goan5 si7 chhut tui3 Siong7-te3 e5 i3-su3.  Sin5-jiah si7 chhin-chhiuN7 sih-na3, ti7 tiap-a2(**tiap8-a2)-ku2 hut-jian5 hian2-hian7 ti7 khong-tiong, lai5 piau2-beng5 u7 chin toa7 e5 tian7-lat8 put-si5 teh un7-heng5 ti7 chit e5 u2-tiu7 tiong chit8-iuN7.
Chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni, Ia5-sou u7 eng7 sin5-jiah lai5 hian2-chhut I e5 eng5-kng, tu2-tu2 si7 chiau3 cheng3 hak8-seng ti7 au7-lai5 sou2 hoe5-siong2 e5 khoan2-sit.  Sui-jian5 sin5-jiah u7 hian2-chhut I e5 eng5-kng, iau2-ku2 lan2 boh8-tit phah-sng3, I teh kiaN5 sin5-jiah e5 choe3 toa7 e5 bok8-tek, si7 kan-ta beh hian2-chhut I e5 eng5-kng na7-tiaN7.  Ki5-sit8 I si7 long2 bo5 teh iau3-kin2 ai3 beh hian2-chhut I e5 Sin5-seng3.  I hoan2-tng2 si7 put-chi2 sio2-sim, m7-ai3 lam7-sam2 kiaN5 sin5-jiah.  I m7-si7 ui7-tioh8 ai3 beh kiong5-pek lang5 e5 sin3-giong2, chiah lai5 kiaN5 sin5-jiah.  Put-ko3 I si7 Siong7-te3, I oe7 khoaN3, na7-si7 hap8-gi5 e5 si5, I si7 hoaN-hi2 hian2-chhut I sin5-seng3 e5 khui3-lat8 lai5 kiaN5 sin5-jiah, thang ka3-si7 I e5 hak8-seng; iu7-koh tek8-piat8 thang hou7 cheng3-lang5 tit-tioh8 sim-sin5 e5 ui3-an kap khoai3-lok8.  Siat-su2 u7 kui toa7-tin7 lang5 hoa7-hoa7 kun2, lai5 kiu5 I tui3 thiN-nih8 lai5 e5 sin5-jiah, hit-si5 I chiu7 chek-pi7 in.  “Ok-tok8 kan-im5 e5 se3-tai7 kiu5 sin5-jiah; tu5 sian-ti Iok-na2 e5 sin5-jiah i2-goa7, bo5 beh sin5-jiah hou7 in.”  Siat-su2 I u7 tu2-tioh8 Mou5-kui2 e5 chhi3, kio3 I tioh8 ui7-tioh8 ka-ki7 lai5 kiaN5 sin5-jiah, thang hou7 chioh8-thau5 pian3 choe3 piaN2, hit-si5 I chiu7 toan3-jian5 ku7-choat8, bo5 beh kiaN5 sim2-mih8.  Chong2-si7 siat-su2 u7 chit8 e5 siau3-lian5 e5 sin-niu5, kiaN-liau2 oe7 ti7 chhu3-piN, peng5-iu2 e5 bin7-cheng5 tu2-tioh8 kian3-siau3;  u7 Na2-in e5 koaN2-hu7 sit-loh8 i kou-siN e5 kiaN2; u7 Ka-pek-long5 e5 soe3-soe3 han3 e5 cha-bou2 gin2-na2 tu2-tioh8 jiat8-piN7, a2-si7 u7 khit-chiah8 ti7 lou7-piN teh chhiN-chham2 au5-kio3, hit-si5 Ia5-sou chiu7 long2 bo5 ian5-chhian5, chek-si5 lai5 ui7-tioh8 in kiaN5 koh(**kok)-iuN7 e5 sin5-jiah.
Lan2 tioh8 oe7 ki3-tit, sui-jian5 Ia5-sou bo5 ui7-tioh8 beh hian2-chhut I e5 eng5-kng, liah8 che choe3 toa7 e5 bok8-tek, chiah lai5 kiaN5 sin5-jiah, iau2-ku2 tui3 I sou2 kiaN5 e5 sin5-jiah chu7-jian5 u7 hian2-chhut I e5 eng5-kng.  “Choe3 si e5 lang5 m7-si7 in-ui7 ai3 hian2-chhut pun2-sin si7 choe3 si e5 lang5, chiah lai5 choe3 si.  Khong2-khai3 e5 lang5 m7-si7 in-ui7 ai3 hian2-chhut pun2-sin si7 khong2-khai3 e5 lang5, chiah lai5 kiaN5 ho2 su7, si-che3 hou7 song3-hiong lang5.  Iau2-ku2 tui3 i e5 sou2 choe3, u7 thang hian2-chhut i e5 choe3 lang5 e5 khoan2.”  Ia5-sou m7-si7 in-ui7 beh hian2-chhut pun2-sin si7 Siong7-te3, chiah lai5 kiaN5 sin5-jiah.  Iau2-ku2 chai7 hiah e5 seng5-sit8 sim u7 kau3-giah8 khui3-lat8 thang li2-kai2 I e5 lang5, sin5-jiah si7 u7 kau3-giah8 thang hian2-chhut I si7 siong7-te3.
Chong2 lai5 kong2, lang5 na7-si7 liah8 sin5-jiah choe3 si7 Siong7-te3 e5 choe3-ho2 e5 khe2-si7, si7 kek8-ki5 bo5 thang o-lo2e su7.  Lang5 na7-si7 liah8 I e5 koan5-leng5 choe3 si7 Siong7-te3 chi3-toa7 e5 eng5-kng, si7 se3-siok8, chhian2-poh8 e5 su-siuN2.  Mou5-se u7 tui3 Siong7-te3 au5-kio3 kong2, “Kiu5 li2 hian2-beng5 li2 e5 eng5-kng,” hit-si5 i u7 thiaN-kiN3 siaN, tui3 i kong2, “Goa2 tek-khak hian2-beng5 goa2 e5 thiaN3-thang3.”  Ki5-sit8 Siong7-te3 chi3-toa7 e5 eng5-kng m7-si7 I e5 koan5-leng5, hoan2-tng2 si7 I e5 jin5-ai3, I e5 tong5-cheng5, I e5 khoan-tai7, I e5 bu5 han7-liong7 e5 jin5-chu5.  Hit ho7 ai3 chin2-kiu3 hit e5 khun3-khou2 e5 ka-teng5, thoat-chhut ti7 hit e5 ian5-siah8 sou2 tu2-tioh8 e5 khun2-pek e5 chhiong-tong7, si7 pi2 kiaN5 sin5-jiah lai5 hou7 chioh8-thau5 piN3-chiaN5 piaN2, cham2-jian5 khah ko-siong7, thang khe2-si7 Siong7-te3 e5 sim.
Chiau3 lan2 sou2 u7 thak8-tioh8 e5, kong2, “Ia5-sou kap I e5 hak8-seng u7 hou7 in chhiaN2 khi3 hu3 hun-in e5 ian5-siah8,”  lan2 kiam2 bo5 chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni, it-hoat ai3 chhiaN2 I lai5 hu3 lan2 e5 hap8-hun-sek; lan2 e5 siau3-lian5 lang5, kiam2 bo5 beh ui7-tioh8 chit e5 chong3-giam5 e5 le2-sek lai5 kin2-sin7 pi7-pan7 sim, chhin-chhiuN7 pi7-pan7 beh hu3 Seng3-chhan e5 khoan2 mah?  Ti7 Ka-na2 chit-tui3 siau3-lian5 e5 hu-hu7, ui7-tioh8 in e5 hap8-hun, an3-choaN2 lai5 pi7-pan7 in e5 sim, lan2 khiok si7 bo5 sim2-mih8 chai-iaN2.  Chong2-si7 lan2 chai-iaN2 in e5 kau3-hoe7 sou2 hoan-hu3 e5 kui-ku2.  Ti7 Chu2 Ia5-sou e5 si5-tai7, Iu5-thai3 lang5 e5 hun-in m7-si7 khoaN3-choe3 ian3-lok8, hoaN-hi2 e5 ho2 jit8-chi2 e5 i3-su3 na7-tiaN7.  Hap8-hun si7 khoaN3-choe3 chin chong3-giam5 e5 su7.  Siau3-lian5 lang5 tioh8 ai3 seng thiaN si7-toa7 (kau3-hoe7) e5 khou2-khng3, seng pi7-pan7 sim, kim3-chiah8 ki5-to2, soa3 hoan2-hoe2 in e5 choe7.  Chiong kun7 hap8-hun e5 si5, in e5 sim-su tioh8 ai3 put-si5 sam3-su Siong7-te3 e5 chi2-i3.  In e5 kou2-cha2 liap8-pi2 u7 chit8 ku3 siok8-gu2 teh kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa pun2-sin u7 phang5 poe chiok-hok lan2 e5 si2-chou2 e5 hun-in, ia7 Bi2-ka-lek8 kap Ka-pek-liat8 si7 choe3 kiaN2-sai3 phoaN7, koh u7 cheng3 thiN-sai3 che7-siaN lai5 gim5-si chiok-ho7 sin-niu5 e5 heng7-hok.
Lan2 e5 kau3-hoe7 tui3 ti7 hun-in e5 le2-sek, iau2 u7 koh-khah ko-siong7 e5 i3-su3 ti7-teh.  Ia5-sou u7 chhut-sek8 Ka-li7-li7 e5 Ka-na2 e5 hun-in, ti7-hia lai5 kiaN5 thau5 chit8-pai2 e5 sin5-jiah, tui3 an2-ni lai5 piau2-si7 I u7 chun-tiong7 hun-in, bi2-hoa3 hun-in e5 le2-sek.  Kau3-hoe7 u7 chu2-tiuN kong2, hun-in si7 sin5-seng3, lang5 tioh8 sin7-tiong7, si7 piau2-beng5 Ki-tok kap I e5 kau3-hoe7 e5 sin5-pi3-tek e5 hap8-it e5 i3-su3.  Sou2-i2 lan2 koat-toan3 m7-thang khin-khoai3, lo2-chho2 lai5 kiaN5 hun-in e5 le2-sek, hoan2-tng2 si7 tioh8 eng7 keng3-ui3, giam5-siok, kin2-sin7, kiaN-ui3 Siong7-te3 e5 sim lai5 chin3-heng5 chiah tioh8.  Si7 lah!  Khak-sit8 hun-in tek-khak si7 boh8-tit chhin3-chhai2.  Siong7-te3 u7 kiat-hap8 in nng7 lang5 e5 sim-koaN, hu7-jin5-lang5 e5 siN3-mia7 kau-tai7 i e5 tiong7-hu, iah8 tiong7-hu e5 siN3-mia7 kau-tai7 i e5 hu7-jin5-lang5; si7 ho2 m7 si7 phaiN2; si7 ho2-giah8, si7 song3-hiong; si7 tioh8 kau3 si2 chiah thang pang3-li7.  Khak-sit8 che si7 jin5-seng chong3-giam5 e5 sun3-kan, khak-sit8 si7 be7 eng7-tit iong5-un2 khin-khoai3 a2-si7 kun2-chhio3 e5 khoan2-sit, si7 tioh8 it-hoat u7 giam5-siok, u7 hoaN-hi2, u7 siu7 kam2-tong7 e5 sim, lai5 beng5-pek8 lan2 e5 Pe7 u7 chaiN2-iuN7 koan-sim ti7 I cheng3 kiaN2-ji5 e5 heng7-hok, soa3 u7 chaiN2-iuN7 ai3 ka7 in chiok-hok, ti7 in e5 it-seng thang tit-tioh8 I e5 un-tian2.
Hun-in u7 chin-choe7 khoan2.
U7 choe7-choe7 lang5 hap8-hun liau2, ti7 bo5 kui2-ni5 e5 tiong-kan, chiu7 piN3-choe3 bo5-bi7 bo5-sou3, bo5 khoai3-lok8 e5 seng-oah8, iah8 u7 choe7-choe7 lang5 hap8-hun liau2, in nng7 lang5 si7 it-seng chin gau5 saN-thiaN3 kau3 lou7-be2.  Hit e5 cheng-chha put-chai7 in e5 hap8-hun si7 u7 sit8-chai7 e5 thiaN3, a2-si7 bo5 thiaN3 e5 bun7-toe5, si7 koan-he7 u7 Siong7-te3 tiam3 ti7 hit e5 hun-in, a2-si7 bo5 e5 bun7-toe5.  Hun-in sui-jian5 u7 sit8-chai7 e5 thiaN3 ti7-teh, iau2-ku2 na7-si7 bo5 u7 Siong7-te3 ti7-teh, iah8 si7 bo5 tho3-tong3.  Lan2 tai7-ke tioh8 put-si5 khou2-khng3 chheng-lian5 lang5 ti7 boe7 hap8-hun e5 i2-cheng5, ai3 u7 siong5-siong5 ki5-to2, u7 chap8-hun e5 sam3-su, i2-kip8 chong3-giam5 e5 koat-sim chiah ho2.  Na7-si7 u7 an2-ni, khak-sit8 hit e5 hap8-hun un2-tang3 si7 oe7 chiaN5-choe3 u7 heng7-hok e5 seng-oah8.  Siat-su2 lan2 na7-si7 u7 chhiaN2 Ia5-sou lai5 hu3 lan2 e5 hun-in, chhin-chhiuN7 cha2-si5 I u7 khi3 hu3 Ka-na2 e5 hun-in chit8 poaN, chiu7 lan2 e5 hun-in e5 jit8, tek-khak bo5 sit-loh8 hit e5 kong-eng5 chiah tioh8.

Te7-5 chiuN	Ki-Tok e5 Gi7-Hun2(**Hun3)

	Ia5-sou khi3 hu3 Ka-na2 e5 hun-in liau2, u7 khi2-sin beh chiuN7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 hu3 PoaN5-ke3-choeh.  Hit e5 lou7 si7 ian5 Ka-li7-li7 chhiN-chhui3 e5 ou5-hoaN7, u7 tui3 chit8 e5 sui2 e5 chhau2-tiuN5 i2-kip8 chit8 e5 sui2 e5 hoe-hng5, kio3-choe3 Ong5-kiong e5 Hoe-hng5 keng-ke3.  I tai7-seng si7 loh8-khi3 Ka-pek-long5, in-ui7 I e5 hak8-seng u7-e5 si7 khia7-khi2 ti7 hit e5 ou5-piN, ia7-si7 in-ui7 ai3 kap pat8-lang5 choe3-tin7 saN-kap chiuN7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 hu3 choeh.  Lan2 u7 thak8-tioh8 kong2, I kap I e5 lau7-bu2 kap hiaN-ti7, i2-kip8 I e5 hak8-seng loh8-khi3 Ka-pek-long5.  In tiam3 hia bo5 kui2-jit8, iah8 bo5 tu2-tioh8 sim2-mih8 tiong7-iau3 e5 su7.  Lan2 si7 ai3 hut-liok8 chit hoan e5 hong2-bun7, put-ko3 ti7 be7 kong2-khi2 pat8-hang7 su7 e5 tai7-seng, chi2-u7 ai3 lan2 oe7 ki3-tit Ka-pek-long5 e5 sou2-chai7.  In-ui7 Ia5-sou e5 lai5-lek8 si7 put-chi2 u7 koan-lian5 ti7 chit e5 sui2-sui2 e5 ou5-piN e5 Ka-pek-long5 e5 siaN5.  Ti7 au7-lai5 Ka-pek-long5 si7 chiaN5-choe3 Ia5-sou e5 te7-ji7 “kou3-hiong”, si7 I ti7 Ka-li7-li7 thoan5-kau3 e5 tiong-sim tiam2, si7 ti7 cheng3 Hok-im-su tiong, lan2 sou2 te7-it chhim-chai e5 choe7-choe7 e5 kou3-su7 e5 poe3(**poe7)-keng2.
	Iu5-thai3 lang5 e5 PoaN5-ke3-choeh kun7 lah.  Ia5-sou u7 tui3 hia lai5 chiuN7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 hu3 choeh, chiau3-khoaN3 I choe3 gin2-na2 e5 si5, hu3 thau5 chit8-pai2 liau2-au7, toa7-bin7 u7 tak8 ni5 khi2-khi3 hu3 choeh e5 khoan2.
	Put-ko3 Ia5-sou chit-pai2 chiuN7 khi3 hu3-choeh, cham2-jian5 u7 cheng-chha e5 sou2-chai7 ti7-teh.  I chit-pang si7 bo5 koh choe3 chit8 e5 ko3-jin5 e5 chham-pai3-chia2, si7 choe3 chit8 e5 kok-bin5 e5 kai2-kek-chia2 lai5 hu3 choeh, sui5-si7(**sui-jian5) I boe7 hian2-jian5 lai5 hian2-chhut pun2-sin si7 Bi2-sai3-a, iau2-ku2 chit hoan I u7 chiuN7 khi3 I e5 Pe7 e5 chhu3, ai3 lai5 heng-khi2 I thoan5-kau3 e5 kang, ti7 chit e5 kok-bin5 e5 kiaN-siaN5.  Tak8 kok e5 kiaN-siaN5 si7 choe3 bin5-chiong3 su-siuN2 e5 tiong-sim.  Kiam2-chhai2 in-ui7 chit e5 in-toaN, I chiah him-bou7 ai3 ti7 I e5 peh-siN3 e5 si7-toa7, i2-kip8 tui3 thong thiN-e7 lai5 chu7-chip8 e5 hoe7-chiong3 e5 bin7-cheng5, lai5 hian2-jian5 chhut-hoat I e5 su2-beng7.
	Chin kho2-sioh, Iu5-thai3 lang5 m7 chai-iaN2 chit e5 si7 ti7 in e5 lek8-su2 tiong e5 chit8 e5 choan2-ki, tu2-tu2 si7 eng3-giam7 Sian-ti Ma2-liap8-ki sou2 ki3-chai3 e5 kong2, “Goa2 chhe chhe-sai3, pi7-pan7 lou7 ti7 Goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5; lin2 sou2 kiu5, sou2 hoaN-hi2 e5 Siong7-te3, chiu3-choa7 lip8-iok e5 thiN-sai3, ko2-jian5 beh kau3, soa3 jip8 tian7-tng5.”
	Ah!  Chit e5 thau5 chit8-pai2 e5 PoaN5-ke3-choeh, in bo5 hoaN-hi2 chiap-lap8 I.  Te7-ji7 pai2 e5 PoaN5-ke3-choeh, in khoan2-thai7 I siaN2-khoan2, lan2 khiok-si7 long2 m7 chai-iaN2.  Put-ko3 te7-saN pai2 e5 PoaN5-ke3-choeh, in u7 teng3 I ti7 Sip8-ji7-ke3.

Hit e5 su7-sit8 lan2 long2 bo5 thang giau5-gi5 siaN2-khoan2, si7 chha-put-to i2-keng tiaN7-tioh8 e5 kiat-lun7.  Bin5-chu2 chu2-gi7 si7 iau2-be7 chhut-si3.  Peh-siN3 to long2 bo5 koan5.  Koan5-peng3 kap tek8-koan5 ma7 long2 si7 kui ti7 chong-kau3-kai3 e5 kui2-chok8, chiu7-si7 keng-hak8-su7 i2-kip8 Hoat-li7-sai3 lang5 e5 chhiu2; in put-chi2 goan2-kou3, ka-ki7 boan2-chiok in e5 chong-kau3 sin3-liam7, ma7-si7 iu5-goan5 kui ti7 cheng3-ti7 kai3 e5 kui3-chok8, chiu7-si7 Hi-lut8 tong2 e5 chhiu2; in su7-su7 ai3 hou7 Hi-lut8 ong5 hoaN-hi2, koh-chai3 Hi-lut8 e5 pun2-hun7, choe3 Lo5-ma2 Hong5-te3 sou2 thiaN3 e5 chit8-e5, chu7-jian5 si7 ai3 peh-siN3 hoan7-su7 than3 cheng3-hu2 e5 i3-su3 nou3!
	Tu2-tu2 si7 chhin-chhiuN7 ti7 tak8 si5-tai7 hiah e5 u7 tek8-koan5 kai-kip e5 lang5 e5 khoan2, Iu5-thai3 lang5 e5 si7-toa7 tiaN7-tioh8 su7-su7 ai3 chiau3 ku7 e5 khoan2-sit.  TaN chit e5 Kai2-kek-chia2, Jiat8-sim-ka, chong-kau3 Kek-beng7-ka Ia5-sou u7 hian2-hian7 ti7 hit e5 chian3-tiuN5, I e5 i3-su3 koat-toan3 si7 m7-ai3 chiau3 ku7 e5 khoan2-sit.  I si7 gau5 tong5-cheng5 peh-siN3.  I ti7 sim-lai7 si7 chin bo5 hoaN-hi2 chiah e5 u7 tek8-koan5 kai-kip e5 lang5, khoaN3-kiN3 in e5 chan5-jim2, chu7-ki2 chheng-gi7, i2-kip8 bu2-jiok8 hiah e5 loan2-jiok8 bu5-nai7 e5 lang5, sim toa7 m7 hoaN-hi2.  I iam3-ouN3 in e5 chong-kau3, khoaN3 si7 khang-khang, heng5-sek, bo5 sim2-mih8 bat Siong7-te3.  I long2 bo5 chit8-sut-a2 lun2-neh, kong-jian5 lai5 piau2-si7 pun2-sin e5 i3-kian3 ti7 in e5 bin7-cheng5.  Sou2-i2 chu7-jian5 si7 boe7 bian2-tit siN-khi2 saN chhiong-tut8 e5 su7.
	Ia5-sou ti7 chit-pang hong2-bun7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, kan-ta u7 tu2-tioh8 nng7-chan5 khah tu3-hian7 e5 su7-kiaN7, chiu7-si7 chheng-khi3 Seng3-tian7, i2-kip8 bian7-hoe7 Ni5-ko-ti2-bou2 e5 su7.
	Seng3-tian7 chai7 tak8 e5 Iu5-thai3 lang5 teh khoaN3, si7 chit8 e5 sin5-seng3 e5 ki3-ho7.  I2-sek-liat8 lang5 siu7-liah8 si3-soaN3 ti7 thong thiN-e7 tak8 sou2-chai7, iau2-ku2 tui3 ti7 tak8 sou2-chai7 in ma7-si7 long2 iau2 oat8-thau5 lai5 khoaN3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 Seng3-tian7, khoaN3-choe3 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 Tian7-tng5, cheng3 kok-bin5 e5 keng3-pai3 hok8-sai7 e5 tiong-sim.  Chai7 Ia5-sou teh khoaN3, Seng3-tian7 si7 u7 heng5 e5 ki3-ho7, teh piau2-beng5 Siong7-te3 u7 tiam3 ti7 in tiong-kan.  I ti7 chap8-ji7 he3 choe3 gin2-na2 e5 si5, u7 kong2, “kiam2 m7-chai goa2 eng-kai ti7 goa2 e5 Pe7 e5 chhu3 mah?”  I ti7 sim-lai7 si7 chin i3-ai3 Siong7-te3 e5 chhu3.  I si7 put-chi2 kin2-sin7 ai3 po2-hou7 hit e5 beng5-u7.  Ni5 ke3 ni5, I e5 sim na2 hun3-khai3, in-ui7 khoaN3-kiN3 Seng3-tian7 tit8-tit8 teh siok8-hoa3, iah8 sim-lai7 chin tong5-cheng5 cheng3 keng3-khian5 e5 chham-pai3-chia2 e5 phoe-pheng5, ngiauh8-ngiauh8-liam7 e5 siaN.  Toa7-bin7 I na2 teh kiaN5 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 si5, si7 i2-keng u7 khng3 chit ho7 tong5-cheng5 e5 sim ti7-teh.
	Che3-si e5 tham-chai5, ti3-kau3 Seng3-tian7 soa3 piN3-choe3 than3-chiN5 e5 sou2-chai7, chit e5 sui2-sui2 chong3-koan e5 goa7-iN7, si7 piN3-chiaN5 boe2-boe7 cheng-siN e5 lau7-jiat8 chhi7, it-chhe3 bo5 m7 chiaN5-choe3 che3-si-thau5 “A-na2 e5 cheng3 kiaN2-sun e5 chhi7-tiuN5 (Bazaar).”  Chhi7-tiuN5-nih8 u7 thiaN-kiN3 lang5 teh soan-jiong2, teh oaN7 chiN5 e5 siaN kau3 chhiang7-chhiang7 kun2, iuN5-a2 si7 teh meh8-meh8 kio3, gu5-a2 kiaN2 si7 teh oaiN2-oaiN2 kio3, hit e5 jiat8-nau7 si7 put-chi2 kiau2-jiau2-tioh8 hiah e5 ti7 lai7-bin7 keng3-khian5 teh le2-pai3 ki5-to2 e5 chham-pai3-chia2 e5 sim-sin5.  Seng3-tian7 si7 piN3-choe3 chit8 cheng2 siu7-iu7 e5 chou-chit, tui3 chit e5 bo5 seng5-sit8 e5 hoat-tou7, Seng3-tian7 u7 tit-tioh8 toa7 e5 chai5-lek8, siu-jip8 si7 put-chi2 choe7 nou3.
	Ki5-sit8 tak8 pai2 na7 u7 siat sim2-mih8 hoat-tou7 ai3 beh kong3-hian3 kong-chiong3 e5 li7-pian7, iu7-koh ti7 hit e5 poe3(**poe7)-au7 u7 kim-chiN5 e5 koan-he7 ti7-teh e5 si5, chiau3 lan2 sou2 chai, si7 khoai3-khoai3 siN-chhut chiong2-chiong2 e5 hu2-pai7 e5 kiat-ko2.  Bian2 kong2, siat-hoat boe7 cheng-siN e5 chhi7-tiuN5, i2-kip8 siat-hoat thang ti7 Seng3-tian7 lai5 hou7 lang5 oaN7 chiN5 si7 iau3-kin2, koh hou7 lang5 u7 chin li7-pian7.  Chong2-si7 sou2 thang hiam5 e5, chiu7-si7 choe7-choe7 tan-sun5 e5 hiong-chhoan lang5, tioh8 tiam3 ti7 Pe7 Siong7-te3 e5 chhu3, lai5 siu7 hit ho7 e5 khi-phian3; chham-pai3-chia2 e5 jiat8-seng5, tioh8 siu7 hit ho7 put hap8-sek e5 seng-li2 sou2 kiau2-jiau2.  Seng3-tian7 u7 tui3 hit ho7 boe7 cheng-siN e5, i2-kip8 oaN7 chiN5 e5, bo5 seng5-sit8 e5 seng-li2-hoat, lai5 tit-tioh8 toa7 e5 siu-jip8.  Cheng3 peh-siN3 long2 chin kian3-siau3 chit e5 su7-cheng5.  Lan2 chai-iaN2, Tian7-tng5 siat chhi7-tiuN5 si7 te7-it hou7 lang5 bo5 hoaN-hi2.  Chong2-si7 su7-sit8 Iu5-thai3 e5 choan5 bin5-chok8, ti7 hiah ku2 e5 tiong-kan, long2 koaiN3-si3 an2-ni, che si7 thang chai in sit8-chai7 si7 i2-keng sit-loh8 keng3-ui3 kap khian5-seng5 e5 sim lah.

	Iok-han7 ti7 i e5 sim-lai7, u7 siuN7-tioh8 ti7 PoaN5-ke3-choeh hit le2-pai3 tiong e5 chit8 jit8 sou2 tu2-tioh8 e5 su7.  Hit-si5 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, lang5 that-that tiN7, chap8-hoe gou7-sek e5 lang5, u7 chu7-chip8 ti7 Seng3-siaN5, sit8-chai7 si7 put-chi2 lau7-jiat8.  Seng3-tian7 e5 chiu-ui5 si7 u7 kui toa7-tin7 e5 chham-pai3-chia2 ti7-teh; in sui5-lang5 u7 chheng7 sui5-lang5 e5 hok8-chong, oan2-jian5 chhin-chhiuN7 hong-siok8 tian2-lam2, in-ui7 hit-si5 lai5 teh hu3 choeh e5 lang5, m7-si7 kan-ta Pa-lek8-su-theng3 ji5-i2, si7 si3-soaN3 ti7 thong thiN-e7 tak8 kok keng3-khian5 e5 Iu5-thai3 lang5, long2 u7 tng2-lai5 hu3 choeh.  I2-sek-liat8 bin5-chok8 tiong, hiah e5 te7-it keng3-khian5 e5, u7 tui3 tak8 sou2-chai7 to3-tng2-lai5 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 chu7-chip8 ti7 Seng3-tian7 lai5 hok8-sai7 Siong7-te3.  Khak-sit8 hit e5 kong-keng2 si7 u7 toa7 kam2-tong7 Ia5-sou e5 sim.
	Si5 ke3 si5, Seng3-tian7 e5 lang5 si7 u7-si5 moa2, u7-si5 khang.  Sin lai5 e5 chham-pai3-chia2, chin3-cheng5 oa2-lai5 mng5-khau2 lun5-liu5 teh theng3-hau7.  Goa7-bin7 u7 chit8 e5 IN7-pang  lang5 sui2-sui2 e5 goa7-iN7, ti7-hia u7 chong3-koan e5 leng2-long5, i2-kip8 eng7 kha2-biau7 e5 ki-kang sou2 tiau-khek e5 thiau7 ti7-teh, ia7 ti7-hia u7 kui toa7-tin7 e5 lang5 teh theng3-hau7 in e5 un5, thang jip8-khi3 chham-pai3.  chong2-si7 ti7 goa7-bin7 u7 choe7-choe7 cheng-siN hau2 kah meh8-meh8 kio3, oaiN2-oaiN2 kio3, u7 oaN7 chiN5 e5, siu chiN5 e5, teh io5 e5 chiN5 siaN, i2-kip8 hiah e5 boe2-boe7 e5 lang5 put hap8-sek e5 soan-jiong2, u7 put-chi2 hiang2 kau3 ti7 Seng3-sou2 e5 lai7-bin7.
	Choe7-choe7 lang5 long2 liah8 che choe3 si7 chu7-jian5 e5 su7.  Sou2-i2 chit-tiap8 in long2 koaiN3-si3 lah.  Khiok ia7 u7 choe7-choe7 lang5 chhin-chhiuN7 ti7 cha2-si5 e5 khoan2, ti7 chit-tiap8 ma7-si7 put-chi2 teh ngiauh8-ngiauh8-liam7.  U7 hit ho7 tui3 hng7-hng7 e5 sou2-chai7 lai5 hu3 choeh e5 lau7-toa7 lang5 u7 an2-ni kong2, “Goan2 e5 si5-chun7 m7-si7 an2-ni nou3.”  Put-ko3 cheng3-lang5 si7 long2 kiaN che3-si e5 koan5-se3, chi2-u7 ti7 sim-lai7 nghiauh8-ngiauh8-liam7 ji5-i2. to m7-kaN2 hian2-jian5 lai5 kong2-khi2.
	Hut-jian5 ti7 mng5-khau2 u7 hoat-seng chin nau7-tong7 e5 siaN, ia7 tak8-lang5 long2 teh chu3-bak8 khoaN3 hit e5 tui3 Ka-li7-li7 lai5 e5 siau3-lian5 e5 Sian-ti.  In-ui7 cheng3-lang5 to i2-keng long2 bat teh kong2-khi2 I e5 su7.  Tui3 Ka-li7-li7 chiuN7 lai5 hu3-choeh e5 lang5, ma7-si7 u7 teh khui-khoah I mia5-siaN.  U7 choe7-choe7 lang5 long2 u7 teh kong2-khi2 hit e5 chhut-mia5 e5 KiaN5 soe2-le2 e5 Iok-han7 u7 chaiN2-iuN7 lai5 kan-cheng3 I.  Cheng3-lang5 ma7-si7 long2 u7 teh kong2-khi2 I ti7 siaN5-nih8 sou2 kiaN5 e5 sin5-jiah.  Tui3 an2-ni, cheng3-lang5 long2 u7 siN-khi2 ki5-koai3 i2-kip8 tham3-kiu5 e5 sim, ai3 khoaN3 Ia5-sou.
	Chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni, Ia5-sou u7 jip8 khi3 Seng3-tian7.  Chit-tiap8 I m7-si7 chiau3 lan2 sou2 teh siuN7 si7 chit8 e5 un-jiu5 khiam-sun3 e5 Ki-tok, ma7 m7-si7 chhin-chhiuN7 ti7 Ka-na2 e5 hun-in hit e5 ho2 kau-poe5 e5 Ia5-sou lah.  Chit-tiap8 I si7 cham2-jian5 koh-iuN7, si7 chiaN5-choe3 chit8 e5 u7 ui-giam5, u7 koan5-peng3 e5 lang5; I e5 bin7-mau7 u7 hian2-chhut u7 koan5-ui-chia2 e5 siu7-khi3, tui3 hit e5 goa7-tiaN5, toa7 hoah8 chiu7 tit8-tit8 jip8--lai5, chhin-chhiuN7 kun-ong5 teh jip8-lai5 beh chek-hoat8 hiah e5 choe3 chho3-gou7 e5 lou5-pok8 chit8 poaN.  I hian2-chhut kek8 siu7-khi3 e5 bin7, lai5 ng3 hiah e5 Seng3-tian7 e5 koan2-li2-chia2, iah8 ti7 tiap-a2(**tiap8-a2)-ku2 e5 tiong-kan cheng7-cheng7, au7-lai5 chiu7 hut-jian5 hoat-chhut hit e5 hiang2-liang7 e5 siaN-im lai5 chek-pi7 in kong2, “Toa3 chiah e5 mih8 chhut-khi3; m7-thang eng7 goa2 e5 Pe7 e5 chhu3, choe3 boe2-boe7 e5 chhu3!”
	Bo5 thang ki5-koai3, I u7 toa7-toa7 phah-chhiN-kiaN in e5 sim.  Cheng3-lang5 e5 bak8-chiu long2 tian2 kah toa7-bu2-lui2, teh ki5-koai3, teh chhiN-kiaN, in-ui7 thiaN kong2, “Goa2 e5 Pe7 e5 chhu3!”  In long2 chin ki5-koai3 teh siuN7, I kong2 chit ho7 oe7, tau3-ti2 I si7 chi7-chui7?  I kaN2 tui3 Seng3-tian7 e5 chi2-to7-chia2, ho2-taN2 lai5 hian2-chhut chit ho7 koan5-ui-chia2 e5 thai3-tou7, I tau3-ti2 si7 chi7-chui7?  I chit8-e7 khoaN3, si7 chin kiau-ngou7, chin chu7-ko e5 lang5, oan2-jian5 chhin-chhiuN7 Ku7-iok e5 sian-ti lang5 e5 chit8-e5, in-ui7 I u7 eng7 soh choe3 piN, koaN2 hiah e5 cheng-siN long2 chhut tian7 e5 mng5-goa7; koh ia7 chhia-to2 oaN7 chiN5 e5 lang5 e5 chiN5, peng3 lin3-tng2 ine5 toh.  Hiah e5 u7 se3-lek8 e5 lang5, khoaN3-liau2 khak-sit8 si7 put-chi2 chhiN-kiaN, ti3-kau3 chhin-chhiuN7 e2-kau2--e5 chit8 poaN, tai7-ke toa7 chhui3 khui-khui, m7-kaN2 chin3-cheng5 lai5 ti2-khong3 I.  Lan2 thang siong2-siong7, hit-si5 keng-hak8-su7 a2-si7 Hoat-li7-sai3 lang5 un2-tang3 u7 kiaN5 oa2 khi3 tui3 I kan-cheng3 kong2, “Seng3-chheh to u7 ki3-chai3 kong2, lan2 tioh8 chiau3 an2-ni lai5 keng3-pai3 hok8-sai7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, koh u7 ki3-chai3 kong2, lan2 tioh8 chiau3 an2-ni lai5 hian3 seng-le2 ti7 I e5 toaN5 le3(**leh).”  Chong2-si7 Ia5-sou si7 toa7 siu7-khi3 in, I e5 siaN si7 chhin-chhiuN7 lui5 teh tan5, chiu7 in3 in kong2, “Goa2 e5 chhu3 beh chheng-choe3 ki5-to2 e5 chhu3; chong2-si7 lin2 hou7 i choe3 chhat8-siu7!”

	Ti7 hit jit8 Ia5-sou u7 tek-choe7-tioh8 kau3-hoe7 e5 thau5-lang5, kau3 chha-put-to be7 thang koh saN-ho5.  Hoat-li7-sai3 lang5 e5 koan5-se3, ti7 cheng3-lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5 u7 siu7-tioh8 I e5 bu2-jiok8.  Cheng3 che3-si e5 than3-chiN5 e5 thau5-lou7 u7 kong-jian5 sit-liau2 the2-bian7.  In koat-toan3 bo5 be7 ki3-tit chit chan5 su7.  Hit jit8 Ia5-sou thang kong2 ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 i2-keng u7 khak-teng7 I e5 un7-mia7.  Koh I ia7 chai-iaN2 chit e5 su7-sit8.
	Koh nng7-ni5 au7, in iu5-goan5 si7 ti7 PoaN5-ke3-choeh e5 si5, tu2-tu2 ti7 siang7 chit e5 sou2-chai7 u7 saN-kap ke3-bou5 lai5 chhiuN2-toat8 I e5 siN3-mia7.  Hit-si5 Iu5-thai3 lang5 tui3 I kiu5 sin5-jiah kong2, “Li2 choe3 chiah e5 tai7-chi3, eng7 sim2-mih8 sin5-jiah hou7 goan2 khoaN3?”  Ia5-sou thiaN-kiN3 in sou2 mng7 chit-ku3 oe7, phah-sng3 I chai in ai3 beh hai7-si2 I.  Sou2-i2 I chiu7 eng7 thiam5-cheng7 e5 thai3-tou7, chiong sin5-jiah lai5 chi2-si7 in kong2, “Lin2 hui2-hoai7 chit e5 tian7 (Goa2 e5 seng-khu e5 Tian7), Goa2 saN-jit8 beh koh khi2 i.”
	Hit-si5 chiau3-khoaN3 si7 bo5 sim2-mih8 lang5 u7 liau2-kai2 I sou2 kong2 chit ku3 oe7.  In tai7-ke chi2-u7 be5-loan7 na7-tiaN7.  Put-ko3 in long2 oe7 ki3-tit chit-ku3 oe7.  Chhin-chhiuN7 I siu7 sim2-phoaN3 e5 si5, I e5 tui3-tek8 ma7-si7 oe7 ki3-tit chit-ku3 oe7, chiu7 kan-cheng3 kong2, “Chit lang5 bat kong2, goa2 oe7 hui2-haoi7 Siong7-te3 e5 tian7, saN-jit8 beh koh khi2 i.”  Iu7-koh I siu7 teng3 ti7 Kok-kok-thaN e5 si5, in ma7-si7 oe7 ki3-tit chit-ku3 oe7, chiu7 siat-tok8 leng2-chhio3 I kong2, “Ai7 ah, li2 hui2-hoai7 tian7, saN-jit8 khi2 i e5, taN tioh8 kiu3 ka-ki7, tui3 Sip8-ji7-ke3 loh8-lai5.”  Lian5 cheng3 hak8-seng to iu5-goan5 siong5-siong5 ki3-tit chit-ku3 oe7, koh ia7 tioh8 kau3 Ia5-sou koh-oah8 liau2-au7, in chiah oe7 liau2-kai2 chit ku3, “ti7 saN-jit8 goa2 beh koh khi2 i” e5 oe7 e5 i3-su3.
	Che si7 Ia5-sou chhut-hoat I e5 kong seng-gai5 e5 khoan2-sit.  I m7-si7 tu2-tu2 eng7 oan2-choan2 ho2 kam2-cheng5 e5 hoat-tou7 lai5 chhut-hoat.  M7-si7!  Tui3 lang5 oan2-choan2 ho2 kam2-cheng5, khiok u7-si5 si7 chin ho2, chong2-si7 u7 si5 kou-put-chiong tioh8 hian2-chhut siu7-khi3 e5 bin7 chiah u7 kau3-giah8.  Hit jit8 bo5 poaN3 lang5 kaN2 mou7-hiam2 chin3-cheng5 lai5 ti2-khong3 I.  Cheng3-lang5 khoaN3-liau2 si7 put-chi2 chhiN-kiaN, put-ko3 u7 toa7-toa7 tong5-cheng5, soa3 ui7 I, ia7 ti7 in e5 sim-lai7 put-chi2 teh hoaN-hi2, u7 khoaN3-kiN3 chit e5 lang5 kaN2 choe3 hit ho7 in sou2 m7-kaN2 choe3 e5 su7.  Hiah e5 choe3 m7-tioh8 e5 lang5, in e5 liong5-sim iu5-goan5 ma7-si7 u7 chan3-seng5 Ia5-sou sou2 choe3 e5 tai7-chi3.  In m7-si7 m7-chai-iaN2 in u7 chho3-gou7 ti7-teh, put-ko3 Ia5-sou u7 chhui-pek in lai5 chim-chiok siuN7 in sou2 choe3 e5 su7.  Ui7-tioh8 ai3 hou7 lang5 hok8-sai7 Siong7-te3 e5 sim-sin5 tit-tioh8 chheng-khi3, bian2 bak-tioh8 la5-sam5, sou2-i2 Ia5-sou chiah u7 hian2-chhut I e5 chong-giam5, tek-seng3 e5 Bi2-sai3-a e5 thang chhiN-kiaN e5 khi3-khai3 lai5 kong-kek in.  Khak-sit8 che si7 “Seng3 IuN5-ko e5 gi7-hun2(**hun3).”  Ti7 hit-si5 Ia5-sou e5 bak8-chiu u7 hian2-chhut put-chi2 thang kiaN-ui3 e5 in3-siong7 ti7-teh.

	Seng3 IuN5-ko e5 gi7-hun2(**hun3)!
	Chit-tiap8 koh tui3 chit hong-bin7 lai5 siuN7 lan2 e5 Chu2 e5 jin5-keh, si7 u7 toa7 li7-ek e5 sou2-chai7 ti7-teh.  An3-choaN2 to u7 chin-choe7 ui2-tai7 e5 oe7-tou5 ka, thai2-oe7 bo5 poaN3-lang5 oe7 hit ho7 hoat siu7-khi3 e5 Ki-tok mah?  Lan2 khah siong5 sou2 khoaN3-kiN3 e5 tou5, long2 si7 oe7 I e5 bin7 si7 un-jiu5, peng5-ho5, ia7 lan2 khah siong5 si7 thoan5-siu7 hit-ho7 gau5 lin5-bin2, khiam-sun3, thiaN3-thang3 e5 Ia5-sou; na7-si7 an2-ni, kiaN-liau2 lan2 sou2 piau2-chhut I e5 siong7 si7 u7 chho3-gou7 ti7-teh, si7 kan-ta I e5 jin5-keh e5 chit8 hong-bin7 na7-tiaN7, iu7-koh kiaN-liau2 bo5 sim2-mih8 oe7 giu2 hit-ho7 u7 lam5-chu2 han3 e5 khi3-khai3 e5 lang5 e5 sim.  In be7 bian2-tit siuN7 kong2, hit ho7 long2 bo5 u7 hoat-chhut oan3-hun7 phaiN2, siu7-khi3 phaiN2 e5 thiaN3-thang3, si7 bo5 kah loa7 nih8 thang kho2-chhu2 e5 su7.  In si7 siuN7 kong2, lang5 ho2-taN2 hian2-chhut gi7-hun2(**hun3) lai5 hou7 lang5 kiaN-hiaN5, che si7 hit ho7 iong2-kam2 e5 lang5 e5 jin5-keh e5 chit8-pou7-hun7.  U7-iaN2, in sou2 siuN7 e5 si7 chin-sit8 e5 oe7.  In-ui7 chit e5 u7 hian2-chhut oan5-choan5 e5 jin5-seng3 e5 Ia5-sou, iu5-goan5 u7 chiap8-chiap8 hoat-chhut siu7-khi3 e5 bin7.
	Lan2 tui3 Ia5-sou lai5 chai-iaN2, siu7-khi3 si7 Sin5-seng3 e5 su7.  Iau2-ku2 lan2 iu5-goan5 si7 tioh8 tui3 Ia5-sou lai5 chai-iaN2, hit ho7 iong2-kam2 e5 jin5-keh-chia2 sou2 hoat-chhut e5 siu7-khi3 si7 sim2-mih8 khoan2.  In-ui7 lan2 e5 siu7-khi3 khah-siong5 si7 chhut tui3 lan2 e5 loan2-jiok8, bo5 iong2-chong3 e5 sim-chi3, si7 chhut tui3 lan2 e5 toan2-khi3, phaiN2 seng3-te7, si7 chhut tui3 lan2 koe3 thau5 loan2-jiok8 boe7-oe7 che3-ap lan2 e5 seng3-cheng5 sou2 ti3--e5.  Lan2 e5 siu7-khi3 khah siong5 si7 chhut tui3 kou3-ki2 e5 sim, ui7-tioh8 siu7 lang5 e5 siong-hai7, ia7 lan2 boe7-oe7 jim2-tit.  Lan2 e5 siu7-khi3 khah-siong5 si7 chin chan5-jim2, chhiN-chham2, long2 boe7-oe7 sia3-bian2 lang5.
	Tui3 an2-ni, lan2 ai3 tiap-a2(**tiap8-a2)-ku2 saN-kap lai5 khoaN3 siu7-khi3 e5 Ki-tok.  I ti7-chia oe7 hiah-nih8 siu7-khi3 hiah e5 tham-chai5, kan-cha3 e5 seng-li2 lang5, si7 in-ui7 in u7 khi-phian3 tan-sun5 e5 peh-siN3 e5 keng3-khian5 e5 sim.  ti7 au7-jit8, I oe7 koh-chai3 hiah-nih8 siu7-khi3 hiah e5 tou7-tng5 oeh8 koh goan5-be5 e5 lang5, bo5 m7-si7 ui7-tioh8 in u7 theh8 in hit e5 chi3 bi5-soe3 e5 An-hioh-jit8 e5 kui-le7 lai5 chou2-tong3 I ti7 An-hioh-jit8 i ho2 piN7-thiaN3 e5 lang5, “sou2-i2 I chiu7 siu7-khi3 si3-koe3 khoaN3 in.”  I ma7-si7 chin siu7-khi3 hiah e5 in2-iu2 chi3 bi5-soe3 e5 chit e5 lai5 ham7-loh8 ti7 choe7-ok e5, kong2, “KiN3-na7 hou7 chiah e5 sin3 Goa2 e5 chi3-bi5-soe3 e5 chit8 e5 siu7 that-gai7, hit lang5 leng7-khou2 u7 toa7 chioh8-bo7 tiau3 i e5 am7-kun2 thiam7 ti7 chhim-ian.”  I u7 put-chi2 siu7-khi3, koh eng7 bo5 lin5-bin2 e5 ki-chhi3 e5 oe7, lai5 lou7-hian7 Keng-hak8-su7 kap Hoat-li7-sai3 e5 chan5-jim2 kap ke2-ho2, kan-cheng3 in long2 si7 teh chou2-chi2 lang5 chhin-kun7 Siong7-te3.  Lan2 na7 khoaN3 Ma2-thai3 te7 23 chiuN, ti7-hia I e5 oe7 sit8-chai7 si7 chin thang chhiN-kiaN.  “Lin2 ke2-ho2 e5 Keng-hak8-su7 kap Hoat-li7-sai3 lang5, u7 chai-e7 ah!  Lin2 si7 ke2-ho2 e5, lin2 si7 pai5-iu, lin2 si7 hun2-peh8 e5 bong7!  Lin2 si7 chhiN-mi5 teh chhoe7-thau5 e5.  Lin2 eng7 tang7 koh oh-tit taN e5 taN3 pak8 he7 ti7 lang5 e5 keng-thau5 teng2, chong2-si7 lin2 m7-kheng2 eng7 chit8 ki chng2-thau5-a2 tin2-tang7 i!  Lin2 pian3-kiaN5 chui2-lou7, liok8-lou7, hou7 chit8 lang5 jip8-kau3; ki3-jian5 jip8, chiu7 hou7 i choe3 te7-gek8 e5 lang5, pi2 lin2 ka-pe7.  Choa5 ah!  Tok8-thang5 e5 lui7 ah!  Lin2 thai3 oe7 to5-siam2 te7-gek8 e5 heng5-hoat8?”
	Che si7 lan2 e5 un-jiu5, khiam-pi e5 Ia5-sou, ti7-tehti7-teh hoat siu7-khi3 e5 si5, sou2 kong2 e5 oe7.  Siat-su2 lan2 na7 ai3 chai-iaN2, hit ho7 sit8-chai7 tioh8 kiaN-hiaN5 e5 siu7-khi3 si7 sim2-mih8 khoan2, siat-su2 lan2 na7 ai3 chai-iaN2, Siong7-te3 tui3 hit ho7 chan5-jim2, ke2-cho3 i2-kip8 ke2-ho2 e5 heng5-ui5 si7 phau7 sim2-mih8 khoan2 e5 i3-kian3, chhiaN2 lan2 lai5 khoaN3 siu7-khi3 e5 Ki-tok e5 thai3-tou7.

Siu7-khi3 si7 Sin5-seng3 e5 su7.  Siat-su2 lan2 na7 si7 chit8 e5 khah ko-siong7 e5 jin5-keh-chia2, lan2 eng-kai si7 tioh8 khah siong5 hoat-siu7-khi3 chiah tioh8, chong2-si7 lan2 e5 siu7-khi3 tioh8 oe7-hiau2 oh8 Ia5-sou Ki-tok e5 siu7-khi3 e5 khoan2-sit.  Lan2 tioh8 chiong I e5 siu7-khi3 lai5 choe3 lan2 e5 bou5-iuN7.
(1) Thau5-chit8 hang7 lan2 tioh8 chai, na7 si7 u7 sim2-mih8 lang5 chho3-gou7 lai5 siong-hai7 tioh8 I pun2-sin e5 si5, I si7 koat-toan3 bo5 siu7-khi3.  Cheng3-lang5 si7 thang chiau3 in e5 i3-su3 lai5 khoan2-thai7 I, ku7-choat8 I, biau2-si7 I, thi2-chhio3 I, ma7 soa3 thang teng3 I ti7 Sip8-ji7-ke3, hou7 I lai5 tu2-tioh8 hit e5 chhi-chham2.  Ti7 Kok-kok-thaN e5 soaN-phiaN5, cheng3-lang5 chit8-siaN chit8 chhui3 to long2 si7 teh leng2-chhio3 I, chong2-si7 I khoaN3 hit ho7 si7 chit8 si5 e5 gu5-gong7 e5 oe7, soa3 tui3 Siong7-te3 kiu5 kong2, “Pe7 ah, sia3-bian2 in, in-ui7 in sou2 choe3 e5, in m7-chai.”
Chong2-si7 na7-si7 u7 sim2-mih8 lang5 kan-cha3, lai5 phah la5-sam5 Siong7-te3 e5 chhu3, u7 sim2-mih8 lang5 ke2-ho2, ti3-kau3 hou7 lang5 iam3-hun7 chong-kau3, u7 sim2-mih8 lang5 ap-pek loan2-jiok8 e5, u7 sim2-mih8 lang5 in2-iu2 siau3-lian5 e5 cha-bou2 gin2-na2 ham7-loh8 ti7 sia5-ok e5 seng-oah8, I chiu7 chek-si5 hoat-chhut chin thang kiaN-hiaN5 e5 bin7 lai5 siu7-khi3, khian3-chek in.
Che chiu7-si7 Ia5-sou e5 thai3-tou7, I long2 bo5 ui7-tioh8 ka-ki7 e5 su7 lai5 siu7-khi3.  Na7-si7 lang5 sian3 I chiaN3-peng5 e5 chhui3-phe2, I ma7 soa3 oat8 to3-peng5 hou7 i.  I u7 hoan-hu3 lan2 tioh8 chiau3 an2-ni lai5 kiaN5.  Siat-su2 na7-si7 lan2 e5 chhui3-phe2 hou7 lang5 sian3-khi3, chiu7 bo5 bun7-toe5.  Chong2-si7 na7-si7 u7 sim2-mih8 loan2-jiok8, bo5 lang5 thang pang-chan7 e5, tu2-tioh8 leng5-jiok8 hou7 lang5 sian3 chhui3-phe2 khi3, che chiu7-si7 choan5-jian5 cheng-chha e5 kou3-su7 lah.
(2) Lan2 iu5-goan5 tioh8 chai, ti7 I e5 siu7-khi3 e5 hoan2-bin7 u7 I e5 thiaN3-thang3 ti7-teh.  Lan2 kiam2 thang siuN7 kong2, ti7 I e5 siu7-khi3 e5 lai7-bin7, si7 bo5 u7 thiaN3-thang3 ti7-teh mah?  m7-si7!  ki5-sit8 I e5 siu7-khi3 long2 si7 chhut tui3 thiaN3-thang3 e5 sim.  In-ui7 I si7 thiaN3-thang3 hiah e5 siu7 ap-pek e5, chiah lai5 oan3-hun7 hiah e5 ai3 ap-pek lang5 e5.  In-ui7 I si7 thiaN3-thang3 hiah e5 tui7-loh8 e5 cha-bou2 gin2-na2, chiah lai5 chiu3-chou2 hiah e5 in2-iu2 in e5 lang5.  In-ui7 I si7 ai3-khoaN3-kiN3 cheng3-lang5 u7 khoai3-lok8 e5 sim thang oa2-lai5 ti7 Pe7 e5 bin7-cheng5, chiah lai5 siu7-khi3, khian3-chek hiah e5 ke2-ho2, pai7-hoai7 chong-kau3 e5 lang5.
(3) Koh chit8 hang7, lan2 tek8-piat8 ai3 chai e5, ia7 thang soa3 choe3 lan2 e5 an-ui3 kap bian2-le7--e5, chiu7-si7 I put-si5 u7 khng3 sia3-bian2 lang5 e5 sim lai5 teh siu7-khi3 lang5.  I si7 put-chi2 siu7-khi3 lang5 khng3 goan5-be5 e5 sim kou3-i3 lai5 kiaN5 phaiN2, ia7 soa3 chin siu7-khi3 lang5 khng3 ke2-ho2, bo5 u7 thiaN3-thang3 e5 sim, kan-ta goan5-kou3 bo5 beh hoan2-hoe2.  Chong2-si7 lang5 na7 u7 hian2-chhut pi-ai e5 bin7-mau7, chiu7 chek-si5 tin2-tang7 I e5 sim lai5 siN-chhut lin5-bin2 kap thiaN3-thang3 e5 liam7-thau5.  Tui3 hiah e5 po7-giok8 i2-kip8 ke2-ho2 e5 lang5, I si7 put-chi2 siu7-khi3, kah na2 lui5 teh tan5 chit8-poaN, lai5 siat phi2-ju7 pai5-thek in.  Tui3 hiah e5 oe7-hiau2 chai choe7, iu-bun7 hoan2-hoe2 sim-lai7 chin ai-siong teh kan-khou2, u7 hian2-chhut ai3 ho2 e5 sim--e5, Ia5-sou chiu7 chek-si5 siat choe7-choe7 e5 phi2-ju7 lai5 bian2-le7 in.  Che si7 Ia5-sou teh hoat siu7-khi3 e5 khoan2-sit.  Lan2 na7-si7 oe7 chiau3 I e5 khoan2-sit, chiu7 thang chiau3 lan2 sou2 ai3 put-koan2 si5 to thang siu7-khi3.


Te7-6 chiuN	Ni5-Ko-Ti2-Bu2

	Lan2 thang siong2-siong7 ti7 hit am3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 siaN5 un2-tang3 u7 toa7 io5-choah, toa7 siu7 kam2-tong7 chiah tioh8.  In-ui7 chit e5 siau3-lian5 e5 sian-siN, u7 ti7 hiah e5 tui3 tak8 sou2-chai7 chu7-chip8 lai5 e5 cheng3 Iu5-thai3 lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5, lai5 pian7-pok, leng5-jiok8 kau3-hoe7 i2-kip8 kok-bin5 e5 thau5-lang5 e5 koan5-se3, soa3 kong-jian5 lai5 kong-kek, kong2 in si7 hou7 kau3-hoe7 piN3-choe3 chit8 cheng2 e5 chhat8-siu7!  Chhi3-siuN7, na7 u7 chhin-chhiuN7 chit khoan2 e5 lang5 lai5 kong-kek lan2 e5 Kam(**Kam3)-tok-hoe7!  A2-si7 ti7 lan2 e5 gi7-hoe7 e5 tiong-kan, u7 chit8 e5 cheng3-lang5 sou2 chun-keng3 e5 seng3-chia2 hian2-chhut chit8 e5 koan5-ui-chia2 e5 siu7-khi3 e5 bin7-mau7, tui3 khau2-bin7 toa7 hoah8 tit8-tit8 jip8-lai5.  ti7 Siong7-te3 kap cheng3-gi7 e5 mia5, lai5 soan-thoan5 au(**au5)-kio3 kong2, lin2 chiah e5 gi5-oan5 long2 si7 li7-iong7 kong-chit ti7-teh tou5-bou5 su-ki2 e5 li7-lou7, lan2 siuN7 siaN2-khoan2?  Lan2 kiam2 bo5 phah-sng3 hit e5 siaN5-nih8 e5 lang5 beh ui7-tioh8 an2-ni, lai5 tam7-poh8 io5-choah mah?
	Khak-sit8, hit am3 ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, ke-ke hou7-hou7 ti7-teh chiah8 am3-png7 e5 si5, ia7 ti7 ke-lou7-nih8, ti7-chia ti7 hia u7 kiat kui-tong2, long2 si7 teh kong2-khi2 chit e5 siau3-lian5, ki5-iN7 e5 sian-ti lang5 i2-kip8 I ti7 Seng3 Tian7 sou2 kiaN5 hit e5 oe7 hou7 lang5 chhiN-kiaN e5 tai7-chi3.  Ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 hiah e5 teh ui7 ki3-seng5 e5 chou-chit e5 lang5, sim-lai7 u7 phau7 hoan2-khong3 kap phoe-pheng5 e5 thai3-tou7, chong2-si7 lian5 ti7 Hoat-li7-sai3 lang5 e5 tiong-kan hiah e5 khah chhim-siuN7 e5, khoaN3-kiN3 I sou2 kiaN5 e5 su7, sim-lai7 ma7-si7 siu7 toa7 e5 kam2-kek.  Put-koan2 siaN2-khoan2, I si7 chit8 e5 seng3-chia2, si7 chit8 e5 iong2-kam2 e5 cheng3-gi7 e5 chian3-su7.  Hit-si5 un2-tang3 u7 chin-choe7 lang5 tai7-ke soe3-soe3 siaN teh kong2, I tek-khak m7-si7 kan-ta chit8 e5 peng5-siong5 e5 lang5 na7-tiaN7.  Hit si5 un2-tang3 tui3 pak-peng5 u7 chin-choe7 Ka-li7-li7 e5 lang5 soa3 toa3 chiong2-chiong2 ki5-iN7 e5 hong-siaN loh8-lai5 lam5-peng5.  Lan2 ia7 thang liau7-siong2, Iok-han7 i2-kip8 i e5 siau3-lian5 e5 tang5-phoaN7, un2-tang3 i2-keng u7 kong2-khi2 KiaN5 soe2-le2 e5 Iok-han7 u7 chaiN2-iuN7 lai5 kan-cheng3 Ia5-sou e5 su7.  In-ui7 hit-si5 cheng3-lang5 long2 si7 sin3-iong7 KiaN5 soe2-le2 e5 Iok-han7 sou2 kan-cheng3 e5 oe7.
	Kiam2-chhai2 Iok-han7 in tai7-ke i2-keng u7 kong2-khi2 ia7 ku2 kaN2.  Chong2-si7 chiau3 khah toa7-bin7 in si7 bo5 kong2 chiah tioh8, ia7 khah toa7-bin7 Ia5-sou u7 chou2-chi2 in.  In-ui7 in na7 kong2-khi2 I sou2 kiaN5 e5 sin5-jiah, lang5 boe7 bian2-tit ai3 lun7-khi2 I e5 tai7-chi3, ia7 kiaN-liau2 hoan2-tng2 oe7 chou2-tong3-tioh8 I sou2 beh choe3 e5 kang, lai5 kan-ta chu7-chip8 choe7-choe7 bo5 li2-kai2 e5 lang5 tiam3 ti7 I e5 sin-piN.  In-ui7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 peh-siN3, si7 bo5 koh-iuN7 Ka-li7-li7 e5 peh-siN3, in khiok si7 u7 teh siuN7 kong2, Siong7-te3 e5 Kok si7 cheng3-gi7 e5 kok, chong2-si7 ki5-sit8 in te7-it koan-sim e5, si7 teh siuN7 kong2, in e5 kok beh chiaN5-choe3 I2-sek-liat8 e5 eng5-kng, ia7 hit-si5 Ia5-ho5-hoa pun2-sin beh choe3 in e5 Ong5, bi2-sai3-a beh choe3 in e5 chi2-to7-chia2, choe3 ban7 koan5-leng5 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 tai7-piau2 lai5 chiang2-li2 toe7-bin7-chiuN7 it-chhe3 e5 koan5-peng3.
	It-poaN e5 Iu5-thai3 lang5 to long2 si7 khng3 chhin-chhiuN7 chit-khoan2 e5 i3-kian3, sou2-i2 I na7 kheng2 kap in tang5-i3, beh lai5 chu7-chip8 kui toa7-tin7 e5 gu5-bin5, jiat8-sim lai5 choe3 I e5 kha-chhiu2, ti7 I e5 sin-piN lai5 eng5-hian2 in e5 kok, che un2-tang3 si7 bo5 oh tit e5 su7, chong2-si7 chit ho7 su7 si7 put-hap8, bo5 koan-he7 ti7 I e5 chin-sit8 e5 ke3-ek8.  I chin-sit8 e5 ke3-ek8 si7 beh the5-ko jin5-lui7 leng5-seng3 e5 seng-oah8 e5 su7-giap8.  Sou2-i2 chiau3-khoaN3 I si7 cham2-jian5 ai3 un2-bat8 I pun2-sin, bo5 ai3 hian2-jian5 ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, ia7 si7 u7 chou2-chi2 it-chhe3 siok8 ti7 si5 boe7-kau3 e5 tak8 teng2-ho7 e5 mia5-siaN.
	Chong2-si7 cheng3-lang5 boe7 bian2-tit ai3 su-siuN2 I e5 tai7-chi3.  Ti7 tak8 kai-kip to u7 chin-choe7 lang5 teh su-siuN2 I.  Iok-han7 u7 keng2-soan2 chit8 e5 tu3-hian7 e5 le7 lai5 chi2-si7 lan2 chai-iaN2 hit-si5 e5 cheng5-keng2.

“U7 chit8 e5 Hoat-li7-sai3 lang5, mia5 Ni5-ko-ti2-bu2, si7 Iu5-thai3 lang5 e5 koaN.”  Chit e5 Ni5-ko-ti2-bu2 u7 chhim-chhim teh siuN7 I sou2 kiaN5 e5 su7, sui-jian5 i e5 tang5-phoaN7 long2 si7 teh hoan2-khong3 Ia5-sou, chong2-si7 i khoaN3-kiN3 chit e5 iong2-kam2e siau3-lian5 e5 sian-ti lang5 sou2 choe3 e5 su7, sim-lai7 toa7-toa7 siu7 kam2-tong7.  I ti7 sim-lai7 chin ki5-koai3 teh sam2-su Ia5-sou e5 su7.  I ai3 chai-iaN2 I e5 tai7-chi3.  Chiau3-khoaN3 i si7 chit8 e5 seng5-sit8 jiat8-seng5 e5 lang5.  Kho2-sioh i si7 u7 khah sio2-taN2, khah po2-siu2 e5 kau3-tou5; chit khoan2 e5 lang5 ti7 tak8 si5-tai7 to long2 si7 bo5 khoai3-khoai3 lai5 piau2-si7 i e5 i3-su3.  Sou2-i2 i u7 ti7 PoaN5-ke3-choeh geh8 am3-mi5, chheng7 tng5-tng5 e5 goa7-tho3, am3-chiN7 ka-ki7 chit8 lang5 thau-chau2 chhut-khi3 kiaN5 ti7 ke-lou7 e5 u7 chhiu7-ng2 am3-am3 e5 sou2-chai7, siuN7 beh chhe7 Ia5-sou, chiu7 kiaN5 kau3 chit8 ui7, chiu7-si7 toa7-bin7 Ia5-sou e5 hak8-seng Iok-han7 u7 kap I saN-kap tiam3 e5 sou2-chai7.
	Lan2 thang siong2-siong7 Iok-han7 u7 an3-nai7 chit e5 chhut-mia5 e5 lang5-kheh, chiuN7 khi3 ti7 i kap i e5 sian-siN sou2 tiam3 hit e5 m7-chiaN5-mih8 e5 lau5-teng2, iah8 i u7 che7 ti7-hia chu3-i3 lai5 thiaN, soa3 ki3-tit i ti7 u7 chit8-jit8 sou2 beh tui3 se3-kai3 lai5 kan-cheng3 e5 su7.  Lan2 teh siuN7 Iok-han7 na7 oe7 thang koh khah gau5 ki3-tit chit chan5-su7 si7 chin ho2, che kiam2 si7 bo5 keng3-khian5 e5 sou2-chai7 mah?  In-ui7 i chi2-u7 ki3 toe2-toe2 kui2-ku3 oe7, beh lai5 choe3 lan2 e5 lou7-eng7.  Sou2-i2 lan2 tioh8 chim-chiok lai5 siuN7 Seng3-chheh sou2 ki3 e5 i2-goa7 e5 i3-su3, soa3 chiau3 lan2 sou2 oe7 e5, lai5 cheng-pou2 loh8-khi3 chiah ho2.
	Lan2 thang liau7-siong2 Ni5-ko-ti2-bu2 si7 him-bou7 ai3 thiaN Ia5-sou kang2-lun7 I sou2 beh kian3-siat e5 Ong5-kok; ia7 iu5-goan5 thang siuN7, i si7 u7 khng3 it-poaN e5 Iu5-thai3 lang5 e5 Siong7-te3 e5 kok e5 koan-liam7 ti7-teh.  I si7 bo5 koh-iuN7 ki5-u5 e5 lang5, iu5-goan5 u7 teh theng3-hau7 I2-sek-liat8 toe7-bin7-chiuN7 e5 ong5-kok, beh tit-tioh8 eng5-kng, chhiong-seng7; ia7 teh siuN7, chu7-jian5 tak8 e5 I2-sek-liat8 lang5, tui3 chhut-si3 chiu7-si7 chiaN5-choe3 hit-e5 ong5-kok e5 chit(**chit8)-oan5.  I si7 u7 toa7-toa7 teh ki5-thai7 Ia5-sou beh chiaN5-choe3 hit e5 sou2 iok-sok e5 Bi2-sai3-a.  I si7 chit8 e5 lau7 toa7-lang5, koh u7 chhang-mia5; ia7 ti7 chong-kau3 kai3 ma7-si7 chit8 e5 koan5-ui-chia2, sou2-i2 kiam2-chhai2 i u7 khng3 chhin-chhiat e5 i3-su3, teh ng3-bang7 i sou2 khou2-khng3 e5 oe7 i2-kip8 i e5 kam2-hoa3, u7 kau3-giah8 oe7 kham-tit thang hou7 cha2-khi2 hiah-nih8 piaN3-mia7, lai5 chhut-thau5 chit e5 siau3-lian5 e5 jiat8-sim ka hoaN-hi2 chiap-lap8.  Ia7 bian2 giau5-gi5, i un2-tang3 u7 teh siuN7, siat-su2 Ia5-sou na7-si7 beh kian3-siat chhin-chhiuN7 i sou2 teh liau5-bang7 e5 ong5-kok, i si7 oe7 chiaN5-choe3 chit8 e5 tong5-chi3 e5 lang5, ia7 put-chi2 u7 lat8 thang pang-chan7 I.
