	Chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni, Ni5-ko-ti2-bu2 u7 hian2-chhut i oe7-thang pang-chan7 I hou7 I thang siu7 i e5 un-cheng5 e5 thai3-tou7, ia7 Ia5-sou tek-khak si7 u7 eng7 thiam5-cheng7, koh u7 ui-giam5 e5 oe7 lai5 chek-pi7 i, hou7 i chek-si5 khiam-pi chiah tioh8.  Sou2-i2 i chiah u7 eng7 hit ho7 chhim-chhim chun-keng3 e5 thai3-tou7, lai5 chheng-hou chit e5 siau3-lian5 e5 hiong-chhoan lang5 kong2, “Liap8-pi2, goan2 chai li2 choe3 sian-siN, si7 tui3 Siong7-te3 lai5 e5, in-ui7 na7 m7-si7 Siong7-te3 kap li2 ti7-teh, chiu7 bo5 lang5 oe7 kiaN5 li2 sou2 kiaN5 chiah e5 sin5-jiah.”
	Lan2 long2 bo5 thiaN-kiN3 Ni5-ko-ti2-bu2 u7 soa3-chiap koh kong2-khi2 sim2-mih8 tai7-chi3, lan2 chi2-u7 thang chhui-chhek ji5-i2, in-ui7 Ia5-sou hut-jian5-kan u7 chou2-chi2 Ni5-ko-ti2-bu2 e5 oe7, ia7 kah-na2 chhin-chhiuN7 u7 liau2-kai2 ti7 i e5 thau5-nau2 lai7 sou2 teh gi5-bun7 e5 bun7-toe5; soa3 lai5 in3-tap i kong2, “Goa2 sit8-sit8 ka7 li2 kong2, lang5 na7 bo5 teng5-thau5 siN, chiu7 boe7-oe7 khoaN3-kiN3 Siong7-te3 e5 kok.”
	Lan2 thang phah-sng3, Ia5-sou u7 koh khah siong5-se3 lai5 soat-beng5 I e5 i3-su3, kong2, “Liap8-pi2, li2 sou2 siuN7 e5, lun7 Siong7-te3 e5 kok e5 i3-su3 si7 choan5-jian5 chho3-gou7 lah.  Li2 iau2-be7 koh kong2 e5 tai7-seng, chhiaN2 iong5-un2 goa2 lai5 chi2-si7 li2 si3-chiaN3 e5 kian3-kai2.  Lun7 goa2 sou2 kian3-siat e5 ong5-kok, long2 bo5 u7 hit ho7 cheng3-ti7 i2-kip8 toe7-chiuN7 e5 koan5-se3 kap tek8-koan5 e5 i3-su3 ti7-teh.  Goa2 e5 ong5-kok chiu7-si7 hit ho7 u7 seng5-sit8 sim e5 lang5 e5 kok;  ia7 bo5 lun7 ta-pou, a2-si7 cha-bou2, hoan7-na7 ti7 sim-toe2, u7 chun5 ui2-tai7 e5 li2-siong2, tiong-sit8 hang5-hok8 Siong7-te3 e5 lang5, chiu7-si7 goa2 e5 ong5-kok e5 chit(**chit8)-oan5.  Sou2-i2 m7-si7 kan-ta tioh8 chhut-si3 choe3 Iu5-thai3 lang5, ma7 m7-si7 u7 Iu5-thai3 lang5 e5 tek8-koan5 chiu7 oe7 thang chiaN5-choe3 goa2 e5 ong5-kok e5 chit(**chit8)-oan5.  Lang5 bo5 hun chi7-chui7, hek8-si7 Iu5-thai3 a2-si7 IN7-pang, na7-si7 bo5 teng5-thau5-siN, bo5 tui3 teng2-bin7, tui3 Siong7-te3 e5 Sin5 lai5 siN, chiu7 boe7-oe7 jip8 ti7 hit e5 seng5-sit8 sim e5 ong5-kok.”
	Lan2 un2-tang3 beh ki5-koai3, an3-choaN2 chit ho7 e5 to7-li2 u7 hiah-nih8 be5-loan7 chit e5 chhim-tim5 e5 chong-kau3-ka Liap8-pi2, Ni5-ko-ti2-bu2 e5 sim le3(**leh)?  Lun7 teng5-thau5-siN e5 to7-li2, chai7 Iu5-thai3 lang5 to m7-si7 hi-han2 e5 oe7.  In bat teh phah-sng3 IN7-pang lang5 na7 lai5 chiap-lap8 Iu5-thai3 kau3, si7 khoaN3-choe3 teng5-thau5-siN e5 i3-su3.  Kiam2-chhai2 i oe7 ju5-loan7 kau3 an2-ni, si7 ui7-tioh8 i u7 thiaN-tioh8 Ia5-sou kong2, tak8-lang5 lian5 Iu5-thai3 lang5 to long2 tioh8 teng5-thau5-siN; iau2-ku2 chiau3 Liap8-pi2 e5 oe7 si7 kong2, tak8 e5 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 chu7-jian5 si7 long2 beh u7 hun7 ti7 hit e5 chiong-lai5 e5 se3-kai3.  Ia5-sou sou2 kong2 e5 oe7, tek-khak si7 u7 cham2-jian5 khah koh-iuN7 ti7 i sou2 teh siuN7 e5 i3-su3.  Tui3 an2-ni i chiah kong2, “Goa2 long2 boe7-thang liau2-kai2, lang5 to i2-keng lau7, chaiN2-iuN7 oe7 teng5-thau5-siN? kiam2 oe7 koh jip8 lau7-bu2 e5 pak-tou2-lai7 lai5 siN mah?”
	Ni5-ko-ti2-bu2 u7 mng7 kong2, chaiN2-iuN7?  Iau2-ku2 Ia5-sou long2 bo5 soat-beng5 hit e5 “chaiN2-iuN7.”  I si7 u7 eng7 lang5 e5 keng-giam7 lai5 chhui-pek i, hou7 i ka-ki7 lai5 phoaN3-toan3 hit e5 tai7-chi3 kong2, “Jiok8-the2 kap Sin5-leng5, a2-si7 chu7-jian5 lang5 oah8 ti7 chit se3-kan kap sin5-leng5 e5 lang5, sim-koaN choan-ng3 Siong7-te3, hit e5 cheng-chha li2 chai.  Tui3 jiok8-the2 siN e5, si7 jiok8-the2; tui3 Sin5 siN e5, si7 Sin5.  Lang5 oe7 siN-chhut hit ho7 sin5-leng5 e5 liam7-thau5, ko-siong7 e5 li2-siong2 e5 iok8-bong7, m7-si7 chhut tui3 ngou2-jian5, a2-si7 chu7-jian5 sou2 oe7 e5.  Hit-ho7 su7 tiaN7-tioh8 si7 tui3 Siong7-te3 e5 Sin5 chiah oe7-thang seng5-chiu7 i.  Na7-si7 beh lai5 lun7-khi2 hit e5 “chaiN2-iuN7,” lan2 chi2-u7 si7 thang kong2 an2-ni na7-tiaN7.  chit e5 i2(**iN7)-siong7 si7 poaN5-ke3 lan2 sou2 oe7 liau2-kai2 e5 su7 lah.  In-ui7 Seng3 Sin5 e5 kam2-hoa3 si7 chhin-chhiuN7 hong, chu7-iu5 chu7-chai7, si7 chin7-chai7 o3-biau7 e5 su7.  Chit-tiap8 li2 thiaN-kiN3 hong teh chhe, ti7 goa7-bin7 e5 chhiu7-chang5.  Iau2-ku2 li2 m7-chai i tui3 ta2-loh8 lai5, ia7 beh tui3 ta2-loh8 khi3.  KiN3-na7 tui3 Seng3 Sin5 siN e5, iah8 si7 an2-ni.  Goa2 e5 kok chiu7-si7 tui3 Seng3 Sin5 teng5-thau5-siN e5, tui3 Siong7-te3 e5 Sin5 sou2 siN e5 lang5 e5 kok.”
	Hit e5 lau7 liap8-pi2 thiaN-liau2 ma7 long2 boe7 hiau2-tit sim2-mih8, soa3 kan-ta mng7 I kong2, “ChaiN2-iuN7 oe7 an2-ni ah?”
	“Li2 choe3 I2-sek-liat8 e5 sian-siN, ia7 m7-chai che mah?  Goa2 kong2, lang5 tioh8 khiam3-eng7 Siong7-te3 e5 Sin5 e5 kam2-tong7, chiah oe7 chiaN5-choe3 sin5-leng5 e5 lang5, chit e5 tan-sun5 e5 su7-sit8, li2 siong7-chhiaN2 to thiaN boe7 hiau2-tit le3(**leh); goa2 na7 ka7 li2 kong2, siok8 ti7 thiN-teng2 e5 khah chhim-o3 e5 su7, lin2 thai3 beh sin3?  In-ui7 chi2-u7 goa2 chiah oe7 thang ka7 lin2 kong2 hit e5 su7.  Bo5 lang5 bat chiuN7 thiN lai5 bat hit e5 su7, chi2-u7 ti7 thiN-nih8 e5 Jin5-chu2, tui3 thiN kang3-loh8 e5 na7-tiaN7.  Li2 iau2-be7 liau2-kai2 goa2 i2-kip8 goa2 e5 kok e5 i2-cheng5, iau2 u7 chin-choe7 thang chhiN-kiaN e5 su7-sit8, li2 tioh8 ai3 bat.  Goa2 m7-si7 chiau3 lin2 sou2 teh siuN7 e5 khoan2, ai3 beh lai5 che7 kun-ong5 e5 giok8-cho7, lai5 hian2-chhut Siong7-te3 e5 koan5-peng3, si7 beh lai5 seng5-siu7 hit ho7 kian3-siau3 e5 Sip8-ji7-ke3, lai5 hian2-chhut Siong7-te3 u7 chaiN2-iuN7 hi-seng I pun2-sin lai5 thiaN3 se3-kan lang5.  Koh chhin-chhiuN7 Mou5-se ku2-khi2 choa5 ti7 khong3-ia2 kiu3 I2-sek-liat8, Jin5-chu2 iah8 tek-khak tioh8 an2-ni siu7 ku2-khi2.”
	ChhiaN2 siong2-siong7 chit e5 lau7 liap8-pi2 chim-chiok thiaN-liau2 i e5 cheng-sin5 chong7-thai3 si7 siaN2-khoan2.  Chit e5 khia7 ti7 Ni5-ko-ti2-bu2 e5 bin7-cheng5 e5 Ia5-sou si7 chit8 e5 bo5 mia5-siaN siau3-lian5 e5 hiong-chhoan lang5; I bo5 seng5-siu7 sim2-mih8 hak8-hau7 e5 kau3-iok8; ma7-si7 bo5 siu7 kau3-hoe7 e5 jim7-kho2, iau2-ku2 ti7 bo5 i3-sek e5 tiong-kan, I u7 tit-tioh8 I e5 toe7-ui7, lai5 chiaN5-choe3 Ni5-ko-ti2-bu2 e5 si7-toa7; koh tui3 i kan-cheng3 pun2-sin si7 tui3 thiN-teng2 loh8-lai5 e5, u7 chai-iaN2 Siong7-te3 e5 ke3-ek8, soa3 kan-cheng3 I si7 beh lai5 chiaN5-choe3 se3-kan e5 chin kng, eng2-oan2 e5 oah8-mia7 e5 goan5-thau5.  Khak-sit8, I na7 m7-si7 chit e5 bong7-siong2-ka, chiu7-si7 ti7 I e5 lai7-bin7 tiaN7-tioh8 si7 u7 hit ho7 sin5-seng3 e5 iau3-sou3 ti7-teh.
	In ti7 saN bian7-hoe7 e5 tiong-kan sou2 kong2 e5 oe7, chiau3 lan2 sou2 oe7-thang chai-iaN2 e5, tai7-khai3 si7 chhin-chhiuN7 teng2-bin7 e5 khoan2-sit.  In e5 tam5-lun7 si7 an3-choaN2 kiat-kiok8, lan2 long2 m7-chai, in-ui7 chiau3 Seng3-chheh sou2 ki3 hit e5 kiat-be2 e5 oe7 si7 kong2, hou7 kiN3-na7 sin3 e5 lang5 tiam3 ti7 I u7 eng2-oah8, m7-ku2 chit ku3 beng5-beng5 si7 Iok-han7 sou2 chu3-kai2 e5 oe7.  Chit e5 toa7 liap8-pi2 thiaN-liau2 m7-chai si7 u7 liau2-kai2 I e5 i2-su3, a2-si7 thiaN-liau2 iu-bun7 chiu7 khi3, lan2 ma7-si7 long2 m7-chai.  Lan2 si7 chin ai3 chai-iaN2 hit e5 kiat-kiok8.  In-ui7 Ni5-ko-ti2-bu2 sui-jian5 si7 u7 khah soe3-ji7, khah sio2-taN2 e5 lang5, iau2-ku2 si7 chit8 e5 seng5-sit8 teh tui-chhe7 chin-li2 e5 lang5, sou2-i2 lun7 i e5 su7 si7 put-chi2 oe7 giu2 lan2 e5 sim.  Hit e5 kiat-kiok8, bo5-lun7 si7 siaN2-khoan2, tui3 hit-si5 khi2, i e5 sim un2-tang3 si7 bo5 boe7-ki3-tit Ia5-sou chiah tioh8.  Chit e5 tai7-chi3 liau2-au7, lan2 u7 koh thiaN-tioh8 I e5 mia5 nng7 pai2.  Iah8 tak8-pai2 i long2 si7 u7 ui7 Ia5-sou.  Iah8 tak8-pai2 ma7-si7 u7 hian2-chhut i e5 sio2-taN2 e5 seng3-chit.  Chhin-chhiuN7 bat u7 chit8 pai2, cheng3 peh-siN3 e5 thau5-lang5 teh-beh kong-jian5 lai5 ti2-tek8 Ia5-sou e5 si5, i u7 eng7 bo5 kau3 loa7 hun-beng5 e5 thai3-tou7 lai5 ui7 I kong2, “Bo5 thiaN lang5 e5 hun-sou3, lan2 e5 lut8-hoat kiam2 u7 teng7 sim2-mih8 lang5 e5 choe7 mah?”  Koh u7 chit8 pai2 Ia5-sou hou7 lang5 teng3-si2, ia7 A-li7-ma2-thai3 e5 Iok-sek beh lai5 bai5-chong3 I e5 sin-si e5 si5, ti7 Seng3-chheh u7 ki3-chai3 kong2, “koh u7 Ni5-ko-ti2-bu2, khi2-thau5 bat mi5-si5 chiu7-kun7 Ia5-sou e5” iah8 lai5, u7 toa3 but8-ioh8 chhiau tim5-hiuN.  Che si7 i choe3-au7 sou2 oe7 thang thoe3 chit e5 siau3-lian5 e5 peng5-iu2 sou2 choe3 e5 su7; i chit-tiap8 sui-jian5 khoaN3-kiN3 Ia5-sou siu7 lang5 hai7-si2, chit e5 su7-sit8 beng5-beng5 si7 teh piau2-beng5 Ia5-sou e5 sit-pai7, iau2-ku2 Ia5-sou si7 i sou2 chun-keng3 e5 chit8 e5 peng5-iu2, sou2-i2 chiah theh8 hiah-nih8 kui3-tiong7 e5 mih8 lai5 beh boah Ia5-sou e5 sin-si.

	Chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni, lan2 tui3 chit-tiap8 khi2 si7 bo5 koh u7 khoaN3-kiN3 Ni5-ko-ti2-bu2 e5 chhut-thau5.  Chong2-si7 lan2 tek-khak boe7-thang chu7 an2-ni lai5 soah--khi3, oaN7 lai5 kong2 pat8-mih8 e5 su7; lan2 boe7 bian2-tit tioh8 theng5 tiap-a2(**tiap8-a2)-ku2 ti7-chia koh lai5 saN-kap siuN7 i sou2 teh be5-loan7 e5 bun7-toe5.
	Lun7 hit e5 bun7-toe5 chi3-chio2 lan2 si7 oe7-thang an2-ni siuN7.  Lan2 tui3 jin5-lui7 chin3-hoa3 e5 su7-sit8, u7 tit-tioh8 chit e5 kau3-hun3 ti7-teh.  Siong7-te3 tui3 lan2 jin5-lui7 si7 u7 chun5 chit8 e5 oan2-tai7 e5 ke3-ek8 ti7-teh.  Siong7-te3 u7 hou7 hit ho7 khah ha7-teng2 e5 siu7-cho7-but8 chiam7-chiam7 chin3-hoa3 kau3 chiaN5-choe3 khah ko-siong7 e5 chun5-chai7-chia2, chiu7-si7 chiaN5-choe3 chit8 e5 chu7-jian5 e5 lang5; chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni, I u7 hou7 chu7-jian5 lang5 chin3-hoa3 kau3 chiaN5-choe3 koh khah ko-siong7 e5 chun5-chai7-chia2, chiu7-si7 chiaN5-choe3 sin5-leng5 e5 lang5, chiu7-si7 hit ho7 kap Siong7-te3 u7 saN kiat-lian5 e5 lang5.  Chu7-jian5 lang5 si7 oe7-thang chin3-hoa3 kau3 chiaN5-choe3 sin5-leng5 e5 lang5, chhin-chhiuN7 chham5-a2, oe7-thang chin3-hoa3 kau3 chiaN5-choe3 boe2-iah8 chit8-poaN.  Iau2-ku2 m7-si7 kong2, tak8 chiah chham5-a2 long2 u7 chin3-hoa3 kau3 chiaN5-choe3 boe2-iah8; ia7 tak8 e5 lang5 ma7 m7-si7 kong2 long2 u7 chin3-hoa3 kau3 chiaN5-choe3 sin5-leng5 e5 lang5.  Lang5 long2 oe7, chong2-si7 bo5 long2 an2-ni.  Ia5-sou u7 kong2, chu7-jian5 lang5 na7-si7 beh tit-tioh8 chiaN5-choe3 sin5-leng5 e5 lang5, tek-khak tioh8 ai3 kap Siong7-te3 u7 jin5-keh-tek e5 lian5-lok8 ti7-teh.  I e5 oah8-mia7 tek-khak tioh8 hou7 Siong7-te3 e5 Seng3 Sin5 chhiong-moa2 lai5 tit-tioh8 oah8-khi3.  Chu7-jian5 lang5 kiam2-chhai2 si7 oe7 chiaN5-choe3 oah8-khi3.  Chu7-jian5 lang5 kiam2-chhai2 si7 oe7 chiaN5-choe3 iu-siu3 e5 lang5, chhin-chhiuN7 chham5-a2 oe7 chiaN5-choe3 iu-liong5 e5 chham5-a2 chit8-poaN.  Iau2-ku2 hit ho7 siang7 iu-liong5 e5 chham5-a2 ma7 boe7 eng7 tit kong2, si7 boe2-iah8.  I si7 iau2 u7 sit-loh8 i e5 chin-sit8 e5 thian-hun7.  Chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni, hit ho7 siang7 iu-siu3 e5 chu7-jian5 lang5, ma7 iau2-boe7 eng7-tit kong2, si7 sin5-leng5 e5 lang5.  I iau2 u7 khiam3-eng7 Siong7-te3 e5 Sin5 thang lai5 tit-tioh8 oah8-mia7 e5 lian5-lok8.
	KiaN5 soe2-le2 e5 Iok-han7 kau3 u7 theng5-tou7 si7 i2-keng u7 ka3-si7 chit tiau5 e5 to7-li2.  I kong2, “Goa2 chi2-u7 si7 oe7-thang pi7-pan7 lin2 e5 sim, eng7 chui2 ka7 lin2 kiaN5 soe2-le2, hou7 lin2 hoan2-hoe2 na7-tiaN7.  Chong2-si7 tok8-tok8 hit e5 lou7-be2 goa2 lai5 e5, chiah oe7-thang hou7 lin2 tit-tioh8 sin5-leng5 e5 oah8-mia7.  Tok8-tok8 I chiah oe7 eng7 chui2 kap Seng3 Sin5 ka7 lin2 soe2.”
	Kiam2-chhai2 lan2 tiong-kan, u7 e5 lang5 si7 chhin-chhiuN7 Ni5-ko-ti2-bu2, khoaN3 che si7 kah-na2-chun2 chin oh-tit e5 oe7.  Chong2-si7 Ia5-sou to i2-keng u7 hiah-nih8 chhut-lat8 lai5 kan-cheng3, lan2 kiam2 m7-si7 tioh8 chim-chiok lai5 siuN7 chiah ho2 mah?  Lan2 tiong-kan choe7-choe7 lang5 si7 kan-ta boan2-chiok hit ho7 u7 koe3 kai2-liong5 e5 chham5-a2, hit ho7 toan-chong, ho2 bou5-iuN7 e5 chu7-jian5 lang5 ji5-i2.  Ki5-sit8 Siong7-te3 e5 Sin5, tui3 lan2 u7 khng3 oan2-tai7 e5 ng3-bang7 ti7-teh.  I chit-tiap8 put-si5 to teh theng3-hau7 lan2.  Seng3 Sin5 si7 chhin-chhiuN7 lan2 tak8-si5 sou2 teh hou-khip e5 khong-khi3 chit8-poaN, chu7-iu5 chu7-chai7 un7-heng5 ti7 lan2 e5 sin-piN.  Lan2 boe7-thang kong2-khi2 i tui3 ta2-loh8 lai5, ia7 tui3 ta2-loh8 khi3.  Lan2 si7 long2 boe7-thang kong2 siaN2-khoan2.  Iau2-ku2 che si7 u7 moa2-moa2 e5 ng3-bang7 e5 su-siuN2.  Lan2 thang sin3, Siong7-te3 e5 Sin5, I e5 chu7-iu5 e5 un7-heng5, tek-khak m7-si7 kan-ta kai3-han7 ti7 lan2 e5 kau3-hoe7 lai7, kan-ta hiah e5 u7 tek8-koan5 e5 cheng3 seng3-tou5 chiah u7 thang tit-tioh8 I e5 chhiong-moa2 na7-tiaN7.
	Siat-su2 lan2 na7 u7 thiaN-kiN3, u7 sim2-mih8 bo5 siu7 kau3-iok8 e5 pou7-peng, tiong2-toa7 ti7 phaiN2 e5 ka-teng5, lai5 oh8 lang5 kong2 choe7-choe7 e5 phaiN2-oe7, ia7 long2 boe7-hiau2 ki5-to2, chong2-si7 i e5 peng5-iu2 tai7-ke chin thiaN3-thang3 i, in-ui7 i choe3 lang5 si7 choan5-jian5 bo5 kou3 tioh8 ka-ki7, ia7 i e5 choe3-au7, si7 chhin-chhiuN7 Ki-tok e5 khoan2, u7 thoe3 pat8-lang5 lai5 si2.  Lan2 tui3 khoaN3-kiN3 chit ho7 su7-sit8, put-tek-put tioh8 siuN7 kong2, hoan7-na7 siok8 ti7 hit ho7 ho2, koh oan5-choan5 e5 heng5-ui5, long2 si7 chhut tui3 teng2-bin7 lai5 e5; lan2 put-tek-put tioh8 siuN7 kong2, che si7 tui3 Ia5-sou sou2 kong2-khi2, hit e5 Siong7-te3 sin5-pi3-tek e5 Seng3 Sin5 hong e5 sou2 kam2-hoa3 e5.  In-ui7 “lan2 m7-chai i tui3 ta2-loh8 lai5, tui3 ta2-loh8 khi3.”



Te7-7 chiuN	KiaN5 Soe2-Le2 e5 Iok-Han7 ChaiN2-IuN7 Si2

	Hiah e5 tui3 tak8-kok lai5 hu3 choeh e5 cheng3-lang5 si3-soaN3 liau2-au7, Ia5-sou u7 koh tiam3 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 loa7-ku2, lan2 long2 m7-chai.  Lan2 thang siong2-siong7, un2-tang3 si7 bo5 loa7-ku2 chiah tioh8.  In-ui7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 peh-siN3 kap Ia5-sou tai7-ke long2 bo5 saN kah-i3.  Hit ho7 u7 toa7 kau3-hoe7 e5 siaN5-chhi7 lang5 khah-siong5 si7 u7 phian-kian3, chu7-ki2 boan2-chiok e5 sim ti7-teh, put-chi2 u7 siu7-tioh8 hiah e5 u7 se3-thau5 e5 bok8-su e5 siaN-im sou2 kam2-hoa3.  U7-iaN2, ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2, u7 kui toa7-tin7 lang5 chak-oa2 lai5 chiu7-kun7 I, ia7 tui3 khoaN3-kiN3 I e5 sin5-jiah sim u7 toa7 siu7 kam2-tong7, iau2-ku2 lan2 u7 thak8-tioh8 chit(**chit8) ku3 khah ki5-koai3 e5 oe7, chiu7-si7 kong2, “Na7-si7 Ia5-sou bo5 eng7 pun2-sin kau-thok in, in-ui7 I chai cheng3-lang5.”  Lan2 thang liau7-siong2 chit ku3 e5 i3-su3 si7 kong2, Ia5-sou chai in iau2-be7 se3-cha, iau2-be7 beng5-pek8 I e5 ke3-ek8 e5 i2-cheng5, si7 hoaN-hi2 lai5 te3 I, chong2-si7 che un2-tang3 si7 bo5 loa7-ku2 e5 su7.  In-ui7 Ia5-sou sou2 him-bou7  e5 m7-si7 in sou2 teh him-bou7 e5.  Ia5-sou sou2 beh kiaN5 e5 lou7 m7-si7 in sou2 ai3 kiaN5 e5.  Ia5-sou e5 li2-siong2 si7 kap in--e5, u7 toa7-toa7 saN tui3-hoan2 ti7-teh.  Sou2-i2 in na7 u7 beng5-beng5 liau2-kai2 hit e5 cheng5-heng5.  Hit-si5 in un2-tang3 beh teng3 I ti7 Sip8-ji7-ke3.
	Tui3 an2-ni Ia5-sou chiu7 kap I e5 hak8-seng saN-kap the3 khi3 ti7 phian-phiah hiong-chhoan e5 sou2-chai7.  Kiam2-chhai2 ti7 I e5 kong-seng-gai5, tui3 chit-tiap8 khi2 peh(**poeh) geh8-jit8 ku2, I u7 tiam7-cheng7 si3-koe3 kiaN5 ti7 Iu5-thai3 toe7 hiah e5 choh-sit lang5, hiong-chhoan lang5 e5 tiong-kan.  Ti7 chit poeh geh8-jit8 ku2, I sou2 u7 kiaN5 e5 chhin-chhiat e5 sin5-jiah i2-kip8 I sou2 u7 kong2 e5 un-hui7 moa2-moa2 e5 ka3-si7 e5 oe7, lan2 long2 bo5 tang3 thang tit-tioh8.  Lan2 khiok long2 m7-chai-iaN2 hit e5 in-toaN.  Chiau3 lang5 e5 i3-su3 lai5 kong2, kiam2-chhai2 si7 in-ui7 tho2 hai2 e5 si5-ki5 kau3, iah8 Iok-han7 tioh8 to3-khi3 Ka-li7-li7 lai5 choe3 i e5 thau5-lou7, sou2-i2 chiah bo5 thang tui3 in thiaN-kiN3 sim2-mih8.  Lan2 chit-tiap8 si7 ai3 chai-iaN2 hiah e5 cheng5-heng5.  Kho2-sioh bo5 thang tit-tioh8, kou-put-chiong lan2 chi2-u7 thang tui3 lan2 sio2-khoa2 chai e5 lai5 chhui-chhek, lai5 phoaN3-toan3 ji5-i2.
	Lan2 bat kap lan2 e5 tong5-chi3 saN-kap pou7-kiaN5 iu5-lek8 ti7 hit ho7 khah kou2-phai3 e5 chhau2-toe7 chng-sia7 mah?  In-ui7 an2-ni, lan2 oe7 tam7-poh8 kam2-siong2-tioh8 in si3-koe3 kiaN5 ti7 Iu5-thai3 toe7 e5 hiong-chhoan hit-si5 e5 cheng5-keng2.  Ia5-sou thau5-chit8 ni5 e5 thoan5-kau3, si7 ho5-peng5, bo5 hian2-jian5.  Te7-ji7 ni5 si7 u7 tu2-tioh8 khun2-pek i2-kip8 toa7 e5 hong-pho.  Te7-saN ni5 si7 u7 tu2-tioh8 lo5-khou2 gui5-hiam2, ia7 choe3-au7 soa3 hou7 lang5 hai7-si2.
	Lan2 thang siuN7 Ia5-sou e5 thau5-chit8 ni5 e5 thoan5-to7, si7 ti7 hit saN ni5 ku2 e5 tiong-kan te7-it u7 kong-chhai2, te7-it khoai3-lok8 e5 ni5.  Chit-tiap8 tu2-tu2 si7 chhou-ha7 e5 si5-chun7.  Ia5-sou u7 thoan5-kau3 ti7 phian-phiah e5 hiong-chhoan e5 sou2-chai7, iah8 Ia5-sou si7 put-chi2 i3-ai3 hiong-chhoan e5 seng-oah8.  Ia5-sou kap hiah e5 siau3-lian5 e5 tang5-phoaN7, sim-koaN put-chi2 khoai3-lok8, long2 bo5 hoan5 bo5 lo2.  In tai7-ke e5 lak-te7-a2-lai7 peng7 bo5 chit8 sian2, iau2-ku2 long2 bo5 teh khoa3-i3, in-ui7 in kau3 ti7 tak8 sou2-chai7, cheng3-lang5 chiu7 long2 chin ho2 khoan2-thai7 in.  Lan2 thang siuN7, chit e5 soe3-soe3 e5 thoan5-the2 tai7-ke choe3-tin7 kiaN5 ti7 hiah e5 chhau2-toe7 lou7 e5 si5, sim-lai7 u7 hoaN-hi2 khoai3-lok8, ia7 na2 kiaN5 na2 giah8-thau5 lai5 hiong2-lok8 hit e5 te5-sek e5 soaN-keng2, lai5 thiaN hit e5 teh lau5 e5 chui2-choaN5 e5 siaN-im; iah8 tak8 pai2 in kiaN5 kau3 ti7 chit8 e5 hiong-chhoan e5 si5, chiu7 theng5 ti7 lou7-thau5 lou7-be2, a2-si7 chhiu7-kha e5 li7-pian7 e5 sou2-chai7, lai5 tui3 kui-toa7-tin7 e5 gin2-na2 kong2-khi2 hit ho7 hoaN-hi2 koh ho2-thiaN e5 kou3-su7; ia7 tui3 toa7-lang5 lai5 thoan5 Pe7 Siong7-te3 e5 hok-im e5 to7-li2; iu7-koh ti7 lou7-nih8 na7 u7 gu7-tioh8 chhut-goa7 e5 lang5-kheh, chiu7 ka7 in chheng2-an, hou7 in ti7 sim-lai7 tit-tioh8 toa7 e5 an-ui3 kap khoai3-lok8.  In u7-si5 kiaN5 kau3 ti7 phian-phiah e5 sip8-ji7-lou7-thau5, u7 gu7-tioh8 chhiN-mi5 e5, kho2-lin5 e5, thai2-ko e5, chiu7 ka7 in i-ho2.  In kiaN5 lou7 liau2 na7 sian7 e5 si5, chiu7 lian5 ti7 soaN-tiong a2-si7 hit ho7 iam7-jiat8 e5 hiuN-sia7, to hoaN-hi2 hioh-khun3 ti7-hia.  In hoan7-su7 si7 long2 bo5 kin2-kip.  Ia5-sou put-si5 to u7 lau5 chit e5 in3-siong7 ti7-teh.  Ti7 chit e5 U2-tiu7 tiong, Siong7-te3 u7 si5-siong5 thiam5-cheng7, bo5 kin2-kip ti7-teh choe3 kang.  Siong7-te3 u7 eng2-oan2 teh kiaN5 tai7-chi3.  Ia5-sou sou2 tioh8 kiaN5--e5, tu2-tu2 si7 teh kiaN5 Siong7-te3 e5 seng-oah8, ia7 I u7 eng7 jit8-jit8 e5 kang-chok kap hioh-khun3 e5 tan-sun5 e5 seng-oah8, lai5 chhian2-beng5 Ki-tok-kau3 e5 to7-li2.  Cheng5-jit8 ti7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 bat thiaN-kiN3 Ia5-sou e5 su7 e5 hiong-chhoan lang5, un2-tang3 tui3 thiN-kng cha2, chiu7 chau2-khi3 chhe7 I; iah8 I un2-tang3 beh kong2 to7-li2 lai5 ka3-si7 in, siat choe7-choe7 hoaN-hi2 e5 phi3-ju7, lai5 the5-ko in e5 cheng-sin5-siong7 e5 seng-oah8, hou7 in it-hoat beng5-pek8 jin5-seng e5 i3-gi7 kap Siong7-te3 e5 thiaN3-thang3.  Iu7-koh u7 e5 lang5 un2-tang3 ai3 chhiaN2 in saN-kap chiah8 e5-hng-tng3.  Sui-bong2 Ia5-sou hou7 hit ho7 khia7 chhau2-chhu3 e5 lang5 chhiaN2 khi3 choe3 lang5-kheh, ma7-si7 long2 boe7 hou7 chu2-lang5 siN-khi2 sim kan-khou2 kam2-kak put-chu7-iu5, a2-si7 phaiN2 se3-bin7 e5 sou2-chai7 ti7-teh.  U7 chit8-jit8 hit keng chhau2-chhu3 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 beh chhoa7 i hit e5 phoa3-piN7 siong-tiong7 kau3 bo5 ng3-bang7 e5 soe3-kiaN2 lai5 chhin-kun7 Ia5-sou, ia7 Ia5-sou un2-tang3 beh hoaN-hi2 thiaN i e5 khou2-cheng5, soa3 chhun I e5 seng3-chhiu2 lai5 i-ho2 i, soa3 hou7 hit e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 e5 sim eng2-oan2 kiat-lian5 ti7 I.  Lan2 thang siuN7, Ia5-sou chhut-hoat lai5 teh soan-thoan5 I e5 hok-im, si7 chhin-chhiuN7 chit e5 khoan2-sit.  Ia5-sou si7 bo5 tui3 khi2-thau5 chiu7 iau-kiu5 in lai5 sun7-hok8 I.  Kiam2-chhai2 Ia5-sou ma7-si7 long2 bo5 pai5-thek in e5 choe7-ok.  Chong2-si7 I oe7-thang tek-seng3 lai5 tit-tioh8 in e5 sun7-hok8, si7 in-ui7 ti7 I e5 sim-lai7 u7 hit ho7 leng5-tek e5 khip-in2-lat8 ti7-teh; koh ia7-si7 in-ui7 choe7-jin5 na7 kun7-oa2 ti7 I e5 bin7-cheng5 e5 si5, chu7-jian5 ka-ki7 oe7 siN-khi2 ai3 oh8 I e5 khoan2-sit e5 sim ti7-teh.
	Siat-su2 ti7 au7-lai5 hit e5 gin2-na2 e5 lau7-bu2, i2-kip8 cheng3 hiong-chhoan lang5 na7 u7 thiaN-kiN3 hong-siaN kong2, Cha2-cheng5 bat lai5 in tau hit e5 chhin-chhiat e5 lang5-kheh, u7 hou7 lang5 hai7-si2 ti7 siaN5-nih8, iah8 I u7 eng7 I e5 koan5-leng5 tui3 si2 koh-oah8; ia7 siat-su2 in chai-iaN2, bat lai5 in tau hit e5 sin5-biau7 e5 lang5-kheh, si7 tui3 thiN-nit8 loh8-lai5 se3-kan ai3 piau2-beng5 Siong7-te3 e5, lan2 kiam2 bo5 siuN7 kong2, in un2-tang3 beh chin khoai3-lok8, lai5 chhim-sin3 Siong7-te3 e5 thiaN3-thang3 kap I e5 jin5-chu5 mah?
	Goa2 bat thak8-tioh8 chit8 pun2 sio2-hak8-hau7 e5 chheh, u7 teh kong2, chai7 sio2-oh8 e5 gin2-na2, a2-si7 hit ho7 bi7 khai-hoa3 e5 lang5 teh khoaN3, ti7 chit e5 u2-tiu7 tiong u7 nng7 khoan2 e5 sin5 ti7-teh.  Thau5-chit8 khoan2 si7 thiaN3-thang3 e5 Sin5, ia7 te7-ji7 khoan2 si7 kong-to7 e5 Sin5.  Thau5-chit8 khoan2 si7 tioh8 eng7 chun-keng3 kap khian5-seng5 e5 sim lai5 hok8-sai7 i, in-ui7 i si7 ho2, si7 thiaN3-thang3 e5 Sin5, iah8 chit e5 Sin5 si7 oe7 choe3 hit ho7 chhin-chhiuN7 Siong7-te3 sou2 beh choe3 e5 tai7-chi3.  Te7-ji7 khoan2 si7 tioh8 eng7 soe2-ji7 tiuN-ti5 e5 sim lai5 hok8-sai7 i, na7 bo5 , kiaN-liau2 in-ui7 i si7 u7 koan5-peng3, koh i e5 kiaN5-choe3 si7 bo5 tiaN7-tioh8, kiam2-chhai2 i beh siu7-khi3 lai5 thiah-lih8 keng3-pai3 i e5 lang5 e5 sin-khu ia7 ku2 kaN2.
	Lan2 thang siuN7, che si7 chin-sit8 e5 oe7.  Ka-li7-li7 hiah e5 choh-sit lang5, tui3 Ia5-sou ai3 thiaN e5 si7 ta2-loh8 chit8 khoan2, che lan2 long2 bian2 giau5-gi5, in tiaN7-tioh8 si7 ai3 thiaN te7-it khoan2 e5 Sin5-koan.

Ti7 hit e5 tng5-tng5 e5 joah8-thiN, lan2 te3 Ia5-sou si3-koe3 kiaN5 ti7 hit e5 phian-phiah e5 hiong-chhoan e5 te7-hng e5 si5, lan2 si7 bo5 an3-sng3 oe7 khoaN3-tioh8 KiaN5 soe2-le2 e5 Iok-han7, i chit-tiap8 iau2-ku2 u7 ti7 lan2 e5 keh-piah saN li7 bo5 loa7-hng7 e5 hit peng5 soaN, teh chhut-lat8 thoan5-kau3.  Chit e5 su7-sit8, lan2 khoaN3-liau2 hoan2-tng2 si7 put-chi2 chhiN-kiaN.  Lan2 kiam2-chhai2 teh siong2-siong7, chit e5 ui2-tai7 e5 KiaN5 soe2-le2 Iok-han7 e5 su3-beng7, ti7 hit chit8 jit8, chiu7-si7 ka7 Bi2-sai3-a kiaN5 soe2-le2, iah8 tui3 i e5 cheng3 hak8-seng lai5 kan-cheng3 kong2, “Li2 khoaN3, Siong7-te3 e5 IuN5-ko, chiu7-si7 tam-tng se3-kan e5 choe7 e5,” ti7 hit chit8 jit8 chiu7 i2-keng chheng-chho2 liau2 chiah tioh8.  Toa7-bin7 i ma7 si7 chai-iaN2 i e5 su3-beng7 si7 i2-keng chheng-chho2, put-ko3 si7 teh theng3-hau7 tioh8 the3-un2 e5 ho7-thau5, si7 ai3 beh thiaN-kiN3 cheng3-lang5 teh hoaN-hi2 e5 siaN, kok-bin5 teh kun-te3 Ki-tok hit e5 heng5-kun e5 ho7-thau5 na7-tiaN7.
Chong2-si7 i long2 bo5 thiaN-tioh8 chit khoan2 e5 ho7-thau5.  Ke3 liau2 kui2-na7 geh8-jit8, i ma7 long2 bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 sim2-mih8; iah8 bo5 thiaN-kiN3 i it-seng sou2 teh theng3-hau7 hit e5 Bi2-sai3-a e5 siau-sit.  I long2 bo5 thiaN-kiN3 sim2-mih8 ho7-thau5, teh thoan5-po3 kong2, Ia5-sou i2-keng u7 kong-jian5 lai5 piau2-si7 I pun2-sin chiu7-si7 Bi2-sai3-a, ia7 I i2-keng u7 kiaN5 chin2-kiu3 e5 su7-giap8 ti7 I2-sek-liat8 lah.
Chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni, KiaN5 soe2-le2 e5 Iok-han7 iau2 si7 teh theng3-hau7 i e5 the3-un2 e5 ho7-thau5.  Ki5-sit8 hit e5 ho7-thau5 si7 i2-keng teh-beh thiaN-kiN3 lah.  Hit e5 ho7-thau5 si7 pi2 i sou2 teh phah-sng3 e5, cham2-jian5 khah kin2 kau3, ia7 si7 cham2-jian5 u7 khah koh-iuN7 e5 khoan2-sit.  Hi-lut8 ong5 i2-kip8 cheng3 Hoat-li7-sai3 lang5 si7 i2-keng u7 teh siat-hoat.  Put-ko3 ti7 hit tiong-kan, i iau2 teh chhut-lat8 lai5 soan-thoan5 Gi7 e5 to7-li2, i2-kip8 hit e5 sou2 beh lai5 e5 Ong5-kok e5 su7; iah8 i e5 thai3-tou7, tui3 i ti7 Iok-tan3 ho5 sou2 keng-giam7 e5, hit e5 bo5 boe7 ki3-tit e5 jit8 i2-lai5, khak-sit8 si7 cham2-jian5 khah u7 oah8-khi3, khah u7 khak-sin3 e5 khoan2-sit ti7-teh,  Toa7-bin7 i chit-tiap8 si7 cham2-jian5 khah khak-chhiat lai5 teh kan-cheng3 i sou2 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 e5 Ia5-sou, in-ui7 ti7 au7-lai5 Ia5-sou chiaN5-choe3 chhut-mia5 e5 si5, cheng3-lang5 long2 teh kong2, “Iok-han7 long2 bo5 kiaN5 sin5-jiah, tok8-tok8 Iok-han7 sou2 kong2 chit lang5 e5, long2 si7 chin.”
Iok-han7 khiok-si7 u7 soa3-chiap teh chin7 i e5 su3-beng7, lai5 soan-thoan5 to7-li2, put-ko3 u7 khah koh-iuN7, u7 tam7-poh8 hian2-chhut i e5 kang si7 teh-beh chin7 lah.  In-ui7 cheng3-lang5 to bo5 koh teh te3 i, ia7 i e5 kam2-hoa3-lat8, ma7-si7 tit8-tit8 teh soe-bi5 khi3.  Cheng3-lang5 si7 khah bo5 chhin-chhiuN7 cha2-cheng5 hiah hoan-geng5 i lah.  Iok-han7 e5 hak8-seng long2 i2-keng u7 teh khoa3-sim in sian-siN e5 kam2-hoa3-lat8 bo5 khi3.  Bo5 kui2 geh8-jit8 cheng5, choan5 se3-kai3 e5 lang5 to long2 si7 teh te3 i; i si7 ti7 I2-sek-liat8-tiong chit8-e5 te7-it u7 koan5-ui-chia2, iau2-ku2 i e5 mia5-siaN tu2-tu2 chin3-pou7 kau3 ti7 kek8-tiam2, hit-si5 i u7 hut-jian5-kan theng5-teh, lai5 po3 lang5 chai-iaN2 hit e5 pi2 i pun2-sin khah toa7 e5 Ia5-sou.  Tui3 hit-jit8 khi2, i u7 chiam7-chiamsoe7-bi5.  Cheng3 hak8-seng long2 m7-chai-iaN2 hit e5 in-toaN.  In kan-ta thiaN-kiN3 hit e5 sin e5 Sian-ti-lang5 e5 mia5-siaN, u7 chiam7-chiam7 teh thau2.  In iu7-koh long2 bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 chiong(**chiong5)-chian5 hiah e5 siong5-siong5 lai5 te3 in sian-siN e5 cheng3-lang5.  In boe7 bian2-tit put-chi2 iu-bun7; in-ui7 in sim-sim liam7-liam7 to-si7 teh su-siong2 teh thiaN3-sioh hit e5 iong2-kam2 thiam5-cheng7 e5 sian-siN, kau3 ti7 chit-tiap8 u7 hou7 lang5 pang3-sak khi3.
Bat u7 chit8-jit8, Iok-han7 e5 hak8-seng u7 kap chit8 e5 Iu5-thai3 lang5 saN-kap pian7-lun7 chin-choe7 hang7 e5 bun7-toe5, ia7 choe3-au7 u7 gi7-lun7 chit8 tiam2, chiu7-sikoan7-he7 chheng-khi3 e5 su7.  Toa7-bin7 chit e5 Iu5-thai3 lang5 si7 bat kap Ia5-sou choe3-he2, iah8 i u7 chiong in nng7 lang5 e5 soe2-le2 saN pi2-kau3, soa3 khoaN3-khin Iok-han7 e5 soe2-le2. Sou2-i2 Iok-han7 e5 hak8-seng chiu7 tong3-boe7-tiau5, tui3 in e5 sian-siN kong2, “(**Liap8-pi2) ah, chiong(**chiong5)-cheng5 kap li2 ti7 Iok-tan3-goa7, li2 sou2 kan-cheng3--e5, li2 khoaN3, i teh kiaN5 soe2-le2, cheng3-lang5 long2 chiu7-kun7 I.”
Khak-sit8 chi2-u7 ti7 chit-si5 Iok-han7 e5 hak8-seng chiah chai-iaN2, in sou2 teh kun-te3 e5 sian-siN e5 ui2-tai7 kau3 chaiN2-iuN7.  In-ui7 Iok-han7 si7 ti7 chit e5 sit-pai7 e5 si5-chun7, te7-it u7 hian2-chhut i e5 ui2-tai7 e5 sou2-chai7.  Iok-han7 u7 tui3 in kong2, “Si7 lah, goa2 e5 si5 i2-keng moa2 lah.  Goa2 na7 li7-khui lin2 khi3, hit-si5 chiu7 beh u7 koh-khah chhan3-lan7 khoai3-lok8 e5 jit8.  Goa2 chi2-u7 teh koan-sim theng3-hau7 hit e5 jit8 lim5-kau3.  Lin2 beh thoe3 goa2 choe3 kan-cheng3; lin2 kiam2 boe7 ki3-tit goa2 u7 put-si5 bat tui3 lin2 kong2, goa2 m7 si7 sim2-mih8 khoan2 e5 lang5, goa2 m7-si7 Ki-tok, goa2 si7 hong7-chhe ti7 I e5 thau5-cheng5 e5 na7-tiaN7.  Goa2 chi2-u7 si7 choe3 sin-kiaN2-sai3 e5 chit8 e5 pi-chian7 e5 peng5-iu2, lai5 teh hoaN-hi2 I e5 seng5-kong.  Goa2 sui-jian5 li7-khui lin2 khi3 ti7 hit e5 thiam5-cheng7 e5 se3-kai3, iau2-ku2 ti7-hia goa2 ma7-si7 oe7 thiaN-kiN3 hit-e5 Sin-kiaN2-sai3 hoaN-hi2 e5 siaN.  Tui3 an2-ni goa2 e5 sim u7 moa2-moa2 e5 hoaN-hi2 khoai3-lok8; I tek-khak heng-ong7, goa2 tek-khak soe-bi5.”
Che sit8-chai7 si7 ui2-tai7 e5 lang5 e5 liam7-thau5.  Tui3 an2-ni, chit e5 ui2-tai7 e5 kiaN5 soe2-le2 Iok-han7, u7 pang3-he7 i e5 chit-bun7.  Chiah e5 si7 i choe3-au7 lai5 kong-jian5 sou2 kong2 e5 oe7, u7 ki3-chai3 lau5 kau3 ti7 kin-a2-jit8 e5.  Koh chit8 geh8-jit8 au7, i u7 hou7 lang5 koaiN ti7 hit e5 Ma2-kai3-ni2-su (Machacrus) e5 ou-am3 e5 kaN-gak8-lai7, lai5 theng3-hau7 si2 e5 jit8.

ChhiaN2 lan2 oe7 ki3-tit, kiong7 koan Hok-im-su long2 si7 tui3 chit8-tiam2 chhut-hoat lai5 kong2-khi2 lan2 e5 Chu2 thoan5-kau3 ti7 Ka-li7-li7 e5 su7. Iu7-koh in saN-e5 tu3-chia2 ti7 in e5 chheh sou2 te7-it koan-sim ai3 sia2 e5, ma7 long2 si7 kan-ta teh lun7 Ka-li7-li7 thoan5-kau3 e5 su7 na7-tiaN7.  Lun7 I ti7 Iu5-thai3 kap Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 e5 su7-cheng5, sit8-chai7 in long2 bo5 sim2-mih8 kong2-khi2, chi2 u7 Ia5-sou beh chiuN7 Ia5-lou7-sat-leng2 hou7 lang5 teng3, hit-si5 in chiah u7 te3 in e5 Sian-siN lai5 kong2 kau3 hit cham7 e5 su7.  In long2 si7 tui3 siang7 chit8 tiam2 chhut-hoat lai5 kong2-khi2 in e5 kou3-su7, kong2, “Ia5-sou thiaN-kiN3 Iok-han7 koaiN-kaN, chiu7 the3-khi3 Ka-li7-li7.”  In-ui7 “Chu2 i2-keng chai Hoat-li7-sai3 lang5 thiaN-kiN3 Ia5-sou chio-tioh8 hak8-seng, pi2 Iok-han7 khah choe7.”  Chit-ku3-oe7 e5 i3-su3, si7 hian2-beng5 Ia5-sou chai Hoat-li7-sai3 lang5 i2-keng teh tng-tan2 I, ia7 chai I un2-tang3 oe7 liam5-piN hou7 in liah8 tioh8.  Che su7-sit8 si7 bo5 hap8-gi5 ti7 I e5 ke3-ek8.  I sui-jian5 si7 tioh8 siu7-liah8 hou7 lang5 koaiN-kaN, soa3 siu7 lang5 hai7 si2.  Chong2-si7 ti7 chit e5 si5-chun7, I si7 boe7 thang seng5-siu7 hit-ho7 e5 tai7-chi3.  In-ui7 I e5 si5 iau2-be7 kau3.
Sou2-i2 I u7 pang3-sak tiam3 ti7 Iu5-thai3 e5 soaN-kan hit e5 khoai3-lok8 e5 thoan5-kau3 e5 su7-giap8, lai5 li7-khui Iu5-thai3, keng-ke3 Sat-ma2-li7-a lai5 chiuN7 khi3 Ka-li7-li7.  Chong2-si7 lan2 iau2-be7 chin3-cheng5 lai5 te3 I chiuN7 khi3 Ka-li7-li7 e5 tai7-seng, ai3 tiap-a2(**tiap8-a2)-ku2 theng5 ti7-chia saN-kap lai5 siuN7 KiaN5 soe2-le2 e5 Iok-han7 e5 choe3-au7.

Chit e5 ou-am3 e5 iau3-sai3, si7 put-chi2 iau3-kin2 teh po2-hou7 lam5-peng5 Pa-lek8-su-theng3 e5 sou2-chai7.  Chit e5 iau3-sai3 si7 chit8 e5 chhiN-chhin3, im-ut, koh si7 eng7 ou-sek e5 he2-soaN-chioh8 sou2 kian3-tiok e5 siaN5-lui2, si7 u7 hian2-chhut u7 chit ho7 sou2-chai7, chiah oe7 thang phah-phoa3 chhin-chhiuN7 Iok-han7 hit ho7 e5 lang5 e5 cheng-sin5.  I si7 ho2-taN2 tui3 Hoat-li7-sai3(##lang5), i2-kip8 tui3 che3-si lai5 kan-cheng3 chin-li2 e5 oe7; ia7 siat-su2 ong5 u7 kiaN5-im5, i ma7 si7 ho2-taN2 kong-jian5 lai5 kan-cheng3 i e5 put-si7.  Chit e5 koaiN3-si3 chu7-iu5 e5 KiaN5 soe2-le2 e5 Iok-han7 u7 siu7 koaiN ti7 chit e5 kaN-lai7, lai5 keng-ke3 hit e5 tng5-tng5 iam7-jiat8 e5 he7-thiN.  Hi-lut8 e5 ong5-kiong si7 khi2 ti7 i sou2 tiam3 hit e5 soaN-teng2.  Ti7 Si2-hai2 e5 hit peng5, i u7 khoaN3-kiN3 cha2-si5 choe3 gin2-na2 sou2 bat thit-tho5 e5 kong-keng2, i2-kip8 khong3-ia2, chiu7-si7 i bat ti7 hia chhut-lat8 lai5 sam3-su Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 su7, lai5 bong7-siong2 Hit e5 sou2 beh lai5 e5 Bi2-sai3-a, i2-kip8 Siong7-te3 kok e5 ng3-bang7.  I chit-tiap8 u7 teh thou2-khui3, teh ki5-koai3, ai3 ah, hit e5 Ong5 kok khoaN3-liau2 thai3 oe7 hiah-nih8 ban7 le3(**leh)!  I sou2 siau7-kai3 e5 Bi2-sai3-a, i2-kip8 ti7 Iok-tan3 ho5 lai5 hioh ti7 Ia5-sou e5 teng2-bin7 hit e5 Seng3 e5 chiN2-a2, taN si7 an3-choaN2?
Cha2-si5 lai5 te3 i e5 hak8-seng, khiok u7 siong5-siong5 lai5 kaN-nih8 hong2-bun7 i, soa3 toa3 goa7-bin7 choe7-choe7 e5 siau-sit lai5 hou7 i chai-iaN2.  Chong2-si7 i sou2 khoa3-sim, sou2 ai3 chai e5, tok8-tok8 si7 koan-he7 i e5 Chu2 e5 siau-sit na7-tiaN7.  Iok-han7 e5 hak8-seng tng Iok-han7 siu7 koaiN liau2-au7, si7 long2 si3-soaN3 liau2-liau2.  Chiong5-tiong khiok u7-e5 u7 thiaN Iok-han7 e5 kan-cheng3 lai5 te3 Ia5-sou kau3 ti7 Ka-li7-li7 e5 sou2-chai7.  M7-ku2 in e5 sim put-tan7 si7 be5-loan7 na7-tiaN7, soa3 put-chi2 sit-bang7.  In-ui7 in long2 bo5 tu2-tioh8 hit ho7 oe7 kam2-tong7 lang5 e5 su7.  Chit e5 Bi2-sai3-a Ia5-sou to long2 bo5 hian2-chhut I e5 koan5-peng3, ma7 si7 bo5 hian2-jian5 piau2-chhut sim2-mih8 khoan2 e5 ki3-ho7, lai5 hou7 in khoaN3-kiN3 I u7 i3-su3 ai3 beh hok8-to3 I2-sek-liat8.  In un2-tang3 beh khi3 ka7 Iok-han7 kong2, Ia5-sou khiok u7 si3-koe3 kiaN5 ti7 cheng3-lang5 e5 tiong-kan, ia7 u7 chin toa7-tin7 e5 lang5 teh chiu7-kun7 I, lai5 chu3-i3 I e5 oe7, chong2-si7 I thai3 oe7 long2 bo5 koan-sim ti7 I sou2 kau-poe5 e5 lang5 e5 phin2-seng3, tui3 an2-ni Hoat-li7-sai3 lang5 u7 thi2-chhio3 I si7 “thiu-hiong3 e5, i2-kip8 choe7-jin5 e5 peng5-iu2.”
Iu7-koh in ma7 un2-tang3 oe7 ka7 IOk-han7 kong2, Ia5-sou sou2 ka3-si7 peh-siN3 e5 oe7, long2 si7 tan-sun5 e5 ka3-si7, long2 si7 soe3-soe3 e5 kou3-su7 i2-kip8 phi2-ju7 liau2-liau2.  Lan2 u7 thak8 tioh8 kong2, bat u7 chit8 jit8 in khoaN3-kiN3 Ia5-sou kiaN5 chit8 e5 toa7-toa7 thang chhiN-kiaN e5 su7, chiu7-si7 hou7 Na2-in e5 chiu2-koaN2 hu7-jin5-lang5 e5 kiaN2 tui3 si2 koh-oah8, hit-si5 “Iok-han7 e5 hak8-seng chiong chiah e5 su7 long2-chong2 po3 in e5 sian-siN chai.”
Chit e5 iong2-kam2 thiam5-cheng7 e5 siu5-jin5 Iok-han7, u7 soe3-ji7 aN3 hi7-khang lai5 thiaN, lai5 siuN7, chhim-chhim teh sam3-su i sou2 thiaN-kiN3 e5 long2-chong2 e5 su7-sit8.
Iok-han7 e5 hak8-seng, ki5-sit8 si7 bo5 sim2-mih8 chai-iaN2 Iok-han7 am3-am3 ti7 sim-lai7 sou2 teh kan-khou2 e5 su7.  Ke3 bo5 loa7-ku2, lan2 u7 thiaN-kiN3 i u7 lou7-chhut chit8 e5 chin thang ki5-koai3 pi3-bit8 e5 cheng5-heng5.  Chit ho7 cheng5-heng5, na7 m7-si7 u7 Seng3-chheh thang choe3 lan2 e5 kun-ku3, lan2 un2-tang3 si7 oh-tit sin3 e5 su7.

Lan2 tiap-a2(**tiap8-a2)-ku2 ai3 chin3-cheng5, oaN7 lai5 saN-kap siuN7 Ia5-sou khi3 ti7 Ka-li7-li7 e5 cheng5-keng2.  Ti7 hiah e5 teh kun-te3 Ia5-sou e5 cheng3-lang5 e5 tiong-kan, u7 khoaN3-kiN3 nng7 e5 bin7-mau7 ia3-sian7, iu-bun7 e5 lang5, u7 hian2-chhut kiaN5 hng7 lou7 ia3-lan2 e5 khoan2-sit.  In kiaN5 oa2-lai5 e5 si5, Ia5-sou u7 oat8-lin3-tng2 lai5 chih-chiap in.  In theng5 tiap-a2(**tiap8-a2)-ku2, chiu7 tui3 Ia5-sou kong2-chhut in e5 sim-lai7 sou2 u7 it-chhe3 teh kan-khou2 e5 bun7-toe5.
“Goan2 e5 sian-siN, KiaN5 soe2-le2 e5 Iok-han7, u7 chhe goan2 lai5 chheng2-kau3 Li2, kong2, Sou2 beh lai5 e5 si7 li2 mah? a2-si7 goan2 tioh8 ng3-bang7 pat8 lang5 ah?”
“Sou2 beh lai5 e5 si7 li2 mah?”  ChhiaN2 lan2 tiap-a2(**tiap8-a2)-ku2 lai5 siuN7 chit tiam2!  Cha2 hit e5 teh soan-thoan5 Ki-tok e5 Iok-han7 chit-tiap8 u7 teh giau5-gi5 I!  Chhi3 siuN7 chit e5 kou3-su7 si7 bo5 chng-thaN7, seng5-sit8, tan-sun5 kau3 chaiN2-iuN7?  Chhi3 siuN7, chit e5 lang5 hiah-nih8 ti3-i3 chhe lang5 lai5 mng7 hit e5 bun7-toe5, tau3-ti2 ti7 i e5 giau5-gi5 e5 sim, u7 kan-khou2 kau3 chaiN2-iuN7?
Tui3 chit e5 tai7-chi3, lan2 beh chaiN2-iuN7 lai5 kong2-khi2?  Iok-han7 kiam2 si7 loan2-jiok8 e5 lang5 mah?  Kiam2 thang kong2 Iok-han7 si7 i2-keng long2 sit-loh8 sin3-giong2, ia7 bo5 kau3-giah8 oe7 kham-tit choe3 Ki-tok e5 sian-hong mah?  Ai3 ah!  M7-si7 lah!  Na7-si7 siuN7 an2-ni e5 lang5, si7 bo5 chit8-sut-a2 chai-bat lang5 tiam3 ti7 giau5-gi5 e5 sim-li2, iah8 si7 be7 the2-thiap lang5 e5 sin3-giong2, tu2-tioh8 io5-tang7 e5 si5, ti7 sim-sin5 sou2 keng-giam7 e5 chhiN-chham2.
Lan2 tioh8 oe7 ki3 tit, kui2-na7 geh8-jit8 ku2, Iok-han7 u7 hou7 lang5 koaiN ti7 hit e5 joah8 koh im-ut e5 kaN-lai7.  I e5 sim-seng3 si7 khoai3 io5-tang7.  Chit-tiap8 i e5 cheng-sin5 put-chi2 kin2-tiuN.  Lian5 hit ho7 te7-it chhim-o3 e5 chong-kau3, to si7 oh-tit chin2-kiu3 hit ho7 lang5 e5 sin3-giong2, lai5 bo5 siuN7-tioh8 hit e5 Ma2-kai3-ni2-su (Machaerus) e5 ou-am3 e5 kaN-gak8 e5 kan-khou2.  Siat-su2 i e5 sim-koaN-thau5 u7 chheng-chhai2, chiu7 oe7 thiaN-tioh8 Sin-kiaN2-sai3 hoaN-hi2 e5 siaN.  Chong2-si7 i iu5-goan5 u7 bo5 chheng-chhai2 e5 jit8 ti7-teh.  In-ui7 Iok-han7 u7 teh liau5-bang7 ti7 be7 si2 e5 tai7-seng oe7 thang khoaN3-kiN3 i it-seng e5 ng3-bang7 tit-tioh8 sit8-hian7.  M7-ku2 Ia5-sou e5 heng5-tong7 si7 kau3-giah8 ban7.  Ti7 Iok-han7 e5 si5-tai7, chhin-chhiuN7 ti7 lan2 kin2-a2-jit8, tak8 pai2 Siong7-te3 u7 ban7-ban7 lai5 chiaN5 I e5 chi2-i3 e5 si5, lang5 e5 sin3-giong2 eng2-eng2 oe7 siu7 toa7 e5 chhi3-giam7.
Chai7 chit e5 ui2-tai7, kou-tok8 e5 sim-sin5, ti7 i e5 it-seng to long2 si7 khng3 sian-kian3 e5 iN7-siong7 lai5 teh keng-ke3 i e5 jit8-chi2, iau2-ku2 kau3 ti7 choe3-au7 beh si2 e5 si5, i e5 sim-lai7 kou-put-chiong tioh8 khng3 giau5-gi5 e5 liam7-thau5, che sng3 m7-si7 sio2-khoa2 su7.
Put-koan2 siaN2-khoan2, ti7 hit ho7 si5-chun7, na7 u7 peng5-iu2 chhin-chhiuN7 Ia5-sou e5 khoan2, thang hou7 lan2 tui3 I tin5-cheng5 lan2 e5 khou2-sim, si7 chin-chiaN3 ban7-heng7 e5 su7.  Ah!  Ia5-sou sit8-chai7 si7 u7 liau2-kai2 lang5 e5 sim.  Ia5-sou put-si5 to oe7 liau2-kai2 lang5 e5 sim.  Ia5-sou si7 bat siu7-chhi3, sou2-i2 I u7 beng5-pek8 lang5 tiam3-ti7 hit ho7 hoan5-bun7 e5 si5, cheng-sin5 e5 kan-khou2 kau3 chaiN2-iuN7.  tui3 an2-ni I u7 hou7 in tng2-khi3 , kio3 in thang ka7 I e5 kho2-lin5 e5 lou5-pok8 Iok-han7 thoan5 ho2 e5 siau-sit, hou7 i thang beng5-pek8 in siong5-siong5 sou2 teh liau5-bang7 hit e5 chhan3-lan7 e5 chham3-gu2, si7 i2-keng sit8-hian7.  “Lin2 tioh8 khi3, chiong lin2 sou2 thiaN-kiN3 sou2 khoaN3-kiN3 e5, ka7 Iok-han7 kong2, chiu7-si7 chhiN-mi5 e5 khoaN3-kiN3, pai2-kha e5 kiaN5, thai2-ko e5 chheng-khi3, chhau3-hi7-lang5 e5 thiaN-kiN3, si2 e5 lang5 koh-oah8, song3-hiong lang5 tit-tioh8 thiaN Hok-im.”
Iok-han7 thiaN-liau2 siaN2-khoan2, lan2 khiok long2 bo5 thiaN-kiN3 an3-choaN2.  Iau2-ku2 lan2 thang phah-sng3 Iok-han7 un2-tang3 u7 tit-tioh8 sin-sin e5 iong2-khi3 kap ng3-bang7 chiah tioh8.  Toa7-bin7 i u7 kian3-siau3 i u7 khng3 hit ho7 giau5-gi5 e5 sim, ia7 soa3 kam2-kak-tioh8 pun2-sin ti7 Chu2 e5 bin7-cheng5 u7 sit-loh8 i e5 chu-keh ia7 ku2 kaN2.  Lan2 chin hi-bong7 ti7 i be7 si2 e5 tai7-seng, u7 lang5 beh khi3 ka7 i kong2-khi2 tng hiah e5 su3-chia2 khi3 e5 si5, Ia5-sou u7 chaiN2-iuN7 the5 khi2 i e5 su7 lai5 o-lo2 kong2, “Hu7-jin5-lang5 sou2 siN e5, chiong5-tiong be7 u7 heng-khi2 khah toa7 ti7 KiaN5 soe2-le2 e5 Iok-han7.”
Chhi3-siuN7 Siong7-te3 e5 KiaN2, I e5 sim khong2-khai3 kau3 chaiN2-iuN7!  Lan2 tioh8 oe7 ki3-tit Iok-han7 tu2-tu2 ka-ki7 teh kian3-siau3 e5 si5, Ia5-sou u7 chheng-chan3 chit e5 kho2-lin5 e5 lou5-pok8, soa3 ai3 lan2 cheng7-cheng7 ti7 lan2 e5 sim-lai7 ka-ki7 siuN7 kong2, tak8 pai2 goa2 u7 kian3-siau3 ka-ki7 e5 chho3-gou7 e5 si5, siat-su2 goa2 na7 u7 sim2-mih8 kho2-chhu2, goa2 sin3 I ma7-si7 un2-tang3 beh kong2-khi2 goa2 e5 kho2-chhu2 nouh!
Lan2 na7-si7 seng5-sit8 sim teh giau5-gi5, teh be5-loan7 sim2-mih8, koat-toan3 m7-bian2 kiaN-liau2 Ia5-sou chai-iaN2.  Lan2 na7-si7 kan-ta boan2-chiok giau5-gi5 e5 sim, chiu7 u7 toa7-toa7 chho3-gou7 ti7-teh.  Lan2 na7-si7 u7 tu2-tioh8 sim2-mih8 boe7-thang sin3-tit e5 su7, chu7-jian5 lan2 si7 ai3 giau5-gi5 i, i2-goa7 bo5 pat8-mih8 hoat-tou7!  Chong2-si7 lan2 tioh8 m7-thang chu7 an2-ni put-si5 khng3 giau5-gi5 e5 sim.  Che si7 u7 bo5 li7-ek e5 sou2-chai7 ti7-teh.  Lan2 tioh8 tui3 lan2 e5 ho2 koh gau5 e5 peng5-iu2 lai5 tin5-cheng5.  Siat-su2 lan2 na7 khoaN3 lan2 e5 bok8-su oe7 kham-tit hou7 lan2 thang hoat-piau2 lan2 e5 kan-khou2, lan2 tioh8 tui3 i lai5 kong2-khi2.  Chong2-si7 siang7 te7-it ho2, chiu7-si7 tui3 lan2 e5 Chu2 lai5 ki5-to2.  Lan2 tioh8 eng7 sut-tit8 bo5 un2-moa5, iu7-koh bo5 kiaN-hiaN5 lan2 e5 sim-cheng5.  Lang5 na7-si7 oe7 thang chhin-chhiuN7 KiaN5 soe2-le2 e5 Iok-han7 e5 khoan2, chiong lan2 sou2 teh giau5-gi5 e5 bun7-toe5 theh8 lai5 ti7 Ki-tok e5 bin7-cheng5, lan2 e5 sin3-giong2, tek-khak si7 boe7 sim2-mih8 chho3-gou7 khi3.
Chit-tiap8 chit e5 kho2-lin5 e5 siu5-jin5 Iok-han7, lian5 i e5 lim5-chiong e5 jit8 to i2-keng pek-oa2 ti7 bin7-cheng5, ma7 iu5-goan5 long2 bo5 kiaN-hiaN5, hoan2-tng2 si7 eng7 sin-seng e5 sin3-giong2 lai5 teh gim5 tek-seng3 li7-piat8 e5 koa.  I e5 lim5-chiong e5 jit8, si7 put-chi2 pek-oa2 lah.  Chong2-si7 i iau2-be7 lim5-chiong e5 tai7-seng, tek-khak u7 tit-tioh8 chit8 e5 ki5-koai3 e5 keng-giam7 chiah tioh8.  Chiu7-si7 u7 chit8-jit8 Hi-lut8 bat lai5 hong2-bun7 i, ti3-kau3 hou7 i put-chi2 chhiN-kiaN.  Iu7-koh u7 chit8-jit8, Hi-lut8 ia7 u7 chhe lang5 khi3 chhiaN2 Iok-han7 lai5 ong5-kiong kap i kong2-oe7.  In nng7 lang5 u7 khah sio-bat.  Chit e5 Hi-lut8 ong5 si7 khah ki5-koai3 e5 lang5, i u7 tui3 chiong2-chiong2 e5 seng3-chit lai5 kiat-chiaN5 chit8 e5 jin5-keh-tek e5 seng-oah8, chiu7-si7 ti7 i e5 seng-oah8 tiong, lan2 chit8-bin7 si7 oe7 thang khoaN3 chhut i e5 ia2-phi2, kan-cha3, houN3-sek kap chan5-jim2, ia7 koh chit8-bin7 ma7-si7 oe7 thang khoaN3 chhut i e5 ho2--chhu3 ti7-teh.  U7-iaN2!  Lan2 koat-toan3 be7-bat thiaN-kiN3 kong2 u7 sim2-mih8 lang5 choan(**choan5)-jian5 phaiN2 kau3 lian5 chit8-sut-a2 e5 ho2 to bo5.  Siong7-te3 u7 chhong3-cho7 lang5, khoan2-sit chhin-chhiuN7 I.  Sou2-i2 sui-jian5 lan2 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 sim2-mih8 lang5 sit8-chai7 si7 chin-chiaN3 phaiN2, iau2-ku2 hit e5 lang5 ma7 bo5 choan5-jian5 phaiN2, ma7 iau2 u7 chit8-sut-a2 e5 ho2--chhu3 chiah tioh8.  Siong7-te3 sou2 hoaN-hi2 ai3 po2-chun5 e5, chiu7-si7 tok8-tok8 chit e5 ho2 e5 tiam2.
Ti7 chit e5 Hi-lut8 khiok-si7 bo5 u7 loa7-choe7 e5 ho2--chhu3 ti7-teh.  I e5 ka-teng5 e5 lek8-su2 si7 bo5 kah loa7-nih8 ho2 thiaN.  I sou2 u7 e5 khoan5-keng2 si7 phaiN2.  Put-ko3 kiam2-chhai2 lan2 thang kong2 si7 bo5 long2-chong2 phaiN2.  Tu2-tu2 chit-chun7 lan2 khiok u7 khoaN3-kiN3 chit e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 lian5-lui7 i e5 seng-oah8, ti3-kau3 ham7-loh8 choe7-koa3, chong2-si7 ti7 khah-cha2, lan2 ma7-si7 iu5-goan5 u7 khoaN3-tioh8 chit8 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 u7 the5-ko i e5 jin5-keh.  Hit e5 u7 the5-ko i e5 jin5-keh e5 hu7-jin5-lang5, khiok m7-si7 i e5 lau7-bu2.  Lan2 u7 thak8 tioh8 Su3-tou5 Heng(**Heng5)-toan7 e5 chit8 cham7, chiu7-si7 teh pai5-liat8 An-the5-o e5 kau3-hoe7 hiah e5 khah tiong7-iau3 e5 kau3-chit-chia2 e5 mia5 pio2, ti7-hia u7 kong2, “kap hun-hong e5 jin5-kun Hi-lut8 tang5 poe5-iuN2 e5 Ma2-liam7.”  Chit e5 su7-sit8 si7 hou7 lan2 put-chi2 ki5-koai3, an3-choaN2 chit e5 pi-chian7 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 lai5 poe5-iuN2 chit nng7 e5 gin2-na2, au7-lai5 chit8 e5 oe7 chiaN5-choe3 kiaN5-im5 e5, chan5-jim2 e5, thai5 lang5 e5; koh chit8 e5 oe7 chiaN5-choe3 jiat8-jiat8 lai5 thoan5 Ki-tok e5 Hok-im e5 lang5.  Lan2 thang siuN7 ti7 chit e5 Hi-lut8 ong5 sou2 u7 tam7-poh8 e5 ho2--chhu3, kiam2 m7-si7 tui3 i e5 ni-bu2 lai5 tit-tioh8 e5 mah?
Hi-lut8 ong5 sim-lai7 si7 u7 him-bou7 Iok-han7, u7 siu7 Iok-han7 kam2-hoa3.  Hi-lut8 ong5 e5 liong5-sim si7 u7 siu7-tioh8 Iok-han7 e5 kam2-tong7.  In-ui7 lan2 u7 thak8-tioh8 kong2, Hi-lut8 ong5 u7 hoaN-hi2 thiaN Iok-han7 e5 oe7, iah8 u7 ui7-tioh8 Iok-han7 kiaN5 choe7-choe7 hang7 e5 su7.  Chhin-chhiuN7 Ma2-kho2 u7 ki3-chai3 kong2, Hi-lut8 ong5 liah8 Iok-han7 khi3 koaiN-kaN, si7 u7 khng3 chit8 hang7 e5 bok8-tek, ai3 chin2-kiu3 Iok-han7 thoat-li7 Lu2-ong5 Hi-lo5-ti2 e5 chan5-jim2 e5 ke3-bou5.  In-ui7 Hi-lo5-ti2 teh oan3-hun7 Iok-han7, tu2-tu2 si7 chhin-chhiuN7 hit ho7 siu7 bu2-jiok8 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 teh oan3-hun7 lang5 e5 khoan2-sit.  Siat-su2 na7 oe7 eng7-tit kong2, ti7 chit se3-kan si7 bo5 lang5 oe7 chhin-chhiuN7 hu7-jin5-lang5 e5 gau5 thiaN3 lang5, ma7-si7 iu5-goan5 oe7 eng7-tit kong2, bo5 lang5 oe7 chhin-chhiuN7 hu7-jin5-lang5 e5 gau5 oan3-hun7 lang5.  U7 chit8 ku3 siok8-gu2 teh kong2, “Ti7 toe7-gek8 bo5 u7 siu7-khi3, chhin-chhiuN7 siu7 bu2-jiok8 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 sou2 hoat e5 siu7-khi3.”  Chit e5 Hi-lo5-ti2 si7 bat kap phaiN2-lang5 saN-kap kiong7-bou5 lai5 hai7-si2 i e5 thau5 chit8 e5 tiong7-hu.  Ia7 Hi-lut8 ong5 choe3 lang5-kheh khi3 in tau e5 si5, Hi-lo5-ti2 chiu7 i2-keng u7 kap i su-thong.  Hi-lut8 ong5 sou2 chhoa7 hit e5 siau3-lian5 e5 A-lat-pek e5 hu7-jin5-lang5, thiaN-tioh8 chit e5 cheng5-heng5, chiu7 chau2 tng2-khi3 in au7-thau5-chhu3 lau7-pe7 e5 sou2-chai7, tui3 an2-ni hou7 Hi-lo5-ti2 i2-kip8 cheng3 kiong-lai7 e5 lang5 long2 chai-iaN2 chit e5 iong2-kam2 e5 sian-ti Iok-han7 u7 kong-jian5 tui3 i e5 tiong7-hu Hi-lut8 kan-cheng3 i e5 put-si7, kong2, “Li2 chhoa7 hiaN-ti7 e5 bou2 si7 put-kai,”  Na7-si7 koan-he7 cheng3-gi7, Iok-han7 lian5 chit8-sut-a2 to bo5 kiaN si7 kun-ong5 a2-si7 lu2-ong5 e5 se3-lek8.  Chong2-si7 Hi-lo5-ti2 koat-toan3 bo5 boe7 ki3-tit Iok-han7.  I u7 si5-siong5 koan-sim teh theng3-hau7 i e5 ho2 ki-hoe7 kau3.

Ke3 saN geh8-jit8 au7, Hi-lo5-ti2 u7 tu2-tioh8 chit8 e5 ho2 e5 ki-hoe7, chiu7-si7 Hi-lut8 ong5 e5 siN-jit8.  Hit-jit8 ong5-kiong lai7 hit e5 chong3-koan e5 thiaN-tng5, u7 ui-gi5 hian2-hek, Hi-lut8 ong5 u7 chiau-thai7 choe7-choe7 e7 eng5-hian2 e5 lang5-kheh, chiu7-si7 u7 toa7-koaN, chhian-chong2, i2-kip8 Ka-li7-li7 e5 chun-kui3 e5 lang5, lai5 hu3 i e5 ian5-siah8.  Mi5 na2 chhim, chiu2-sek8 na2 jiat8-nau7.  Lian5 tiam3 ti7 soaN e7 gak8-lai7 e5 siu5-jin5 to oe7 thang thiaN-kiN3 hit e5 im-gak8, i2-kip8 soan-jiang2 e5 siaN.  Hit am3 Hi-lo5-ti2, tng cheng3-lang5-kheh put-chi2 khoai3-lok8 e5 si5; u7 hou7 i e5 sui2-sui2 e5 cha-bou2-kiaN2 Sat-lo5-bi2 lai5 chiap-thai7 lang5-kheh, soa3 ti7 in e5 bin7-cheng5 thiau3-bu2, u7 put-chi2 kam2-kak cheng3-lang5, tit-tioh8 toa7 e5 hat-chhai2.  Sat-lo5-bi2 chiau3 lan2 sou2 khoaN3 si7 chit8 e5 koe3-thau5 chu7-iu5 e5 cha-bou2 gin2-na2.  I e5 thiau3-bu2 si7 kek8-ki5 e5 kha2-biau7, oe7 giu2 lang5 e5 ngou2-koan, si7 hiah e5 toan-cheng3 e5 Iu5-thai3 lang5 sou2 m7-kaN2 khoaN3--e5.  chong2-si7 cheng3 lang5-kheh si7 put-chi2 ai3 khoaN3 i e5 sui2-sui2 e5 se3-bin7; tai7-ke long2 toa7-toa7 hat-chhai2.  Hit-si5 Hi-lut8 ong5 si7 i2-keng poaN3 chui3, khoaN3-liau2 sim-koaN put-chi2 hoaN-hi2 khoai3-lok8, chiu7 ti7 cheng3 lang5-kheh e5 bin7-cheng5, tui3 cha-bou2-gin2-na2 chiu3-choa7 kong2, KiN3-na7 li2 sou2 kiu5 goa2--e5, sui-jian5 goa2 e5 kok e5 chit8-poaN3, goa2 ia7 beh hou7 li2.
Chit e5 cha-bou2 gin2-na2 thiaN-liau2 sim-lai7 put-chi2 hun7-loan7; chiu7 chau2 chhut-khi3 kap i e5 lau7-bu2 chham-siong5.  Au7-lai5 i liam5-piN koh chau2 jip8-lai5 kiN3 hiah e5 toa7-siaN teh han2-hoa7 e5 lang5-kheh, hit-si5 i e5 bak8-chiu u7 hian2-chhut chin koh-iuN7 koh chhiN-kiaN e5 gan2 kong.  Sou2-i2 in chiu7 tiam7-tiam7 bo5 koh phah-chhiu2, ma7 bo5 koh toa7-siaN lai5 han2-hoa7.  Cheng3 chiu2-chui3 e5 lang5 u7 hian2-chhut keng2-seng2 e5 bin7-sek, lai5 thiaN chit e5 siau3-lian5 cha-bou2 gin2-na2 eng7 hiang2-liang7 e5 siaN, sou2 teh iau-kiu5 hit e5 chan5-jim2 e5 su7, kong2, “Goa2 ai3 li2 chiong KiaN5 soe2-le2 Iok-han7 e5 thau5-khak toe2 ti7 poaN5-nih8 chek-si5 hou7 goa2.”
In tai7-ke sui-jian5 si7 phaiN2, iau2-ku2 thiaN-liau2 sim-lai7 ma7 oe7 iu-bun7 kian3-siau3.  In tai7-ke chai, chit e5 seng3 e5 sian-ti Iok-han7 si7 cheng3-lang5 sou2 keng3-ai3 e5, iah8 si7 kau3-giah8 chai-iaN2 Hi-lo5-ti2 si7 ui7-tioh8 sim2-mih8 in-toaN lai5 teh iau-kiu5 Iok-han7 e5 thau5-khak.  lian5 hit e5 phang5-poe e5 Hi-lut8 thiaN-liau2 chhiN-kiaN, chiu7 hian2-chhut keng2-seng2 e5 bin7-mau7.  Kiat-kiok8 Hi-lo5-ti2 u7 tit-tioh8 tek-seng3.  Hi-lut8 ong5 u7 ham7-loh8 ti7 i e5 oah8-tauh.  Chit e5 seng3-cheng5 pai7-hoai7 e5 Hi-lut8, si7 iau2 u7 beng5-u7 koan-liam7 ti7-teh, sou2-i2 i be7 thang siam2-pi7 sou2 iok-sok e5 oe7.  “Ong5 chiu7 toa7 iu-bun7; chong2-si7 ui7-tioh8 i sou2 chiu3 e5 choa7, koh u7 tang5-toh e5 lang5 ti7-teh, sou2-i2 m7 ai3 the-si5.  Ong5 chiu7 chek-si5 chhe chit8 e5 si7-oe7, hoan-hu3 i khi3 kaN-nih8, thai5 i e5 thau5-khak.”
“Ong5 chiu7 toa7 iu-bun7.”  Si7 lah, chong2-si7 ti7 au7-lai5 Hi-lut8 ong5 u7 it-hoat iu-bun7 kan-khou2, si7 ui7-tioh8 i u7 thiaN-kiN3 cheng3-lang5 long2 teh chiu3-chou2 i.  “In-ui7 cheng3-lang5 long2 liah8 Iok-han7 choe3 sian-ti.”  Hit e5 chhui-pek i lai5 thiaN Iok-han7 e5 oe7, ia7 chhui-pek i kiaN5 choe7-choe7 ho2-su7 e5 liong5-sim, u7 hou7 i khoaN3-kiN3 te7-gek8 e5 chhiN-chham2 kau3 hian7-hian7.  Bo5 lun7 si7 chhiN2, a2-si7 khun3, i put-si5 to chu-chu teh su-siong2 Iok-han7 e5 su7.  Hit e5 bak choe7-choe7 huih e5 si2 e5 bin7, tui3 hit-si5 khi2 put-si5 u7 hian2-chhut ti7 i e5 bak8-chiu-cheng5.  Ke3 bo5 loa7-ku2, i u7 thiaN-tioh8 Ia5-sou teh kiaN5 sin5-jiah, hit-si5 i e5 liong5-sim u7 chhui-pek i hoat-chhut chit8-cheng2 be5-sin3 e5 kiaN-sim lai5 au5-kio3 kong2, “KiaN5 soe2-le2 Iok-han7 tui3 si2-lang5 tiong koh-oah8!”  Sui-jian5 si7 u7 pat8 lang5 tui3 i kong2, I kiam2-chhai2 si7 I2-li7-a, a2-si7 sian-ti lang5 e5 chit8-e5; iau2-ku2 i ma7 si7 m7 sin3, koh au5-kio3 kong2, “Bo5, i si7 Iok-han7 lah.  Goa2 sou2 thai5-thau5 e5 Iok-han7 i2-keng koh-oah8.  In-ui7 i u7 tui3 si2-lang5 tiong koh-oah8, sou2 i2 u7 chiah e5 koan5-leng5 tui3 i hian2-chhut!”
Hi-lut8 ong5 e5 siu7 bu2-jiok8 e5 liong5-sim u7 chek-pi7 i kau3 chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni.
Chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni, kiat-kiok8 ti7 chit8 e5 geh8-kng mi5, Hi-lut8 ong5 sou2 chhe e5 si7-oe7 u7 lai5 kaN-nih8 hong2-bun7 Iok-han7, hit-si5 Iok-han7 chiah thiaN-kiN3 i e5 the3-un2 e5 ho7-thau5.  Si7-oe7 u7 chiong hit e5 iau2 teh lau5 huih e5 thau5-khak lai5 toe2 ti7 poaN5-nih8, phang5 lai5 ti7 cheng3-lang5-kheh e5 bin7-cheng5; ia7 cha-bou2 gin2-na2 chiu7 phang5 hit e5 thang chhiN-chhin3 e5 seng3-li7-phin2 khi3 hou7 i e5 lau7-bu2.  Iok-han7 e5 hak8-seng thiaN-kiN3, chiu7 lai5 siu hit e5 bo5 thau5 e5 sin-si khi3 bai5-chong3 ti7 bong7-nih8, ia7 “to3-lai5 chiong in sou2 kiaN5 e5 pai5-liat8 hou7 Ia5-sou thiaN.”  Chhin-chhiuN7 an2-ni, chit e5 iong2-kam2 kou-tok8 e5 sian-ti, u7 siu7 chhian-soa2 khi3 ti7 hit e5 Bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 e5 se3-kai3, ti7 hia lai5 theng3-hau7 i e5 Chu2; in-ui7 koh nng7 ni5 au7, hit e5 Seng3-li7 e5 Ki-tok, beh tui3 Sip8-ji7-ke3 tit8-tit8 chhut-hoat khi3 kau3 ti7 hit e5 si2-lang5 e5 se3-kai3, lai5 soan-thoan5 I e5 Hok-im, soa3 lai5 ko-ki2 I e5 chian3-ki5, khia7 I e5 Sip8-ji7-ke3 ti7 hit e5 sin5-pi3 e5 Se3-kai3.  Iok-han7 u7 ti7-hia koh-chai3 chiap-tioh8 “Siong7-te3 e5 IuN5-ko, chiu7-si7 tam-tng se3-kan e5 choe7 e5.”
